### [1] [Track fitting at the full LHC collision rate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14793)
*Pierre Billoir,Thomas Boettcher,Michel De Cian,Lennart H. Uecker*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: LHCb实验在大型强子对撞机Run 3期间采用全软件触发系统，提出了基于参数化卡尔曼滤波器（parameterised Kalman filter）的快速径迹拟合算法，在500块GPU上以仅2%的处理时间增加为代价，显著提升了动量分辨率、不变量质量分辨率和背景抑制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHCb实验在LHC Run 3数据采集前进行了重大升级，采用了全软件触发系统（all-software trigger）。需要在30 MHz的全碰撞频率下实时完成带电粒子轨迹的参数估计，这对算法的计算效率提出了极高要求。

Method: 提出了一种参数化卡尔曼滤波器（parameterised Kalman filter），用解析参数化（analytical parameterisations）替代计算昂贵的磁场图查询（magnetic field map lookups）和数值积分方法，同时保留卡尔曼滤波的数学框架。该算法运行在第一级触发系统的约500块GPU上。

Result: 该算法仅增加2%的处理时间，但显著提升了动量分辨率，使D0和J/ψ强子的不变量质量分辨率（invariant mass resolutions）提升约两倍；同时展现出更强的抗探测器错位（detector misalignment）鲁棒性，并将在标准选择工作点下对偶然本底（accidental background）的剔除能力提升一倍以上，且不损失真实径迹效率。

Conclusion: 参数化卡尔曼滤波器在实时触发环境中成功替代了原有的部分径迹拟合算法（partial track fitting algorithm），在极小的计算开销增加下实现了关键的物理性能提升，为LHCb高频率环境下的在线径迹重建提供了有效方案。

Abstract: The LHCb experiment at the Large Hadron Collider underwent a major upgrade before the LHC Run 3 data taking period, employing an all-software approach in its trigger system. Here we present a fast implementation of a Kalman filter, used in the first trigger stage since the 2025 data taking period, allowing to determine parameter estimates of charged-particle trajectories at the full LHCb collision frequency of 30 MHz. This approach replaces computationally expensive magnetic field map lookups and numerical integration methods with fast analytical parameterisations while maintaining the mathematical framework of Kalman filtering. Implemented on approximately 500 GPUs within the first-level trigger, the algorithm has replaced the previous partial track fitting algorithm in the real-time trigger environment at the cost of a 2% increase in processing time. Compared to the previous fitter this parameterised Kalman filter shows a significantly improved momentum resolution, resulting in a factor of two improvement in the invariant mass resolutions for reconstructed D0 and J/ψ hadrons. It additionally demonstrates greater robustness against detector misalignment effects and substantially sharpens the discrimination between genuine particle trajectories and accidental background, more than doubling the rejection of the latter at no cost to genuine-track efficiency, for a standard selection working point.

</details>


### [2] [A Differential Neutral-to-Charged Current Double-Proton Observable for Studying Short-Range Correlations in Neutrino--Argon Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14942)
*A. Bueno,D. Garcia-Gamez,C. Martin-Morales*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出通过测量中微子-氩反应中中性流与带电流双质子产生率的比率（作为质子对相对动量的函数），来直接探测短程关联（SRC）对双核子发射的贡献，从而首次提供弱相互作用双核子发射同位旋结构的实验探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双核子发射是中微子-原子核相互作用建模中最大的不确定性来源之一，但目前尚无中微子测量能约束其中的短程关联（short-range correlation, SRC）成分。为填补这一空白，需要提出一种可直接探测SRC贡献的实验方案。

Method: 利用带电流（charged-current）反应将丰沛的中子-质子SRC对转化为可观测的质子对，而中性流（neutral-current）反应中质子-质子SRC对的丰度低约20倍，因此SRC贡献可忽略。计算两者双质子产生率的比率，作为质子对相对动量的函数；该比率在高相对动量区域因带电流SRC主导而趋于下降，中性流样本则提供主要由末态相互作用和多核子过程决定的平滑基准。

Result: 模拟预测该比率存在抑制，其幅度与SRC分数成比例。比率中的通量归一化（flux normalization）和关联探测器系统误差（correlated detector systematics）在很大程度上相互抵消，使该测量在现有液氩时间投影室（liquid-argon time projection chamber）中可行。

Conclusion: 该可观测量无需依赖精确的SRC贡献值，即可首次直接实验探测弱相互作用双核子发射的同位旋结构（isospin structure），为中微子-核相互作用建模提供关键约束。

Abstract: Two-nucleon emission is a leading uncertainty in neutrino--nucleus interaction modeling, and no neutrino measurement constrains its short-range-correlation (SRC) component. We propose such a measurement: the ratio of neutral-current to charged-current two-proton production in neutrino--argon interactions as a function of the proton-pair relative momentum. Charged-current interactions convert the abundant neutron--proton SRC pairs into visible proton pairs, whereas neutral-current interactions lack an analogous SRC contribution because proton--proton pairs are about twenty times less abundant. The ratio is therefore predicted to decrease at large relative momentum, where the charged-current SRC contribution dominates, while the neutral-current sample provides a smooth reference determined mainly by final-state interactions and multinucleon processes. Simulations predict a suppression whose magnitude scales with the SRC fraction. Flux normalization and correlated detector systematics largely cancel in the ratio, making the measurement feasible with existing liquid-argon time projection chambers. Independently of the precise SRC contribution, this observable provides the first direct experimental probe of the isospin structure of weak two-nucleon emission.

</details>


### [3] [The study of bulk damage of high gamma-irradiated $n^+$-in-$p$ silicon diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15056)
*M. Mikestikova,P. Federicova,P. Gallus,R. Jirasek,J. Kozakova,J. Kroll,J. Kvasnicka,V. Latonova,I. Mandic,K. Masek,P. Novotny,R. Privara,P. Tuma,I. Zatocilova*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了高总电离剂量伽马辐照（gamma irradiation）对p型硅传感器体损伤（bulk damage）的影响，发现体泄漏电流随总电离剂量线性增加，损伤系数依赖于初始电阻率和氧浓度；有效掺杂浓度和全耗尽电压先显著下降后回升，初始下降归因于受主去除效应（acceptor removal），且未观察到退火效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表征高总电离剂量下伽马辐照对p型硅传感器产生的位移损伤（displacement damage），重点探究泄漏电流、有效掺杂浓度及全耗尽电压随剂量的演化规律。

Method: 采用不同类型n⁺-in-p硅二极管（不同氧浓度和体电阻率），通过二次离子质谱（Secondary-Ion Mass Spectrometry, SIMS）测定氧含量；使用⁶⁰Co伽马源辐照至0.50–8.28 MGy总电离剂量，并在60°C退火80分钟；利用IV/CV特性及瞬态电流技术（Transient Current Technique, TCT）测量全耗尽电压、电场分布和空间电荷符号。

Result: 体泄漏电流随总电离剂量线性增长，损伤系数依赖初始电阻率和氧浓度；有效掺杂浓度与全耗尽电压先随剂量增加显著下降，后在特定剂量处开始回升；未观察到退火效应对泄漏电流和CV特性的影响。

Conclusion: 伽马辐照引起的体损伤行为可通过受主去除效应解释有效掺杂浓度的初始下降；研究结果为高剂量环境下p型硅传感器的辐照损伤机制提供了定量依据。

Abstract: The bulk damage of $p$-type silicon sensors caused by gamma irradiation with high total ionizing doses has been investigated. The study was carried out on different types of $n^+$-in-$p$ silicon diodes with different oxygen concentrations and silicon bulk resistivities. The Secondary-Ion Mass Spectrometry technique was used to determine the relative concentration of oxygen in the individual samples. The measured diodes were irradiated by a $^{60}$Co gamma source to total ionizing doses ranging from 0.50 up to 8.28 MGy, and annealed for 80 minutes at 60°C. The main goal of the study was to characterize the gamma-radiation induced displacement damage by measuring IV and CV characteristics, and the evolution of the full depletion voltage with the total ionizing dose. The Transient Current Technique was used to verify the full depletion voltage and to extract the electric field distribution and the sign of the space charge in the silicon diodes irradiated to the lowest and the highest delivered total ionizing doses.
  The results show a linear increase of the bulk leakage current with the total ionizing dose, with the damage coefficient being dependent on initial resistivity and oxygen concentration of the silicon diode. The effective doping concentration and full depletion voltage decrease significantly with an increasing total ionizing dose, before starting to increase again at a specific dose. We assume that the initial decrease in the effective doping concentration is caused by the effect of acceptor removal. An additional notable finding of this study is that the bulk leakage current and CV characteristics of the gamma-irradiated diodes do not show any evidence of an annealing effect.

</details>

### [4] [Revisiting Data Quality Control and Multiple-star Modeling in Wide Binary Gravity Tests: Confirmation of MOND-type Gravitational Anomaly at Low Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14450)
*Kyu-Hyun Chae,Youngsub Yoon*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过广泛的统计检验（包括加速度平面检验、$\tilde v$分布检验和$\tilde v$中值轮廓检验）重新审视了宽双星系统中的数据质量控制与多星系统建模问题。结果表明，适当的数据质量控制或合理的多星建模变化无法消除低加速度引力异常，反而确认了MOND型引力异常的存在。研究声称未发现低加速度引力异常的结论，是由于未对牛顿区数据中的多星系统比例进行校准、在引力检验中未考虑数据质量控制引入的偏差，或低加速度区统计量不足所致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽双星（wide binary stars）为直接探测低加速度区域的引力行为提供了天然实验室，但近期研究在标准引力与MOND型引力之间产生了矛盾结论，尤其凸显了数据质量控制与多星系统（三体及更高阶）建模的关键作用。本研究旨在系统性地重新审视这些争议性问题，澄清数据质量与多星建模是否足以解释已观测到的低加速度引力异常。

Method: 研究基于宽双星在天球投影上的二维速度（sky-projected 2D velocities），采用三种统计检验方法：加速度平面检验（acceleration-plane test）、$\tilde v$分布检验（$\tilde v$-distribution test）以及$\tilde v$中值轮廓检验（median-$\tilde v$-profile test），其中$\tilde v$为天球二维相对速度与两颗恒星之间牛顿环速之比。

Result: 适当的数据质量控制或合理的多星建模变化无法消除低加速度引力异常（low-acceleration gravitational anomaly），反而确认了MOND型引力异常，这与近期宽双星轨道的真实MOND解（realistic MOND solutions）一致。声称未发现引力异常的结论是以下原因造成的：未利用牛顿区数据校准多星系统比例、引力检验中未考虑数据质量控制引入的偏差，或低加速度区域统计量不足。

Conclusion: 前期声称支持标准引力或无偏离的结论源于方法论的缺陷，而非数据质量或多星建模本身。宽双星数据在低加速度区域确实表现出与MOND型引力相一致的异常，该异常具有稳健性。

Abstract: Wide binary stars provide natural laboratories for directly probing gravity in the low-acceleration regime, as dark matter inferred from any viable gravity has negligible effects on their internal dynamics. Various recent studies including Bayesian 3D analyses have shown that wide binaries with separations greater than several thousand astronomical units experience MOND-type gravity with a boost factor of $γ\approx 1.3-1.6$. However, results claiming preference for, or no deviation from, standard gravity have also been published during the same period, particularly highlighting the roles of data quality control and realistic modeling of multiple-star (i.e., triple and higher-order) systems that host hidden companion stars. Here we carefully reexamine the issues of data quality control and modeling multiple-star systems in statistical gravity tests based on sky-projected 2D velocities of wide binary stars. Through extensive tests including the acceleration-plane test, the $\tilde v$-distribution test, and the median-$\tilde v$-profile test (where $\tilde v$ is the sky-plane 2D relative velocity normalized by the Newtonian circular velocity between the two stars), we show that proper data quality control or reasonable variation in multiple-star modeling cannot remove the low-acceleration gravitational anomaly but confirms the MOND-type gravitational anomaly, particularly consistent with recent realistic MOND solutions of wide binary orbits. We find that studies claiming no evidence for the low-acceleration gravitational anomaly are consequences of bypassed calibration of the fraction of multiple-star systems using the Newtonian-regime data, bias-introduction in data quality control that is not taken into account in gravity tests, or insufficient statistics in the low-acceleration regime.

</details>


### [5] [Relativistic Tidal Transitions of Saturated Kerr Boson Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14627)
*Yi-kun Li*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过数值计算Kerr时空中的准束缚态，发现旋转黑洞周围的超轻玻色子云在潮汐共振跃迁中的相对论性矩阵元与氢原子波函数近似结果差异最高达21.67%，修正量在10%以上时云体99%质量位于轨道间距7%以内，且预测的云体消耗变化最高达13.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋转黑洞可以束缚超轻玻色子形成宏观云体，双星伴星的潮汐场会扫过其能级结构并引发共振跃迁。现有估计大多采用类氢波函数（hydrogenic wave functions），但在云体增长最有效且Kerr几何显著扭曲其准束缚态（quasibound states）时，这种近似可能不够准确。因此需要计算相对论性修正的潮汐跃迁矩阵元。

Method: 对$|211\rangle$、$|322\rangle$和$|433\rangle$三类云体的数值饱和分支（saturation branches）进行了计算。方法结合了Kerr准束缚模式、相对论性双线性归一化（relativistic bilinear normalization）以及Kerr度规的绝热四极扰动（adiabatic quadrupolar perturbation）。覆盖了5个$\Delta m=-2$的跃迁通道，并使用精确牛顿多极矩（Newtonian multipoles）和独立复围道构造对四极矩阵元进行了验证。

Result: 相对论性矩阵元与类氢近似值差异最高达21.67%。当云体99%质量位于轨道间距7%以内时，修正仍超过10%。分量分解显示，78.7%–82.5%的对数变化来自径向模式轮廓（radial mode profile），13.3%–16.2%来自双线性归一化，相对论性潮汐几何贡献较小。在Landau–Zener绝热性（adiabaticity）处于中间区域的共振中，修正后的矩阵元使预测的云体消耗变化最高达13.7%。

Conclusion: 相对论性云体结构对穿过饱和云体共振（saturated-cloud resonances）的双星演化历史具有定量重要性，类氢近似在相关参数区间内存在不可忽略的偏差。

Abstract: Rotating black holes can bind ultralight bosons in macroscopic clouds whose level structure is swept by the tidal field of a binary companion. Existing estimates of the resulting resonant transitions have largely used hydrogenic wave functions, even where the cloud grows most efficiently and the Kerr geometry appreciably deforms its quasibound states. I compute tidal transition matrix elements on the numerically determined saturation branches of the $|211\rangle$, $|322\rangle$, and $|433\rangle$ clouds. The calculation combines Kerr quasibound modes, their relativistic bilinear normalization, and an adiabatic uadrupolar perturbation of the Kerr metric. Across five $Δm=-2$ channels, the relativistic matrix element differs from its hydrogenic value by as much as $21.67\%$. Corrections above $10\%$ persist when $99\%$ of the cloud lies within $7\%$ of the orbital separation. A component-resolved comparison attributes $78.7-82.5\%$ of the logarithmic change to the radial mode profile and $13.3-16.2\%$ to the bilinear normalization; the relativistic tidal geometry supplies a smaller additional correction. Exact Newtonian multipoles and an independent complex-contour construction confirm the quadrupole matrix elements. For resonances with intermediate Landau--Zener adiabaticity, the corrected matrix elements change the predicted cloud depletion by up to $13.7\%$. Relativistic cloud structure is therefore quantitatively important for binary histories that cross saturated-cloud resonances.

</details>

# math.SP [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [The divisor of the twisted Selberg zeta function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14981)
*Moritz Doll,Anke Pohl*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 针对带有限维酉表示（unitary representations）缠绕的几何有限无限面积双曲轨道曲面（geometrically finite infinite-area hyperbolic orbisurfaces），建立了以拉普拉斯共振（Laplace resonances）的魏尔斯特拉斯乘积（Weierstrass product）、Barnes G-函数、伽马函数及表示奇异性度（singularity degrees）表达的塞尔伯格zeta函数（Selberg zeta function）分解公式，并将其推广到具有轨道奇点（orbifold singularities）和酉缠绕的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Borthwick、Judge和Perry先前关于塞尔伯格zeta函数的分解结果推广到更一般的几何与表示设定中，包括双曲轨道曲面上的轨道奇点以及酉缠绕，并解释塞尔伯格zeta函数的零点与极点所对应的谱与几何含义。

Method: 通过建立塞尔伯格zeta函数与拉普拉斯共振、Barnes G-函数、伽马函数以及表示奇异性度之间的分解公式（factorization formula），以魏尔斯特拉斯乘积形式表达。

Result: 得到了一个将塞尔伯格zeta函数的零点和极点解释为轨道曲面及其表示的谱与几何实体的分解公式；该公式同时推广了先前结果至轨道奇点和酉缠绕情形；在无缠绕情形下，轨道奇点也贡献了一个此前未被观测到的分离项。

Conclusion: 所建立的分解公式揭示了塞尔伯格zeta函数的解析结构与其所关联的双曲轨道曲面的拉普拉斯共振及几何奇异性之间的深层联系。

Abstract: For the Selberg zeta function of geometrically finite infinite-area hyperbolic orbisurfaces with twists by finite-dimensional unitary representations, we establish a factorization formula in terms of a Weierstrass product of the Laplace resonances of the considered hyperbolic orbisurface, Barnes G-functions, gamma functions, and the singularity degrees of the representation. We thereby provide an interpretation of the zeros and poles of the Selberg zeta function by spectral and geometric entities of the orbisurface and the representation. This formula generalizes the factorization result by Borthwick, Judge and Perry to hyperbolic orbisurfaces with orbifold singularities as well as to unitary twists. Also in the untwisted case, the presence of orbifold singularities yields a separate, previously unobserved contribution to the factorization formula.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.quant-gas'></div>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Collective dynamics of harmonically trapped 1D quantum droplets under linear gravitational-like confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14969)
*Saurab Das,Jayanta Bera,Ajay Nath*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在一维（1D）扩展Gross-Pitaevskii框架下，研究了二元玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中谐波束缚的量子液滴（quantum droplet）在恒定线性（类引力）势下的动力学。结果表明单极（呼吸）模式频率对线性微扰不敏感，展示了集体激发的鲁棒性；质心（COM）运动则表现出与相互作用相关的输运行为；线性势能在有限时间内可产生具有增强计量灵敏度的量子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超稀量子流体在类引力线性势作用下的集体激发、输运及量子计量特性，探究外场对量子液滴动力学行为的影响。

Method: 基于一维扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation），纳入LHY修正（Lee-Huang-Yang correction），采用分步傅里叶法（split-step Fourier method）进行数值模拟，并结合量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）和Wigner准概率分布（Wigner quasi-probability distribution）表征量子态演化。

Result: 单极（呼吸）模式频率对线性微扰渐近不敏感，质心响应随势阱频率增加单调减小；弱束缚下质心输运显著增强，强束缚则抑制输运；线性势能在有限时间内可产生具有增强计量灵敏度的量子态，且强束缚将高灵敏度区间的阈值推向更大强迫强度。

Conclusion: 线性类引力势对一维超稀量子流体的内部集体激发影响有限，但对质心输运和量子计量特性具有显著的调控作用，揭示了外场调控超冷原子体系中量子态演化的潜在路径。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of harmonically confined quantum droplets in a binary Bose Einstein condensate within the one dimensional extended Gross Pitaevskii framework, including LHY corrections, under a constant linear (gravitational like) potential. By analyzing the COM and width dynamics, we show that the monopole (breathing) mode remains governed by the harmonic confinement, with a frequency asymptotically insensitive to the linear perturbation, demonstrating the robustness of internal collective excitations against uniform external forcing. In contrast, the COM exhibits interaction-dependent transport, with weak confinement producing large susceptibility and rapid displacement, whereas strong confinement suppresses transport even under large forcing. The COM response decreases monotonically with increasing trap frequency. We further characterize the evolving quantum state through the quantum Fisher information and Wigner quasi-probability distributions, showing that the linear potential enables controlled generation of states with enhanced metrological sensitivity over finite times, while stronger confinement shifts the onset of the high-sensitivity regime to larger forcing strengths. Numerical simulations based on the split-step Fourier method confirm the dynamical stability of the obtained solutions. These results illustrate the impact of linear gravitational like trap on the collective excitations, transport, and quantum metrological properties of 1D ultradilute quantum fluids.

</details>


### [8] [Parallel analog quantum simulation in homogeneous quantum gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14977)
*Diego Hernández Rajkov,Alberto Terenzi,Marcia Frómeta Fernández,Nicola Grani,Massimo Inguscio,Giulia Del Pace,Giacomo Roati*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在超冷原子（ultracold atomic gases）平台上实现了一种可独立控制的多路复用量子模拟（multiplexed quantum simulation）配置。通过在单一原子云中分别调控多个量子模拟单元，作者在两组代表性系统中验证了该方法：一是在费米气体超流转变附近制备不同温度的子系统，二是并行模拟具有独立可调参数的约瑟夫森哈密顿量（Josephson Hamiltonian）系统。该方案为强关联超冷物质的动力学与输运哈密顿量的系统研究提供了一种通用途径，并可推广至多种原子种类、几何构型和维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模拟量子计算（analog quantum simulation）是研究经典计算无法处理的强关联量子系统的重要手段。虽然超冷原子气体已被证明是一个高度灵活且可控的平台，但现有方法通常仅能实现单一量子模拟单元的控制，缺乏在同一原子云内对多个独立模拟单元进行分别调控的能力。本文旨在将这种控制水平扩展到多路复用配置，以实现更强的并行性与参数可调性。

Method: 本文基于单一超冷原子云，通过塑造盒型阱（box-trap）势阱并分别控制蒸发冷却（evaporative cooling）轨迹，独立调控多个量子模拟单元。第一组实验中，在幺正费米气体（unitary Fermi gas）的超流转变附近制备不同温度的子系统；第二组实验中，在多个约瑟夫森结量子模拟单元中并行模拟约瑟夫森哈密顿量，每个单元的参数均可独立调节，且具备用于初始化动力学的局域相位控制（local phase control）。

Result: 实验成功实现了两种代表性多路复用量子模拟：一是在跨越超流转变的温度范围内，从同一原子云中制备出不同温度的子系统；二是并行运行多个参数可调的约瑟夫森结量子模拟单元，并实现了局域相位控制以初始化动力学过程。这些结果验证了多路复用配置在超冷原子平台上的可行性与灵活性。

Conclusion: 该多路复用方案为系统研究强关联超冷物质中的动力学和输运哈密顿量提供了通用且可扩展的途径。它可进一步推广至不同的原子种类、势阱几何形状和空间维度，从而大幅拓展模拟量子模拟的实验能力与应用范围。

Abstract: Analog quantum simulation offers a powerful way to study strongly correlated quantum systems that are beyond the reach of classical computation. In this context, ultracold atomic gases have been demonstrated to be an exceptionally versatile and well-controlled platform for implementing various quantum Hamiltonians. In this work, we extend this level of control to a multiplexed configuration in which distinct quantum-simulation units are independently controlled and engineered starting from a single atomic cloud. We demonstrate multiplexed operation in two representative settings. First, by shaping box-trap potentials and separately controlling the evaporative cooling trajectories, we prepare subsystems at various temperatures across the superfluid transition of the unitary Fermi gas. Second, we demonstrate parallel quantum simulation of the Josephson Hamiltonian across distinct Josephson-junction quantum simulation units with individually tunable parameters, including local phase control to initialize the dynamics. Our scheme provides a versatile route toward systematic studies of dynamics and transport Hamiltonians in strongly correlated ultracold matter. Moreover, it is readily extendable to a wide range of atomic species, geometries, and dimensionalities.

</details>


### [9] [A magnetic monopole in a superfluid bubble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15093)
*Marianna Sorba,Andrea Richaud*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究证明，球形超流体外壳（spherical superfluid shell）中的大量量子涡旋（quantum vortices）动力学在形式上等价于球面上带电粒子在磁单极子（magnetic monopole）场中的运动，并以此为基础预言了回旋加速器式的涡旋运动，以及与木星极地多边形气旋簇类似的涡旋项链结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁单极子作为规范场（gauge fields）、拓扑学（topology）、几何相位（geometric phases）和电荷量子化（charge quantization）的交汇点，作为基本粒子仍未被实验发现；作者试图在超流体这一凝聚态体系中实现涌现的狄拉克单极子（emergent Dirac monopole）框架。

Method: 作者通过解析理论建立球形超流体壳中量子涡旋的动力学方程，证明其形式等效于球面上带电粒子在磁单极子场中的运动；单极子电荷由超流密度（superfluid density）固定并自动满足狄拉克量子化条件（Dirac's quantization condition），并通过格罗斯–皮塔耶夫斯基方程（Gross--Pitaevskii equation）数值模拟进行定量验证。

Result: 涌现的单极子描述预言了回旋加速器式的涡旋运动，与格罗斯–皮塔耶夫斯基模拟定量一致；两个同号电荷的极涡（polar vortices）引发的拓扑阻挫（topological frustration）导致赤道涡旋项链（equatorial vortex necklace）的形成——该构型与木星极地周围的多边形气旋簇相似——随后通过类似开尔文–亥姆霍兹不稳定性（Kelvin--Helmholtz-like instability）发生破裂。

Conclusion: 涡旋项链可被视为吴–杨规范修补（Wu--Yang gauge patching）的量子化类比，球形超流体为实验实现和探索狄拉克单极子物理的基本方面提供了一个多功能平台。

Abstract: Magnetic monopoles lie at the crossroads of gauge fields, topology, geometric phases, and charge quantization, yet they remain elusive as fundamental particles. Here we show that an emergent Dirac-monopole framework arises naturally from the dynamics of massive quantum vortices in a spherical superfluid shell. Their dynamics is formally equivalent to that of interacting charged particles constrained to a sphere in the field of a magnetic monopole. The monopole charge is fixed by the superfluid density and automatically satisfies Dirac's quantization condition. The emergent monopole description predicts cyclotron-like vortex motion, in quantitative agreement with Gross--Pitaevskii simulations. We further show that topological frustration induced by two like-charged polar vortices gives rise to the formation of an equatorial vortex necklace, a configuration reminiscent of the polygonal cyclone clusters observed around Jupiter's poles, before its subsequent breakup through a Kelvin--Helmholtz-like instability. Within this framework, the vortex necklace may be viewed as a quantized analogue of Wu--Yang gauge patching. Our results establish spherical superfluids as a versatile platform for realizing and exploring fundamental aspects of Dirac-monopole physics.

</details>

### [10] [Coloring Black Holes: Epistemic and Aesthetic Choices in Astronomical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14928)
*Rodrigo Ochigame,Emilie Skulberg,Jeroen van Dongen*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，事件视界望远镜（EHT）在2019年发布的黑洞阴影图像并非数据的唯一还原结果，而是在多个可行方案中经选择或平均后得到的产物。作者认为，EHT真正有价值的证据并非最终的单张图像，而是通过特定选择所展现出的有限变异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EHT发布了首张基于观测的黑洞阴影图像，但其数据处理过程中存在大量主观选择，研究者难以轻易判定哪种方法是正确的。本文旨在揭示这些认识论（epistemic）与美学（aesthetic）选择对最终图像的影响。

Method: 论文考察了从极其嘈杂且稀疏的观测数据中处理出单张图像的各阶段流程，探讨其中涉及的多重可行方案——包括选择单一方法或在各阶段对不同方法的结果进行平均。此外，还模拟了若EHT做出不同选择，图像可能呈现的面貌。

Result: 研究发现，EHT最终公布的图像只是无数种可呈现方式之一。通过对比不同选择下的图像变异性，作者认为EHT产生的最有价值证据并非单张图像本身，而是在特定选择框架下所展现的有限变异性。

Conclusion: EHT的黑洞图像结果高度依赖于数据处理过程中的人为选择。真正的科学证据应来自对结果变异范围的系统性检验，而非单一图像。

Abstract: In 2019, the first image of a black hole's shadow based on observation was released by the Event Horizon Telescope Collaboration (EHT). This paper shows that despite the EHT's emphasis on a single image as its final result, there were countless plausible ways of rendering the data, among which researchers could not easily choose. To obtain a single image from the extremely noisy and sparse data, it was necessary to select one of multiple plausible approaches, or to average the results from different approaches, at each stage of data processing. We examine the epistemic and aesthetic choices involved at various stages, and explore what the images would have looked like if the EHT had made different choices. We suggest that the most valuable evidence produced by the EHT comes not from the single image it ultimately advertised as its central result, but from the demonstration of the limited variability that emerged from the specific choices made.

</details>

### [11] [Thin-Shell Wormholes from Entropy-Induced Black-Hole Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14130)
*Jonathan A. Rebouças,Edson Otoniel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个统一的熵修正框架，通过修正的黑洞熵诱导有效时空几何，系统研究了薄壳虫洞（thin-shell wormholes）的构造与稳定性。在引入广义熵降函数并重新表述Darmois-Israel衔接条件后，作者对八种熵方案进行了分析，发现对称构造必然伴随负表面能密度，恒定压结（constant-barotropic）分支均为线性径向不稳定，而可变Chaplygin壳层能够实现稳定构型，稳定性取决于熵几何、喉径和状态方程径向指数的共同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索修正黑洞熵如何通过热力学路径诱导有效时空几何，为研究薄壳虫洞提供统一热力学框架，并系统比较不同熵方案对虫洞结构及稳定性的影响。

Method: 基于广义熵降函数 $F_{\mathcal S}(r)=1-4πM/\mathcal S'(r)$ 构造对称剪裁粘贴虫洞（cut-and-paste wormholes），将Darmois-Israel衔接条件直接用降函数和熵导数重新表述，推导表面应力、壳层能量条件组合、守恒方程和径向有效势，并应用于八种熵方案：Bekenstein–Hawking、Barrow、Tsallis–Cirto、Rényi、Kaniadakis、对数、圈量子引力启发式以及指数熵。

Result: 对称构造要求在可容许的正降函数区域内表面能量密度恒为负；熵形变可显著修正视界结构、允许喉区以及表面应力的位置。在所考察的参数域内，所有恒定压结分支均为线性径向不稳定。可变Chaplygin壳层可支持稳定构型，稳定性由熵几何、喉径和壳层状态方程径向指数共同决定。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一框架，用于比较熵诱导的黑洞几何作为薄壳虫洞种子，并表明稳定性并非仅由熵形变决定，而是取决于熵形变与喉部局域物质动力学响应的相互作用。

Abstract: Modified black-hole entropies can induce effective spacetime geometries and thereby provide a thermodynamic route for investigating thin-shell wormholes. In this work, we construct symmetric cut-and-paste wormholes from the generic entropic lapse function $F_{\mathcal S}(r)=1-4πM/\mathcal S'(r)$ and formulate the Darmois--Israel junction conditions directly in terms of the lapse and of the entropy derivatives. We derive the surface stresses, shell energy-condition combinations, conservation equation, and radial effective potential, and then apply the formalism to the Bekenstein--Hawking, Barrow, Tsallis--Cirto, Rényi, Kaniadakis, logarithmic, loop-quantum-gravity-inspired, and exponential entropy prescriptions. The analysis shows that the symmetric construction requires negative surface energy density throughout every admissible positive-lapse domain, although entropy deformations can significantly modify the horizon structure, the allowed throat region, and the localization of the surface stresses. Within the parameter domains considered here, all examined constant-barotropic branches are linearly radially unstable, despite quantitative changes in their near-horizon scales. In contrast, a variable Chaplygin shell can support stable configurations, with the stability domains determined jointly by the entropic geometry, the throat radius, and the radial exponent of the shell equation of state. These results establish a unified framework for comparing entropy-induced black-hole geometries as thin-shell wormhole seeds and show that stability is governed not by the entropy deformation alone, but by its interplay with the dynamical response of the matter localized at the throat.

</details>


### [12] [A note on the conformal geometry of the 2-sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14133)
*Jörg Frauendiener*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从共形因子的角度研究了二维球面（2-sphere）的几何，发现了一个唯一对称无迹张量，并由此推导出具有闵可夫斯基结构（Minkowski structure）的线性二阶偏微分方程（PDE），最终证明每个二维球面都能等距嵌入闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨二维球面上共形因子（conformal factor）的几何结构，特别是将给定度量重新缩放为圆度量（round metric）的共形因子集合。

Method: 在球面上发现了一个唯一的对称无迹（symmetric and trace-free）张量，该张量补充了里奇张量（Ricci tensor），使其成为无散（divergence-free）对称张量；基于此张量推导出一个线性二阶偏微分方程，其解空间承载自然的闵可夫斯基结构。

Result: 存在无穷多个这样的闵可夫斯基结构空间，它们之间通过可视为由“4-向量”（4-vectors）参数化的等距变换（isometries）相联系；每个二维球面都能以典范方式等距嵌入（isometrically embedded）到一个闵可夫斯基空间中。

Conclusion: 二维球面的共形几何与闵可夫斯基结构之间存在深刻的联系，球面可以自然地嵌入闵可夫斯基空间，这为理解二维球面的几何性质提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We discuss the geometry of the two-dimensional sphere. Our perspective focuses on the set of conformal factors that rescale a given metric to a round metric. We find that there exists a unique symmetric and trace-free tensor on the sphere which complements the Ricci tensor to a divergence-free symmetric tensor. Using this tensor, we derive a linear second-order PDE whose solution space carries a natural Minkowski structure. We show that there are in fact infinitely many such spaces, all related by isometries which can be thought of as being parametrised by ``4-vectors''. Finally, we show that every 2-sphere can be isometrically embedded in a Minkowski space in a canonical way.

</details>


### [13] [An effective Friedmann equation for a bouncing anisotropic universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14153)
*Syed Moeez Hassan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了反弹聚合物量子化Bianchi-I时空的广义有效弗里德曼方程和雷乔杜里方程，并严格证明了文献中数值发现的物质能量密度与反弹处各向异性剪切之间的关系对于任意物质内容精确成立，同时给出了该关系中常数的显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在聚合物量子化（polymer quantization）框架下研究Bianchi-I时空的反弹动力学，旨在澄清物质能量密度与各向异性剪切（anisotropic shear）在反弹点处的精确关系，该关系此前仅在数值层面被发现，缺乏严格的理论证明。

Method: 采用聚合物量子化方法处理Bianchi-I时空，推导出广义的有效弗里德曼方程（effective Friedmann equation）和雷乔杜里方程（Raychaudhuri equation）；通过解析推导证明反弹处物质能量密度与各向异性剪切的关系对所有物质内容普遍成立，并给出关系常数的显式表达式。

Result: 成功推导了反弹聚合物量子化Bianchi-I时空的广义有效动力学方程；严格证明了物质能量密度与各向异性剪切在反弹点处的关系对所有物质类型精确成立，并导出了该关系中各常数的显式形式。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上确认了聚合物量子化Bianchi-I宇宙模型中物质能量密度与各向异性剪切之间的普遍关系，为理解量子引力框架下各向异性宇宙的反弹行为提供了解析基础。

Abstract: We derive generalized effective Friedmann and Raychaudhuri equations for a bouncing polymer quantized Bianchi-I spacetime. We further prove that the relation numerically derived in the literature between the matter energy density and the anisotropic shear at the bounce holds exactly for any type of matter content, and derive explicit expressions for the constants that appear in that relation.

### [14] [Reconstructions of Horndeski Subclasses by Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14154)
*Marco C. Mendoza Marcos,Ana A. Avilez Lopez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于晚期宇宙学观测数据（宇宙学计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）和重子声学振荡（Baryonic Acoustic Oscillations）），利用高斯过程（Gaussian Processes，GP）贝叶斯技术，重构了Horndeski理论中两类子理论（Brans-Dicke子类和Cubic Galileon子类）的宇宙学演化，发现Brans-Dicke子类在红移区间z∈(0.4,1.7)优于ΛCDM模型，而Cubic Galileon子类在全观测红移范围内支持标量场随时间演化的暗能量密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验并区分Horndeski类标量-张量引力理论中不同子类的宇宙学表现，利用当前高精度观测数据对修正引力理论进行重构，以探索暗能量及引力常数随时间演化的可能性。

Method: 采用高斯过程贝叶斯技术，对Horndeski理论中Brans-Dicke和Cubic Galileon两个子类分别进行数据驱动的重构；输入数据包括来自宇宙学计时器的哈勃率（Hubble rate）模型无关测量，以及来自重子声学振荡的哈勃率和距离测量。

Result: 对于Brans-Dicke子类，最可能的高斯过程重构在红移范围z∈(0.4,1.7)内优于ΛCDM模型；对于Cubic Galileon子类，最可能的重构在全观测红移范围内支持标量场对引力的修正及暗能量密度随时间演化。

Conclusion: 两类子理论均能在特定红移范围内与观测数据一致，且表现出偏离ΛCDM的演化行为；研究同时表明所考虑的理论与引力波传播速度的约束相兼容。

Abstract: In this work we reconstruct two subclasses of theories from the Horndeski class, the most general scalar-tensor theories of gravity with second-order equations, according to a variety of late-universe cosmological data: model independent measurements of Hubble rate from Cosmic Chronometers, as well as Hubble rate and distance measurements from Baryonic Acoustic Oscillations. In the modified gravity family considered, the scalar field is non-minimally coupled to gravity leading to time variations in the gravitational constant at cosmological scales. The theories considered are also consistent with constraints on the propagation speed of gravitational waves. The reconstruction is carried out by using the Gaussian Processes bayesian technique either for the Brans-Dicke and the Cubic Galileon subclasses of Horndeski theory. We find that the most likely Gaussian Process reconstruction for the data favors a cosmology from the Brans-Dicke subclass over $Λ$CDM in the range $z \in (0.4, 1.7)$, and for the Cubic Galileon subclass we find that the most likely reconstruction indeed favors modifications of the scalar field to gravity with time evolving dark energy density in the whole range of redshift observations.

</details>


### [15] [Breaking the Degeneracy: Spectral Hardening of Accretion Disks around Rotating Hayward Black Holes in Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14164)
*Sandip Dutta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转正则黑雅（Hayward）黑洞被宏观暗物质（dark matter, DM）晕包围时薄吸积盘的热力学与观测特征，发现量子启发的核心正则性与宏观暗物质晕对辐射效率产生叠加增强，并在低频到中频区域引发黑洞几何与暗物质环境之间的宏观简并性（degeneracy），该简并仅在多波长光谱的极端Wien尾处结构性破除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转正则Hayward黑洞在宏观暗物质晕环境下薄吸积盘的观测特征，并区分纯粹几何效应（非奇异黑洞）与纯粹天体物理效应（暗物质环境）在观测上的差异。

Method: 将时空严格建模为三区域复合模型：内部de Sitter极限正则化的Hayward核、中间由指数球密度分布（exponential sphere density profile）描述的无压尘埃暗物质壳层、以及渐近平坦的外部真空。通过质量分布函数匹配各区域，计算了最内稳定圆轨道（Innermost Stable Circular Orbit, ISCO）、辐射效率（radiative efficiency）、局域热通量和多色黑体光谱光度（multi-colour blackbody spectral luminosity）的修正，并在四种构型（Kerr真空、Hayward真空、Kerr+DM、Hayward+DM）间进行了系统比较。

Result: 四种构型的比较显示ISCO存在严格的分层压缩；量子启发的核心正则性与宏观暗物质晕对辐射效率产生叠加增强，对于高自旋黑洞（j=0.8）可达约14.4%；在低到中频区域，纯几何构型（Hayward真空）与纯天体物理构型（Kerr+DM）之间存在宏观简并性。

Conclusion: 该宏观简并性仅在多波长光谱的极端Wien尾处被结构性破除，这为未来高频光谱偏振测量（high-frequency spectropolarimetry）提供了区分非奇异黑洞与经典暗物质环境的关键诊断印迹。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic and observable signatures of thin accretion disks surrounding rotating, regular Hayward black holes embedded within a macroscopic dark matter (DM) envelope. The spacetime is rigorously modelled as a three-region composite: an inner Hayward core regularised by a de~Sitter limit, an intermediate DM shell modelled as a pressureless dust envelope governed by an exponential sphere density profile, and an asymptotically flat outer vacuum. By matching these regions via the mass profile, we compute the explicit modifications to the Innermost Stable Circular Orbit (ISCO), radiative efficiency, local thermal flux, and multi-colour blackbody spectral luminosity. A systematic comparison across four distinct configurations (Kerr vacuum, Hayward vacuum, Kerr\,+\,DM, and Hayward\,+\,DM) reveals a strict hierarchical compression of the ISCO. We demonstrate that the quantum-inspired core regularity and the macroscopic DM halo exert an additive enhancement on the radiative efficiency, reaching $\sim 14.4\%$ for highly spinning black holes ($j=0.8$). However, this additive behaviour introduces a profound macroscopic degeneracy between purely geometric (Hayward vacuum) and purely astrophysical (Kerr\,+\,DM) configurations at low-to-intermediate frequencies. We establish that this degeneracy is structurally broken only in the extreme Wien tail of the multi-wavelength spectrum, providing a critical diagnostic footprint for future high-frequency spectropolarimetry to distinguish non-singular black holes from classical dark matter environments.

</details>


### [16] [Probing Quantum Gravity through Chaotic Orbits and Strong-Field Effects in Kerr Black Holes Embedded in Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14170)
*Shubham Kala,Sara Saghafi,M. Yousaf,Hemwati Nandan,Ahmadjon Abdujabbarov,Chengxun Yuan,G. Mustafa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文运用庞加莱截面（Poincaré sections）、李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponents）、Kolmogorov-Sinai熵（KS entropy）和加权Birkhoff平均（weighted Birkhoff averages, WBA）等多种非线性动力学方法，系统研究了被完美流体暗物质（PFDM）包围的量子改进旋转黑洞中的光子动力学，揭示了量子修正参数和暗物质参数对零测地线运动及混沌行为的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子引力修正和暗物质（PFDM）共同作用下旋转黑洞周围光子的非线性动力学行为，特别是从规则运动（regular motion）向混沌运动（chaotic motion）的转变机制，以及这些效应对轨道稳定性和可观测量（如黑洞阴影）的潜在影响。

Method: 采用庞加莱截面可视化相空间结构，利用李雅普诺夫指数量化轨道的初始条件敏感性，采用KS熵独立衡量动力学复杂性，并通过加权Birkhoff平均（WBA）提供区分规则和混沌轨道的定量判据。

Result: 量子改进参数和PFDM参数的增大会导致不变环面（invariant tori）变形和碎裂，相空间中涌现出散乱混沌区域；李雅普诺夫指数表明两个参数均增强了光子轨迹对初始条件的敏感性；KS熵证实混沌行为随量子修正和暗物质修正的增加而增长；WBA方法提供了可靠的相空间结构映射。

Conclusion: 量子引力修正和暗物质的联合效应显著改变了调控光子运动的有效势（effective potential），产生规则与混沌区域共存的丰富混合相空间结构；该结果对强场区域的黑洞阴影和引力透镜（gravitational lensing）效应具有重要的观测意义。

Abstract: We study the nonlinear photon dynamics in quantum improved rotating black hole surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) using several methods of analysis, including Poincaré sections, Lyapunov exponents, Kolmogorov-Sinai (KS) entropy and weighted Birkhoff averages (WBA). In particular, we examine the effect of quantum-improved parameter $(\tildeω)$ and PFDM parameter $(ζ)$ on the null geodesic motion hence stability of circular orbit. Poincaré sections illustrate the transition from regular to chaotic motion as these parameters increase, characterized by the deformation and fragmentation of invariant tori and the emergence of scattered chaotic regions in phase space. The stability properties of null circular orbits are quantified through the Lyapunov indicators, revealing that both the quantum improvement parameter and the PFDM parameter enhance the sensitivity of photon trajectories to initial conditions. The KS entropy provides an independent measure of dynamical complexity and confirms the growth of chaotic behavior with increasing quantum and PFDM corrections. Additionally, the WBA method offers a robust quantitative criterion for distinguishing regular and chaotic orbits and allows a detailed mapping of the phase-space structure. The results demonstrate that the combined effects of quantum gravity corrections and PFDM significantly modify the effective potential governing photon motion, leading to a rich mixed phase-space structure with coexisting regular and chaotic regions. These findings underscore the crucial role of quantum and dark matter contributions in shaping photon dynamics near rotating black holes and suggest possible observational implications on black hole shadows and gravitational lensing in strong-field regimes.

### [17] [Novel topological subclass in Bardeen-AdS-class black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14173)
*Yu-Die Wan,Peng Zhao,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于φ-映射拓扑流理论（φ-mapping topological current theory），系统研究了耦合非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）的正则Bardeen-AdS类黑洞的热力学拓扑。在基础拓扑族W^{0-}内部发现了一个新的内次级子类（inner secondary subclass）\widetilde{W}^{0-}，该子类全局拓扑电荷W=0，具有内-外视界环绕数符号[-,+]。两个临界耦合参数将参数空间划分为不同的拓扑相，数值结果验证了该拓扑形式对无奇点规则黑洞的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正则Bardeen-AdS类黑洞是一类无奇点（singularity-free）几何，其拓扑分类（topological classification）尚未被充分探索，因此需要对其热力学拓扑结构进行系统研究。

Method: 采用φ-映射拓扑流理论（φ-mapping topological current theory）进行理论分析，并在两个典型AdS半径L=1和L=15处实施数值计算，以识别不同参数区域下的拓扑结构与相变。

Result: 在W^{0-}拓扑族内部发现了一个新的内次级子类\widetilde{W}^{0-}，其全局拓扑电荷W=0、内-外视界环绕数符号为[-,+]；该子类源于在基础解序列末端附加一个额外稳定分支。两个临界耦合参数\hat{m}_{01}和\hat{m}_{02}将参数空间划分为不同的拓扑相：m_0≥\hat{m}_{01}和\hat{m}_{02}<m_0<\hat{m}_{01}区域属于\widetilde{W}^{0-}子类，而0<m_0≤\hat{m}_{02}区域对应常规W^{0-}拓扑。

Conclusion: 数值结果验证了热力学拓扑形式（thermodynamic topological formalism）对无奇点正则黑洞的自洽性，完善了针对非线性电动力学正则黑洞的拓扑判别准则，并为后续基于同一形式的高维旋转正则黑洞拓扑研究提供了理论参考。

Abstract: Based on the $φ$-mapping topological current theory, we systematically investigate the thermodynamic topology of regular Bardeen-AdS-class black holes coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics, a class of singularity-free geometries whose topological classification remains underexplored. We implement numerical calculations at two typical AdS radii $L=1$ and $L=15$. Within the fundamental $W^{0-}$ topological family, we identify a novel inner secondary subclass $\widetilde{W}^{0-}$. This result only refines and enriches the internal branch structure of the $W^{0-}$ family under the established classification scheme of five topological classes and four topological subclasses for black hole thermodynamics. This new subclass has a vanishing global topological charge $W=0$ with an inner-outer horizon winding-number signature $[-,+]$. Unlike standard $W^{0-}$ solutions that realize topological extension via embedded $(+,-)$ winding pairs, $\widetilde{W}^{0-}$ arises from attaching an extra stable branch to the end of the base solution sequence. Two critical coupling parameters $\hat{m}_{01}$ and $\hat{m}_{02}$ divide the full parameter space into distinct topological phases: Type I black holes with $m_0\ge\hat{m}_{01}$ and Type II solutions with $\hat{m}_{02}<m_0<\hat{m}_{01}$ belong to $\widetilde{W}^{0-}$, while the parameter region $0<m_0\le\hat{m}_{02}$ corresponds to the conventional $W^{0-}$ topology. Our numerical results verify the self-consistency of the thermodynamic topological formalism when applied to singularity-free regular black holes, refine the topological discrimination criteria tailored to nonlinear-electrodynamics regular black holes, and provide theoretical references for subsequent topological investigations of higher-dimensional rotating regular black holes under the same formalism.

### [18] [Coupled by Design: Computing Kerr-Newman Quasinormal Modes with a Hybrid SpectralPINN Solver](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14216)
*Alexandre M. Pombo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将SpectralPINN求解器从单个可分离方程的Kerr无电荷极限扩展到求解两个耦合主偏微分方程系统，用于计算Kerr-Newman黑洞的准正则模（quasinormal modes），计算并系统表征了光子球分支的矢量主导模式，频谱误差在10⁻⁴至10⁻⁷量级，并利用数据集观察了特征值排斥现象及对黑洞电荷质量比的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期SpectralPINN求解器仅能处理单个可分离方程的无电荷Kerr极限情形，无法处理Kerr-Newman黑洞中引力场与电磁场耦合导致的真正两场耦合问题，需要将求解能力扩展到耦合主偏微分方程组。

Method: 将\texttt{SpectralPINN}求解器扩展应用于求解两个耦合主偏微分方程（coupled master PDEs）系统，从而计算Kerr-Newman黑洞的准正则模，覆盖引力-电磁耦合的两场问题。

Result: 相对频率误差最差情形约10⁻⁴，多数情形约10⁻⁷；计算数据集涵盖ℓ=4以内两分支共五种光子球模和两种近水平模；首次系统计算并表征了矢量主导的光子球分支；利用数据集观察了特征值排斥（eigenvalue repulsion）现象，排除了所解析域内的极化间排斥，并预测了爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）对黑洞电荷质量比（charge-to-mass ratio）的约束。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效解决了Kerr-Newman耦合两场系统的准正则模计算问题，精度高、覆盖范围广，并为进一步约束黑洞参数提供了数据基础。

Abstract: We extend our \texttt{SpectralPINN} solver to the computation of Kerr-Newman quasinormal modes by applying it to solve the system of two coupled master PDEs -- advancing from the single, separable equation of the uncharged Kerr limit to a genuinely coupled two-field problem. The coupling between the gravitational and electromagnetic fields gives rise to two families of solutions: the photon-sphere, connecting with Kerr; and near-horizon, disconnected from the Kerr limit, each with two branches of solutions depending on the leading field: the gravitational- and vector-led. Benchmarking against publicly available datasets shows relative frequency errors of $\sim 10^{-4}$ worst case and $\sim10^{-7}$ for most cases. The computed public dataset spans five photon-sphere modes, both gravitational- and vector-led, up to $\ell=4$, as well as two fundamental gravitational-led near-horizon modes. The vector-led photon-sphere branch is computed and systematically characterized for the first time. We apply the dataset and observe the onset of the eigenvalue repulsion reported by Dias \textit{et al.}, to exclude an inter-polarization repulsion within the resolved domain, and to forecast Einstein Telescope constraints on the black-hole charge-to-mass ratio.

### [19] [Acceleration radiation and HBAR thermodynamics for atoms falling into a BTZ black hole: A CQM quantum-optics approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14281)

TL;DR: 本文证明，在 Boulware 类真空中自由落入 Bañados-Teitelboim-Zanelli (BTZ) 黑洞的原子会以 Hawking 温度 $T_H$ 发射具有普朗克谱（Planck spectrum）的辐射，且该辐射与相对等效原理（relative equivalence principle）相关。尽管 BTZ 黑洞具有 $(2+1)$ 维引力的拓扑性质，其热力学与辐射性质仍受近视界共形量子力学（conformal quantum mechanics, CQM）支配，并衍生出与 Bekenstein-Hawking 熵 $S_{\mathrm{BH}}=A/4$ 成比例的 HBAR 熵 $S_{\mathcal P}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用量子光学（quantum optics）框架，将每个原子解释为探测器（detector），分析原子与场模式的相互作用；通过相对等效原理描述加速真空场模式相对于下落原子的效应。

Result: 原子在 BTZ 黑洞背景中以 Hawking 温度 $T_H$ 发射普朗克谱辐射；随机初始时间的原子云可产生热 Hawking 型辐射；辐射场衍生出与 Bekenstein-Hawking 熵 $S_{\mathrm{BH}}=A/4$ 成比例的 HBAR 熵 $S_{\mathcal P}$，且正确包含 $1/4$ 比例因子。

Conclusion: BTZ 黑洞的热力学与辐射性质受近视界共形量子力学 (CQM) 统一支配，该共形行为适用于所有背景场，表明低维引力与高维引力在黑洞热辐射方面具有普适规律。

Abstract: Atoms falling freely into a Bañados-Teitelboim-Zanelli (BTZ) black hole in a Boulware-like vacuum are shown to emit radiation with a Planck spectrum at the Hawking temperature $T_{H}$. This leads to thermal Hawking-like radiation for a cloud of falling atoms prepared with random initial times. Moreover, the radiation is related to the relative equivalence principle, with the vacuum field modes accelerated with respect to the falling atom. The physics of the atom-field interactions is most easily described within a quantum optics approach, where each atom can be interpreted as a detector. Despite the topological nature of gravity in $(2+1)$ dimensions, the thermodynamic and radiation properties of BTZ black holes are still universally governed by the same near-horizon conformal quantum mechanics (CQM) applicable to higher-dimensional gravity. This universal conformal behavior is exhibited by all fields in the background of generic black holes, and generates an HBAR entropy $S_{\mathcal P}$ associated with the photon radiation field that mimics the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S_{\mathrm{BH}}=A/4$, proportional to the black-hole horizon area, and with the correct $1/4$ proportionality factor.

### [20] [Upwind embedded boundary SBP operators: New high order numerical schemes for arbitrarily shaped domains with Cartesian grids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14403)
*Conner Dailey*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在嵌入式边界求和分部（embedded boundary summation by parts, SBP）框架下推导了新的有限差分算子，通过提高内部和边界闭包的精度阶数、改进谱性质并推广至迎风格式，实现了对波动方程更好的色散关系保持特性，并在三维多块网格含切除球的曲标量波动方程算例中验证了其鲁棒性与精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 嵌入式边界SBP方法已在非线性问题（如黑洞切除模拟）中展现出实用性，但现有算子在内部和边界闭包的精度阶数以及光谱特性上仍有提升空间。本文旨在推导新型算子，以降低边界误差并改善网格上的谱性质。

Method: 在嵌入式边界SBP框架内，通过引入插值/外推算子匹配边界闭包的精度，推导了新型有限差分算子。新算子提高了内部和边界闭包的精度阶数，并推广至迎风（upwind）格式，改进了传统SBP方案对波动方程的色散关系保持（dispersion relation preserving）特性。

Result: 新算子有效降低了边界误差；迎风格式的引入使得谱性质优于传统SBP方案。在三维多块网格中心块嵌入切除球（excision sphere）的曲标量波动方程（curvilinear scalar wave equation）测试中，验证了新型嵌入式算子的鲁棒性和准确性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的新型嵌入式边界SBP算子在精度和谱特性上均优于传统方法，适用于含复杂嵌入边界的非线性波动问题，如黑洞切除模拟等。

Abstract: Embedded boundary summation by parts (SBP) methods define finite differencing based derivative operators with the added feature that the boundary need not coincide with a grid cell, allowing a boundary to be embedded on a regular Cartesian grid. This is achieved by the introduction of interpolation/extrapolation operators that match the accuracy of the boundary closure. These methods have been used to perform black hole excision simulations on a domain with a spherical boundary embedded in a regular Cartesian grid, demonstrating their usefulness for nonlinear problems. In this work, new operators are derived using this embedded boundary framework to increase the order of accuracy of the interior and boundary closure while minimizing the boundary error. Additionally, these novel operators improve the spectral properties on the grid by generalizing to an upwind scheme that has better dispersion relation preserving properties compared to traditional SBP schemes for wave equations. These operators are tested with the curvilinear scalar wave equation on a 3D multiblock grid with an excision sphere embedded in the center block to demonstrate the robustness and accuracy of these novel embedded operators.

### [21] [Scalarization of Charged Black Hole in Gauss-Bonnet Extended Starobinsky-Maxwell Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14620)

TL;DR: 本文在Starobinsky引力（Starobinsky gravity）耦合高斯-博内不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）的框架下重新审视黑洞自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization），发现了一种之前未被报道的多分支（multi-branch）结构：标量化解分裂为两个光滑分支，它们在一个共同的最小视界半径处连接。引入麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field）后，该多分支结构仍然存在，并在特定参数范围内出现新的额外孤立分支。通过标准麦克斯韦热力学关系验证，所有带电带毛解（charged hairy solutions）均精确满足热力学第一定律（first law）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Starobinsky引力中加入高斯-博内不变量项以驱动标量化，并进一步引入麦克斯韦场以研究带电情形。通过数值求解场方程，追踪标量化解的分支结构，并利用标准麦克斯韦热力学关系检验热力学第一定律的有效性。

Result: 发现静态球对称标量化解分为两个光滑分支，在共同的最小视界半径处相连，形成之前未被报道的多分支结构。引入麦克斯韦场后，该多分支结构保持不变，且在特定参数范围内出现一个新的额外孤立分支。所有带电带毛解均精确满足热力学第一定律。

Conclusion: Starobinsky引力框架下的黑洞标量化呈现出比以往认识更丰富的分支结构，并且热力学一致性在带电情形下依然成立。

Abstract: We re-examine spontaneous scalarization of black holes within Starobinsky gravity supplemented by the Gauss-Bonnet invariant. A novel feature is uncovered: scalarized solutions split into two smooth branches that connect at a common minimal horizon radius, a multi-branch structure previously unreported for static, spherically symmetric scalarization. Extending the theory with a Maxwell field, we find that this multi-branch structure persists, while a new additional disconnected branch emerges within certain parameter ranges. We thoroughly analyse the transition from a single smooth branch to two disconnected branches. Lastly, we verify, employing the standard Maxwell thermodynamic relations, that all charged hairy solutions obey the first law exactly.

### [22] [Random walks around black holes and low-frequency X-ray variability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14626)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强引力场下的湍流流体中嵌入的尘埃颗粒的随机动力学尚未充分理解，而传统模型难以解释吸积过程中观测到的固有变异性（intrinsic variability）。作者希望建立一种基于弯曲空间几何的随机游走框架，以更准确地描述吸积到致密天体时的随机过程。

Method: 将尘埃颗粒的随机动力学表述为Riemannian流形（Riemannian manifold）上的随机游走（random walk），并求解黑洞背景上的Fokker-Planck方程；同时模拟大量初始分布在同心壳层（density profile由薄盘结构方程设定）上的粒子轨迹，以计算通过视界的粒子通量。

Result: 与平直空间相比，黑洞背景下尘埃颗粒的逃逸概率更高，原因是事件视界附近径向元（radial cells）被拉伸，使得粒子在被捕获前有更大的空间体积可游走。低频端光谱指数比平直空间更浅（主要由时间 dilation 导致），高频端则更陡。Schwarzschild权重谱与Cygnus X-1硬态下的低频X射线变异性观测基本一致。

Conclusion: 几何漂移（geometric drifts）可能在描述随机吸积过程（stochastic accretion processes）中具有重要性；弯曲空间几何效应是解释观测到的低频X射线变异性的一个关键因素。

Abstract: The stochastic dynamics of a grain embedded within a turbulent fluid subject to strong gravitational fields can be formulated as a random walk on a Riemannian manifold. Such curvature-weighted walks provide a framework to model the intrinsic variability of accretion onto compact objects. By solving the relevant Fokker-Planck equation on a black hole background, we find the counterintuitive result that the escape probability of a grain is actually higher compared to flat space. This is a consequence of the stretching of radial cells near the event horizon: there is a greater spatial volume for the particle to wander through before being captured. By simulating a large number of grain trajectories, initially distributed on concentric shells with a density profile set by the thin-disc structure equations, we also study particle fluxes through the horizon. Shallower spectral indices emerge at low frequencies relative to flat space, primarily due to time dilation, and steeper ones at high frequencies. We find that Schwarzschild-weighted spectra broadly match observations of low-frequency X-ray variability from systems like Cygnus X-1 in their hard state, suggesting that geometric drifts may be important in describing stochastic accretion processes.

</details>


### [23] [Warped Spacelike Singularities and the $C^0$-Inextendibility of Birmingham-Kottler Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14741)
*Bobby EkaGunara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了在某一类翘曲类空奇点（warped spacelike singularities）处连续洛伦兹延拓（continuous Lorentzian extension）的局部障碍，并将其应用于单视界Birmingham-Kottler时空族，证明了其在非正宇宙常数和特定纤维条件下的$C^0$不可延拓性（$C^0$-inextendibility）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在奇点处时空能否进行连续洛伦兹延拓，特别是对于不具球对称性的翘曲类空奇点，现有旋转形变（rotational deformation）方法不再适用，需要寻找更一般的判据。

Method: 通过径向压缩（radial compression）终端因果痕迹（terminal causal traces）构造紧致时序分隔器（compact chronological separator），并利用纵向平移（longitudinal translations）产生在延拓坐标系中均匀受控但固有发散（diverge intrinsically）的径向切片距离（radial-slice distances）。同时，在全局Kruskal坐标中构造典范单视界Birmingham-Kottler时空，并对类时测地线（timelike geodesics）的有限固有时端点（finite proper-time ends）进行分类。

Result: 给出了两个可积性条件（integrability conditions）、相对翘曲因子的单调性条件（monotonicity condition）以及纵向因子的发散性（divergence of the longitudinal factor）作为局部障碍的判据；证明了在非正宇宙常数（nonpositive cosmological constant）且纤维满足$\text{Ric}_{γ_Σ}=(n-2)kγ_Σ$的条件下，单视界Birmingham-Kottler时空族是$C^0$不可延拓的。

Conclusion: 该局部障碍不要求闭纤维（closed fiber）具有任何对称性，且所得不可延拓性结果不依赖于纤维的同质性（homogeneity）、可定向性（orientability）或单连通性（simple connectivity），适用范围更广。

Abstract: We establish a local obstruction to continuous Lorentzian extensions at a class of warped spacelike singularities. The criterion is expressed through two integrability conditions, a monotonicity condition on the relative warp factors, and divergence of the longitudinal factor; it does not require any symmetry of the closed fiber. The main geometric step is a radial compression of terminal causal traces, which replaces the rotational deformation available in spherical symmetry. The compression yields a compact chronological separator in an adapted boundary chart. Longitudinal translations then produce radial-slice distances that diverge intrinsically while remaining uniformly controlled in the extension chart. Next, we construct the canonical one-horizon Birmingham-Kottler spacetime in global Kruskal coordinates and classify all finite proper-time ends of its timelike geodesics. Every boundary-approaching finite maximizer supplied by a putative extension is thereby forced to the singular end. The local obstruction and the geodesic classification imply $C^0$-inextendibility for the one-horizon Birmingham-Kottler family with nonpositive cosmological constant and every closed connected fiber satisfying $\text{Ric}_{γ_Σ}=(n-2)kγ_Σ$, without assumptions of homogeneity, orientability, or simple connectivity.

</details>


### [24] [Orbital Dynamics and Gravitational-Wave Signatures of EMRIs in Self-Dual Loop Quantum Gravity Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14746)
*Yu Wang,Meilin Liu,Haiguang Xu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在自对偶圈量子引力（self-dual loop quantum gravity, LQG）黑洞时空中研究了极端质量比旋近（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）的轨道动力学和引力波信号，通过Fisher矩阵分析表明EMRI观测有望为量子引力效应提供约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圈量子引力（LQG）预测经典黑洞时空存在量子修正，这种修正可能在强场区域留下可观测印记。现有研究缺乏对LQG修正下极端质量比旋近（EMRI）系统引力波信号特征的系统分析，因此有必要评估EMRI作为探测量子引力效应的途径。

Method: 研究基于静态球对称的自对偶LQG黑洞几何，其中包含两个量子参数：聚合物参数$P$和最小面积参数$a_0$。通过分析有效势与轨道结构，系统研究量子修正对圆轨道稳定性和强场轨道行为的影响。利用轨道演化构建引力波波形，采用Newman-Janis算法构造自对偶时空的旋转扩展以得到LQG修正的Kerr几何，最后使用Fisher矩阵分析法评估未来空间引力波探测器对量子参数的约束能力。

Result: LQG修正改变了近视界（near-horizon）轨道动力学；与经典Schwarzschild情形相比，量子效应在长时旋近阶段累积，导致引力波信号出现明显偏离。在旋转扩展的LQG修正Kerr几何中，自旋与量子修正之间存在相互作用。Fisher矩阵分析表明EMRI观测有望对量子参数给出潜在约束。

Conclusion: EMRI观测为探测黑洞时空中的量子引力效应提供了一条有前景的途径。

Abstract: Loop quantum gravity (LQG) predicts quantum modifications to classical black-hole spacetimes, which may leave imprints on the dynamics and gravitational-wave signals of compact objects in the strong-field regime. In this work, we investigate the orbital dynamics and gravitational-wave signatures of extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) in a self-dual loop quantum gravity black hole spacetime. We analyze test-particle motion in the static, spherically symmetric self-dual LQG geometry characterized by two quantum parameters: the polymeric parameter $P$ and the minimal area parameter $a_0$. The effective potential and orbital structure are systematically studied, and we quantify the influence of quantum corrections on circular-orbit stability and strong-field orbital behavior. Compared with the classical Schwarzschild spacetime, LQG corrections modify the near-horizon orbital dynamics. Based on the orbital evolution, we construct gravitational-wave waveforms and investigate the impact of quantum corrections on waveform morphology. We find that LQG effects accumulate during the long inspiral phase, leading to noticeable signal deviations from the classical case. To incorporate rotation, we construct a rotating extension of the self-dual spacetime using the Newman--Janis algorithm. The resulting LQG-corrected Kerr geometry is used to analyze orbital motion, revealing the interplay between spin and quantum corrections in strong-field trajectories. Finally, we perform a Fisher matrix analysis to estimate potential constraints on quantum parameters from future space-based gravitational-wave detectors. Our results indicate that EMRI observations provide a promising avenue to probe quantum gravitational effects in black-hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [25] [The radial action for massive particles in spherically symmetric geometries: Exact resummation at any PM order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14802)
*Donato Bini,Giorgio Di Russo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了多种球对称时空（Schwarzschild、Schwarzschild-Tangherlini、D3-膜）中有质量粒子沿双曲型测地线的径向作用量，在eikonal极限下利用特殊函数实现了重求和，并推广了先前仅适用于零测地线的结果。进一步在4维Schwarzschild黑洞时空中，借助量子Seiberg-Witten曲线方法，建立了有质量情形下径向作用量与量子a-圈（重整化角动量）的简单关系，但尚未得到对偶a_D-圈的重求和表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于径向作用量与散射角的重求和结果仅适用于零测地线（null geodesics），本文将其推广到有质量粒子（massive particles）情形，并探索量子Seiberg-Witten曲线（quantum Seiberg-Witten curves）方法在径向方程中的进一步应用。

Method: 对于Schwarzschild、Schwarzschild-Tangherlini以及D3-膜时空，在有质量粒子沿双曲型测地线（hyperboliclike geodesics）的条件下计算径向作用量，并在eikonal极限下使用特殊函数（超几何函数、Fox-Wright函数）实现重求和（resummation）。对于4维Schwarzschild黑洞，采用量子Seiberg-Witten曲线方法处理有质量标量场的径向方程，建立径向作用量与量子a-圈（reormalized angular momentum）的关系。

Result: 得到了有质量粒子径向作用量与散射角的重求和表达式；在4维Schwarzschild情形下，证明了有质量标量场的径向作用量和量子a-圈存在简单关系，并给出了完全重求和的表达式；对偶a_D-圈仅得到展开形式，尚未获得重求和表达。

Conclusion: 本文将有质量粒子沿双曲型测地线的径向作用量推广到了可重求和的形式，深化了量子Seiberg-Witten曲线与黑洞散射问题之间的联系；对偶a_D-圈的重求和仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: We compute the massive particles radial action along hyperboliclike geodesics in various spherically symmetric spacetimes: the standard $4d$ Schwarzschild spacetime, its $d$-dimensional genralization known as Schwarzschild-Tangherlini solutions and for the D3-branes spacetimes, showing useful resummation properties in terms of special (hypergeometric, Fox-Wright) functions in the eikonal limit and generalizing previous results valid for null geodesics. As a consequence, the scattering angle can be resummed too, and we explicitly display the resummed expressions.
  In addition, in the more interesting situation of a $4d$ Schwarzschild black hole spacetime, following the approach of the quantum Seiberg-Witten curves to the radial equation associated with a massive scalar field, we show that the quantum $a$-cycle (or, equivalently, the \lq\lq renormalized angular momentum") is simply related to radial action also in this massive case, providing fully resummed expressions. Finally, we display the explicit, expanded-form expression of the dual $a_D$-cycle, for which, however, no resummed expressions have been derived yet.

</details>


### [26] [Chaos bound violation by spinning particles in Gauss-Bonnet-AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14863)
*Xiaowei Li,Mengxuan Wu,Guoping Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转试探粒子在 Gauss-Bonnet 反德西特时空（Gauss-Bonnet anti-de Sitter spacetime）中混沌界限（chaos bound）的违反现象，重点分析了 Gauss-Bonnet 参数和时空维度对 Lyapunov 指数（Lyapunov exponent）的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在修改引力理论（modified gravity theories）中，时空维度与 Gauss-Bonnet 耦合参数如何影响混沌界限的有效性，特别是旋转粒子在 Gauss-Bonnet-AdS 时空中的混沌行为。

Method: 通过分析不同时空维度（五、八、九维）下旋转试探粒子的 Lyapunov 指数随粒子自旋、Gauss-Bonnet 参数及角动量的变化规律，研究混沌界限的违反机制。

Result: 五维时空中 Lyapunov 指数随粒子自旋单调增长；八、九维时空中呈现先减后增的非单调行为。Gauss-Bonnet 参数通过重塑近地平线几何调控违反行为：五维中 Lyapunov 指数与表面引力（surface gravity）的偏离先增后减，高维中界限更易被违反。角动量增大会增强混沌，但当 Gauss-Bonnet 参数和黑洞电荷较小时，时空维度起主导作用。

Conclusion: 时空维度和 Gauss-Bonnet 参数是影响修改引力理论中混沌界限有效性的重要因素。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the violation of the chaos bound for spinning test particles in Gauss-Bonnet anti-de Sitter spacetime, focusing on the regulatory roles of the Gauss-Bonnet parameter and spacetime dimensionality. In five-dimensional space time, the Lyapunov exponent grows monotonically with particle spin. In contrast, in eight- and nine-dimensional spacetimes, it exhibits non-monotonic behavior-first decreasing and then increasing-reflecting the nonlinear nature of higher-dimensional tensor couplings. The Gauss-Bonnet parameter significantly modulates the violation by reshaping the near-horizon geometry: in five dimensions, the deviation of the Lyapunov exponent from the surface gravity first increases and then decreases with the Gauss-Bonnet parameter, whereas in the higher dimensions the bound is more easily violated. Increasing the total angular momentum of the particle also enhances chaos; however, when the Gauss-Bonnet parameter and black hole charge are small, the spacetime dimensionality, rather than the angular momentum, dominates. These results establish the spacetime dimensionality and the Gauss-Bonnet parameter as important factors governing the validity of the chaos bound in modified gravity theories.

</details>


### [27] [Kerr black holes without primary hairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14910)
*J Ovalle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类由参数{𝒎,𝒂}唯一定义的正则轴对称黑洞几何族，该族在正则时空、可积奇点构型与作为极限情形的Kerr解之间连续插值。其主要特征包括：无需𝒂≈𝒎即可存在准极端构型，以及为从初始正则构型到Kerr黑洞形成的分析描述提供可能框架。

Method: 构造了一类正则轴对称（regular axisymmetric）黑洞几何族，该族由两个参数{𝒎,𝒂}完全表征，并保留了Kerr事件视界（Kerr event horizon）。该族在正则时空、具有可积奇点（integrable singularities）的构型与作为极限的Kerr解之间形成插值。

Result: 该几何族具有两个核心特征：(i) 在无需𝒂≈𝒎的条件下即可存在准极端（quasi-extremal）构型；(ii) 为从初始正则构型到Kerr黑洞形成的分析描述提供了潜在的理论框架。

Conclusion: 该正则轴对称黑洞几何族为连接正则时空与Kerr黑洞解提供了统一的参数化框架，并可能为理解Kerr黑洞的形成过程提供分析途径。

Abstract: We present a class of regular axisymmetric black hole geometries fully characterized by the parameters $\{{\cal M},a\}$ and possessing the Kerr event horizon. This family interpolates between regular spacetimes, configurations with integrable singularities, and the Kerr solution as a limiting case. Its main features are: (i) the existence of quasi-extremal configurations without requiring $a \approx {\cal M}$; and (ii) a possible framework toward an analytical description of Kerr black hole formation from an initially regular configuration.

C 80, 120 (2020) arXiv:1907.06410 . It points out and corrects several mathematical inconsistencies in the original article. These include a flawed simplification of a Liénard-type equation, unjustified omissions of integration constants, and an incorrect use of the variation-of parameters method. ### [29] [Noncommutative black holes: Topological bulk-boundary correspondence and Binary Merger Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15150)
*Ankit Anand,Anshul Mishra,Aditya Singh,Saeed Noori Gashti,Neeraj Kumar,Phongpichit Channuie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文使用微扰展开和广义离壳自由能（generalized off-shell free-energy）框架，研究了非对易时空中带电AdS黑洞的热力学拓扑结构，发现非对易效应会定性改变热力学行为，且体-边界描述具有相同的全局热力学拓扑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于非对易时空下的精确解析临界热力学量无法获得，需借助微扰方法分析非对易效应如何修正带电AdS黑洞的热力学性质和拓扑结构。

Method: 采用洛伦兹涂抹（Lorentzian-smeared）物质分布描述非对易时空，对非对易参数进行微扰展开（perturbative expansion），并通过数值分析验证展开表达式；利用广义离壳自由能框架计算拓扑相空间的绕数（winding number），刻画相变特征。

Result: 非对易效应引入了与标准Reissner-Nordström AdS黑洞定性不同的热力学行为；体（bulk）描述和边界（boundary）描述具有完全相同的全局热力学拓扑结构；非对易修正改变了熵和最终黑洞质量等关键热力学量，并影响第二定律所隐含的残余质量下限。

Conclusion: 非对易时空的引入会非平凡地改变带电AdS黑洞的热力学拓扑，体-边界拓扑一致性为全息对应提供了新的证据；同时，非对易修正对热力学第二定律的约束条件产生重要影响。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic topology of charged AdS black holes in a non-commutative spacetime sourced by Lorentzian-smeared matter distributions. Since exact analytical solutions for the critical thermodynamic quantities are not available, we employ a perturbative expansion in the non-commutative parameter and validate the resulting expressions through numerical analysis. Using the generalized off-shell free-energy framework, we explore the topological structure of the thermodynamic phase space and evaluate the corresponding winding number that characterizes the phase transitions. Our results reveal that non-commutative effects introduce qualitative modifications to the thermodynamic behavior compared with the standard Reissner-Nordström AdS black hole. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the bulk and boundary descriptions possess an identical global thermodynamic topology, providing strong evidence for the correspondence between their topological structures. We also investigate the lower bound on the remnant mass implied by the second law of black-hole thermodynamics and observe that non-commutative corrections modify key thermodynamic quantities, with particular emphasis on the entropy and the final black-hole mass.

### [30] [Nonlinear Gravitational Wave Interactions in an Expanding Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15170)
*Fan Zhang,Lee Lindblom,Zhi-Peng Peng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过数值模拟探索了膨胀宇宙中引力波（gravitational waves）的非线性相互作用，发现能量从初始谱峰波长向更长和更短波长级联（cascade），且该级联随振幅的标度行为与四波散射模型（four-wave scattering models）的预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解膨胀宇宙中引力波的非线性相互作用机制，特别是能量在不同波长之间的输运行为，以及验证引力波湍流（gravitational-wave turbulence）的理论模型。

Method: 在宇宙学模型中对随机引力波系综（random ensembles of gravitational waves）进行数值演化，模拟过程中空间体积增长超过一个数量级。通过设置不同的引力波振幅进行演化，对比级联行为与四波散射模型的预测。

Result: 引力波谱演化显示能量从初始谱峰波长同时向更长和更短波长方向级联。不同振幅下的演化结果表明，级联行为以四波散射模型预测的方式随振幅标度（scale with amplitude）。

Conclusion: 膨胀宇宙中引力波的非线性相互作用支持四波散射模型对引力波湍流的描述，为理解宇宙学尺度上的引力波能量输运提供了数值依据。

Abstract: This study explores the nonlinear interactions between gravitational waves in an expanding universe. Random ensembles of gravitational waves are evolved numerically in cosmological models whose spatial volumes increase by more than an order of magnitude during these simulations. These evolutions show the spectra of the gravitational waves evolving as energy cascades away from the wavelengths at the peak of the initial spectra toward both longer and shorter wavelengths. Evolutions performed at different gravitational wave amplitudes are shown to produce cascades that scale with amplitude in the way predicted by the four-wave scattering models of gravitational-wave turbulence.

</details>
