# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [31] [Decoherence and More Coherence in the Radiative Decay of the $Z$ Boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12015)
*Kun Cheng,Tao Han,Harman Singh,Youle Su*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该文以Z玻色子辐射衰变为例，研究了标准模型手征相互作用下τ⁻τ⁺γ自旋态在全三体相空间中的量子信息特征，发现光子辐射可导致费米子对发生退相干或单调增强纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对撞过程终态辐射（final state radiation）可视为与未观测自由度的相互作用，常在纠缠态退相干（decoherence）语境下被讨论。本文旨在定量研究辐射如何改变费米子对的自旋态。

Method: 选择Z玻色子辐射衰变（radiative decay）作为代表案例，基于标准模型的手征相互作用（chiral interactions），在全三体相空间（three-body phase space）中对τ⁻τ⁺γ自旋态进行详细的解析研究，并采用多种量子信息观测量（quantum information observables）进行刻画。

Result: 发现若干显著特征：发射的光子可导致费米子对产生退相干（decoherence），也可能导致纠缠（entanglement）的单调增强（monotonic enhancement）。

Conclusion: 终态辐射对费米子对自旋态的影响并非单纯的退相干，而是呈现复杂的量子信息行为，包括纠缠增强的可能性，这对理解高能过程中的量子关联具有重要意义。

Abstract: Final state radiation in collider processes can be interpreted as interactions with unobserved degrees of freedom and is often discussed within the context of decoherence of an entangled state. We consider the radiative decay of the $Z$ boson as a representative example and perform a detailed analytical study of the $τ^-τ^+γ$ spin state, as determined by the chiral interactions of the Standard Model, over the complete three-body phase space. We explore various quantum information observables to quantify how the $τ^-τ^+$ spin state changes with the photon radiation. We find some striking features, for example that the emitted photon could either lead to decoherence or monotonic enhancement of entanglement for the fermion pair.

</details>


### [32] [Candia-v2: Logarithmic expansions for DGLAP evolution in $x$-space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14151)
*Casey Hampson,Marco Guzzi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 Candia-v2，一个将 x 空间 Candia 算法推广到量子色动力学（Quantum Chromodynamics, QCD）中次次次领头阶（N³LO）精度的开源软件包，通过高效的对数展开技术求解非极化核子部分子密度的 DGLAP 演化方程，并相较于原版 C 实现显著提升了效率与 API 设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将 Candia 算法从原有精度推广至次次次领头阶（N³LO），以满足量子色动力学（QCD）中更高精度非极化核子部分子密度（parton densities）演化计算的需求。

Method: 采用一种高效的对数展开技术（logarithmic expansion technique），该技术可系统地推广至 QCD 的所有阶（all orders），并在 x 空间（x-space）中求解 DGLAP 演化方程（DGLAP evolution equations）。

Result: Candia-v2 实现了 N³LO 精度的 DGLAP 演化计算，相比原版 C 实现显著提升了计算效率，并改进了应用程序接口（API）。

Conclusion: Candia-v2 作为一个开源软件包，已在 GitHub 上以 GPLv3 许可证公开发布，为高精度 QCD 部分子演化研究提供了更高效的工具。

Abstract: We present Candia-v2, an open-source software package that generalizes the $x$-space Candia algorithm to next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order (N$^{3}$LO) accuracy in Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD). The code solves the DGLAP evolution equations for unpolarized nucleon parton densities using a highly efficient logarithmic expansion technique that can be systematically extended to all orders in QCD. Candia-v2 supersedes the previous original C implementation of the algorithm with significantly increased efficiency and improved API. The software is publicly available on GitHub under the GPLv3 license.

</details>


### [33] [Searching for the $N$-naturalness tower of neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14243)
*Sofia Lonardi,Manuel Ettengruber,Philipp Eller*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次利用公开中微子数据对N-自然性（N-naturalness）模型中的中微子塔（neutrino tower）进行实验搜寻，并对参数空间（r, N）给出了排除界限，其中Majorana中微子情形下N ≤ 10⁴且r ≥ 0.1的区域已被排除，这意味着N=10⁴的无精细调节基准场景被否定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层级问题（hierarchy problem）是粒子物理标准模型中的悬而未决难题，N-自然性（N-naturalness）模型通过引入N个暗扇区（dark sectors）及变化希格斯质量参数（varying Higgs mass parameter）来试图解决这一问题。作者旨在利用现有中微子实验数据对该模型进行首次实验检验。

Method: 采用全局分析方法（global analysis），对公开的中微子数据进行联合分析，在正常顺序（normal ordering）与倒转顺序（inverted ordering）以及中微子为Majorana或Dirac情形下，对N-自然性模型的参数空间（r, N）施加约束并推导排除界限（exclusion limits）。

Result: 对于Majorana中微子情形，N ≤ 10⁴且r ≥ 0.1的参数区域已被排除。这一结果直接否定了N=10⁴、无需精细调节的规范与引力统一（gauge and gravitational unification around M_GUT）这一N-自然性框架的基准场景（benchmark scenario）。

Conclusion: 中微子实验数据对N-自然性模型给出了有意义的实验约束，尤其在Majorana中微子条件下排除了该模型最受青睐的无精细调节参数区域，表明这一层级问题解决方案面临实验挑战。

Abstract: We present the first experimental search for the $N$-naturalness tower of neutrinos using a global analysis of publicly available neutrino data. As a potential solution to the hierarchy problem, the $N$-naturalness model employs a varying Higgs mass parameter among $N$ dark sectors and encodes the required fine-tuning of the placement of the sectors in a parameter $r$. We report exclusion limits on the parameter space ($r$, $N$), for normal and inverted ordering and in case the neutrino is Majorana or Dirac. In the case of a Majorana neutrino, we can rule out $N\leq 10^4$ sectors with $r\geq 0.1$. This is particularly exciting as it shows that a gauge and gravitational unification around $M_{GUT}$, which is a benchmark scenario of the $N$-naturalness framework with $N=10^4$ without fine-tuning, is ruled out by neutrino experiments.

</details>


### [34] [Production Effects and Final-state Interactions in $π_1 \to 3π$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14300)
*D. Winney,S. Gonzàlez-Solís,M. Mikhasenko,Ł. Bibrzycki,C. Fernández-Ramírez,V. Mathieu,G. Montaña,A. Pilloni,L. Qiu,A. Rodas,A. P. Szczepaniak*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于COMPASS合作组“自由等压线（freed-isobar）”技术对$π_1(1600)$介子的$3π$衰变道进行分析，利用Khuri-Treiman形式论构建了统一描述产生效应与末态相互作用的框架，通过对$π_1$自由等压线数据集进行全局拟合，提取了短程产生与Deck机制的贡献，并获得了总$3π$不变质量依赖关系，为未来提取$ρπ$道中的$π_1$极点位置奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: COMPASS合作组近期利用“自由等压线”技术分析了$J^{PC}=1^{-+}$奇特介子$π_1(1600)$的$3π$信号道，该技术揭示了$P$-波$ππ$子道的线形修正来自末态相互作用（final state interactions）与产生过程（如Deck机制），但缺乏统一的理论描述。本文旨在建立一个同时包含产生效应与末态相互作用的统一形式论，以精确理解不同产生机制的相对强度与复杂相位。

Method: 采用Khuri-Treiman形式论（Khuri-Treiman formalism）构建统一框架，该形式论与低能幺正性（unitarity）、解析性（analyticity）和交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）一致，并以初始产生振幅为种子。在此基础上，对COMPASS的$π_1$自由等压线数据集进行全局拟合（global fit），得到$π_1\to3π$衰变振幅的多维参数化。

Result: 通过全局拟合识别了短程产生（short-range production）与Deck机制（Deck mechanism）对$3π$末态的不同贡献，并提取了总$3π$不变质量依赖关系。$ππ$质量谱的精确线形（lineshape）被证明可用于确定不同产生机制的相对强度与复杂相位。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一形式论成功描述了$π_1(1600)$信号道中的产生效应与末态相互作用，所得总$3π$不变质量依赖关系为未来在$ρπ$道中提取$π_1$极点位置（pole position）提供了关键输入。

Abstract: We investigate the $π_1(1600)$ signal channel of $3π$ in the $J^{PC} = 1^{-+} \,[ππ]_{1^{--}}π~P$-wave. This channel has recently been analyzed by the COMPASS collaboration using the ``freed-isobar" technique which provides direct experimental access to the lineshape modifications of the $P$-wave $ππ$ sub-channel arising from both final state interactions and production processes such as the Deck mechanism. We motivate a unified formalism combining production effects and final state interactions using the Khuri-Treiman formalism, which is consistent with low-energy unitarity, analyticity, and crossing symmetry, seeded by an initial production amplitude. We demonstrate that the precise lineshape of the $ππ$ mass spectrum can be used to determine the relative strength and complex phase of different production mechanisms contributing to the $3π$ final state. We conduct a global fit of the $π_1$ freed-isobar data set, yielding a multi-dimensional parameterization of the $π_1\to3π$ decay amplitude at COMPASS as a function of both decay and production variables. We identify the contributions from short-range production and the Deck mechanism and extract the total $3π$ invariant mass dependence which will be important for a future extraction of the $π_1$ pole position in the $ρπ$ channel.

</details>


### [35] [Relativistic corrections and high-energy resummation for exclusive heavy quarkonium photoproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14986)
*Maxim Nefedov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文计算了高能重求和系数函数中O(v²)修正对矢量重夸克偶素（vector heavy quarkonia）光生过程的贡献，并发现该修正虽在给定标度下可忽略，但能部分抵消O(v²)修正对重整化标度（renormalization scale）μ_F的依赖性，从而增强预测的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有高能重求和（high-energy resummation）框架对重夸克偶素（heavy quarkonia）光生过程的描述需要纳入O(v²)阶次修正，以更精确地考虑相对论效应和标度依赖性，从而提高理论预测的可靠性。

Method: 采用重求和（resummation）方法，计算了高能系数函数中O(v²)修正项，该修正包含了O(v² α_sⁿ ln^{n-1}(x/ξ))形式的贡献；并通过Gremm-Kapustin关系将结果用物理矢量介子质量（M_V）和相对重夸克速度（⟨v²⟩）表达。

Result: 在标度μ_F=M_V下，所计算的O(v²)修正数值上可忽略不计；但该修正能部分抵消O(v²)修正中由重整化标度（μ_F）变化引起的贡献，从而改善对LO系数函数在α_s中O(v²)修正的标度依赖行为。

Conclusion: 该O(v²)修正有助于提高对矢量重夸克偶素光生过程高能重求和预测的稳健性（robustness）。

Abstract: The $O(v^2)$ correction to the high-energy resummed coefficient function for the exclusive photoproduction of vector ($1^{--}$) heavy quarkonia off hadrons is computed, thereby taking into account corrections of $O(v^2 α_s^n \ln^{n-1}(x/ξ))$. When expressed in terms of the physical vector-meson mass ($M_V$) and the relative heavy-quark velocity ($\langle v^2 \rangle$) using the Gremm-Kapustin relation, the computed correction turns out to be negligible at the scale $μ_F=M_V$. However, it partially cancels the $μ_F$ dependence of the $O(v^2)$ correction to the LO coefficient function in $α_s$, thereby improving the robustness of the predictions.

</details>


### [36] [Radiative corrections in neutral-current (anti)neutrino elastic scattering at $\text{GeV}$ energies I: Nucleon targets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15050)
*Yi Chen,Oleksandr Tomalak,Bing-Song Zou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在有效场论框架下引入了GeV能量中性流（中微子/反中微子）-核子弹性散射的辐射修正，将截面分解为软函数和硬函数，阐明了振幅和截面层面上的（反）中微子味依赖性，并改进了低能中性流过程的量子色动力学（QCD）贡献。单核子水平的辐射修正幅度与奇异夸克贡献相当，且与BNL E734和MiniBooNE实验数据高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有中性流（neutral-current）中微子-核子弹性散射计算缺乏在GeV能区下完整的辐射修正处理，特别是有效场论（effective field theory）框架下的系统分解和味依赖性分析尚未被充分研究。

Method: 在有效场论框架中引入辐射修正（radiative corrections），将散射截面分解为软函数（soft function）和硬函数（hard function），并分别在振幅和截面两个层面上分析（反）中微子味依赖性（flavor dependence）；同时改进了低能中性流过程中量子色动力学（QCD）的贡献计算。

Result: 单核子水平的辐射修正幅度达到与奇异夸克（strange quark）贡献相当的量级；模型预测与BNL E734和MiniBooNE两个实验合作组的实验数据展现出极好的一致性（excellent agreement）。

Conclusion: 本文发展的有效场论辐射修正方法能够准确描述GeV能区的中性流中微子-核子弹性散射过程，该修正不可忽略，且理论结果得到实验验证。

Abstract: We introduce radiative corrections in neutral-current (anti)neutrino-nucleon elastic scattering at $\text{GeV}$ energies within the effective field theory framework. We factorize cross sections into soft and hard functions, clarify the (anti)neutrino flavor dependence at both amplitude and cross-section levels, and improve the quantum chromodynamics (QCD) contributions to low-energy neutral-current processes. The radiative corrections at the single-nucleon level reach a magnitude comparable to the contributions from strange quarks. We also compare our results with the experimental data from BNL E734 and MiniBooNE collaborations, finding excellent agreements with the experimental data.

</details>


### [37] [Next-to-next-to-leading order QCD corrections to pion (kaon)-induced exclusive Drell-Yan process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15214)
*Yu Jia,Bernard Pire,Qin-Tao Song,Guang Tang,Zhe-Yu Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在广义部分子分布（GPD）因子化框架下，计算了π⁻p → γ*(→ l⁺l⁻) + n 和 K⁻p → γ*(→ l⁺l⁻) + Λ 过程在领头扭度（leading twist）下的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正，发现修正显著且为正，对解释未来J-PARC实验数据至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日本J-PARC未来实验计划提供高能π介子与K介子束流，可用于研究由介子诱导的遍举Drell-Yan过程，该过程对应逆深度虚介子产生（inverse deeply virtual meson production）。为在理论预言与实验数据之间实现精确比较，需要计算高阶QCD修正。

Method: 采用广义部分子分布（generalized parton distribution, GPD）因子化框架（factorization framework），在广义Bjorken极限（generalized Bjorken limit, Q² ≫ |t|, Λ²_QCD）下进行领头扭度（leading twist）精度的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）QCD修正计算。

Result: 计算表明，NNLO QCD修正幅度显著且为正值（positive），表明该修正项不可忽略。

Conclusion: 纳入NNLO QCD修正是获得可靠理论预言的必要条件，对于将理论预言与未来J-PARC实验数据进行面对面对比（confrontation）具有不可或缺的重要性。

Abstract: The high-energy pion and kaon beams proposed for future experiments at J-PARC offer a unique opportunity to investigate exclusive Drell-Yan processes induced by pions or kaons, which correspond to inverse deeply virtual meson production with $M=π,K$. To facilitate precise comparisons between theoretical predictions and forthcoming experimental data, we calculate the next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD corrections to the processes $π^- p\to γ^*(\to l^+l^-) + n$ and $K^- p\to γ^*(\to l^+l^-) + Λ$. Our calculations are performed within the generalized parton distribution (GPD) factorization framework, accurate to leading twist in the generalized Bjorken limit ($Q^2\gg |t|,\,Λ_{\rm QCD}^2$). We find that the NNLO QCD corrections are substantial and positive; therefore, their inclusion is imperative for reliable theoretical predictions in confrontation with future experiments.

</details>


### [38] [New approach to the estimation of the lowest boundary of an axion mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14156)
*Sevinj O. Huseynova,Vali A. Huseynov,Nigar E. Musazade,Sevinj Y. Rzayeva*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过考虑电子反常磁矩，在恒定均匀磁场中分析电子能谱，并将其应用于氢原子超精细结构中的三重态-单重态跃迁，理论估计出轴子（axion）质量的最低边界应大于5.885微电子伏特，并指出太阳黑子中电子发射太阳轴子（solar axion）的磁场强度阈值与轴子质量相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对轴子质量的最低边界进行理论估算，以限定轴子（axion）这一假想粒子的质量范围，从而为暗物质或超出标准模型的新物理提供约束。

Method: 在恒定均匀磁场中分析电子能谱，纳入电子的反常磁矩（anomalous magnetic moment）；将所得能谱结果应用于氢原子电子（该电子同时处于质子库仑场和质子磁矩产生的磁场中）；将轴子质量下限的约束思想应用于氢原子s能级超精细结构（hyperfine structure）分裂产生的相邻能级间的三重态-单重态跃迁（triplet-singlet transition）。

Result: 轴子质量应大于5.885微电子伏特（microelectron-Volt）；磁场中电子发射轴子得以实现的最小磁场强度由轴子质量决定；假设部分太阳轴子由太阳黑子（sunspots）中的电子发射，可预期轴子质量最低边界约为10微电子伏特量级。

Conclusion: 轴子质量存在一个理论上的最低边界，该边界可通过氢原子超精细结构中的磁跃迁过程加以约束，且与太阳黑子磁场强度存在关联。

Abstract: In this work, we have performed the theoretical estimation of the lowest boundary of an axion mass. We have analyzed the energy spectrum of the electron in a constant homogeneous magnetic field, taking into account its anomalous magnetic moment. We have applied the obtained results on the energy spectrum of the electron in a constant homogeneous magnetic field with allowance for its anomalous magnetic moment to the hydrogen atom electron, which is located in addition to the Coulomb field of the proton, as well as in the magnetic field produced by the magnetic moment of the proton. We have applied the idea of the restriction for the lowest boundary of the axion mass to the triplet-singlet transition between two adjacent levels obtained as a result of the hyperfine structure splitting of the s-levels in the hydrogen atom. We have concluded that the mass of an axion ought to be more than 5.885 microelectron-Volt. We have determined that the minimum value of the magnetic field strength at which the axion emission by the electron in a magnetic field starts to be realized is determined by the axion mass. This result enables us to estimate the expected value of the lowest boundary for the axion mass (of the order of 10 microelectron-Volt), assuming that some part of the solar axions is emitted by the electrons located in sunspots.

</details>


### [39] [Thermal Masses and Bubble-Wall Friction in Cosmological Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14867)
*Carlo Branchina,Stefania De Curtis,Luigi Delle Rose,Alessio Notari,Giuliano Panico,Matthew Starbuck*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了第一性宇宙学相变中气泡壁摩擦问题，发现通过一致引入热质量（thermal masses）可以抑制红外交联玻色子（infrared gauge bosons）的虚假增强贡献，使规范玻色子成为次主导，壁速度主要由顶夸克摩擦决定，从而降低摩擦计算对红外等离子体区域的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation）方法中，红外规范玻色子（infrared gauge bosons）的贡献因无质量近似被人为放大，成为主要的不确定来源。本研究旨在通过一致引入热质量（thermal masses）来评估这一不确定性对摩擦计算的实际影响。

Method: 在玻尔兹曼方程的两种核心部分——李维尔算符（Liouville operator）和碰撞积分（collision integrals）中一致地引入热质量，系统分析其对非平衡扰动源项和相互作用率的影响。

Result: 热质量对顶夸克的源项和相互作用率产生大致相互抵消的影响，仅带来百分比量级的变化；但对红外规范玻色子的贡献产生强烈抑制，将主导动量尺度移至温度量级，使规范玻色子成为次主导贡献。

Conclusion: 在单粒子扩展标准模型（singlet-extended Standard Model）中的示例表明，壁速度主要由顶夸克摩擦决定；热质量有效降低了摩擦计算对等离子体中难以控制的红外区域（infrared sector）的敏感性。

Abstract: Bubble-wall friction controls the dynamics of first-order cosmological phase transitions. In Boltzmann-equation approaches, a major uncertainty arises from infrared gauge bosons, whose contribution is artificially enhanced in the massless approximation. We study the impact of thermal masses by including them consistently in both the Liouville operator and the collision integrals. Thermal masses suppress the source term for out-of-equilibrium perturbations while also reducing interaction rates. These effects largely cancel for top quarks, giving only percent-level changes, but they strongly suppress the infrared gauge-boson contribution, shifting the dominant momenta to scales of order the temperature. As a result, gauge bosons become subleading and wall velocities are close to those obtained from top-quark friction alone. We illustrate this in the singlet-extended Standard Model. Our results show that thermal masses reduce the sensitivity of friction calculations to the poorly controlled infrared sector of the plasma.

</details>


### [40] [Model-Independent and Data-Driven Extraction of the Photon Distribution Function at the Electron--Ion Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14958)
*Cong Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于截面比（cross-section ratio）的反演方法，用于在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）上提取部分子分布函数（distribution functions）。通过将卷积结构约化为乘法形式，该方法利用实验微分截面与微扰可算理论输入的比值直接关联目标分布函数，并讨论了软光子辐射、有限区间宽度和实验接收度等实际因素对理论输入构造的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）实验中，提取部分子分布函数（distribution functions）是核心物理目标之一。现有方法通常依赖复杂的卷积反演，计算代价高且易受系统误差影响。本文旨在发展一种基于截面比（cross-section ratio）的简化反演方法，以更直接、稳健地从实验数据中提取分布函数。

Method: 从一般因子化公式（factorization formula）$dσ = H \otimes f$ 出发，该研究证明对于特定的轫致辐射（bremsstrahlung）过程和适当选择的微分观测量，卷积结构可简化为乘法形式。在此基础上定义比值 $R = dσ_{\mathrm{exp}} / dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}$，其中 $dσ_{\mathrm{exp}}$ 为实验测量的微分截面，$dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}$ 为微扰可算的理论输入，进而建立 $R$ 与目标分布函数 $f$ 的关系。最后，研究考察了软光子辐射、有限区间宽度（finite-bin-width）效应和实验接收度（experimental acceptance）对理论输入构造的影响。

Result: 成功建立了截面比 $R$ 与目标分布函数 $f$ 之间的直接关系，表明在特定轫致辐射过程和合适观测量下，卷积反演可转化为更简单的代数运算。同时给出了在包含软光子辐射、有限区间宽度效应和实验接收度等实际条件下，如何合理构造理论输入 $dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}$ 的方案。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于截面比的反演方法为EIC上提取分布函数提供了一种优于传统卷积反演的理论框架，尤其适用于轫致辐射过程，且能够纳入实验中的多种实际修正因素。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate a cross-section-ratio-based inversion method for extracting distribution functions at the Electron--Ion Collider (EIC). Starting from the general factorization formula $dσ= H \otimes f$, we show that, for an appropriate bremsstrahlung process and suitably chosen differential observables, the convolution structure can be reduced to a multiplicative form. On this basis, we define the ratio $R = \frac{dσ_{\mathrm{exp}}}{dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}},$ where $dσ_{\mathrm{exp}}$ is the experimentally measured differential cross section and $dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}$ is a perturbatively calculable theoretical input. We then establish the relation between $R$ and the target distribution function $f$. Finally, we investigate how the theoretical input $dσ_{\mathrm{hard}}$ should be constructed when soft-photon radiation, finite-bin-width effects, and experimental acceptance are taken into account.

</details>


### [41] [Spacelike-Collinear Scattering by the Method of Regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15126)
*Wen Chen,Einan Gardi,Rourou Ma,Yao Ma,Yang Zhang,Zehao Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用区域法（Method of Regions）研究规范理论散射振幅的类空共线极限（spacelike-collinear limit）。研究发现，分裂振幅（splitting amplitude）对非共线部分子（non-collinear partons）运动学（kinematics）的依赖来源于一个独特的“隐藏区域”（hidden region），该区域在类时极限（timelike limit）中不存在。作者提出隐藏区域是不同交叉相关渐近极限失去解析联系（analytically connected）的机制，并开发了系统识别隐藏区域的算法。通过超杨-米尔斯理论（super Yang-Mills theory）的五点振幅计算，验证了隐藏区域贡献能完全解释运动学依赖的因子化破坏（factorisation-violating）分裂振幅，并揭示了其与软胶子（soft）和Glauber圈动量（Glauber loop momenta）的关联，从而解释了Wilson线（Wilson-line）计算的普适性（universality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规范理论散射振幅的共线极限分裂振幅已知会违背严格共线因子化（collinear factorisation），其对非共线部分子的色关联（colour dependence）虽早已明确，但两圈及以上层次产生的运动学依赖（kinematic dependence）的物理来源尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这一运动学依赖的起源，并阐明不同交叉相关渐近极限（如类空与类时共线极限）之间解析联系的丧失机制。

Method: 采用区域法（Method of Regions）对五点振幅在类空共线极限下的渐近展开进行分析，识别出区别于类时极限的“隐藏区域”（hidden region）。随后，开发了一套系统识别所有隐藏区域的通用算法，并将其应用于超杨-米尔斯理论（super Yang-Mills theory）的五点振幅计算，对完整集合的基积分（basis integrals）逐一计算隐藏区域贡献。

Result: 发现一个独特的隐藏区域仅存在于类空共线极限的五点振幅渐近展开中，而在类时极限中完全缺失。该隐藏区域贡献精确地恢复了已知的运动学依赖的因子化破坏分裂振幅（factorisation-violating splitting amplitude）。在动量空间（momentum space）中，该隐藏区域的特征是软胶子（soft）和Glauber圈动量（Glauber loop momenta）。

Conclusion: 隐藏区域是导致类空与类时共线极限间因子化行为差异的根本机制，也是交叉相关渐近极限失去解析联系的原因。由于隐藏区域对应于软和Glauber动量构型，这使得Wilson线计算能够捕捉完整的运动学依赖，从而解释了该效应在不同规范理论中的普适性（universality）。

Abstract: We study the spacelike-collinear limit of gauge-theory scattering amplitudes using the Method of Regions. The corresponding splitting amplitude violates strict collinear factorisation through its dependence on the non-collinear partons. While the associated colour dependence has long been known, starting at two loops the splitting amplitude also acquires dependence on their kinematics. We show that this kinematic dependence originates from a unique hidden region present in the asymptotic expansion of the five-point amplitude in the spacelike-collinear limit, but absent in the timelike limit. More generally, we propose that hidden regions provide the mechanism by which crossing-related asymptotic limits cease to be analytically connected. We develop a general algorithm for the systematic identification of hidden regions. Applying it to the five-point amplitude in super Yang-Mills theory, we compute the hidden-region contributions to the complete set of basis integrals and recover the exact kinematically dependent factorisation-violating splitting amplitude. In momentum space, the hidden region is characterised by soft and Glauber loop momenta. This explains why the Wilson-line calculation captures the complete kinematic dependence, thereby accounting for the observed universality across gauge theories.

</details>


### [42] [Massive On-shell Splitting Functions in Spinor-Helicity Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15191)
*Yi-Ning Wang,Chao Wu,Jiang-Hao Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Soper-Weinberg共线旋量的在壳构造形式理论，系统推导了标准模型中所有领头阶和次领头阶的大质量共线分裂函数（massive collinear splitting functions），并建立了与无质量分裂函数之间的匹配字典，为精确对撞机物理和部分子簇射（parton shower）开发提供了灵活的计算工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在壳旋量-螺旋度方法已成功导出无质量QCD分裂函数，但对于包含有限质量效应的大质量粒子，尚缺乏完整的在壳构造方案。

Method: 基于Soper-Weinberg共线旋量（Soper-Weinberg collinear spinors），利用庞加莱群的光前伽利略子群（light-front Galilean subgroup）变换性质；将大质量动量和旋量相对于固定光矢分解，使得对准区域（alignment regime）的展开显式化；领头阶结构匹配到无质量三点振幅，次领头阶通过沿另一光矢的希格斯动量（Higgs momentum）探测次领头旋量分量，并关联到无质量四点振幅。

Result: 导出了所有标准模型粒子的完整领头阶和次领头阶大质量分裂函数；建立了无质量与有质量耦合系数在三点和四点层面的系统匹配字典；通过递归自举关系（recursive bootstrap relation）和伽利略对称性导出的普适替换规则，获得了更高点分裂函数。

Conclusion: 该构造框架自然扩展到有效场论算符和更高微扰阶，为精确对撞机物理和部分子簇射开发提供了灵活的计算工具。

Abstract: Collinear splitting functions govern parton evolution, parton showers, and resummation at high-energy colliders. While on-shell spinor-helicity methods have successfully yielded massless QCD splitting functions, a complete on-shell construction for massive particles, systematically incorporating finite-mass effects, is less developed. We present an on-shell constructive formalism for massive collinear splitting functions based on Soper-Weinberg collinear spinors, whose transformation properties follow from a light-front Galilean subgroup of the Poincaré group. Decomposing massive momenta and spinors with respect to fixed lightlike vectors $n$ and $\bar n$ makes the expansion in the alignment regime $m<p_T\ll p_+$ manifest. The leading-order structures are matched to massless three-point amplitudes, while an additional Higgs momentum along $\bar n$ probes the subleading spinor components and relates them to massless four-point amplitudes. We derive the complete set of leading and subleading massive splitting functions for all Standard Model particles and establish a systematic matching dictionary between massless and massive coupling coefficients at both the three- and four-point levels. Higher-point splitting functions are obtained through the recursive bootstrap relation with a universal substitution rule as a consequence of the Galilean symmetry. This constructive framework extends naturally to effective field theory operators and higher perturbative orders, providing a flexible computational tool for precision collider physics and parton shower development.

</details>


### [43] [Particle production from bubble collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15279)
*Anish Ghoshal,Pratyay Pal,Alessandro Strumia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出宇宙学相变中超相对论气泡碰撞产生重粒子的传统模型存在参数化高估和规范依赖性等缺陷，并提出了一种类似高能碰撞部分子描述的新形式体系，该体系基于准直壁中量子之间的在壳散射来解释硬粒子的产生，并应用于暗物质、轻子生成、引力子产生及原初引力波等物理场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学相变（cosmological phase transition）中超相对论（ultra-relativistic）气泡碰撞可以产生远高于相变能标的粒子，但现有基于标量背景离壳衰变（off-shell decay）的建模在参数化估计上过高且依赖于规范（gauge）和场空间坐标（coordinate choice in field space）的选择，因此需要更可靠的形式体系。

Method: 提出一种新形式体系（formalism），类比高能碰撞中的部分子描述（partonic description）。在超相对论极限下，碰撞气泡近乎自由穿过（free passage），硬粒子的产生来自构成洛伦兹收缩壁（Lorentz-contracted walls）的量子之间的在壳散射（on-shell scatterings）。

Result: 将这一方法应用于重标量（heavy scalar）、费米子（fermion）和矢量粒子（vector particle）的产生，并探讨了其对暗物质（dark matter）、轻子生成（leptogenesis）、引力子产生（graviton production）及原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）的影响。

Conclusion: 新形式体系避免了传统模型的参数化高估和依赖性问题，为宇宙学相变中重粒子产生提供了更自洽的描述，并具有多个天体物理学和宇宙学领域的重要应用前景。

Abstract: Collisions of ultra-relativistic bubbles during cosmological phase transitions can produce particles much heavier than the transition scale. Previous analyses modelled this process as the off-shell decay of the scalar background. We show that its results parametrically overestimate hard particle production and depend on the gauge choice and the coordinate choice in field space. We propose an alternative formalism, analogous to the partonic description of high-energy collisions. In the ultra-relativistic limit, the colliding bubbles undergo nearly free passage and hard production arises from on-shell scatterings among the quanta constituting the Lorentz-contracted walls. We apply this approach to heavy scalar, fermion, and vector particle production, and study the implications for dark matter, leptogenesis, graviton production and primordial gravitational waves.

### [45] [On the geometry of Coulomb branches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15177)
*Ben Webster*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文对三维 N=4 规范理论的库仑分支（Coulomb branch）给出了一种统一的几何描述，通过环面紧化（toric compactification）的爆破（blowup）来刻画其在有理、K-理论和椭圆设定下的结构；并利用局部描述对库仑分支的辛叶（symplectic leaf）进行分类，同时讨论了与函子性和横向希尔伯特方案（transverse Hilbert scheme）相关的若干问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Braverman–Finkelberg–Nakajima 定义的库仑分支是一类重要的辛奇点（symplectic singularity），但缺乏跨有理/K-理论/椭圆三种设定的统一几何描述，且其辛叶分类和与 transverse Hilbert scheme 的关系尚需澄清。

Method: 对所有三种设定，采用环面紧化的爆破构造库仑分支的几何实现；利用局部描述对库仑分支的辛叶进行分类，并将其零维叶的分类归结为更小库仑分支的对应分类；修正 Gannon 与作者关于库仑分支函子性定理中的一个不必要假设，并细化 Bielawski–Foscolo 的方法以阐明与 transverse Hilbert scheme 的联系。

Result: 给出了库仑分支在有理、K-理论和椭圆设定下的统一几何描述；完成了库仑分支的辛叶分类，并将 transverse slice 描述为更小库仑分支零维叶的分类结果；移除了函子性定理中一个不必要的假设，精炼了与 transverse Hilbert scheme 的关系。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种统一的几何框架理解三维 N=4 规范理论的库仑分支，建立了辛叶分类及其与更小库仑分支的联系，并澄清了函子性和 transverse Hilbert scheme 方面的遗留问题。

Abstract: Coulomb branches of 3-dimensional $N=4$ gauge theories, as defined by Braverman--Finkelberg--Nakajima, form a large and interesting class of symplectic singularities. In this paper, we give a geometric description of these varieties in terms of blowups of toric compactifications, uniformly across the rational, $K$-theoretic, and elliptic settings, which in physics are often associated with 3-, 4-, and 5-dimensional versions of these theories. We use the resulting local description to classify the symplectic leaves of Coulomb branches and describe their transverse slices in terms of the classification of zero-dimensional leaves of certain smaller Coulomb branches.
  We also discuss related topics, including removing an unnecessary hypothesis from a theorem of Gannon and the author on functoriality for Coulomb branches, and clarifying the relationship with transverse Hilbert schemes by refining the approach of Bielawski and Foscolo.

### [46] [Neural operators solve inverse problems for constitutive model discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15049)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 训练后的神经算子仅需一次前向传播即可从实验数据集推断应变能密度函数，实现近瞬时材料表征。在未见数据、含噪声数据、信息缺失数据、不同空间离散化数据以及不同尺寸几何体数据上均验证了预测能力。

Abstract: Characterizing the mechanical response of materials traditionally requires solving optimization problems in which model parameters are calibrated or trained to minimize the discrepancy between model predictions and experimental data. This process can be computationally expensive and time-consuming. To overcome this limitation, we propose two neural operator architectures that directly map experimentally measured data to the constitutive functions governing the mechanical response of the material: Physics-Augmented Neural Operators (PANO) and Constitutive Artificial Neural Operators (CANO). The proposed neural operators approximate the mapping between the infinite-dimensional input space of full-field displacement measurements and net reaction forces, and the infinite-dimensional output space of hyperelastic strain-energy density functions. The displacement fields are encoded through Laplacian eigenfunctions to obtain discretization-independent and noise-robust predictions. Our framework constrains the output space to physically admissible material models that satisfy fundamental physical requirements by design. The neural operators are trained on simulated data tuples of displacement fields and reaction forces for a range of material models. Once trained, the neural operators enable near-instantaneous material characterization and require only a single forward pass to infer the strain-energy density function from a given experimental dataset. We test the predictive power of the neural operators for unseen data, noisy data, data with missing information, data from different spatial discretizations, and data from geometries of different sizes.

### [47] [Overlapping Network Community Detection Using Sparse Backbones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14531)
*Zihe Zhou,Samin Aref*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Highway的可扩展重叠社区检测（overlapping community detection, OCD）算法，通过利用输入网络的稀疏骨干（sparse backbone）实现高效的社区推理，在728个基准网络上的对比实验中，该算法在重叠归一化互信息（overlapping normalized mutual information）指标上领先最强基线6.9%，并在其他四项性能指标中均排名第二，展现了良好的精度-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实网络中的社区结构广泛存在，提取社区有助于从药物发现到市场细分等多个应用领域。然而，现有重叠社区检测算法难以在检测质量与可扩展性（scalability）之间取得合适的平衡。

Method: Highway算法利用输入网络的稀疏骨干结构进行高效的社区推理。研究采用728个Lancichinetti-Fortunato-Radicchi（LFR）基准网络，将Highway及其消融版本（ablated version）与10种现有OCD算法进行了对比评估。

Result: 基于五项性能指标的评估显示，Highway在重叠归一化互信息指标上排名第一，相比最强基线提升了6.9%；在其他四项性能指标中均排名第二。对比结果表明，Highway与其骨干过程（backbone procedure）结合，实现了适合的精度-效率权衡。

Conclusion: Highway算法表现出有竞争力的检测性能，能够较好地平衡检测质量与可扩展性。该算法已开源，并作为CDlib库的一部分提供。

Abstract: Community structures are common in real networks, and extracting them provides valuable insight in applications ranging from drug discovery to market segmentation. Overlapping community detection (OCD) is the task of clustering networked data in which nodes may belong to multiple clusters. Existing OCD algorithms often struggle to achieve a suitable balance between detection quality and scalability. We, therefore, propose Highway, a scalable OCD algorithm that exploits the sparse backbone of the input network to perform efficient community inference. We used 728 Lancichinetti-Fortunato-Radicchi benchmark networks to compare Highway and its ablated version against 10 existing OCD algorithms. Our results, based on five performance measures, demonstrate a competitive performance for Highway. It ranks first in overlapping normalized mutual information with a 6.9% improvement over the strongest baseline. It also ranks second in all the other four performance measures. These comparative results suggest that Highway coupled with its backbone procedure offers a suitable accuracy-efficiency trade-off. The Highway algorithm is open-source and available as part of the CDlib library.

</details>

### [48] [Comprehensive study of timing resolution in plastic scintillator detectors with wavelength-shifting fiber and silicon photomultiplier readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14290)
*Haohui Che,Guang Yang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文通过半解析框架、玩具蒙特卡洛验证和完整Geant4光学光子模拟，系统研究了波长位移（WLS）光纤耦合硅光电倍增管（SiPM）读出塑料闪烁体探测器的定时分辨率，建立了从闪烁发光到电子学量化的完整光子探测链解析模型，并通过大规模参数扫描生成了探测器优化设计图谱和查找表。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确掌握塑料闪烁体探测器的定时分辨率（timing resolution）对于高能物理、医学成像等领域的关键应用至关重要，但目前缺乏一个能够完整覆盖光子探测全链并定量关联各物理参数的统一解析框架。

Method: 采用三层次研究方法：首先建立半解析模型，将定时分辨率$\sigt$表达为探测光电子产额$\Npe$、闪烁体衰减常数（$\taur$, $\taud$）、WLS再发射时间（$\tauwls$）、光纤数值孔径、几何结构及读出电子学参数的函数；其次通过玩具蒙特卡洛模拟（每参数点$2\times 10^5$事件，80个网格点覆盖8种光纤类型和$\Npe$范围5–200）进行验证；最后用完整Geant4光学光子模拟在真实探测器几何中跟踪闪烁、波长位移和光纤传输全过程，提供第一性原理光电子产额校准。

Result: 半解析模型与玩具蒙特卡洛的吻合度达$0.9997 \pm 0.0015$；完整Geant4模拟证实了解析模型的定时预测并提供了光电子产额校准；涵盖7种闪烁体材料、8种WLS光纤、5种SiPM模型、5种电子学配置、3种读出拓扑和3种边界条件的全面参数扫描生成了定量设计图谱和查找表。

Conclusion: 所提出的半解析框架能够准确预测塑料闪烁体探测器的定时分辨率，经多层次模拟充分验证；生成的设计图谱和查找表可为探测器优化提供直接参考。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of the timing resolution achievable in plastic scintillator detectors read out through wavelength-shifting (WLS) fibers coupled to silicon photomultipliers (SiPMs), combining a semi-analytical framework, toy Monte Carlo validation, and full Geant4 optical photon simulation. The analytical model traces the complete photon detection chain: scintillation emission, WLS fiber re-emission, optical transit time dispersion, SiPM single-photon time resolution, and electronics quantization. It expresses the timing resolution $\sigt$ as a function of the detected photoelectron yield $\Npe$, scintillator decay constants ($\taur$, $\taud$), WLS re-emission time ($\tauwls$), fiber numerical aperture, detector geometry, and readout electronics parameters. The analytical predictions are validated at two levels. First, toy Monte Carlo simulations ($2\times 10^5$ events per parameter point across 80 grid points spanning 8 fiber types and $\Npe$ from 5 to 200) achieve analytical-to-MC agreement of $0.9997 \pm 0.0015$. Second, full Geant4 optical photon simulations track the entire scintillation, wavelength-shifting, and fiber transport chain in realistic detector geometries, confirming the analytical timing predictions and providing first-principles photoelectron yield calibration. A comprehensive parameter scan covering 7 scintillator materials, 8 WLS fiber types, 5 SiPM models, 5 electronics configurations, 3 readout topologies, and 3 boundary conditions produces quantitative design maps and lookup tables for detector optimization.

*P. Federičováa,A. Affolder,K. Affolder,A. Awais,G. A. Beck,A. J. Bevan,Z. Chen,J. Dandoy,I. Dawson,V. Fadeyev,J. Fernandez-Tejero,E. C. Hill,S. Hirose,L. Hommels,T. Ivison,C. Jessiman,K. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为满足高亮度大型强子对撞机（High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider, HL-LHC）升级后严苛的运行需求，ATLAS实验需用全新的全硅内径迹探测器（Inner Tracker, ITk）替换现有内探测器，其中外跟踪层需部署约18,000个ATLAS18 n+-in-p硅条带传感器，因此必须建立大规模、标准化的质量控制（Quality Control, QC）体系以保障传感器性能。

Method: 通过跨多个国际机构的多年QC计划，对ITk条带传感器进行机械与电气一致性评估，流程包括IV/CV特性表征、全条带测试、长期电流稳定性监测、视觉检查与计量学测试；为实现每月约500个传感器的高通量处理，实施了标准化测试程序、数据监测与完整性检查软件包、统一数据格式以及自动化分析工具。

Result: 标准化框架确保了多站点生产期间一致的通过/失败评估与集中化数据处理，有效识别了传感器充电效应、漏电流稳定性、不可恢复的IV击穿以及晶圆内条间隔离不足等关键趋势与异常；超过91%的生产批次（总计590余批）经测试后被直接接受。

The silicon sensors, available in eight geometries tailored to two barrel and six endcap module types, respectively, are designed to tolerate fluences of up to 1.6 x 10^15 neq/cm2 and ionizing doses of 66 Mrad. A comprehensive, multi-year Quality Control (QC) program is underway across multiple international institutes to evaluate these ITk strip sensors for mechanical and electrical conformity. The QC process includes IV/CV characterization, full strip tests, long-term current stability monitoring, visual inspection, and metrology tests. To manage the high throughput of about 500 sensors per month, the collaboration has implemented standardized test procedures, software packages for data monitoring and integrity checks, unified data formats, and automated analysis tools. The standardization ensures consistent pass/fail evaluation and centralized data handling that enables effective identification of trends and anomalies at all sites during multi-year production. The design supports zero-back-20 pressure operation toward the ASIC and allows adaptation of the readout bandwidth to different21 experimental conditions. Synchronization between multiple DAQ systems is achieved through22 a common clock and trigger distribution network, experimentally demonstrated with sub-100 ps23 precision.24 The system has been developed to support detector characterization, laboratory measurements,25 and beam-test campaigns for the 4DPHOTON detector concept. Hardware organization, firmware26 architecture, synchronization strategy, and performance measurements are presented.

### [51] [Comparative study and optimization of SDHCAL hadronic energy reconstruction methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15023)
*Tanguy Pasquier,Gérald Grenier,Imad Laktineh*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文对ILD探测器概念下半数字强子量能器（SDHCAL）中的强子簇射能量重建方法进行了详细研究，利用粒子流算法（PFA）APRIL比较了线性、二次、分裂和多项式回归四种重建公式，发现分裂法与多项式回归在低能分辨率和高端线性度之间取得了最佳平衡，并指出未来引入T-SDHCAL精确时间信息可进一步提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对ILD探测器概念下半数字强子量能器（Semi-Digital Hadronic Calorimeter, SDHCAL）中的强子能量重建问题，评估不同重建公式对线性度和能量分辨率的影响，并探索未来改进方向。

Method: 利用单$K^0_L$事件和双喷注（dijet, $u,d,s$）事件样本，在线性、二次、分裂（split）和多项式回归（polynomial regression）四种重建公式下，结合粒子流算法（Particle Flow Algorithm, PFA）APRIL进行比较分析；同时针对桶部（barrel region）非垂直粒子入射引入角度校正（angular corrections）。

Result: 所有方法整体表现良好，其中分裂法和多项式回归在不同能量范围内提供了最佳折中：在低能区改善分辨率，同时不损害高能区的线性度。对于双喷注事件，高能区的分辨率主要受限于PFA混淆效应（PFA confusion）的敏感性。

Conclusion: 上述结果指向未来改进的潜力，即通过将T-SDHCAL的精确时间信息（precise timing information）集成到APRIL中，可进一步减少混淆效应、增强强子能量重建性能，进而服务于下一代轻子对撞机（next-generation lepton colliders）。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of hadronic shower energy reconstruction methods for the Semi-Digital Hadronic Calorimeter (SDHCAL) within the ILD detector concept, using the Particle Flow Algorithm (PFA) APRIL. Using samples of single $K^0_L$ and dijet ($u,d,s$) events, we compare linear, quadratic, split, and polynomial regression-based reconstruction formulas, focusing on their impact on linearity and resolution. The study also addresses angular corrections required in the barrel region due to non-perpendicular particle incidence. Results show that while all methods achieve good overall performance, the split method and the polynomial regression provide the best compromise across different energy regimes, offering improved resolution at low energies without compromising linearity at higher energies. For dijets, sensitivity to PFA confusion dominates the resolution at high energies. These findings highlight the potential of future improvements, notably the integration of precise timing information from the T-SDHCAL into APRIL, to further reduce confusion and enhance hadronic energy reconstruction for next-generation lepton colliders.

### [52] [Phase coherence control of a programmable high-Tc superconductor created by light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14567)
*Viktoria Yursa,Igor Vaskivskyi,Anze Mraz,Damjan Svetin,Sergej Raznjevic,Vinko Srsan,Saso Sturm,Tomaz Mertelj,Mikhail Feigelman,Dragan Mihailovic*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究首次在铝-硅异质结（aluminium-silicon heterojunction）中报道了一种由飞秒激光脉冲创建并完全控制的光可编程超导态（LiPS），其特征包括可调控的超导临界温度（1.8–8.5 K）、Berezinski-Kosterlitz-Thouless拓扑转变特征、量子相位无序以及磁通钉扎与蠕变行为，其起源归因于光脉冲对界面失配位错（MDs）形成的莫尔超晶格（Moiré-like superlattice）的调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找由光创建的超导态（superconductivity created by light）已有半个多世纪，但始终缺乏直接证据证明存在真正的零电阻态（zero-resistance state），即其宏观量子相位相干性（macroscopic quantum phase coherence）由光创建并控制。本工作旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 使用飞秒激光脉冲（femtosecond laser pulses）在铝-硅异质结（Al-Si heterojunction）上创建并全控光可编程超导态（LiPS），通过调控脉冲序列（pulse sequences）来增加或擦除超导临界温度（1.8–8.5 K），并利用高分辨率电子显微镜（high-resolution electron microscopy）观察莫尔超晶格（Moiré-like superlattice）的周期变化及拓扑孤子扭结（topologically protected soliton-like kinks）。

Result: LiPS态在低温下呈现Berezinski-Kosterlitz-Thouless拓扑转变特征，而在2 K以上则表现出量子相位无序（quantum phase disorder）特征；在磁场中观察到与二维（2D）相位相干体系一致的磁通钉扎（vortex pinning）与蠕变（creep）行为。光脉冲可通过调控界面失配位错（MDs）形成的莫尔超晶格周期来控制系统，并产生沿位错线的拓扑保护孤子扭结。

Conclusion: LiPS的发现开辟了设计亚稳长程相位相干超导态（metastable long-range phase coherent superconducting states）的路径，有望推动光工程量子电路（light-engineering of quantum circuits）、量子处理器中的局域能隙调控（local gap tuning）以及基于可开关超导性（switchable superconductivity）的新型器件的发展。

Abstract: The quest for superconductivity created by light extends for more than half a century, yet direct evidence of a true zero-resistance state -whose macroscopic quantum phase coherence is both created and controlled by light -- has remained elusive. Here we report for the first time on a complex but robust light-programmable superconducting (LiPS) state at an aluminium-silicon heterojunction that is created and fully controlled with femtosecond laser pulses. The superconducting critical temperatures -- ranging from 1.8-8.5 K, can be increased or erased at will by the application of tailored pulse sequences. At low temperatures the LiPS state shows features characteristic of a Berezinski-Kosterlitz-Thouless topological transition, but another distinct state appears at temperatures above 2 K, which shows clear signatures of quantum phase disorder. In the presence of a magnetic field we observe behaviour characteristic of vortex pinning and creep consistent with the 2-dimensional (2D) nature of the phase coherent system. The origin of the LiPS effect is attributed to light pulse control of the Moire-like superlattice of misfit dislocations (MDs) that naturally occur as a result of discommensurations between Al and Si lattices at the interface, and is clearly observable by high-resolution electron microscopy. We show how light pulses can be used to control the superlattice periodicity and highlight the appearance of topologically protected soliton-like kinks along the dislocation lines, important for imparting metastability to the system. The demonstration of LiPS opens a route to the design of metastable long-range phase coherent superconducting states, leading to light-engineering of quantum circuits, local gap tuning in quantum processors and novel devices utilizing switchable superconductivity.

### [53] [Spin fluctuation-mediated unconventional superconductivity in ThFeAsN from first-principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14677)
*Guang-Yu Guo,Jau-Wen Liu,Mitsuaki Kawamura*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 利用从头算超导密度泛函理论（ab initio superconducting density functional theory），考虑电子-声子耦合、静态与动态库仑排斥以及自旋涨落（spin fluctuation）介导的配对相互作用，计算表明 ThFeAsN 是一种自旋涨落介导的多带超导体，其超导转变温度（$T_c$）为 22.4 K，超导序参量（SC order parameter）为 $d_{xy}$-波，在不同费米面（Fermi surface sheet）上具有不同符号，与实验一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁基超导体中超导配对机制、高 $T_c$ 起源以及超导序参量对称性仍是凝聚态物理与材料物理中重要的未解问题。本研究旨在通过第一性原理计算澄清 ThFeAsN 这一具体铁基高温超导体的超导性质。

Method: 采用从头算超导密度泛函理论（ab initio superconducting density functional theory）进行计算，全面考虑了电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）、屏蔽的静态与动态电子-电子库仑排斥（screened static and dynamic electron-electron Coulomb repulsion）以及自旋涨落（spin fluctuation）介导的配对相互作用。

Result: 计算揭示 ThFeAsN 是一个自旋涨落介导的多带超导体（multiband superconductor），计算得到的 $T_c$ 为 22.4 K，且具有 $d_{xy}$-波超导序参量，在不同费米面片（Fermi surface sheet）上符号不同，与实验结果一致；同时给出了准粒子态密度（quasiparticle density of states）与超声衰减系数（ultrasonic attenuation coefficient）等可被实验验证的独特超导性质。

Conclusion: 计算结果与实验吻合，验证了自旋涨落介导的配对机制在 ThFeAsN 中的主导作用，并提供了一系列可被实验直接检验的独特超导性质，为理解铁基超导体的配对机制与序参量对称性提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Superconducting (SC) pairing mechanism, origin of high $T_c$ and symmetry of SC order parameter in Fe-based superconductors are among the important unsolved problems in condensed matter and materials physics. We study the SC properties of ThFeAsN, a Fe-based high $T_c$ superconductor, by {\it ab initio} superconducting density functional theory calculations with electron-phonon coupling, screened static and dynamic electron-electron Coulomb repulsion and spin fluctuation (SF) mediated pair-interaction fully taken into account. Our calculations reveal that ThFeAsN is a SF-mediated multiband superconductor with the calculated $T_c$ of 22.4 K and the $d_{xy}$-wave SC order parameter with different signs on different Fermi surface sheets, in consistent with experiments. We also present distinct SC properties such as quasiparticle density of states and ultrasonic attenuation coefficient which can be immediately verified by experiments.

### [54] [Imaging and characterization of spontaneous vortices in a proximity-induced superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14697)
*Iku Nakaaki,Kotaro Taki,Mio Nomura,Haruna Ishimaru,Minagi Yono,Jun Chen,Hiroyo Segawa,Akiko Nakamura,Taku Moronaga,Minoru Tachiki,Shuuichi Ooi,Shunichi Arisawa,Tsutomu Nojima,Takashi Uchino*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描超导量子干涉器件显微镜（scanning SQUID microscope）实验，在近零场条件下观察到临近耦合超导纳米复合物中自发产生的涡旋（spontaneous vortices），揭示了其多种极性、尺寸和形状，并证明其磁场分布比场诱导的Abrikosov涡旋更复杂、穿透深度更长（~1至~10微米），指出此类涡旋源于约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）与热相位涨落（thermal phase fluctuation）的竞争，其形貌记录了相变早期局域相位差的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）是理解连续二级相变（continuous second-order phase transition）的核心，但其在超导体中导致的拓扑缺陷（topological defects）——即量子化涡旋（quantized vortices）的几何特征尚未被充分研究和理解，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用临近耦合超导纳米复合物（proximity-coupled superconducting nanocomposite）作为成像体系，利用扫描超导量子干涉器件显微镜（scanning SQUID microscope）对自发涡旋进行成像和磁场分布测量，并与场诱导的Abrikosov涡旋进行对比。

Result: 在近零场条件下，观测到极性、尺寸和形状各异的自发涡旋；其磁场分布比场诱导的Abrikosov涡旋更扩展且复杂，穿透深度（penetration depth）更长，范围约为1至10微米。

Conclusion: 自发涡旋是在冷却过程中由约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）与热相位涨落（thermal phase fluctuation）竞争而产生；涡旋的形貌大概率冻结了其形成时刻的信息，为理解相变早期阶段的局域相位差异（local phase differences）提供了线索。

Abstract: Observation of spontaneous symmetry breaking is crucial to our understanding of a continuous second-order phase transition from a disordered system into an ordered one, which often leads to the formation of topological defects. In the case of superconductors, such topological defects are identified as quantized vortices. However, their geometrical characteristics have not been well investigated and understood yet. For the imaging of spontaneous vortices, we employ a proximity-coupled superconducting nanocomposite. Here we show from scanning superconducting quantum interference device microscope measurements that vortices with different polarities, size and shapes are observed stochastically especially under near zero-field conditions. The field distributions of the spontaneous vortices are more extended and intricate than those of the field induced Abrikosov vortices, yielding longer penetration depths ranging from ~1 to ~10 micrometer. The spontaneous vortices are created during cooling as a result of the competition between Josephson coupling and thermal phase fluctuation, both of which are inherently present in this proximity-coupled system. The morphology of the vortices most likely imprints the information that is frozen at the time of vortex formation, providing insights into the local phase differences that are present in the early stage of the phase transition.

</details>


### [55] [$c$-axis strain tuning of superconductivity and symmetric elastoresistivity in CsV$_3$Sb$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14803)
*Xiaoran Yang,Yutong Li,Chunyi Li,Qi Tang,Jiawen Zhang,Yu Song,Huiqiu Yuan,Xingye Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过结合面内单轴应变与直接c轴压缩实验，独立解耦了Kagome金属CsV₃Sb₅中不同对称性应变通道对电荷密度波（CDW）序与超导电性的竞争调控作用，揭示了c轴晶格控制在调控该体系中交织电子态中起主导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome金属CsV₃Sb₅中电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）序与超导电性之间存在对晶格畸变高度敏感的复杂竞争关系。此前基于压电器件的实验无法区分面内（A₁g,₁）与面外（A₁g,₂）对称应变通道各自的具体作用，从而阻碍了对该体系关键物理机制的深入理解。

Method: 本文将面内单轴应变（in-plane uniaxial strain）与直接c轴压缩（direct c-axis compression）相结合，独立访问并解缠了CsV₃Sb₅中不同对称性分辨的应变响应通道。通过测量纯弹阻系数（pure elastoresistivity coefficients），提取了面外交叉耦合系数m₁₃与面内响应系数m₁₁+m₁₂，并对比了二者的行为特征。

Result: c轴压缩驱动超导转变温度T_c出现巨大且线性的增强，同时抑制了T_CDW；该面外变形的调控效率远高于面内应变，且符号相反。面外交叉耦合系数m₁₃的幅值约等于面内响应m₁₁+m₁₂，但符号相反；与尖锐的面内峰值响应不同，m₁₃在CDW转变附近呈现类似序参量（order-parameter-like）的onset行为。

Conclusion: 研究确立了c轴晶格控制在调控CsV₃Sb₅中交织电子态中起主导作用，并为在层状量子材料（layered quantum materials）中解析应变耦合的电子响应提供了一条普适路径。

Abstract: The kagome metal CsV$_{3}$Sb$_{5}$ hosts an intriguing interplay between charge-density-wave (CDW) order and superconductivity that is highly sensitive to lattice distortions. However, determining the specific roles of the in-plane ($A_{1g,1}$) and out-of-plane ($A_{1g,2}$) symmetric strain channels has been hindered by their intrinsic mixing in conventional piezo-based experiments. Here, we combine in-plane uniaxial strain with direct $c$-axis compression to independently access and disentangle these symmetry-resolved responses in CsV$_{3}$Sb$_{5}$. We reveal that $c$-axis compression drives a massive, linear enhancement of the superconducting transition temperature ($T_c$) alongside a suppression of $T_{\rm CDW}$. The tuning efficiency of this out-of-plane deformation acts with an opposite sign and far exceeds that of in-plane strain, demonstrating that $c$-axis lattice control dictates the phase competition. Furthermore, by isolating the pure elastoresistivity coefficients, we find that the out-of-plane cross-coupling coefficient ($m_{13}$) is comparable in magnitude but opposite in sign to the in-plane response ($m_{11}+m_{12}$). Unlike the sharply peaked in-plane response, $m_{13}$ exhibits a distinct, order-parameter-like onset across the CDW transition. Our results establish that out-of-plane lattice control plays a dominant role in tuning the intertwined states in CsV$_{3}$Sb$_{5}$ and provide a general pathway for resolving strain-coupled electronic responses in layered quantum materials.

### [56] [Magnetic Order in bilayer Ruddlesden-Popper Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15228)
*Yiming Wang,Guijing Duan,Zhiguang Liao,Kuan-Sen Lin,Rong Yu,Qimiao Si*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文基于近期发现的双层镍氧化物La₃Ni₂O₇高温超导现象，提出了一种理解其正常态密度波序中磁关联的新概念框架：将系统描述为有效局域磁矩（effective local moments）在RKKY与超交换（superexchange）相互作用下的组合，由此产生的磁有序波矢接近(π/2, π/2)，并清晰解释了相关的自旋动力学（spin dynamics）。结果与关于该密度波序磁关联的最新实验一致，并讨论了非常规超导电性（unconventional superconductivity）的潜在意涵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于高温超导在双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇的相图中靠近密度波序（density wave order）发展，阐明该有序态的性质对于理解超导机制至关重要。

Method: 基于大量实验证据表明该系统处于临近轨道选择型Mott相（orbital-selective Mott phase）的不良金属（bad metal）态，作者提出了一种概念上新的描述方式：将系统的磁关联视为有效局域磁矩在RKKY相互作用（Ruderman–Kittel–Kasuya–Yosida interaction）与超交换相互作用（superexchange interaction）共同作用下的结果。

Result: 该框架导出的磁有序波矢接近Q=(π/2, π/2)，同时能够清晰地解释相关的自旋动力学行为。所得结果与快速涌现的关于该双层镍酸盐密度波序磁关联的实验数据一致。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解双层镍酸盐密度波序中的磁关联提供了新的理论视角，并讨论了该框架对非常规超导电性（包括该体系及相关多轨道系统）的潜在意涵。

Abstract: The recent discovery of high-temperature superconductivity in the bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ has led to extensive interest in the correlation physics of its normal state. Given that the superconducitivity develops near a density wave order in the phase diagram, it is important to elucidate the nature of this order. Based on the accumulated experimental evidence for a bad metal state in proximity to an orbital-selective Mott phase, here we describe magnetic correlations of the system in a conceptually new way -- in terms of effective local moments experiencing a combination of RKKY and superexchange interactions. This gives rise to a magnetic order with a wavevector that is close to $\mathbf{Q}=(π/2,π/2)$ and, at the same time, yields a clear understanding of the associated spin dynamics. Our results are consistent with the rapidly emerging experiments about the magnetic correlations in the density wave order of the bilayer nickelate. Implications for unconventional superconductivity in this and related multiorbital systems are discussed.

### [57] [High-Q superconducting microwave resonators using MBE titanium nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15230)

Method: 采用分子束外延（MBE）技术在c面蓝宝石上生长TiN薄膜；利用X射线衍射表征结晶质量；采用3 μm/6 μm/3 μm 间隙/中心带/间隙线构型的四分之一波长共面波导谐振器（quarter-wavelength CPW resonator），在吊挂几何结构（hanger geometry）中进行微波测量。

Result: (111)取向的TiN薄膜与蓝宝石之间形成陡峭且结晶良好的界面，X射线摇摆曲线半高宽仅为18角秒，为迄今报道的最低值。首次观察到蓝宝石衬底中存在亚表面缺陷（sub-surface defects），这些缺陷会引发外延TiN层中的结构缺陷。在5.8 GHz、10 mK条件下，TiN谐振器在单光子极限（⟨n⟩∼1）下的内品质因子超过10⁶，在⟨n⟩∼10⁶时上升至超过20×10⁶。

Conclusion: 本研究展示的高品质TiN薄膜在超导量子比特等领域具有重要应用前景，并为未来制备具有结晶势垒的外延约瑟夫森结以实现高相干性量子比特提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Using molecular beam epitaxy, we have realized thin films of titanium nitride (TiN) on c-plane sapphire that exhibit the lowest observed full-width at half maximum X-ray rocking curve width of 18 arcsec. Though the (111) oriented TiN exhibits an abrupt and crystalline interface with sapphire, for the first time we observe sub-surface defects in the sapphire substrate, which nucleate structural defects in the epitaxial TiN layer. Using quarter-wavelength coplanar waveguide (CPW) resonators in a 3 \textmu m/6 \textmu m/3 \textmu m gap/strip/gap lines in a hanger geometry, we find the internal quality factor of the TiN resonators to be $>10^{6}$ in the single-photon $\langle n \rangle \sim 1$ limit at 5.8 GHz and 10 mK, rising to $>20 \times 10^{6}$ at $\langle n \rangle \sim 10^{6}$. The results are of high interest for applications of superconducting TiN in several areas, and provide a path towards epitaxial Josephson junctions with crystalline barriers in the future for high coherence qubits.

### [58] [Altermagnetic spin textures coupled to superconductors: Domain wall spin-triplet superconductivity and supercurrent-induced torques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15249)
*Yasir Dar,Mathias S. Scheurer,Constantin Schrade*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文研究了空间变化的交变磁体（altermagnet）与常规 s 波超导体耦合时库珀对（Cooper pairs）的形式，发现超导电性主要出现在交变磁畴（altermagnetic domains）之间的区域，并揭示了畴壁（domain wall）诱导的类塞曼场（Zeeman field）和自旋轨道场（spin-orbit field）产生自旋三重态热点（triplet hotspots）、节点与全能隙超导区域的转变以及超电流驱动的四极矩力矩（quadrupolar torque）等效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺少对交变磁体杂散场（stray fields）的系统研究，且交变磁纹理（altermagnetic textures）对巡游电子（itinerant electrons）的非平凡影响新近才被揭示，因此需要探讨空间变化的交变磁体与 s 波超导体耦合中库珀对的具体形式。

Method: 以平面径向畴壁（planar radial domain wall）为具体模型，分析交变磁有序参量（altermagnetic order parameter）的空间变化对自旋单态配对（spin-singlet pairing）的破坏作用，以及由此导致的超导电性在交变磁畴间的局域分布。

Result: 超导电性主要出现在交变磁畴之间的区域；畴壁处产生的类塞曼场和自旋轨道场形成了空间分离的自旋三重态热点，并引发了节点超导区域与全能隙超导区域之间的转变；超电流能通过准粒子（quasiparticle）中介产生一个继承交变磁有序对称性的四极矩力矩。

Conclusion: 考虑交变磁有序参量的空间非均匀性对于理解超导近邻效应（superconducting proximity effect）至关重要，交变磁纹理与超导体的混合系统为局域调控库珀对以及检测交变磁有序提供了独特的机会。

Abstract: Motivated by the absence of sizable stray fields and the recently discovered highly non-trivial impact of altermagnetic textures on itinerant electrons, we here study the form of Cooper pairs in spatially varying altermagnets coupled to conventional $s$-wave superconductors. As a consequence of the detrimental impact of altermagnetism on spin-singlet pairing and the local symmetry reduction caused by textures in the magnetic order parameter, we show that superconductivity predominantly impacts the regions between altermagnetic domains. Focusing on a planar radial domain wall for concreteness, we show that emergent Zeeman and spin-orbit fields create spatially separated triplet hotspots and transitions between nodal and fully gapped superconducting regions, whose structure is set by both the domain wall and the altermagnetic order parameter. We also identify a reciprocal effect, where a supercurrent generates a quasiparticle-mediated quadrupolar torque that inherits the symmetry of the altermagnetic order. Our results show that accounting for spatial inhomogeneities in the altermagnetic order parameter is essential for an understanding of the superconducting proximity effect and suggest that hybrid systems of altermagnetic textures and superconductors offer unique opportunities for local engineering of Cooper pairs and for detecting altermagnetic order.

Method: 采用量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）数值计算方法，对囚禁在简谐势阱中、具有吸引相互作用的双组分费米子体系进行模拟。

Abstract: We provide quantum Monte Carlo calculations of a two-component Fermi system interacting with an attractive interaction confined in harmonic traps. We investigate the role of the interaction's scattering length and effective range and show its important role in modifying shell effects in the structure of these systems. We show that in the strongly interacting regime, where the scattering length is large, the dominant role to shell effects is due to the effective range. These conclusions are very relevant for nuclear physics, in particular for neutron-rich systems, and open the way to perform new atomic experiments that can help to explain the disappearance of shell-effects in nuclei.

### [60] [Twisted Yangians of types BI, CI, DI and Drinfeld type current relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14692)
*Vidas Regelskis*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文针对BI、CI、DI型分裂对称对，引入了一种由扭曲反射方程（twisted reflection equation）控制的转置表示（transposed presentation），在R矩阵框架内推导了特殊扭曲Yangian（special twisted Yangian）$SY^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$和拓展扭曲Yangian（extended twisted Yangian）$X^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$的Drinfeld型电流表示（Drinfeld-type current presentation），证明了其与R矩阵表示的同构，并得到了张量积分解、Poincaré-Birkhoff-Witt基以及余理想余积（coideal coproduct）的若干结构性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲Yangian（twisted Yangians）是一类与分裂对称对（split symmetric pairs）相关的量子代数，其R矩阵表示与Drinfeld表示之间的同构关系此前仅由Lu, Wang和Zhang提出猜想，尚未被严格证明。本文旨在通过引入新的转置表示结构，建立这两种表示之间的显式同构，并揭示相关代数的代数结构性质。

Method: 作者首先引入了一种新的转置表示（transposed presentation），该表示受扭曲反射方程（twisted reflection equation）控制，并与生成矩阵的高斯分解（Gaussian decomposition）自然相互作用。随后，在R矩阵表示（$R$-matrix presentation）框架内，推导了特殊扭曲Yangian和拓展扭曲Yangian的Drinfeld型电流表示，其中Serre关系以闭合电流形式给出。通过提取系数，恢复出Lu提出的Drinfeld表示。

Result: 建立了R矩阵表示与Drinfeld表示之间的同构，证实了Lu, Wang和Zhang的猜想。获得了$X^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$的张量积分解，将其分解为Drinfeld表示下的扭曲Yangian与一个由可数个中心变量生成的多项式环的直积。还在Drinfeld生成元（Drinfeld generators）下构造了Poincaré-Birkhoff-Witt基，并描述了低阶Drinfeld模（low Drinfeld modes）上的余理想余积结构。

Conclusion: 本文为BI、CI、DI型分裂对称对的扭曲Yangian提供了完整的R矩阵与Drinfeld表示之间的等价性证明，并揭示了其丰富的代数结构，包括张量积分解、PBW基和余理想余积，为后续研究这类量子代数的表示论及其在数学物理中的应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study twisted Yangians associated with the split symmetric pairs of types BI, CI and DI. We introduce a new presentation of these algebras, which we call the transposed presentation, governed by a twisted reflection equation that interacts naturally with the Gaussian decomposition of the generating matrix. Working entirely within the $R$-matrix presentation, we derive Drinfeld-type current presentations of the special twisted Yangian $SY^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$ and of the extended twisted Yangian $X^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$, in which the Serre relations are stated in a closed current form. Extracting coefficients recovers the Drinfeld presentation due to Lu. As a consequence, we establish the isomorphism between the $R$-matrix and Drinfeld presentations of these twisted Yangians conjectured by Lu, Wang and Zhang. As a byproduct, we obtain a tensor product decomposition of $X^{\mathrm{tw}}(\mathfrak{g}_N)$ into the twisted Yangian in the Drinfeld presentation and a polynomial ring in countably many central variables. We also obtain Poincaré-Birkhoff-Witt bases in the Drinfeld generators and describe the coideal coproduct on the low Drinfeld modes.

</details>

### [61] [Misalignment production of isotropized vector dark matter?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14267)
*Chong-Bin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出通过暴涨期间的多矢量凝聚体（multi-vector condensate）的错位机制（misalignment mechanism）经由动力学耦合产生暗物质，并采用各向同性化背景矢量场以缓解各向异性约束，但发现非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）与等曲率涨落（isocurvature fluctuations）施加的约束互不相容，无论涨落处于弱混合（weak-mixing）还是强混合（strong-mixing）区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前暗物质产生机制中，矢量场模型常面临各向异性的严格约束；本文旨在引入各向同性化的多矢量凝聚体，通过暴涨时期的动力学耦合实现暗物质的错位产生，同时探讨该方案下非高斯性与等曲率涨落约束的相容性。

Method: 采用多矢量凝聚体在暴涨期间通过动力学耦合（kinetic coupling）实现错位机制（misalignment mechanism）产生暗物质；通过施加各向同性化背景矢量场（isotropized background vector fields）来规避各向异性约束；分别在弱混合（weak-mixing）与强混合（strong-mixing）两种涨落区域检验模型的一致性。

Result: 无论涨落处于弱混合还是强混合区域，非高斯性与等曲率涨落对模型施加的约束均不兼容，表明该暗物质产生方案在现有约束下无法同时满足两类观测要求。

Conclusion: 通过多矢量凝聚体错位机制产生暗物质的方法，尽管通过各向同性化背景缓解了各向异性问题，但最终无法调和非高斯性与等曲率涨落约束之间的矛盾，因此该模型在理论上存在根本性困难。

Abstract: We present dark matter production by the misalignment mechanism of a multi-vector condensate through kinetic coupling during inflation. We impose isotropized background vector fields to release the model from the stringent constraint of anisotropy. However, it turns out that the constraints imposed by non-Gaussianity and isocurvature fluctuations are incompatible with each other, regardless of whether the fluctuations are in the weak-mixing or strong-mixing regime.

</details>


### [62] [Pushing the Primordial Frontier: Cosmological Collider Signatures at Strong Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14529)
*Javier Huenupi,Claudio Muñoz,Gonzalo A. Palma,Spyros Sypsas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套非微扰（nonperturbative）处理多场暴胀（multifield inflation）中原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）的解析框架，通过对曲率-等曲率混合强度 λ 进行全阶重求和，得到了树图级双谱（tree-level bispectra）的精确积分表示，并揭示了强混合区域中功率谱和双谱的显著增强及其非微扰标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多场暴胀中曲率扰动（curvature perturbation）与等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbation）的混合效应是产生原初非高斯性的重要机制，但传统微扰传输理论（transfer perturbation theory）在强混合区域（strong-mixing regime）失效，亟需一种不依赖于 λ 小量展开的非微扰处理方法。

Method: 利用曲率扰动 ζ 和等曲率扰动 σ 耦合系统的精确线性解，构造戴森式传播子（dressed propagators），并针对三种相互作用项 $\dotζ^2σ$、$\dotζ\,σ^2$ 和 $σ^3$ 推导出树图级双谱的精确积分表示。该方法对曲率-等曲率传输效应进行了对 λ 的全阶重求和（resummation to all orders），且适用于任意熵质量（entropy mass）μ 取值。

Result: 得到了双谱贡献在压缩极限（squeezed limit）下的闭式表达式（closed-form expressions），在弱混合（weak-mixing）极限下恢复了著名的宇宙学对撞机（cosmological-collider）和准单场（quasi-single-field）结果。在强混合区域，功率谱和双谱均出现显著增强，导出约化非高斯振幅（reduced non-Gaussian amplitude）的独特非微扰标度律。

Conclusion: 该工作为超越弱耦合近似的多场暴胀建立了新的解析窗口，为研究强混合暴胀动力学中的宇宙学对撞机信号、原初黑洞产生（primordial-black-hole production）和圈图修正（loop corrections）提供了一个系统性的框架。

Abstract: We develop an analytic treatment of primordial non-Gaussianity in multifield inflation that is nonperturbative in the constant curvature--isocurvature mixing strength $λ$. Using exact linear solutions for the coupled curvature perturbation $ζ$ and isocurvature perturbation $σ$, we construct dressed propagators and derive exact integral representations for the tree-level bispectra generated by the interactions $\dotζ^2σ$, $\dotζ\,σ^2$, and $σ^3$. This formalism resums curvature--isocurvature transfer to all orders in $λ$ and applies for arbitrary values of the entropy mass $μ$. We obtain closed-form expressions for the leading squeezed limit of the bispectrum contributions and recover the well-known cosmological-collider and quasi-single-field results in the weak-mixing limit. In the strong-mixing regime, where conventional transfer perturbation theory breaks down, we find that both the power spectrum and the bispectrum can be dramatically enhanced, giving rise to distinctive nonperturbative scaling laws for the reduced non-Gaussian amplitude. Together, these results open a new analytic window onto multifield inflation beyond the weak-coupling approximation and establish a framework for studying cosmological-collider signals, primordial-black-hole production, and loop corrections in strongly mixed inflationary dynamics.

</details>


### [63] [Probing Graviton Mass with MeerKAT PTA and SKA--PTA Forecasts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14790)
*Zhi-Chao Zhao,Sai Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用MeerKAT脉冲星计时阵列（MPTA）4.5年数据对引力子质量（graviton mass）给出约束，并对未来平方公里阵列PTA（SKA-PTA）的探测能力进行预测，结果与广义相对论（general relativity）一致，且未来灵敏度有望提升一个数量级以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验引力子质量是否为有限值，是对广义相对论（general relativity）在纳赫兹（nanohertz）频段下基本引力理论的直接检验，而脉冲星计时阵列（Pulsar Timing Array, PTA）为这一检验提供了独特手段。

Method: 对有质量引力子（massive graviton）的修正色散关系（modified dispersion relation）及对应的张量关联函数（tensor correlation function）进行建模，在三种噪声配置（DATA、ER、ALT）下对角度-关联测量（angular-correlation measurements）执行贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）。

Result: 90%置信水平的引力子质量上限分别为：$m_g < 2.10 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$（DATA）、$m_g < 2.58 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$（ER）、$m_g < 2.25 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$（ALT）。单极（monopolar）和偶极（dipolar）贡献的引入未显著改变这些界限，确认约束主要由四极张量关联（quadrupolar tensor correlation）驱动。所有结果与广义相对论一致。对SKA-PTA的预测表明，10年观测基线可达到$m_g \sim 10^{-24}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$，50年基线可达到$m_g \sim 10^{-25}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$。

Conclusion: 当前及未来的脉冲星计时阵列在纳赫兹频段具有检验引力基本理论的强大潜力，未来SKA-PTA的灵敏度将比当前极限提升一个数量级以上。

Abstract: We present constraints on the graviton mass using the 4.5-year data release from the MeerKAT Pulsar Timing Array (MPTA) and provide forecasts for the upcoming Square Kilometre Array PTA (SKA--PTA). By modeling the modified dispersion relation and the corresponding tensor correlation function for massive gravitons, we perform Bayesian inference on the angular-correlation measurements under three noise configurations (DATA, ER, ALT). Our 90\% credible upper limits on the graviton mass are $m_g < 2.10 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$ (DATA), $m_g < 2.58 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$ (ER), and $m_g < 2.25 \times 10^{-23}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$ (ALT). Including monopolar and dipolar contributions does not significantly alter these bounds, confirming that the constraints are driven by the quadrupolar tensor correlation. All results remain fully consistent with general relativity. For SKA--PTA, we forecast sensitivities down to $m_g \sim 10^{-24}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$ with a 10-year observing baseline and $m_g \sim 10^{-25}\,\mathrm{eV}/c^{2}$ with a 50-year observing baseline, representing order-of-magnitude improvements over current limits. This work demonstrates the power of current and future PTA observations to test fundamental aspects of gravity in the nanohertz band.

### [64] [Cosmic string gravitational wave backgrounds at LISA: II. Reconstruction of conventional signals over astrophysical foregrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15219)
*Androniki Dimitriou,Daniel G. Figueroa,Peera Simakachorn,Isak Stomberg,Bryan Zaldivar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本论文利用模拟推断工具GWBackFinder，在LISA所有主要已知天体物理前景噪声（SOBHB、WD、ExWD、EMRI、MBHB）存在的情况下，研究宇宙弦（cosmic-string）信号的参数重建能力。结果表明，实现弦张力（string tension）Gμ误差≲10%所需的最低Gμ值约为10⁻¹¹，远高于不考虑前景噪声或仅考虑部分前景噪声时的估计值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对LISA探测宇宙弦信号的估计未充分考虑全部已知天体物理前景噪声（foregrounds），导致对弦张力（string tension）Gμ重建精度的评估过于乐观。本文旨在更真实地量化LISA在完整前景噪声背景下对宇宙弦信号的探测能力。

Method: 使用基于模拟的推断（Simulation-based Inference）软件包GWBackFinder，对LISA噪声、五种天体物理前景以及宇宙弦信号进行联合推断（joint inference），并在不同注入的弦张力Gμ值范围内开展系统性分析。

Result: 实现弦张力Gμ重建误差≤10%所需的最低Gμ值约为10⁻¹¹，该值比无前景噪声下的先前估计高约10⁵倍，比仅考虑SOBHB和WD前景噪声时的估计高约10²倍。

Conclusion: 完整的天体物理前景噪声对LISA重建宇宙弦信号的能力有显著削弱作用，弦张力Gμ需达到约10⁻¹¹以上才能实现可靠重建。本研究是系列工作的第二篇，旨在量化LISA对代表性宇宙弦模型的测量能力。

Abstract: We study the reconstruction of conventional cosmic-string signals with LISA in the presence of all major known astrophysical foregrounds expected in the LISA band. These include stellar-origin black-hole binaries (SOBHBs), galactic (WDs) and extragalactic (ExWDs) white dwarfs, extreme-mass-ratio-inspirals (EMRIs), and massive black-hole binaries (MBHBs). Using the Simulation-based Inference package GWBackFinder, we perform a joint inference on the LISA noise, foregrounds, and signal, across a range of injected string tensions $Gμ$. We find that reconstructing tensions with an error $\lesssim 10\%$ requires values as large as $Gμ\gtrsim 10^{-11}$, i.e. a factor $\sim10^5$ larger than previous estimates with no foregrounds, and $\sim 10^2$ larger compared to estimates accounting only for SOBHB and WD foregrounds. This work is the second in a series initiated in Ref. arXiv:2508.05395, which aims to quantify LISA's ability to measure representative cosmic-string models.

### [65] [Renormalisation of Inhomogeneous Random Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12459)
*Luca Avena,Diego Garlaschelli,Rajat Subhra Hazra,Frank den Hollander*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究非齐次随机图（inhomogeneous random graphs）在重整化变换（renormalisation transformation）下的迭代极限行为，证明该过程收敛到一个两参数随机图族（two-parameter family of random graphs），该族作为普适类（universality class）中的吸引子（attractor）存在，并依据权重分布尾部特征分为轻尾（light-tailed）与重尾（heavy-tailed）两种标度极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非齐次随机图在迭代重整化变换下的极限行为，揭示其普适类结构。

Method: 将顶点赋予独立同分布（i.i.d.）随机权重，边连接概率为权重的二元函数，自环概率为权重的一元函数。采用贪心算法（greedy algorithm）将顶点聚为等大小组，定义聚合边与聚合自环，迭代该重整化变换直至收敛。

Result: 在轻尾区，标度极限为齐次 Erdős–Rényi 随机图；在重尾区，标度极限为具有稳定无限均值随机权重和指数断连函数（exponential disconnection function）的非齐次随机图。不同区需采用不同标度。

Conclusion: 迭代重整化非齐次随机图的极限行为由连接函数与随机权重分布的选取共同决定，分属轻尾与重尾两种普适类。

Abstract: We consider inhomogeneous random graphs in which vertices are assigned i.i.d.\ random weights, pairs of distinct vertices are connected by an edge independently with a probability that is a bi-variate function of the weights of the vertices, and single vertices are connected to themselves by a self-loop independently with a probability that is a uni-variate function of the weight of the vertex. We apply a renormalisation transformation in which vertices are aggregated into groups of equal size according to a greedy algorithm, namely, distinct groups of aggregated vertices are connected by an aggregated edge if and only if there is at least one edge connecting two constituent vertices across the groups, while a group of aggregated vertices is connected to itself by an aggregated self-loop if and only if there is at least one self-loop at an internal vertex or one edge connecting a pair of distinct internal vertices. We analyse what happens when the renormalisation transformation is iterated. In particular, we show that, starting from appropriately scaled connection functions, the iterated renormalised graphs converge to a two-parameter family of random graphs, acting as an attractor in a universality class. We consider a light-tailed regime, for which the scaling limit is a homogeneous Erdős--Rényi random graph, and a heavy-tailed regime, for which the scaling limit is an inhomogeneous random graph with stable infinite-mean random weights and an exponential disconnection function. Different scalings are needed for the two regimes. Which of the two regimes prevails depends on the choice of the connection functions and the choice of the law of the random weights.

</details>


### [66] [Absence of blow-up in the 3D Navier-Stokes equations with transport noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15140)
*Antonio Agresti*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明，在适当选择的输运噪声（transport noise）驱动下，三维纳维-斯托克斯方程（Navier-Stokes equations）以高概率存在全局时间光滑解，且该正则化效应对亚临界函数空间（subcritical function spaces）中大球内的初始数据一致成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立具有大初始数据的三维纳维-斯托克斯方程（3D Navier-Stokes equations, NSEs）的全局时间光滑性（global-in-time smoothness）是一个长期未解决的公开问题。

Method: 在三维NSEs中引入适当地选择的输运噪声（transport noise），这是一种具有物理动机的随机扰动（stochastic perturbation）。

Result: 加入该输运噪声后，三维NSEs以高概率（high probability）存在全局时间光滑解（global-in-time smooth solutions）。该正则化效应（regularizing effect）对亚临界函数空间（subcritical function spaces）中任意大球内的初始数据一致成立（uniformly）。

Conclusion: 适当地选择的输运噪声能够正则化三维NSEs，使其在概率意义下克服大初始数据带来的全局光滑性困难。

Abstract: Establishing the global-in-time smoothness of solutions to the 3D Navier-Stokes equations (NSEs) with large initial data remains a long-standing open problem. In this paper, we prove that the 3D NSEs driven by a suitably chosen transport noise -- a physically motivated stochastic perturbation -- admit global-in-time smooth solutions with high probability. This regularizing effect holds uniformly for initial data in arbitrarily large balls of subcritical function spaces with positive smoothness.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Non-conservative multi-body interactions are typically associated with instabilities and activity in driven, field-mediated systems. Here we show that they can also promote stable static structures. Combining experiments and simulations in a minimal, acoustically levitated three-particle system, we tune the relative strength of conservative and non-conservative contributions to the force field. The conservative component favors a symmetric equilibrium configuration, whereas the non-conservative 3-body contribution selects a flattened isosceles triangle. Our results identify non-conservative multi-body forces as a mechanism for static structure selection in driven-dissipative matter in the absence of an effective-energy landscape.

### [68] [Memory-Driven Self-Propulsion and Flocking of Chemically Active Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14451)
*Samuel Kovach,Trevor GrandPre*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）反应调控活性相分离（active phase separation）理论，发现延迟反应反馈（delayed reaction feedback）会使液滴变形、自发极化并产生自推进运动，在多液滴系统中记忆效应导致极性集群和行波迷宫，揭示了反应记忆作为活性相分离的控制参数，连接了凝聚体重塑、自发运动和集体组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）持续受到生化反应的改造，这类反应常表现出非马尔可夫的、依赖于历史过程的动力学（history-dependent dynamics），现有理论尚缺乏对这类反应如何影响相分离行为的系统理解。

Method: 发展了一个包含非马尔可夫反应的活性相分离理论框架，通过引入延迟反应反馈（delayed reaction feedback）机制，理论分析记忆时间与反应周转时间（reaction turnover time）可比拟时凝聚体的动力学不稳定性及后续行为。

Result: 延迟反应反馈使静止液滴失稳并自发产生极性自推进态（polar, self-propelled state）；在多液滴系统中，持续的记忆尾迹（persistent memory wakes）介导液滴间的对齐，形成极性集群（polar flocks），在高浓度下进一步产生行波迷宫（traveling labyrinths）。

Conclusion: 反应记忆（reaction memory）是活性相分离的一种控制参数（control parameter），它统一了凝聚体重塑、自发运动和集体组织，并为细胞内的集群行为（flocking-like behavior）提供了一种可能的理论路径。

Abstract: Biomolecular condensates are continually remodeled by biochemical reactions that can exhibit non-Markovian, history-dependent dynamics. We develop a theory of active phase separation with non-Markovian reactions and show that delayed reaction feedback destabilizes stationary droplets: when the memory time becomes comparable to the reaction turnover time, condensates deform and spontaneously acquire a polar, self-propelled state. In multidroplet systems, persistent memory wakes mediate alignment, producing polar flocks and, at higher concentrations, traveling labyrinths. These results establish reaction memory as a control parameter of active phase separation, linking condensate remodeling, autonomous motility, and collective organization, and suggest a possible route to flocking-like behavior within cells.

### [69] [Numerical and experimental framework for bending elasticity of highly flexible slender structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14594)
*Shunsuke Nomura,Satsuki Shibuya,Isamu Hashiguchi,Ryuichi Tarumi,Tomohiko G. Sano*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种混合物质点法（hybrid-MPM）计算框架，用于模拟细长结构（如弹性管和卷尺弹簧）的三点弯曲实验。该框架将拉格朗日有限元（Lagrangian finite element）与欧拉有限差分（Eulerian finite difference）框架相结合，能够有效处理弯曲过程中截面变形与长度方向弯曲的耦合问题，以及复杂的接触力学。数值模拟结果与桌面实验及经典理论吻合良好，验证了该框架在包含复杂接触的大变形结构预测中的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长结构（slender structures）的变形依赖于其截面的细长度（slenderness），弹性和几何特性内在耦合。当管材和管道受弯时，截面变形显著（即 Brazier 失稳）。尽管三点弯曲实验是标准测试，但数值模拟因需要实现复杂接触力学（contact mechanics）而尚不充分。

Method: 采用混合物质点法（hybrid material point method, hybrid-MPM）构建计算框架，整合了拉格朗日有限元（Lagrangian finite element）与欧拉有限差分（Eulerian finite difference）两种框架。以弹性管（elastic tubes）和卷尺弹簧（tape springs）作为典型算例，模拟其截面与长度方向弯曲耦合的特征弯曲变形。

Result: 数值模拟的预测结果与桌面实验（desktop experiments）及经典理论（classical theory）一致，吻合程度良好。

Conclusion: hybrid-MPM 框架为预测涉及复杂接触的大变形结构（例如软体机器人（soft robots）和可展开结构（deployable structures））提供了鲁棒的计算工具。

Abstract: Slender structures are highly flexible, spanning several orders of magnitude in length scale. Their deformation depends on the slenderness of their cross sections, highlighting that the elasticity and geometry of structures are intrinsically coupled. The deformation of the cross-section becomes significant, particularly when tubes and pipes are subjected to bending, known as the Brazier instability. Although the bending performance of slender structures is quantified experimentally using a canonical three-point bending test, their numerical counterparts remain under-explored because complex contact mechanics must be implemented in simulations. In this study, we develop a computational framework to simulate experimental three-point bending tests using a hybrid material point method (hybrid-MPM) approach, which integrates Lagrangian finite element and Eulerian finite difference frameworks. We adapt our framework to elastic tubes and tape springs as canonical examples that exhibit characteristic bending deformation in which the cross-sectional and lengthwise bending are coupled. The predictions of numerical simulations are validated against desktop experiments and classical theory. The excellent agreement between the simulation and the experiments implies that the hybrid-MPM framework provides a robust computational framework for predicting the large deformation of structures involving complex contact, such as soft robots and deployable structures.

</details>


### [70] [Amoeboid swimming of active vesicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14714)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现囊泡根据活性强度与频率表现出多种动力学区域：同步振荡（synchronized oscillations）、准周期形变（quasiperiodic shape changes）、非推进态与推进态之间的转变（transitions between non-propelling and propelling states），以及间歇运动（intermittent motion）。

Abstract: We investigate the shape dynamics and migration of weakly deflated active vesicles driven by processes acting either directly in the membrane or transmitted by the cytoskeleton. For a force-free vesicle, local membrane incompressibility suppresses rigid-body translation, so that migration arises from time-dependent shape deformations. Assuming small excess area enables a systematic analysis of the coupled deformation and migration dynamics in free space, i.e. in the absence of substrate adhesion or confinement. Depending on the strength and frequency of the activity, the vesicle exhibits several dynamical regimes, including synchronized oscillations, quasiperiodic shape changes, transitions between non-propelling and propelling states, and intermittent motion.
