### [71] [Density-driven reentrant polymer transitions via saturable bridging crowders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14838)
*Monmee Phukan,Hitesh Garg,Satyavani Vemparala*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粗粒化分子动力学模拟证明，仅凭单一物种的吸引性拥挤剂（attractive crowder）的体积分数 $φ_c$ 就能驱动聚合物发生完整的再入式线圈-小球-线圈转变（reentrant coil-globule-coil transition），并揭示可饱和几何桥接（saturable geometric bridging）是连接中性聚合物和带电聚合物再入现象的最小机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 再入式线圈-小球-线圈转变已在多种软物质系统中被观察到，但驱动该转变的最小要素（minimal ingredients）尚不明确。本文旨在确定仅靠单一参数的改变是否足以引发该转变。

Method: 采用粗粒化分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究与单一物种的吸引性拥挤剂相互作用的聚合物。同时引入纯排斥性拥挤剂作为对照，并对带电聚合物与显式抗衡离子（explicit counterions）的系统进行模拟。

Result: 在低 $φ_c$ 下，拥挤剂桥接远距离单体，驱动协同塌缩（cooperative collapse）；在高 $φ_c$ 下，单体结合位点饱和，桥接连通性被抑制，导致再入式膨胀（reentrant expansion）。纯排斥性拥挤剂仅产生单调压缩，维持自回避行走（self-avoiding walk, SAW）链统计；而桥接效应破坏了SAW的普适性（universality），使得构象分布在 $φ_c$ 变化时完整追踪线圈-小球-线圈轨迹。对于带电聚合物，静电作用放大而非抑制再入现象。

Conclusion: 可饱和几何桥接是驱动拥挤环境中中性与带电聚合物再入现象的最小机制。

Abstract: Reentrant coil-globule-coil transitions, in which a polymer collapses and then reexpands as a single parameter is varied, have been observed across diverse soft matter systems, yet the minimal ingredients required to produce them remain unclear. Using molecular dynamics simulations of coarse-grained polymers interacting with a single species of attractive crowder, we show that crowder volume fraction $φ_c$ alone is sufficient to drive a complete reentrant transition. At low $φ_c$, crowders bridge distant monomers and drive cooperative collapse; at high $φ_c$, saturation of monomer binding sites suppresses bridging connectivity and produces reentrant expansion. This density-driven transition is absent with purely repulsive crowders, which produce only monotonic compaction while preserving self-avoiding walk (SAW) chain statistics. In contrast, bridging breaks SAW universality: the rescaled size distributions no longer collapse onto a universal curve, and the conformational distributions trace the full coil-globule-coil trajectory as $φ_c$ is varied. For charged polymers with explicit counterions, electrostatics amplifies rather than suppresses reentrance: bridging crowders displace counterions from the chain, and upon saturation the unscreened backbone charges drive expansion well beyond the original chain size. Saturable geometric bridging thus emerges as a minimal mechanism linking reentrant phenomena across neutral and charged polymers in crowded environments.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用综述（review）方式，首先介绍Persson接触理论的发展背景，随后深入讨论纯法向弹性接触中的理论框架，特别是利用偏微分方程（partial differential equations）求解接触压力概率密度与界面间隙的方法，并考察这些基础结果在摩擦学其他领域复杂界面性质研究中的应用。

Result: 系统梳理了Persson理论在纯法向弹性接触中的核心求解框架，并展示了其基础结果（如接触压力概率密度与界面间隙）在更复杂界面问题中的延伸应用。

Conclusion: 本文提出了若干关于Persson理论未来研究的建议，期望有助于研究者快速掌握该理论的最新进展，并促进其在摩擦学与固体力学领域的进一步发展与应用。

Abstract: The stochastic process model of rough surface contact, widely known as Persson's theory of contact, serves as a representative multi-scale model that has been extensively applied across various fields of tribology. In this chapter, we briefly introduce the background of the development of Persson's theory of contact. We thoroughly discuss Persson's theory for purely normal elastic contact, with a special focus on solving the probability density of the contact pressure and the interfacial gap using partial differential equations. Subsequent applications of these fundamental results in addressing more complex interfacial properties in other fields of tribology are also examined. Finally, several recommendations regarding future studies of Persson's theory are proposed. This review article is expected to assist researchers in quickly familiarizing themselves with the current state of the art of Persson's theory and to attract more attention from tribologists and solid mechanicians, thereby contributing to the development and application of Persson's theory of contact.

</details>


### [73] [Plug Flow and Cavitation in Rough Lubricated Contacts: Molecular Dynamics of Single- vs. Two-Component Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15008)
*Shubham Agarwal,Martin H. Müser*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过非平衡分子动力学模拟，研究了粗糙可变形表面在边界润滑和混合润滑条件下的滑动摩擦，比较了水、正十二烷及不相溶双组分润滑剂在粗糙接触中的摩擦学性能，发现双组分润滑剂具有最低摩擦和材料转移，并能维持栓式流动（plug flow）至更低滑动速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缩小理想化光滑界面模拟与真实粗糙承载接触之间的差距，并探究无聚合物刷（polymer brush）情况下双组分润滑（two-fluid lubrication）能否在粗糙接触中实现类似的有益摩擦学特性。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学模拟（non-equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations），在边界润滑和混合润滑条件下对粗糙可变形表面进行润滑滑动模拟，比较水、正十二烷以及不相溶双组分润滑剂在相同几何条件下的表现。

Result: 单组分润滑剂复现了已有趋势：水比正十二烷具有更强的速度依赖性但承载能力更低。强限制（strong confinement）和大高度梯度（large height gradients）的组合可导致粗糙碰撞后的栓式流动和空化（cavitation）。对于高表面张力液体（水），空化提供了远超过空腔尺度的剪切应力突然释放机制。双组分润滑剂表现出最低摩擦和材料转移，维持栓式流动至最低滑动速度，且是唯一形成折叠唇（folding lips）并可能发展为瞬态磨损颗粒（transient wear particles）的系统。

Conclusion: 双组分润滑在粗糙接触中无需聚合物刷即可实现低摩擦和低材料转移，但伴随折叠唇和瞬态磨损颗粒的形成，表明其磨损机制与单组分体系存在本质差异。

Abstract: We present non-equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations of lubricated sliding between rough, deformable surfaces under conditions representative of boundary and mixed lubrication. One aim is to reduce the gap between highly idealized simulations of smooth interfaces and real, rough, load-bearing contacts. Another aim is to determine whether favorable tribological properties of two-fluid lubrication reported for solvated hydrophilic-hydrophobic polymer-brush interfaces can also be realized in rough contacts without brushes. To this end, we compare aqueous (water), hydrocarbon ($n$-dodecane), which has a similar equilibrium viscosity to water at ambient conditions, and immiscible two-fluid lubrication under identical geometric conditions. For the single-component lubricants, the simulations reproduce established trends: Water shows stronger speed dependence but reduced load-bearing capacity than $n$-dodecane, despite their similar ambient viscosities. Beyond this expected behavior, the simulations reveal that the combination of strong confinement and large height gradients can cause plug flow and cavitation after asperity collisions. For a high-surface-tension liquid like water, cavitation provides a mechanism for abrupt shear-stress release observable on scales much exceeding the size of the cavity. The mixed lubricant exhibits the lowest friction and material transfer, while maintaining plug flow to the lowest sliding velocity. It is also the only system in which folding lips form, occasionally developing into transient wear particles at high speeds.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）方法，同时考虑局部相分离（local phase separation）、润湿现象（wetting phenomena）以及流体动力学效应（hydrodynamic effects）。

Result: 通道空间限制使活性粒子推进速度降低但定向运动持续时间延长；粒子取向动力学（orientational dynamics）不局限于二维，与已知的“取向猝灭（orientational quenching）”现象不同；光强增大会导致局部场及粒子速度的强烈波动。

Abstract: The coupled dynamics of local fields exert a drastic influence on the light-activated self-propulsion of a Janus particle in a binary solvent under spatial confinement. In this work, we investigate this problem using numerical simulations that account for local phase separation and wetting phenomena, as well as hydrodynamic effects. We find that confining the binary solvent within a channel results in a reduction of the active particle's propulsion speed and an extension of the duration of its directed motion. Furthermore, the orientational dynamics of this self-propelled particle are not restricted to two dimensions, unlike the phenomenon known as "orientational quenching". Increasing the light intensity leads to strong fluctuations in the local fields and, consequently, in the particle's speed. In this context, the significance of key physical parameters governing the efficiency of particle motion control is elucidated.

### [75] [Fluidic hysterons and memory in flow networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15122)
*Abhineet Singh Rajput,Amir A. Pahlavan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过微流控通道中锚定的弹性纤维，利用非线性弹性-水动力反馈（elastohydrodynamic feedback）实现了一种流体磁滞子（fluidic hysteron），并展示了通过旁路通道调节双稳性以及阵列中从Preisach非相互作用到雪崩式相互作用的转变，建立了记忆涌现的纯水动力路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有磁滞子（hysteron）实验实现主要依赖固态力学系统的结构双稳性（如屈曲、突弹失稳等），缺乏通过流体动力学途径构建磁滞子及其网络的方案。

Method: 在微流控通道中锚定一根弹性纤维，利用粘性加载使纤维变形、变形改变水力阻力、流动再分配改变加载的非线性弹性-水动力反馈机制；引入平行旁路通道作为几何载荷线（geometric load line），并在纤维阵列中调节单一几何参数。

Result: 单个纤维形成由尖点突变（cusp catastrophe）组织的流体磁滞子；旁路通道可重塑甚至消除双稳性，并介导纤维间的长程水动力相互作用；阵列中单一几何参数的改变驱动从具有返回点记忆（return point memory）的非相互作用Preisach regime向具有雪崩式开关及返回点记忆破坏的相互作用regime的转变。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了被动的纯水动力途径实现磁滞子网络，其中记忆来源于流-结构反馈（flow-structure feedback）和全局水力约束，而非固态多稳性或外部控制。

Abstract: Hysterons provide a minimal description of memory in driven matter: bistable elements with distinct switching thresholds whose interactions generate hysteresis, avalanches, and return point memory or its violation. Experimental realizations have so far been dominated by solid state mechanical systems, where bistability is usually encoded structurally through buckling, snap through, or geometric incompatibility. Here we realize hysteron physics through a hydrodynamic route. A single elastic fiber anchored in a microfluidic channel becomes bistable through nonlinear elastohydrodynamic feedback: viscous loading deforms the fiber, deformation reshapes hydraulic resistance, and flow redistribution modifies the loading. This feedback produces a fluidic hysteron whose onset is organized by a cusp catastrophe in geometric control parameters. A parallel bypass channel acts as a geometric load line that reshapes, and can even eliminate, bistability while simultaneously mediating long ranged hydraulic interactions between fibers. In arrays, varying a single geometric parameter drives a transition from a non interacting Preisach regime with return point memory to an interacting regime with avalanche like switching and return point memory violation. These results establish a passive hydrodynamic route to hysteron networks, in which memory emerges from flow structure feedback and global hydraulic constraints rather than solid state multistability or external control.

### [76] [Catalytic Crosstalk: Cooperative Enzyme Dynamics in Artificial Crowded Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15234)
*Rik Chakraborty,Manisha Jhajhria,Arnab Maiti,Nividha,Priyanka,Snigdha Thakur,Krishna Kanti Dey*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验上，在人工拥挤环境中共定位过氧化氢酶和脲酶，测量二者的催化活性和动力学行为。理论上，将酶建模为二聚体活性粒子（dimeric active particles），构建一个最小模拟框架以定性再现实验观察到的协同效应。

Result: 实验结果表明，在拥挤介质中共定位时，两种酶相互增强彼此的催化活性和动力学行为，导致反应速率和迁移率净增加，呈现出一种涌现性多体效应。模拟框架定性捕捉了这种协同现象。

Conclusion: 酶间合作可以抵消拥挤带来的不利影响，为理解酶在复杂生物环境中如何维持催化效率提供了新的见解。

Abstract: In cellular environments, enzymes operate under densely crowded conditions that often hinder catalytic efficiency by limiting substrate diffusion and essential conformational dynamics. While reports suggest that crowding can often lead to inhibition of enzyme's catalytic activity, persistent efficiency of cellular biochemistry hints at underlying cooperative mechanisms among these molecules. Here, we experimentally demonstrate catalytic crosstalk between two enzymes - catalase and urease - in artificially crowded environments. Our results reveal that when co-localized in dense media, these enzymes mutually enhance each other's catalytic activity and dynamic behavior. This cooperative interaction leads to a net increase in reaction rates and mobility, suggesting an emergent many-body effect in enzyme assemblies. Modeling enzymes as dimeric active particles, we propose a minimal simulation framework that qualitatively captures the observed synergy. Our findings show that inter-enzyme cooperation can counteract the detrimental effects of crowding, offering insights into how enzymatic efficiency is sustained in complex biological milieu.

### [77] [Tunable Mpemba effect in a polymer-bead system with inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15266)
*Hosung Kwak,Yongjoo Baek,Hawoong Jeong*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个受实验启发的模型，通过系统惯性控制姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）。该模型描述了一个经历变性转变的聚合物，其力-延伸曲线存在一个减缓松弛的平台。当初始温度较高或拉伸力较弱时，珠子积累更大动能，从而更快跨越平台产生姆潘巴效应；增加珠子质量可拓宽该机制的初始温度范围；类似机制也产生逆姆潘巴效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出一个受实验启发的模型，在该模型中可以通过系统惯性来控制姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect），从而深化对这一反常松弛现象的理解。

Method: 采用一个描述聚合物变性转变（denaturation transition）的模型，其力-延伸曲线包含一个减缓松弛的平台。通过改变初始温度、拉伸力大小以及珠子质量，研究系统惯性对松弛动力学的影响。

Result: 当系统在较高温度或较弱拉伸力下初始制备时，珠子积累更大的动能，能够更快跨越平台，从而产生姆潘巴效应。增大珠子质量可拓宽该效应的初始温度范围。类似机制也产生逆姆潘巴效应（inverse Mpemba effect）。

Conclusion: 系统惯性可用于控制姆潘巴效应的产生，且通过调节初始温度、拉伸力和珠子质量可调控该效应及逆姆潘巴效应。

Abstract: We propose an experimentally motivated model in which the Mpemba effect can be controlled through the system's inertia. The model describes a polymer undergoing a denaturation transition whose force-extension curve contains a plateau that slows relaxation. When the system is initially prepared at a higher temperature or under a weaker stretching force, the bead accumulates greater kinetic energy, allowing it to cross the plateau more rapidly and thereby producing the Mpemba effect. Increasing the bead mass broadens the range of initial temperatures over which this mechanism operates. A similar mechanism also generates the inverse Mpemba effect.

</details>

### [78] [Phonons in low-dimensional confined systems: Emergent non-reciprocity in 1D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14232)
*Yuan Gao,K. A. Muttalib*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将低维体系中的位移场映射到自旋自由度的一般性方法，以描述受限振荡效应。通过一维谐振链验证，该方法在长波极限下产生有质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermions），并揭示了由于全链面外运动受限而导致声学模（acoustic modes）缺失的特征。引入短程非谐相互作用后，在略高于能隙的能量尺度上系统发生（量子）相变，进入具有自发时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB, $\hat{T}^2=+1$）的非互易态（nonreciprocal state）。该模型虽然总粒子数不守恒，但存在一个被忽视的 $U(1)$ 对称性对应守恒的“极化电荷”（polarization charge），因此可以通过测量有序相内外人造规范场（artificial gauge fields）的诱导率（inductivity）变化来探测非互易性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维固态或冷原子体系中，离子/原子自由度在约束方向上的振荡受到限制，传统的正则量子化（canonical quantization）声子描述并不理想。因此需要建立一种更一般的理论框架来刻画这类受限振荡特征。

Method: 提出一种将位移场映射到自旋自由度（spin degrees of freedom）的一般性方案，将原本不受限系统中的受限振荡特征引入进来。通过一维谐振链（1D harmonic chain）验证该方法的有效性，并在长波极限下导出有质量狄拉克费米子。随后引入短程非谐相互作用（anharmonicities），分析能量略高于能隙时的量子相变行为。

Result: 在长波极限下得到有质量狄拉克费米子，证实声学模缺失是体系面外运动受限的信号。在略高于能隙的能量尺度上，非谐相互作用驱动系统发生量子相变，进入具有自发时间反演对称性破缺（$\hat{T}^2=+1$）的非互易态。模型具有一个被忽视的 $U(1)$ 对称性，对应守恒的极化电荷。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一种描述低维体系受限振荡的新框架，并通过极化电荷的守恒性质连接了非互易性与人造规范场的诱导率测量，为实验探测该非互易有序相提供了可行的检测方案。

Abstract: An important feature of solid-state or cold atom systems in low dimensions is the restricted oscillations of ionic/atomic degrees of freedom in the confining directions, for which the conventional phonon from canonical quantization is not an ideal description. In this work we propose a general recipe to introduce this feature to otherwise unrestricted systems by mapping displacement fields to spin degrees of freedom. We demonstrate the validity of the approach with a 1D harmonic chain, and the results lead to massive Dirac fermions at long distances, showing the absence of acoustic modes as the signature of confined out-of-plane motion of the entire chain. We then introduce a short-range interaction via anharmonicities and show that for energy scale slightly above the gap, it gives rise to a (quantum) phase transition to a nonreciprocal state with spontaneous time reversal symmetry breaking (TRSB) of the type $\hat{T}^2=+1$. Despite the non-conserved total particle number, the model holds an under-appreciated $U(1)$ symmetry with conserved "polarization charge", so that the nonreciprocity can be probed by measuring the change of inductivity to artificial gauge fields in and out of the ordered phase.

Method: 采用倒装芯片工艺，通过铟凸点互连（indium bump interconnects）将SiMOS双量子点芯片与超导铝谐振器芯片键合，实现微波耦合至量子点栅极（quantum dot gate）。利用谐振器对量子点系统中的电荷跃迁（charge transitions）进行检测。

Conclusion: 倒装芯片键合（flip-chip bonding）是一种可行的SiMOS量子点器件集成方法，可同时工作在直流与微波频率，并有望用于谐振器基技术如自旋-光子耦合（spin-photon coupling）。

Abstract: Heterogeneous integration provides a promising route to combine semiconductor quantum dot devices and superconducting microwave circuits, while allowing each component to be fabricated using an optimized process flow. Here, we demonstrate a flip-chip integrated platform for dispersive readout of silicon metal-oxide semiconductor (SiMOS) quantum dot devices. A SiMOS double quantum dot chip is bonded to a superconducting aluminum resonator chip using indium bump interconnects to enable microwave coupling to the quantum dot gate. We show that the developed flip-chip process is compatible with cryogenic operation of both the SiMOS device and the superconducting resonator, and demonstrate resonator-based detection of charge transitions in the quantum dot system. The readout signal-to-noise ratio follows a dependence of $\sqrt{t}$ with the integration time, reaching SNR = 1 at an integration time of approximately 0.3 ms. These results establish flip-chip bonding as a viable integration approach for SiMOS quantum dot devices operating at both dc and microwave frequencies, with potential applications for resonator-based techniques such as spin-photon coupling.

### [80] [Curvature Converts Phonon Hall Viscosity into Phonon Angular Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14868)
*Pablo A. Morales*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出在平坦晶膜中，弯曲（curvature）可将原本不与声子霍尔黏滞（phonon Hall viscosity）耦合的弯曲模式（flexural mode）转化为霍尔活性通道，从而产生面内声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）和稳态场奇扭矩（field-odd torque），该扭矩可用现有扭矩传感器检测，并为原子级薄晶体中的声子霍尔黏滞提供新的探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平坦晶膜中，弯曲模式不与声子霍尔黏滞耦合，导致无法通过该通道探测霍尔效应。为此，论文旨在揭示静态曲率如何开启霍尔活性弯曲通道，并评估其可观测的物理效应。

Method: 通过理论分析，将静态曲率分为无迹曲率（tracefree curvature）和平均曲率（mean curvature），分别讨论它们与霍尔活性剪切（Hall-active shear）以及普通面内弹性（in-plane elasticity）的耦合机制，并计算统计各向同性浅波纹（statistically isotropic shallow ripples）下的时间平均扭矩。

Result: 曲率可产生沿表面法向的面内声子角动量，且时间平均扭矩具有由霍尔黏滞固定的符号，大小与均方曲率成正比。以$α$-RuCl$_3$的体霍尔黏滞为标度，估算得到几层厚晶膜的扭矩约为$10^{-22}\,\mathrm{N\,m}$，处于现有扭矩传感器的探测范围内。

Conclusion: 弯曲-剪切响应（flexural-to-shear response）可作为探测原子级薄晶体中声子霍尔黏滞的有效手段，为实验测量声子霍尔效应提供了可行路径。

Abstract: In a flat crystalline membrane, the low-energy spectrum is dominated by a flexural mode that does not couple to phonon Hall viscosity. We show that static curvature converts normal motion into in-plane strain and thereby opens a Hall-active flexural channel. Tracefree curvature couples directly to Hall-active shear, while mean curvature acts indirectly through the shear generated by ordinary in-plane elasticity. Together, these channels generate in-plane phonon angular momentum along the surface normal. For statistically isotropic shallow ripples, the time average has a definite sign fixed by the Hall viscosity, producing a steady field-odd torque proportional to the mean-square curvature. Using the measured bulk Hall viscosity of $α$-RuCl$_3$ to set the scale, we estimate a torque of order $10^{-22}\,\mathrm{N\,m}$ for a few-layer membrane, within reach of demonstrated torsional sensors. The same flexural-to-shear response provides a probe of phonon Hall viscosity in atomically thin crystals.

*Grigory A. Starkov*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值分析Corbino盘几何结构中的电子流，预测了偶数-奇数效应（even-odd effect）在小磁场下电阻敏感性增强的清晰信号，该信号在弹道-断层扫描渡越区最为显著，并随温度升高而消失；同时发现该效应对实验观测到的运动学粘度反常标度的贡献可能较小。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用数值分析方法对Corbino盘几何结构中的电子流进行全区间模拟，并拓展了特征线法（method of characteristics）以处理长寿命奇次谐波，从而将线性化玻尔兹曼方程（linearized Boltzmann equation）转化为一组积分方程。

Result: 预测了偶数-奇数效应的清晰信号——在小磁场B→0下电阻敏感性∂R/∂(B²)增强；该增强在弹道-断层扫描渡越区（crossover from the ballistic to the tomographic regime）最为显著，随温度进一步升高而逐渐消失。估计表明在实验温度范围内该效应较小。

Conclusion: 实验观测到的运动学粘度（kinematic viscosity）反常标度是否归因于偶数-奇数效应可能需要更谨慎的考量；此外，特征线法的扩展为处理长寿命奇次谐波提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: In two dimensions, the geometric constraints due to Pauli blocking and conservation laws lead to the even-odd effect exhibited by the electron-electron scattering lengths: electron-electron collisions are more efficient at relaxing the even angular harmonics of the distribution function than the odd ones. Inspired by a recent experiment on the magnetotransport in the Corbino disk geometry, we numerically analyze the electron flows in this geometry across all the regimes.
  We predict a clear signature of the even-odd effect - enhancement of the resistance sensitivity $\partial R/\partial(B^2)$ at small magnetic fields $B\rightarrow 0$. This enhancement is most prominent at the crossover from the ballistic to the tomographic regime, and gradually disappears when the temperature is further increased. Our estimates suggest that in the temperature range of the experiment, the effect should be small. This implies that the attribution of the anomalous scaling of the kinematic viscosity, that was observed in the experiment, to the even-odd effect might need more careful consideration.
  As a side note, we show how the method of characteristics can be extended to treat the long-lived odd harmonics, which allows one to recast the linearized Boltzmann equation as a system of integral ones.

Method: 研究先生成无序马约拉纳纳米线的配对高温与低温电导模拟数据，随后训练两种神经网络：(1) 基于Shifted Window U-Net Transformer扩散启发式架构，从热展宽的高温测量中重构低温电导；(2) 基于Video Vision Transformer的网络，直接从高温电导预测低温拓扑能见度（topological visibility）。

Abstract: Identifying Majorana zero modes in semiconductor--superconductor nanowires requires ultra-low temperature transport measurements in dilution refrigerators, making device screening slow and resource-intensive. Here, we investigate whether high-temperature conductance data can be used to infer low-temperature Majorana nanowire properties before committing devices to dilution-refrigerator characterization. We generate paired high- and low-temperature conductance simulations for disordered Majorana nanowires and train neural networks to perform two related tasks. Second, we train a Video Vision Transformer-based network to predict the low-temperature topological visibility directly from high-temperature conductance, obtaining $R^2 \approx {0.80}$. These results demonstrate that machine-learning models can recover and infer low-temperature Majorana features from experimentally easier high-temperature data, providing a practical route for rejecting poor devices early thus avoiding slow and resource-intensive dilution refrigeration for non-promising devices. This high-temperature screening approach could substantially accelerate the experimental feedback loop for Majorana nanowire device development.

### [84] [Spin Hall Effect in Collinear Ferromagnets from Spin-Group Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15112)
*Qing Zhang,Yizhuo Song,Jiahao Shentu,Jianting Dong,Jia Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过将自旋-轨道耦合视为破坏自旋群对称性的微扰，阐明了共线铁磁体中自旋霍尔效应的微观起源，识别出时间反演偶（T-even）和时间反演奇（T-odd）两种自旋霍尔机制，并通过第一性原理计算证实了显著的各向异性磁自旋霍尔效应。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）作为破坏自旋群对称性（spin-group symmetry）的微扰进行处理，分别在SOC的一阶和二阶展开下识别主导的自旋霍尔机制，并结合第一性原理计算进行验证。

Result: SOC一阶下识别出两种T-even自旋霍尔效应机制（磁化无关的常规贡献和磁化依赖的反常霍尔电荷输运通道）以及一种T-odd磁自旋霍尔效应（magnetic spin Hall effect, MSHE）；SOC二阶下发现一种新的T-odd平面自旋霍尔机制。第一性原理计算显示，当磁矩偏离主晶轴时，磁自旋霍尔效应呈现显著各向异性且量值可与T-even自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductivity, SHC）相比拟。

Abstract: Magnetic materials support both time-reversal-even (T-even) and time-reversal-odd (T-odd) spin Hall currents, yet their underlying microscopic origins remain elusive. Here, we elucidate the spin Hall effect (SHE) in collinear ferromagnets by treating spin-orbit coupling (SOC) as a perturbation that breaks spin-group symmetry, thereby revealing how magnetic order activates distinct spin Hall response. To first order in SOC, we identify two dominant T-even SHE mechanisms: a magnetization-independent conventional contribution and a magnetization-dependent channel associated with anomalous Hall charge transport. At the same order, the leading T-odd magnetic spin Hall effect (MSHE) originates from the exchange interaction between the conventional spin current and the local magnetization. At second order in SOC, we further uncover a distinct T-odd planar spin Hall mechanism. Our spin-symmetry analysis is corroborated by first-principles calculations, which reveal a pronounced anisotropic magnetic spin Hall effect whose magnitude can be comparable to the T-even spin Hall conductivity (SHC) when the magnetic moment is tilted away from the principal crystallographic axes. These findings clarify the microscopic origins of the SHC in collinear ferromagnets and pave the way for ferromagnet-based spin current sources with versatile properties in spintronic applications.

### [85] [Gyrotropy from Extrinsic Geometry in Twisted Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15189)
*Spenser Talkington,Eugene J Mele*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了扭转双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）中的回转性（gyrotropy）作为层间电子相干性（interlayer electronic coherence）的信号，揭示了由系统物理几何引发的外禀几何回转性（extrinsic geometric gyrotropy）与由电子态结构相关的内禀相干回转性之间的区别，并强调在分析扭转材料性质时必须分离这两种贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转双层材料中，层间电子相干性是一个关键物理量，但如何通过光学响应（如回转性）区分外禀几何效应与内禀电子态贡献尚不明确，需要在不同材料体系中加以澄清。

Method: 首先使用经典的一维线阵列双层模型（bilayer array of one-dimensional wires）说明外禀几何回转性；随后在扭转双层石墨烯中，利用Bistritzer-MacDonald框架计算电导率，并与实验室参考系（lab frame）中可测量的电导率进行比较；最后分析扭转双层MoTe₂在纯净模型、弱应变（weak strain）和位移场（displacement fields）下的回转性行为。

Result: 在时间反演对称（time-reversal symmetric）的双层体系中，即使没有层间耦合，外禀几何回转性仍然存在，且与电子态结构无关；扭转双层石墨烯的回转性完全源自层间相干性；Bistritzer-MacDonald框架计算的电导率与实验室框架下可测的电导率存在显著差异；在弱应变和位移场作用下，扭转双层MoTe₂中的几何回转性可主导相干回转性。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了在分析扭转材料性质时，必须将外禀物理几何（extrinsic physical geometry）的贡献与内禀电子态（intrinsic electronic states）的贡献分离开来。

Abstract: Gyrotropy in twisted bilayer graphene can be used as a signature of interlayer electronic coherence. Gyrotropy can emerge in the absence of interlayer coupling in time-reversal symmetric bilayer systems. This gyrotropy originates from the extrinsic geometry associated with the physical geometry of the system and is independent of the structure of the electronic states. We first illustrate this effect for a purely classical bilayer array of one-dimensional wires. Next we study twisted bilayer graphene and show that the gyrotropy is entirely due to interlayer coherence. In doing so we observe that conductivities calculated in the Bistritzer-MacDonald frame differ significantly from conductivities measurable in the lab frame. Finally we consider twisted bilayer MoTe2, first as a pristine model where the gyrotropy exactly vanishes, and then with weak strain and displacement fields where we show that the geometric gyrotropy can dominate the coherent gyrotropy. Our results call attention to the necessity to separate the contribution of extrinsic physical geometry from the contribution of intrinsic electronic states to the properties of twisted materials.

</details>


### [86] [Long-range and steady-state entanglement of driven-dissipative nitrogen vacancy centers using microwaves as a drive and synthetic antiferromagnet as a dissipator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15259)
*Federico Garcia-Gaitan,Branislav K. Nikolic*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文微观推导了包含两个驱动-耗散氮-空位中心（NVC）的琳德布拉德量子主方程，在单一处于热平衡的磁浴环境中，预测了长程稳态纠缠的精确条件，并指出合成反铁磁体是最优耗散环境，估计100纳米间距下稳态纠缠度（concurrence）可达约0.28。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钻石中两个远距离氮-空位中心（nitrogen-vacancy centers, NVCs）之间的长程纠缠在量子传感和量子计算中具有重要应用潜力，但将NVC的纠缠稳定到稳态面临显著挑战，通常需要将环境调至非平衡（nonequilibrium）状态。

Method: 从微观层面出发，针对两个驱动-耗散NVC体系（驱动源为微波辐射，耗散由一个保持热平衡（equilibrium）的单磁浴提供），推导出琳德布拉德量子主方程（Lindblad quantum master equation）。

Result: 该方程预测了NVC长程稳态纠缠的精确条件，指出合成反铁磁体（synthetic antiferromagnet）是耗散环境的最优选择。基于现有实验的真实参数，估算两个间距约100纳米的NVC的稳态纠缠度（concurrence）可达约0.28。

Conclusion: 通过微观推导的琳德布拉德主方程，在平衡态磁浴环境中实现了对两个远距离NVC稳态纠缠的理论预测与优化，为固态量子比特的纠缠稳定化提供了新途径。

Abstract: The search for optimal schemes and dissipative environments for mediating long-range entanglement between two distant nitrogen-vacancy centers (NVCs) in diamond is the subject of ongoing vigorous efforts due to potential applications of such microscopic solid-state qubits in quantum sensing and quantum computing. However, stabilizing entanglement of NVCs into steady-state poses a significant challenge, typically requiring tuning the environment into a {\em nonequilibrium} state. Here we microscopically derive a Lindblad quantum master equation for a system of two driven-dissipative NVCs, where the drive is microwave radiation and dissipation is provided by a single magnetic bath that is kept in {\em equilibrium}. This equation allows us to predict precise conditions for long-range and steady-state entanglement of NVCs, while it also suggests synthetic antiferromagnet as an optimal choice for a dissipative environment. By using realistic parameters from available experiments, we estimate steady-state concurrence reaching $\mathcal{C}\simeq 0.28$ for two NVCs separated by $\sim 100 \: \mathrm{nm}$.

### [87] [A Self-Dual Frame Formalism of the SO(3) Yang-Mills Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14204)
*Hanwen Liu*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究闭定向黎曼4-流形上自对偶2-形式丛的SO(3)联络，通过极分解将规范自由度消去并转化为正定对称矩阵场h，证明Yang-Mills方程等价于一个完全确定的二阶系统Φ_g(h)=0，并建立了变分公式、不可约性、椭圆正则性和线性化算子的Fredholm指标定理。特别地，当h=e^{2ω}g时，该方程退化为反自对偶性与常数量曲率条件，从而每个正Yamabe不变量的反自对偶共形类都给出一个全局解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在4维黎曼流形上，Yang-Mills理论的核心难题之一是对杨-米尔斯方程进行系统约化，消除规范冗余并建立与几何结构的直接联系。本文旨在通过极分解方法将SO(3)联络转化为一个确定的对称矩阵场，从而将Yang-Mills方程转化为一个完全可解的确定二阶系统，并探索其与反自对偶性和数量曲率的内在关系。

Method: 考虑闭定向黎曼4-流形(M,g)上的自对偶2-形式丛Λ^+上的SO(3)联络。在自对偶曲率构成定向标架的开区域上，利用逐点极分解（pointwise polar decomposition）消去规范自由度（gauge freedom），将联络替换为一个正定对称矩阵场h。通过分析h唯一确定的相容联络A(h)，将Yang-Mills方程等价地转化为确定二阶系统Φ_g(h)=0，并建立其变分公式、自动不可约性（automatic irreducibility）、椭圆正则性（elliptic regularity）以及线性化算子的Fredholm指标定理（Fredholm index theorem）。

Result: 证明了Yang-Mills方程与Φ_g(h)=0的等价性；对于形如h=e^{2ω}g的矩阵场，Φ_g(h)=0等价于反自对偶性（anti-self-duality）加上常数量曲率条件6√2；每个正Yamabe不变量（positive Yamabe invariant）的反自对偶共形类均给出全局解。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个将SO(3) Yang-Mills理论约化为正定对称矩阵场h的几何框架，揭示了Yang-Mills方程与反自对偶性和常数量曲率之间的深刻联系，并为正Yamabe不变量情形下的全局解存在性提供了新途径。

Abstract: For a closed oriented Riemannian $4$-manifold $(M,g)$, we consider $\operatorname{SO}(3)$ connections on the bundle $Λ^+$ of self-dual $2$-forms. On the open locus where the self-dual curvature is an orientation-preserving frame, pointwise polar decomposition removes the gauge freedom and replaces the connection by a field $h$ of positive definite symmetric matrices. We show that $h$ determines a unique compatible connection $A(h)$ and that the Yang--Mills equation is equivalent to the exactly determined second order system $$ Φ_g(h):=F_{A(h)}^+h^{-1}-g=0. $$ We establish a variational formulation, automatic irreducibility, elliptic regularity, and a Fredholm index theorem for the linearized operator. For matrix fields of the form $h=e^{2ω}g$, the equation $Φ_g(h)=0$ is equivalent to anti-self-duality and constant scalar curvature $6\sqrt{2}$. Consequently, every anti-self-dual conformal class of positive Yamabe invariant gives a global solution.

</details>


### [88] [Lipschitz continuity of the cut time for globally hyperbolic spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14374)
*Alec Metsch*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在全局双曲时空（globally hyperbolic spacetime）中证明了聚焦时间（focalization time）和切割时间（cut time）的局部Lipschitz连续性，并推导了零锥（null cone）附近的 Lipschitz 常数定量估计以及零方向上的延拓判据，进而得出点切割轨迹（cut locus）的 Hausdorff 余维数至少为1。这些结果将 Itoh-Tanaka 和 Li-Nirenberg 在完备黎曼流形上的经典 Lipschitz 连续性结论推广到了 Lorentz 几何（Lorentzian geometry）框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将完备黎曼流形上关于聚焦时间和切割时间的Lipschitz连续性经典结果（如 Itoh-Tanaka 和 Li-Nirenberg 的工作）推广到 Lorentz 几何场景，特别是全局双曲时空中的因果结构分析。

Method: 采用 Itoh-Tanaka 的方法，并根据 Lorentz 背景进行适当调整。通过证明未来因果锥（future causal cone）上聚焦时间在某开子集上的局部 Lipschitz 连续性，以及切割时间在类时切向量（timelike tangent vector）附近邻域内的局部 Lipschitz 连续性来推进论证。

Result: 证明了全局双曲时空中固定点的聚焦时间在未来因果锥的开子集上局部 Lipschitz 连续；切割时间在对应的类时切向量邻域内也局部 Lipschitz 连续。给出了零锥附近 Lipschitz 常数的定量估计，并提供了 Lipschitz 性质延拓至零方向（null directions）的判据。由此进一步推出点切割轨迹的 Hausdorff 余维数至少为1。

Conclusion: 本文的结果是 Itoh-Tanaka 和 Li-Nirenberg 在完备黎曼流形上的经典 Lipschitz 连续性结论在 Lorentz 几何中的自然推广，为全局双曲时空中因果结构的正则性分析提供了新的理论支撑。

Abstract: We prove that, for a fixed point in a globally hyperbolic spacetime, the focalization time is locally Lipschitz continuous on the open subset of the future causal cone where it is finite. We also show that the cut time is locally Lipschitz continuous in a neighborhood of any timelike tangent vector whose associated geodesic is defined at least up to (and including) its cut time. Furthermore, we derive quantitative estimates for the Lipschitz constant near the null cone and provide a criterion ensuring that the Lipschitz property extends to null directions. As a consequence, we show that the cut locus of a point has Hausdorff codimension at least $1$. These results extend classical Lipschitz continuity results for complete Riemannian manifolds due to Itoh-Tanaka and Li-Nirenberg. Our approach follows the method of Itoh-Tanaka, suitably adapted to the Lorentzian setting.

### [89] [SPH methods in the modelling of compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14828)
*Stephan Rosswog*

TL;DR: 该综述系统总结了基于光滑粒子流体动力学（Smoothed Particle Hydrodynamics, SPH）方法的致密天体模拟现状，涵盖牛顿与广义相对论框架下的SPH方法进展，以及白矮星-白矮星、中子星-中子星和中子星-黑洞等双星系统的并合模拟，重点关注引力波驱动的并合过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为研究人员提供SPH方法在致密天体模拟领域的全面技术概述与最新进展，帮助理解该数值方法在牛顿引力、广义相对论及动态时空背景下的适用性与局限性。

Method: 采用综述性组织架构：首先介绍SPH方法在牛顿理想气体动力学中的基本原理、无网格导数（meshless derivatives）及激波处理等最新技术；随后单独章节阐述广义相对论SPH（包括狭义相对论极限）及全数值相对论框架下物质与动态时空（dynamical spacetime）的联合演化；最后按系统类型（白矮星-白矮星、中子星-中子星、中子星-黑洞）依次讨论模拟现状。

Result: 论文识别并分类了SPH方法在三种典型致密双星系统中的模拟成果：引力波驱动的并合（gravitational-wave-driven merger）主导了当前研究重点，同时简要涵盖了高恒星密度环境中发生的动力学碰撞（dynamical collision）情形。

Conclusion: SPH方法已从牛顿理想气体动力学扩展到全广义相对论数值模拟，成为研究致密天体双星并合及其引力波信号的重要工具；白矮星-白矮星、中子星-中子星和中子星-黑洞系统在不同物理条件下的并合行为已得到系统考察，但各系统仍存在待解决的数值与物理挑战。

Abstract: We review the current status of compact object simulations that are based on the Smoothed Particle Hydrodynamics (SPH) method. The first section of this review is dedicated to SPH as a numerical method for Newtonian, ideal gas dynamics and it should be fairly self-contained. It begins with the basics of the method, but also describes recent advances including various meshless derivatives or methods for treating shocks. A separate chapter summarizes general relativistic SPH, including its special relativistic limit, and it explains in some detail the recent development of full numerical relativity in SPH where matter is evolved together with a dynamical spacetime. The remainder of the review has an astrophysical focus, here we discuss the status of the simulations of white dwarf--white dwarf, neutron star--neutron star and neutron star--black hole systems. For each type of system the emphasis is on gravitational-wave-driven mergers, but we also briefly summarize dynamical collisions that can occur in locations with large stellar densities.

### [90] [A self-consistent Higgs-portal framework for dark matter--admixed neutron stars: Collider-motivated benchmarks meet multimessenger constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14979)
*Adamu Issifu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在自洽的相对论平均场框架中，通过扩展带有有质量Z′矢量中介子的希格斯门户模型，研究了暗物质混合中子星。该框架通过全局粒子分数Fχ自洽表征暗物质含量，消除了传统单流体模型中外设暗物质费米动量的需要。研究发现增加Fχ会系统性地软化核物质状态方程、降低最大中子星质量最多约29%、增加星体致密性，并推导了声速等热力学量的精确解析表达式。微观层面，重子-暗物质相互作用以Z′矢量排斥通道为主，建立了WIMP模型与中子星多信使现象学之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单流体模型在描述暗物质混合中子星时，需要外部预设暗物质费米动量作为输入，缺乏自洽的机制将暗物质与重子物质（baryonic matter）的动力学耦合纳入统一框架。本文旨在建立一个自洽的单流体相对论平均场（relativistic mean-field）理论框架，通过引入有质量Z′矢量中介子来动态耦合重子物质与暗物质（dark matter）两个扇区。

Method: 基于扩展的希格斯门户模型（Higgs-portal model），引入一个有质量Z′矢量中介子来描述重子物质与暗物质之间的密度依赖排斥相互作用。暗物质含量通过全局粒子分数Fχ=Nχ/NB表征，局域暗物质密度自洽确定为nχ=FχnB。采用NL3ωρ、DD2和FSU2R三种状态方程（EOS）进行数值计算。

Result: 增加Fχ会系统性地软化核物质状态方程，将最大中子星质量降低最多约29%，同时增加星体致密性并改变致密物质的热力学响应。推导了声速、声速密度导数和绝热指数的精确解析表达式，为评估暗物质混合状态方程的因果性和热力学稳定性提供了严格基准。微观上，重子-暗物质相互作用以Z′矢量排斥通道为主导。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了基于对撞机动机的弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）模型与中子星多信使现象学之间的直接联系，对未来引力波（gravitational-wave）和X射线观测具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We investigate dark matter (DM)-admixed neutron stars (NSs) within a self-consistent single-fluid relativistic mean-field framework by extending the Higgs-portal model with a massive $Z^\prime$ vector mediator. The resulting density-dependent repulsive interaction dynamically couples the baryonic matter (BM) and DM sectors, allowing the DM content to be characterized by the global particle fraction, $F_χ=N_χ/N_B$, with the local DM density determined self-consistently as $n_χ=F_χn_B$, thereby eliminating the need for the externally prescribed DM Fermi momentum adopted in previous single-fluid models. Using the NL3$ωρ$, DD2, and FSU2R EOSs, we show that increasing $F_χ$ systematically softens the nuclear equation of state (EOS), reduces the maximum NS mass by up to $\sim29\%$, increases stellar compactness, and modifies the thermodynamic response of dense matter. We further derive exact analytical expressions for the adiabatic speed of sound, its density derivative, and the adiabatic index, providing a rigorous benchmark for assessing the causality and thermodynamic stability of DM-admixed EOSs. At the microscopic level, the BM--DM interaction is shown to be dominated by the repulsive $Z^\prime$ vector channel. Our framework establishes a direct connection between collider-motivated WIMP models and the multimessenger phenomenology of NSs, with potential implications for future gravitational-wave and X-ray observations.

### [91] [Swift gives a new BAT-GLIMPSE: Gamma-ray Localization using Imaging and Mosaic techniques for Pointing and Slew Epochs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15130)
*S. Ronchini,T. Parsotan,J. DeLaunay,J. A. Kennea*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文介绍BAT-GLIMPSE，一个用于Swift-BAT数据的全自主、开源、低延迟伽马射线瞬变源定位管线。该管线结合了编码掩模成像（coded-mask imaging）与镶嵌（mosaic）技术，能够在指向观测和航天器机动（slew）期间进行定位搜索，填补了Swift卫星在机动期间无法自主触发探测的关键空白。在66个伽马暴样本上的验证显示，管线成功恢复43个事件的弧分级定位（arcminute positions），典型偏移≤5角分；约88%发生在机动期间的GRB被成功恢复。在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次观测运行中，BAT-GLIMPSE与NITRATES协同工作，使Swift-BAT的弧分级定位率估计翻倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Swift卫星上的Burst Alert Telescope（BAT）具有弧分级（arcminute）精度的伽马射线瞬变源定位能力，但由于航天器机动（slew）期间星上触发（onboard triggering）被禁用，无法自动探测和定位该时间段内发生的瞬变源，形成观测盲区。

Method: BAT-GLIMPSE是一个全自主、开源的低延迟定位管线，利用BatAnalysis软件包，结合编码掩模成像（coded-mask imaging）与镶嵌（mosaic）技术，并根据航天器姿态自动选择适当的分析方法，从而在指向观测和机动期间均可进行定位搜索。

Result: 在66个GUANO通报的伽马暴（GRB）样本上验证：成功恢复43个事件的弧分级定位，与已发表的定位结果一致，典型偏移≤5角分；约88%发生在航天器机动期间的GRB通过成像或镶嵌分析被成功恢复。在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次观测运行（O4）中，BAT-GLIMPSE对寻找引力波的伽马射线对应体发挥了关键作用。

Conclusion: BAT-GLIMPSE填补了Swift卫星在机动期间无法自主定位的空白，与NITRATES管线协同运行，预计可使Swift-BAT的星上弧分级定位率翻倍，充分释放Swift任务在时域天体物理（time-domain astrophysics）和多信使天体物理（multi-messenger astrophysics）中的潜力。

Abstract: The Burst Alert Telescope (BAT) onboard the Neil Gehrels Swift Observatory is capable of localizing gamma-ray transients with arcminute precision, enabling rapid multi-wavelength follow-up. However, onboard triggering is disabled during spacecraft slews, preventing the autonomous detection and localization of transients occurring during these intervals. We present here BAT-GLIMPSE, a fully autonomous, open-source pipeline for the low-latency localization of transient gamma-ray sources in Swift-BAT data. Making use of the BatAnalysis package, the pipeline combines coded-mask imaging and mosaic techniques, automatically selecting the appropriate analysis according to the spacecraft attitude and enabling localization searches during both pointing observations and spacecraft slews. We validate the performance of BAT-GLIMPSE on a sample of 66 GRBs reported in GUANO circulars. The pipeline successfully recovers arcminute positions for 43 events, consistent with published localizations, with typical offsets of $\lesssim5$ arcminutes. Approximately $88\%$ of the GRBs occurring during spacecraft slews are recovered through imaging or mosaic analyses. During the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run, the role of BAT-GLIMPSE was crucial in the search for gamma-ray counterparts of gravitational waves, particularly in response to pre-merger alerts which triggered the slew of the Swift spacecraft with extremely low latency. Operating synergistically with NITRATES, BAT-GLIMPSE fills the critical gap left by slew intervals and, together, the two pipelines are estimated to double the onboard arcminute-localization rate of Swift-BAT, unlocking the full potential of the Swift mission for time-domain and multi-messenger astrophysics.

### [92] [Star-triangle duality estimates for triangular and honeycomb permutation models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14917)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 给出六角格子临界键维度估计值为 2.634929344884，通过单键对偶关系（single-bond duality relation）推导出三角格子临界键维度估计值为 1.475661534848。

Conclusion: 星-三角块作为基本单元是对偶性分析的关键所在，所给出的两种格子的临界键维度数值为后续随机张量网络及相关模型研究提供了参考。

Abstract: We study a duality analysis in conjunction with the star-triangle transformation for symmetric-group permutation models on the triangular and honeycomb lattices. The calculation is motivated by the permutation-model description of random tensor networks and by earlier duality analyses of replicated spin glasses. The essential point is that the finite-basis unit is not a bare bond but a star-triangle block. Our analysis estimates the critical bond dimension for the honeycomb lattice to be 2.634929344884, and the associated single-bond duality relation yields the triangular-lattice estimate 1.475661534848.

### [93] [Magic Without Entanglement: Exact Revivals and Their Fisher Information Origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14222)
*Rishabh Jha,Karun Gadge*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多体动力学中魔法（magic）与纠缠（entanglement）作为独立量子资源的结构性关系：在稳定子态（stabilizer state）下，第二稳定子Rényi熵的曲率与量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）成正比，建立了计算资源与计量资源之间的双向桥梁；通过对任意森林图（forest graph）上的对易Ising演化构造Clifford剪枝电路，获得了热力学极限下具有有限魔法密度和零纠缠密度的家族；并在Ising淬火和 kicked Floquet链中解析求解了任意系统大小和热力学极限下的准确解，揭示了魔法与纠缠的不同复兴周期等关键现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔法与纠缠虽被公认为独立的量子资源，但二者在多体动力学中的精确关系尚未明确，本文旨在揭示这一关系背后的结构原理。

Method: 通过第二稳定子Rényi熵的曲率与量子Fisher信息的等比例关系建立理论桥梁；利用Clifford剪枝电路对森林图上的对易Ising演化进行图论构造；采用Pauli基矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state）进行大规模数值验证。

Result: 建立了稳定子态下第二大Rényi熵曲率与量子Fisher信息之间的归一化比例关系；构造了热力学极限下有限魔法密度与零纠缠密度的图论家族；在Ising淬火和kicked Floquet链中解析得到了有限魔法密度、不同复兴周期以及Clifford点处的零魔法但有限纠缠等精确结果。

Conclusion: 魔法与纠缠在多体动力学中具有独立的结构性关系，切向几何（tangent geometry）决定了初始增长、微扰复兴提升和热力学魔法极小值的稳定性；所建立的切向桥梁可通过已有的量子Fisher信息测量实验协议检测魔法。

Abstract: Magic and entanglement are independent quantum resources, yet their exact relation in many-body dynamics has remained elusive. We uncover two structural principles. First, at any stabilizer state, the curvature of the second stabilizer Rényi entropy under an arbitrary Hermitian generator equals the quantum Fisher information up to a fixed normalization, creating a bidirectional bridge between computational and metrological resources. Second, for commuting Ising evolution on any forest graph, a Clifford pruning circuit yields the full stabilizer-Rényi family at arbitrary size and in any spatial embedding, thereby furnishing a graph-theoretic construction of families with finite magic density and vanishing entanglement density in the thermodynamic limit. We solve two paradigmatic one-dimensional realizations central to quantum simulation -- an Ising quench and a kicked Floquet chain -- exactly for arbitrary system size and directly in the thermodynamic limit, revealing finite magic density with vanishing entanglement density, distinct magic and entanglement revival periods, and Clifford points with zero magic but finite bipartite entanglement. The same tangent geometry fixes initial growth, perturbative revival lifting, and stability of thermodynamic magic minima. Large-scale Pauli-basis matrix-product-state calculations verify all predictions, and the tangent bridge yields a concrete protocol for detecting magic through established quantum-Fisher-information measurements.

</details>


### [94] [Efficient quantum algorithm for Heisenberg spin systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14401)
*Sergey Bravyi,David Gosset,Yinchen Liu,Benjamin Wong*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类由Suzuki和Fisher于1971年提出的海森堡型量子自旋系统族（包括二分图上的海森堡反铁磁体），证明了其基态与吉布斯态是半径为1的Lee-Yang张量，并推导出第一激发态与基态之间的能隙（spectral gap）的下界为2μ（μ为Z方向磁场）。基于此结果，构建了高效的量子绝热算法（quantum adiabatic algorithm）来求解该族模型的基态能量。证明方法基于一项新不等式，将半正定算子的能隙与其Lee-Yang半径联系起来，是对作者先前工作的定量加强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统的基态能量计算是量子计算与凝聚态物理中的核心难题。作者试图为一大类具有特殊零自由性（zero-freeness）性质的海森堡型量子自旋系统建立能隙下界，进而设计高效的量子算法，弥合统计力学中Lee-Yang理论（Lee-Yang theory）与量子计算复杂性之间的鸿沟。

Method: 方法核心是建立一项新不等式，将半正定算子（positive semidefinite operator）的谱能隙与其Lee-Yang半径（Lee-Yang radius）定量关联起来。这是对作者先前工作的定量强化，从而将Lee-Yang张量的零自由性性质转化为对能隙的严格下界估计。

Result: 对所有属于该族的海森堡型量子自旋哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），证明了其第一激发态与基态之间的能隙下界为2μ，其中μ是Z方向的磁场强度。基于这一能隙下界，为求解该族任意模型的基态能量构造了一个高效的量子绝热算法。

Conclusion: 该工作为一大类具有Lee-Yang零自由性性质的量子自旋系统提供了谱能隙的严格下界，并由此获得了高效的量子绝热算法。所发展的能隙—Lee-Yang半径不等式具有潜在更广泛的应用价值，可能推广到其他物理或数学场景中。

Abstract: We consider a broad family of Heisenberg-type quantum spin systems that were studied by Suzuki and Fisher in 1971. This family includes, for example, the Heisenberg antiferromagnet on any bipartite graph. The ground and Gibbs states of these models are Lee-Yang tensors with radius 1: they are associated with multilinear polynomials that possess an extraordinary zero-freeness property inside the unit polydisk in the complex plane. For each Hamiltonian in this family we show that the spectral gap between the first-excited and ground-state energies is lower bounded by $2μ$, where $μ$ is the magnetic field along the $Z$ direction. Using this result we obtain an efficient quantum adiabatic algorithm for the ground energy of any model in this family. The proof is based on a new inequality that relates the spectral gap of a positive semidefinite operator to its Lee-Yang radius -- a quantitative strengthening of prior work of the authors that may find applications elsewhere.

### [95] [Emergence and Recovery of (logical) Kochen-Specker Contextuality via Hamilton Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14629)
*Jayashree Karmakar,Biswadeep Chatterjee,Rafiuddin Gazi,Anushko Chattopadhyay,Ananya Chakraborty,Snehasish Roy Chowdhury,Amit Mukherjee,Manik Banik*

TL;DR: 本文提出“哈密顿延拓（Hamilton extension）”这一构造性方法，证明逻辑Kochen-Specker（KS）语境性可以从KS可着色向量集中涌现。通过分析四维向量集，发现六向量父集是生成KS矛盾的最小规模，揭示了语境性的新结构路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逻辑KS语境性（logical KS contextuality）传统上被视为特定测量构型的内在属性，本文旨在探索其能否从更基础的KS可着色结构中通过系统化方法涌现，从而揭示语境性的新来源。

Method: 提出哈密顿延拓（Hamilton extension）构造性程序：为四维向量集中的每个实向量关联一个测量语境，并在不同父向量的哈密顿延拓子代之间诱导额外测量语境，从而改变原有的相容性结构，使KS可着色构型转变为不可着色构型。

Result: 哈密顿延拓后，五向量父集保持KS可着色，而适当选择的六向量父集即可生成逻辑KS矛盾，表明六向量是产生KS矛盾的最小父集规模。该过程还能恢复因顶点-顶点扩充（apex-vertex augmentation）而丢失的逻辑语境性。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了语境性的一种新结构生成路径，为构建紧凑型KS集提供系统框架，并对基于语境性的量子信息协议以及非经典性的图论研究方法具有潜在意义。

Abstract: Logical Kochen-Specker (KS) contextuality is widely regarded as an intrinsic property of specially constructed measurement configurations. We show instead that it can emerge from KS-colorable vector sets through a constructive procedure we call the Hamilton extension. Defined for four-dimensional vector sets, the Hamilton extension associates each real vector with a measurement context while inducing additional measurement contexts among Hamilton-extended children of distinct parent vectors. These emergent contexts fundamentally alter the compatibility structure, transforming KS-colorable configurations into KS-uncolorable ones and recovering logical contextuality lost under apex-vertex augmentation. We establish a sharp and optimal threshold -- the Hamilton extension of every five-vector parent set remains KS-colorable, whereas suitably chosen six-vector parent sets already generate logical KS contradictions. Thus, six vectors constitute the smallest parent set capable of generating KS contradiction through this mechanism. Our results reveal a new structural route to contextuality, provide a systematic framework for constructing compact KS sets, and have implications for contextuality-based quantum information protocols and graph-theoretic approaches to nonclassicality.

Abstract: We study the effect of magnetic vector potentials on periodic Grover walks on finite graphs. We regard the vector potential as a perturbation of a periodic Grover walk and investigate the robustness of its periodicity. Our analysis reveals that the response to such perturbations depends on the spectral structure of the underlying graph. In particular, when the graph possesses at least one non-simple eigenvalue, we derive a Hermitian matrix that characterizes the robustness of its periodicity. As a consequence, we show that the perturbed dynamics is asymptotically described by a continuous-time quantum walk generated by this Hermitian matrix.

### [97] [Superadditivity for Entanglement-Assisted Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15151)
*Hao-Chung Cheng,Mario Berta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明，即使纠缠辅助容量（entanglement-assisted capacity）对量子信道具有可加的单字母刻画（additive single-letter characterization），通信的可靠性（reliability）却可以表现出严格的超可加性（strict superadditivity）：Petz-Rényi 信道信息在 α∈[1/2,1) 范围内严格超可加，导致纠缠辅助随机编码错误指数（random-coding error exponent）在多副本编码下获得增强。该现象在测量信道（measurement channel）上被解析验证，且仅需可分、经典关联的输入边际即可实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已知纠缠辅助容量具有可加性，意味着联合编码（joint encoding）不能提高最终通信速率。但可靠性（即错误指数）是否也具有相同性质尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示容量可加性并不自动延伸至通信可靠性，并证明即使在不改变可加容量的情况下，可靠性仍可被多副本编码增强。

Method: 通过分析 Petz-Rényi 信道信息（Petz-Rényi channel information）在 α∈[1/2,1) 范围内的超可加性，研究纠缠辅助随机编码错误指数在多副本（multi-copy）编码下的行为。论文以测量信道（measurement channel）作为具体模型进行解析分析，该类信道是纠缠破坏的（entanglement-breaking）且无辅助容量（unassisted capacity）可加。

Result: 严格证明了 Petz-Rényi 信道信息在 α∈[1/2,1) 范围内存在严格的超可加性，这意味着纠缠辅助随机编码错误指数在多副本编码下获得真正增强。该超可加性可在测量信道上被解析展示，且仅需一种可分（separable）、经典关联（classically correlated）的两副本信道输入边际即可实现，不要求传输系统之间存在纠缠。

Conclusion: 跨越信道使用次数的相关性虽然不能提高纠缠辅助通信的最终速率（即容量），但可以增强其可靠性（即错误指数）。这揭示了容量可加性与可靠性可加性之间的根本性分离，为量子通信编码理论提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The entanglement-assisted capacity of a quantum channel admits an additive single-letter characterization, implying that joint encodings across channel uses cannot increase the ultimate communication rate. Here, we show that this additive picture does not extend to communication reliability. Specifically, we prove that the Petz-Rényi channel information can be strictly superadditive for every $α\in[1/2,1)$, yielding a genuine multi-copy enhancement of the entanglement-assisted random-coding error exponent, even though the entanglement-assisted capacity remains additive. We establish this phenomenon analytically already for measurement channels, which are entanglement-breaking and have additive unassisted capacity. Remarkably, this strict superadditivity is witnessed by a separable, classically correlated two-copy channel-input marginal, demonstrating that no entanglement between the transmitted systems is required. Our results show that, although correlations across channel uses cannot increase the ultimate rate of entanglement-assisted communication, they can enhance its reliability.

</details>


### [98] [Counterexamples to additivity of minimum output $p$-Rényi entropy of quantum channels for $p>3/4$ and $0\leq p<1/4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15210)
*Debbie Leung,Benjamin Lovitz,Peixue Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于Rényi阶数p>3/4或0≤p<1/4，存在投影诱导的量子信道使得最小输出p-Rényi熵的非可加性成立，从而将未解决的区间缩小至[1/4,3/4]。证明结合了两种相关随机投影构造：面向p>3/4的乘积-共轭贝尔态证据（product-conjugate Bell-state witness）和面向p<1/4的转置-互补秩亏证据（transpose-complement rank-defect witness）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最小输出熵的可加性（additivity）是量子信息论（quantum information theory）中的一个核心问题。尽管已知在Rényi阶数p>1、冯·诺依曼点（von Neumann point）p=1以及p接近0时存在非可加性，但区间0<p<1的大部分范围此前尚未得到解决。

Method: 证明采用两种相关的随机投影构造方法：对于p>3/4，使用乘积-共轭贝尔态证据；对于p<1/4，使用转置-互补秩亏证据。两种构造分别对应于Rényi阶数区间的高端和低端，从而覆盖了0<p<1中除[1/4,3/4]之外的所有参数区域。

Result: 证明了对于满足p>3/4或0≤p<1/4的任意Rényi阶数p，存在有限维投影诱导的量子信道（projection-induced quantum channels），使得最小输出p-Rényi熵的可加性失效。这将未解决的区间从整个(0,1)缩小至[1/4,3/4]。此外，本文的估计还改进了最小输出冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）可加性违反所需输出维数阈值。

Conclusion: 最小输出p-Rényi熵的非可加性在0<p<1的绝大部分区间内成立，仅剩[1/4,3/4]这一中间区域有待进一步研究。该结果推进了对量子信道容量和熵可加性基本问题的理解。

Abstract: Additivity of minimum output entropies is a central problem in quantum information theory. Nonadditivity is known for every Rényi order $p>1$, at the von Neumann point $p=1$, and near $p=0$, while most of the interval $0<p<1$ has remained open. We prove that for every Rényi order $p$ satisfying either $p>3/4$ or $0\leq p<1/4$, there exist finite-dimensional projection-induced quantum channels such that additivity of the minimum output $p$-Rényi entropy fails. The proof combines two correlated random-projection constructions: a product-conjugate Bell-state witness for $p>3/4$, and a transpose-complement rank-defect witness for $p<1/4$. Thus the unresolved part of $0<p<1$ is reduced to $[1/4,3/4]$. Our estimates also improve the output dimension threshold for additivity violation of minimum output von Neumann entropy, first established in Belinschi, Collins and Nechida.

</details>


### [99] [Locality of deep thermalisation through the lens of entanglement teleportation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15276)
*Saptarshi Mandal,Alan Sherry,Sthitadhi Roy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究深度热化（deep thermalisation）现象中的局域性（locality）问题。当一个子系统被分为两个因果断开（causally disconnected）的子区域时，深度热化的出现受到测量诱导纠缠传送（measurement-induced entanglement teleportation）的根本限制。在一般局域相互作用系统中，深度热化和纠缠传送的时间尺度均随子区域间距呈对数增长，表现出涌现局域性（emergent locality）；而在特定特殊电路中，深度热化的时间尺度为有限值，导致真正的非局域性（genuine non-locality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在投影测量驱动下，量子态系综在子系统上涌现普遍性的深度热化现象中，局域性或非局域性所扮演的角色。

Method: 将子系统划分为两个在幺正动力学下始终保持因果断开（causally disconnected）的分离子区域，分析测量诱导纠缠传送（measurement-induced entanglement teleportation）与深度热化（deep thermalisation）之间的关系，并考察一般局域相互作用系统与特殊电路两种情况。

Result: 在一般局域相互作用系统中，深度热化和纠缠传送的时间尺度均随子区域间距呈对数增长，体现出涌现局域性（emergent locality）；但在特定特殊电路中，测量结果的随机性被完美传递到子系统的态系综，深度热化的时间尺度为有限值，导致真正的非局域性（genuine non-locality）。

Conclusion: 深度热化现象中的非局域性表象受到测量诱导纠缠传送的根本限制，但局域相互作用系统可以恢复涌现局域性，而特殊电路则可突破这一限制。

Abstract: Deep thermalisation characterises the emergence of universal quantum state ensembles on subsystems due to projective measurements on their complement. We study the notion of locality, or lack thereof, in this phenomenon by considering a subsystem partitioned into two disjoint subregions which remain causally disconnected at all times under unitary dynamics. We show that the onset of deep thermalisation in this geometry is fundamentally bounded by measurement-induced entanglement teleportation between the subregions. While measurements on the environment generate entanglement across the disconnected partitions -- suggesting an apparent non-locality -- we demonstrate that generic locally interacting systems exhibit an emergent locality. Specifically, the timescales for both deep thermalisation and entanglement teleportation scale logarithmically with the distance separating the subregions. Exceptions to this include special circuits where the randomness of the measurement outcomes is perfectly transmitted to the ensemble of states of the subsystem, conditioned on the outcomes; in such cases the timescale for deep thermalisation is finite leading to genuine non-locality.

Conclusion: 该方案为非平衡动力学（non-equilibrium dynamics）中的量子优势实验提供了一个可行的基准测试方法。

Abstract: The applications for which quantum computers will clearly outperform classical computers are still being identified and benchmarking such an advantage is challenging. We propose a scalable verification scheme for non-equilibrium quantum simulation based on stabilizer scars, a special class of quantum many-body scars, whose structure ensures both classical simulability and efficient direct fidelity estimation. Assuming a physically motivated error model, we show that the fidelity of quantum simulating these states bounds the fidelity of classically intractable simulations, providing a benchmark for quantum-advantage experiments in non-equilibrium dynamics.

Motivation: 理解复杂系统在有序与混沌之间的转变是非平衡物理学的核心挑战。虽然经典可积系统的弱扰动会产生规则与混沌轨迹共存的混合相空间，但相互作用量子多体系统中的类似行为至今难以捉摸。

Method: 该方法是一种混合量子-经典（hybrid quantum-classical）反馈协议：每次迭代将短时量子演化与经典优化相结合，将动力学投影回低纠缠变分流形（low-entanglement variational manifold），从而从混沌演化中有效提取相干性。

Result: 稳定后的轨迹揭示了从非线性变分动力学中涌现出的量子多体混合相空间（quantum many-body mixed phase space），这在经典或少体量子系统中没有直接对应物。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一个通用的框架，可用于算法性地发现和控制此前实验无法触及的相干动力学。

Abstract: Understanding how complex systems transition between order and chaos is a central challenge of nonequilibrium physics. While weak perturbations of classical integrable systems give rise to a mixed phase space of coexisting regular and chaotic trajectories, analogous behavior in interacting quantum many-body systems has remained elusive. Here we develop and experimentally implement a hybrid quantum-classical feedback protocol that autonomously discovers and stabilizes long-lived regular trajectories in a superconducting quantum processor. Each iteration combines short-time quantum evolution with classical optimization that projects the dynamics back onto a low-entanglement variational manifold, effectively distilling coherence from chaotic evolution. The stabilized trajectories reveal a quantum many-body mixed phase space emerging from nonlinear variational dynamics, without a direct analogue in classical or few-body quantum systems. Our results establish a versatile framework for algorithmic discovery and control of coherent dynamics previously inaccessible to experiment.

Abstract: Circuit quantum electrodynamics embeds Josephson junction qubits within superconducting cavities, and has emerged as a leading approach to quantum computing and quantum simulation. Despite the many permutations of circuit geometry that have been explored, Josephson connectivities have so far been planar, making them effectively low-dimensional. Here we show that a non-planar qubit -- a $3\times3$ crossbar Josephson array -- gives rise to flux-tunable $\mathbb{Z}_3$ combinatorial gauge symmetry (CGS), potentially enabling spin-liquid behavior when networked into a lattice. The observed excitation spectrum shows excellent agreement with predictions from a neural network trained to generate variational quantum states, demonstrating that we have predictive power over our high-dimensional quantum system. Fine-structure splittings near the CGS point are compatible with weak tunneling or symmetry breaking due to experimental imperfections. We additionally use the superconducting cavity to externally induce symmetry breaking, observing a restoration of symmetry at the CGS point where ground states differ only by a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ phase. This work initiates a general program exploring lattice gauge theories using the toolbox of circuit quantum electrodynamics. More broadly, introducing non-planar Josephson connectivities opens a vast space for experimental and theoretical exploration of structures in almost any imaginable dimensionality and geometry.

### [103] [Disorder-enhanced compressibility of Floquet random quantum circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14296)
*Francesca De Franco,Dante M. Kennes,David J. Luitz,Matteo Rizzi,Markus Schmitt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前量子硬件受噪声和退相干（decoherence）限制，导致高保真度幺正电路（unitary circuit）的深度受限。因此需探索时间演化算符的可压缩性（compressibility）如何依赖于底层多体系统（many-body system）的动力学区域。

Method: 以一维Floquet随机电路为测试平台，调控相互作用与局域无序（on-site disorder）之间的竞争；采用张量网络模拟（tensor-network simulation），通过算符纠缠熵（operator-entanglement entropy）和时序外关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOCs）表征算符增长（operator growth）。

Result: 弱无序下算符快速 scrambling；强无序下OTOC波前传播缓慢，算符纠缠呈现对数或近对数增长。优化浅层砖墙电路（brickwall circuits）逼近Floquet演化后发现：在固定对数保真度密度（logarithmic fidelity density）下，强无序电路的压缩深度显著小于弱无序电路。

Conclusion: 局域化（localized）或慢速 scrambling 的动力学区域为含噪设备上的压缩量子模拟提供了有利条件。

Abstract: Current quantum hardware is limited by noise and decoherence, which restrict the depth of unitary circuits that can be implemented with high fidelity. We investigate how the compressibility of time-evolution operators depends on the dynamical regime of the underlying many-body system. As a testbed, we study a one-dimensional Floquet random circuit with a tunable competition between interactions and on-site disorder. Using tensor-network simulations, we characterize operator growth through the operator-entanglement entropy of the Floquet unitary as well as of out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs). We find rapid operator scrambling at weak disorder, while strong disorder leads to slow OTOC-front propagation and logarithmic or near-logarithmic operator-entanglement growth over the accessible time window. We then optimize shallow brickwall circuits to approximate the Floquet evolution and show that strong-disorder circuits can be compressed to substantially smaller depths than weak-disorder circuits at fixed logarithmic fidelity density. These results suggest that localized or slowly scrambling dynamics provide a favorable regime for compressed quantum simulation on noisy devices.

### [104] [Circuit complexity lower bounds for quantum spin glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14384)
*Omar Al-Ghattas,David Gamarnik*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在量子p-自旋玻璃模型中，要制备能量接近最优值的n量子比特态，电路深度必须满足下界：当平均相互作用度随n增长时，深度为Ω_p(log n)；在有限平均度的情形下，足够大的度因子会完全排除固定深度电路的制备可能性。这一结果为随机量子哈密顿量提供了类似“无能级平凡态”的障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信息理论的一个核心问题是：来自标准多体模型的态（states）的电路复杂度（circuit complexity）是多少？已有工作表明最优能量与乘积态（product states）能实现的最佳能量之间存在间隙，但尚不清楚浅层电路（shallow circuits）能否弥合这一间隙，因为即使深度为一的电路也能产生纠缠（entanglement）。

Method: 本文将态制备下界（state-preparation lower bounds）问题重新表述为由浅层电路索引的高斯过程（Gaussian processes）的一致控制（uniform control）问题，从而为NLTS类问题开辟了一条概率论路径。研究涵盖了平均相互作用度随n增长和有限平均度两种不同 regime。

Result: 在平均相互作用度随n增长时，对所有足够大的固定p，任何制备归一化能量在最优值固定正常数范围内的n量子比特态的电路，深度必须为Ω_p(log n)。在有限平均度 regime 下，对每个固定D，足够大的度因子会排除深度为D的近乎基态（near-ground states）的制备。这两个结果均对任意数量辅助量子比特（ancilla qubits）的电路一致成立。

Conclusion: 本文为随机量子自旋玻璃（random quantum spin glasses）而非基于编码的哈密顿量提供了类似Freedman-Hastings“无能级平凡态”（No Low-Energy Trivial States, NLTS）问题的障碍，从而将NLTS类问题推广到随机哈密顿量的概率论框架中。

Abstract: A central question in quantum information theory is the circuit complexity of states arising from standard many-body models. We study this question for quantum $p$-spin glasses, random Hamiltonians whose interactions act on $p$-tuples of qubits through Pauli strings. Anschuetz, Gamarnik, and Kiani (arXiv:2404.07231) showed that the optimum energy is separated from the best energy achievable by product states. This leaves open whether shallow circuits can close the gap, since even depth-one circuits can generate entanglement.
  We show that the entanglement needed to close the product-state gap cannot be generated at shallow depth. When the average interaction degree grows with $n$, we prove that, for all sufficiently large fixed $p$, any circuit preparing an $n$-qubit state whose normalized energy is within a fixed positive constant of the optimum must have depth $Ω_p(\log n)$. In the bounded-average-degree regime, we prove a fixed-depth obstruction: for every fixed $D$, a sufficiently large degree prefactor rules out depth-$D$ preparation of near-ground states. Both results hold uniformly over circuits with an arbitrary number of ancilla qubits.
  Our results give an obstruction in the spirit of the No Low-Energy Trivial States problem of Freedman and Hastings (arXiv:1301.1363), but for random quantum spin glasses rather than code-based Hamiltonians such as those of Anshu, Breuckmann, and Nirkhe (arXiv:2206.13228), whose ground states admit polynomial-size preparation circuits. This setting opens a probabilistic route to NLTS-like questions: we recast state-preparation lower bounds for random quantum Hamiltonians as uniform control of Gaussian processes indexed by shallow circuits.

Method: 作者对量子接触过程的离散化版本进行数值分析，并构造了一种系统性的连续插值方法，以连接离散化与连续时间版本的结果。

Abstract: We numerically analyze a discretized version of the quantum contact process, a non-equilibrium model having a competition between a coherent infection process and a dissipative recovery process. Previously, the continuous-time version has been discussed to have a phase transition in a novel quantum universality class, while experimental investigations of a related process have pointed towards the transition being in the classical directed percolation class. We demonstrate that these differences stem from details of the discretization of the process and construct a systematic way to continuously interpolate between these results. Finally, we provide evidence that the modification of the universality class is due to destructive interference effects, showing a clear quantum-mechanical origin.

Conclusion: 网络对称性和粒子数奇偶性在决定多体系统的能谱行为中起关键作用，半填充下的粒子-空穴对称性为抵抗塞曼分裂提供了保护机制。

Abstract: We investigate interacting spinless electrons on finite molecular ring networks described by a tight-binding Hubbard Hamiltonian. Special attention is devoted to the role of the network symmetries in determining the structure of the many-body spectrum and the Mulliken classification of the eigenstates. Using group-theoretical methods, we examine the evolution of the spectra in the presence of an external magnetic flux. The Zeeman effect lifts degeneracies and results in combination with the Coulomb interaction to avoided crossings in symmetry sectors. We identify a qualitatively distinction between systems with an even and odd number of particles. At half-filling, particle-hole symmetry (duality) protects selected symmetry sectors against Zeeman splitting.

### [107] [A Geometric Theory of Fermion-to-Qubit Encodings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14883)

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出费米子-量子比特变换（fermion-to-qubit transformations）不仅仅是用于量子模拟的算法工具，还定义了内在几何表示，其结构编码了超越谱等价的物理信息。基于Bravyi–Kitaev (BK) 和 Xia–Bian–Kais (XBK) 编码，作者构建了加权超图（weighted hypergraphs）与耦合空间（coupling space）的几何框架，发现了两个几何普适类（geometric universality classes），并通过多个多体模型验证了该几何描述能一致地捕捉编码量子哈密顿量的结构演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将费米子-量子比特变换仅视为将多体哈密顿量转化为量子比特表示以进行量子模拟的算法工具；本文旨在揭示这些变换还定义了内在的几何表示，其结构携带超越谱等价的物理意义，从而建立理解编码哈密顿量的新几何框架。

Method: 基于加权超图和耦合空间表示构建几何框架：在BK表示中定义了几何可观测量（geometric observable），用于比较动能与相互作用超图的代数连通性（algebraic connectivity），并推导了该可观测量对相互作用强度的精确解析依赖关系；在XBK表示中，通过耦合空间中的概率测度（probability measures）与最优传输（optimal transport）描述编码哈密顿量的演化。

Result: 在BK表示中发现了两个几何普适类以及源于编码二叉树结构的精确谱组织（exact spectral organization）；利用最优传输量化了与谱分析无关的相互作用驱动重组（interaction-driven reorganization）。在Hubbard、自旋less tV、单杂质Anderson和Kitaev模型上的应用表明，基于连通性和传输的几何描述能一致地捕捉不同多体系统中编码量子哈密顿量的结构演化。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了超图几何（hypergraph geometry）作为理解费米子-量子比特编码的新框架，揭示了这些变换不仅是计算映射，更是量子多体哈密顿量的几何表示。

Abstract: Exact fermion to qubit transformations are conventionally regarded as algorithmic tools that translate many-body Hamiltonians into qubit representations for quantum simulation. Here we show that they also define intrinsic geometric representations whose structure encodes physically meaningful information beyond spectral equivalence. We develop a geometric framework based on weighted hypergraphs and coupling space representations constructed from the Bravyi--Kitaev (BK) and Xia--Bian--Kais (XBK) encodings. Within the BK representation, we introduce a geometric observable that compares the algebraic connectivities of the kinetic and interaction hypergraphs, derive its exact analytical dependence on interaction strength, and uncover two geometric universality classes together with an exact spectral organization originating from the binary tree architecture of the encoding. The complementary XBK representation describes the evolution of encoded Hamiltonians through probability measures in coupling space, where optimal transport quantifies interaction-driven reorganization independently of the spectral analysis. Applications to the Hubbard, spinless tV , single impurity Anderson, and Kitaev models demonstrate that these connectivity and transport based geometric descriptions consistently capture the structural evolution of encoded quantum Hamiltonians across distinct classes of many-body systems. Our results establish hypergraph geometry as a new framework for understanding fermion-to-qubit encodings,revealing that they serve not only as computational mappings but also as geometric representations of quantum many-body Hamiltonians.

### [108] [Implicit differentiation of tensor network algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15030)
*Lander Burgelman,Anna Francuz,Paul Brehmer,Lukas Devos,Jutho Haegeman,Frank Verstraete,Bram Vanhecke*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于自动微分（automatic differentiation）的投影纠缠对态（PEPS）变分优化方法中，能量梯度的评估既是计算瓶颈，又频繁遭遇数值不稳定性（numerical instabilities），亟需解决这两方面的问题。

Method: 采用隐式微分（implicit differentiation）技术，将梯度计算的核心步骤重新表述为收缩环境（contraction environment）的单一特征方程（characteristic equation）；基于收缩环境的内在对称性（intrinsic symmetries）选择该特征方程的适当参数化方式，从而消除来自收缩算法子程序导数的全局梯度不稳定性。

Result: 该方法降低了梯度计算的成本并改善了其随问题规模的扩展性（scaling）；直接移除了全局梯度计算中的数值不稳定性，这些不稳定性原本源于收缩算法子程序（subroutines of the contraction algorithm）的导数。

Conclusion: 该方法极大地简化了基于稳定梯度的投影纠缠对态（PEPS）优化的实际实现过程。

Abstract: The current leading approach to the variational optimization of projected entangled-pair states (PEPS) is based on automatic differentiation, which allows for a convenient evaluation of the energy gradient with respect to the local variational degrees of freedom. However, evaluating the energy gradient not only remains a major computational bottleneck of the optimization procedure, but also suffers from frequent numerical instabilities. In this work, we adopt recent advances in implicit differentiation techniques to address these challenges in PEPS optimization. By reformulating the core step of the gradient computation in terms of a single characteristic equation for the contraction environment, we reduce the cost of the gradient computation and improve its scaling with the problem size. By choosing a suitable parametrization of this characteristic equation based on the intrinsic symmetries of the contraction environment, we can directly remove instabilities from the global gradient computation that would otherwise arise from the derivatives of subroutines of the contraction algorithm. Finally, we demonstrate how this approach drastically simplifies the practical implementation of stable gradient-based PEPS optimization.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架在弱耦合（weak coupling）之外无法确定精细平衡关系（detailed balance relation）的类比项和两个耦合强度常数（coupling strength constants）。因此亟需一种新方法，既能获得超出弱耦合的精确描述，又能提供可行的实验路径来测量这些基本参数。

Method: 采用GKLS主方程的数学等价形式，导出二能级系统与强耦合环境的精确理论框架。该框架基于三个未被弱耦合理论涵盖的参数。此外，提出一个基于固态电子量子点器件的实验协议，用以揭示这些参数。

Result: 该框架具有物理直觉性，能揭示问题背后的物理机制，并复现了已有结果，例如系统热化至非正则态（non-canonical state）。所提议的固态量子点实验方案有望使强耦合下的基本参数成为可观测量。

Conclusion: 该工作为强耦合量子系统提供了精确的理论框架与可行的实验途径，对深化强耦合问题的基本理解具有推动作用。

Abstract: We employ a mathematically equivalent form of the GKLS master equation to arrive at an exact theoretical description of a two-level system strongly coupled to the environment. The framework, while intuitive, shedding light on the physics of the problem, and agreeing with existing results, such as thermalisation to a non-canonical state, is based around three parameters that are unknown outside of the weak coupling regime -- the analogue to the detailed balance relation, and two coupling strength constants. As a way forward, we propose a feasible experimental protocol based on a solid-state electronic quantum dot device, through which the fundamental parameters of the problem can be revealed, which would further the fundamental understanding of strong coupling.

</details>


### [110] [On the origin of finite entanglement scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15124)
*Luke Hodgkiss,Laurens Lootens,Atsushi Ueda,Bram Vanhecke,Frank Verstraete*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过开发一种稀疏线性求解器，隐式计算二维张量网络对其定义参数的前向和后向导数，解决了临界系统矩阵乘积态近似所引发的实际扰动的开放问题，并证明了这些扰动与共形场论预测存在显著差异。该算法还提供了一种规避传统自动微分不稳定性、用于投影纠缠对态变分优化的原始方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限纠缠标度（finite entanglement scaling）是张量网络（tensor network）生态系统的基础支柱之一，但临界系统（critical systems）中矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）近似所引发的实际扰动形式一直是一个未解决的开放问题。

Method: 开发了一种稀疏线性求解器（sparse linear solver），以隐式方式计算二维张量网络（2-dimensional tensor networks）对其定义参数的前向导数（forward derivatives）和背向导数（backward derivatives）。

Result: 证明了临界系统中矩阵乘积态近似所引发的实际扰动与共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）预测的扰动存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 所提出的算法不仅解决了临界系统中矩阵乘积态扰动形式这一开放问题，还提供了一种可用于投影纠缠对态（projected entangled pair states, PEPS）变分优化的原始方法（primitive），能够规避传统自动微分方法（automatic differentiation methods）中存在的不稳定性问题。

Abstract: The concept of finite entanglement scaling forms one of the pillars on which the tensor network ecosystem is built. In this paper, we resolve the open problem of determining the actual perturbations induced by matrix product state approximations of critical systems, and we demonstrate that these can be quite different than the ones predicted by conformal field theory. To that aim, we develop a sparse linear solver to calculate the forward and backward derivatives of 2-dimensional tensor networks with respect to their defining parameters in an implicit way. This algorithm is of independent interest as it provides a primitive for the variational optimization of projected entangled pair states that circumvents the instabilities plaguing traditional automatic differentiation methods.

</details>


### [111] [Periodic orbits and quantum many-body scars in integrable spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15132)
*Elena Petrova,Maksym Serbyn,Marko Ljubotina*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过周期轨道（periodic-orbit）框架研究可积XYZ/XXZ自旋-1/2链中的量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars），利用Bethe-ansatz量子数识别疤痕轨道及其支撑本征态，揭示了零动量磁振子对（zero-momentum magnon pairs）在疤痕现象中的微观机制，并展示了该结构在打破可积性后依然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体疤痕作为热化动力学（thermalising dynamics）的例外现象，其与可积性（integrability）之间的关联尚不清楚。本文旨在澄清这一关系。

Method: 将周期轨道框架应用于可积XYZ/XXZ自旋-1/2链，发展了一种能量分辨（energy-resolved）方法以定位和追踪跨能谱的周期轨道；利用Bethe-ansatz量子数识别疤痕轨道及其支撑本征态，并分析Bethe方程中零动量磁振子对的退耦效应。

Result: 识别出疤痕轨道族，并发现其支撑本征态具有由零动量磁振子对包裹的公共弦核（common string core）结构；在Bethe-ansatz框架内重建了疤痕本征态及相关塔（tower），解析地解释了等间距塔间距（equidistant tower spacing）的起源；该结构在加入横向场打破可积性后仍持续存在。

Conclusion: 建立了量子疤痕的周期轨道图像与可积模型代数结构之间的直接联系，表明疤痕动力学的关键特征可在Bethe-ansatz框架内得到解析理解。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars provide an exception to generic thermalising dynamics, but their relation to integrability remains unclear. Here we apply the periodic-orbit framework to the integrable XYZ/XXZ spin-1/2 chain, developing an energy-resolved approach that enables us to locate and track periodic orbits across the spectrum. We identify families of scarred orbits and resolve their supporting eigenstates in terms of Bethe-ansatz quantum numbers, revealing a common string core dressed by zero-momentum magnon pairs. This allows us to reconstruct both the scarred eigenstates and the associated towers directly within the Bethe ansatz, and explain the equidistant tower spacing analytically from the decoupling of zero-momentum magnon pairs in the Bethe equations, providing a microscopic realisation of scar phenomenology in an integrable setting. We further show that this structure persists upon breaking integrability with a transverse field, with the periodic orbits continuing to govern the dynamics. Our results establish a direct connection between the periodic-orbit picture of quantum scarring and the algebraic structure of integrable models, showing that key features of scar dynamics can be understood analytically within the Bethe ansatz framework.
