### [112] [Backpropagating Pauli Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15184)
*Sheng-Hsuan Lin,Etienne Granet,Kevin Hémery,Henrik Dreyer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于泡利传播模拟（Pauli propagation simulation）的反向传播算法，用于量子电路（quantum circuit）中的参数梯度计算。该算法在计算复杂度上与标准稀疏泡利模拟技术相当，梯度精度与可观测量期望值同阶，同时通过利用量子电路可逆性将内存成本降低 $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ 倍，并将函数评估效率相比有限差分法（finite difference method）提升 $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ 倍。通过横场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）和三维海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）的基态制备以及二维时间演化电路压缩任务验证了方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子电路的经典优化中，参数梯度的高效准确计算是核心需求。现有反向模式自动微分（reverse-mode automatic differentiation）内存成本过高，有限差分法（finite difference method）函数评估次数过多，亟需一种兼顾计算效率、内存开销和梯度精度的梯度计算方法。

Method: 基于泡利传播模拟（Pauli propagation simulation）开发反向传播算法，利用泡利算符在量子电路中的传播特性计算参数梯度。通过量子电路的可逆性（reversibility）实现反向传播，将内存成本从标准反向模式自动微分的 $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ 倍降低至常数倍，同时函数评估次数相比有限差分法减少 $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ 倍。

Result: 该算法的计算复杂度与标准稀疏泡利模拟技术相当，梯度精度与对应可观测量期望值（observable expectation values）同阶。在横场伊辛模型的一维、二维、三维以及三维海森堡模型的低能态制备电路优化中验证了有效性，并在二维时间演化电路压缩任务中展示了实际应用能力。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子电路的经典优化提供了一种高效、准确的梯度计算方案，特别适用于态制备（state preparation）和时间演化压缩（time-evolution compression）等任务。同时支持在优化过程中监测和正则化算子复杂度度量，如算子稳定子雷尼熵（operator stabilizer Rényi entropy）。

Abstract: We develop a backpropagation algorithm for evaluating parameter gradients in quantum circuits using Pauli propagation simulation. The method has computational complexity comparable to that of standard sparse Pauli simulation techniques, while producing gradients whose accuracy is of the same order as the corresponding observable expectation values. By exploiting the reversibility of quantum circuits, the algorithm reduces the memory cost by a factor of $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ compared with conventional reverse-mode automatic differentiation, where $n_\text{param}$ denotes the number of parameters in the circuit. Compared with finite difference methods, the algorithm is $\mathcal{O}(n_\text{param})$ more efficient in function evaluations. These features enable efficient and accurate classical optimization of quantum circuits for applications such as state preparation and time-evolution compression, while also allowing operator-complexity measures such as the operator stabilizer Rényi entropy to be monitored and regularized during optimization. We demonstrate the method by optimizing low-energy state-preparation circuits for transverse-field Ising models in one, two, and three dimensions and for the three-dimensional Heisenberg model, and by compressing two-dimensional time-evolution circuits.

</details>


### [113] [Coulomb blockade in microscopic material defects as a source of decoherence and noise in solid-state quantum circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15252)
*R. Banerjee,L. P. Lindoy,M. Hegedus,A. Hutcheson,T. Hawkins,E. Daghigh-Ahmadi,S. Samaddar,T. Barker,J. P. Goff,A. Ya. Tzalenchuk,I. Rungger,S. E. de Graaf*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描栅极显微镜（scanning gate microscopy）在超导电路中识别出一种此前未被认识的退相干机制，该机制源于金属颗粒中的库仑阻塞（Coulomb blockade）和微波驱动电荷隧穿（microwave-driven charge tunnelling）。这类颗粒在标准制备工艺的薄膜器件中普遍存在，其危害性与双能级系统（two-level system, TLS）缺陷相当，但物理机制根本不同。该发现挑战了“相干寿命主要由TLS缺陷限制”的主流范式，并指出消除金属颗粒是提升相干性和降低噪声的可行途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态量子器件的相干性和噪声受限于材料中的表面、界面及结构缺陷，但将这些退相干机制与其微观材料起源联系起来——这是制定有效缓解策略的关键——一直是一个悬而未决的挑战，阻碍了相干性的提升。

Method: 作者采用扫描栅极显微镜（scanning gate microscopy）对工作中的超导电路进行原位表征，识别并分析了器件中金属颗粒引起的库仑阻塞（Coulomb blockade）和微波驱动电荷隧穿（microwave-driven charge tunnelling）效应。

Result: 研究发现，这类由金属颗粒导致的退相干机制在标准光刻工艺制备的薄膜器件中普遍存在，且其危害性与双能级系统（two-level system, TLS）缺陷相当。传统表征技术会错误地将这种损耗归因于其他与微波功率无关的过程。

Conclusion: 该发现挑战了“相干寿命主要由TLS缺陷限制”的主流范式，表明金属颗粒是一类广泛存在但此前被忽视的退相干来源。消除制备过程中的金属颗粒为抑制该机制、提升超导量子器件的相干性和降低噪声提供了清晰而实用的路径。

Abstract: A critical limitation of solid-state quantum devices arises from the materials from which they are fabricated: uncontrolled surfaces, interfaces, and structural imperfections introduce numerous sources of loss and decoherence. Despite extensive efforts, linking these decoherence mechanisms to their microscopic material origins -- essential for developing effective mitigation strategies -- remains an outstanding challenge that has slowed coherence improvements. Here, using scanning gate microscopy on live superconducting circuits we identify a previously unrecognised decoherence mechanism originating from Coulomb blockade and microwave-driven charge tunnelling in metallic grains. Such grains are ubiquitous in thin-film devices fabricated by standard lithography processes. By characterising multiple defects across different devices, we find such defects to be as common and as debilitating to device performance as two-level system (TLS) defects, while originating from a fundamentally different physical mechanism. Importantly, conventional characterisation techniques would misattribute this loss to other, microwave power-independent processes. Our observations thus reveal a widespread source of decoherence in superconducting circuits, challenging the prevailing paradigm that coherence lifetimes are primarily limited by TLS defects. Eliminating metallic grains during fabrication provides a clear and practical route to suppress this mechanism, offering a pathway towards improved coherence and reduced noise in microwave-based solid-state quantum devices.

</details>

### [114] [Gravity-Induced Thermal Rectification in Gaseous Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14136)
*Rongxiang Luo,Chao Yang,Juncheng Guo,Qiyuan Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与数值模拟证明，仅依靠重力（gravity）即可在气体系统中诱导和调控热整流（thermal rectification, TR），实现近乎完美的单向热传导，并在多粒子相互作用体系及混合气体中表现出整流方向可调的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热整流依赖结构不对称性或材料非均匀性，本研究旨在探索重力作为单一驱动因素能否在气体系统中独立产生热整流效应，从而揭示热输运（thermal transport）的新机制。

Method: 采用二维通道中单气体粒子在温差热浴间的简约模型（minimal model）进行解析推导，并通过数值模拟（numerical simulation）扩展至相互作用多粒子系统及气体混合物。

Result: 重力场可在宽参数范围内产生几乎完美的单向热传导；整流效率（rectification efficiency）与热功率（heat power）之间存在内在权衡（trade-off）；在相互作用多粒子系统中重力诱导的热整流依然存在；混合气体中整流方向可发生反转。

Conclusion: 重力介导的热流控制为热输运提供了新的基本认知，并为气体热二极管（gaseous thermal diode）的设计提供了原理性指导。

Abstract: Thermal rectification (TR) typically relies on structural asymmetry or material heterogeneity. Here, we show that gravity alone can induce and modulate TR in gaseous systems. Using a minimal model of a single gas particle confined in a two-dimensional channel between heat baths at different temperatures, we analytically demonstrate that gravitational fields generate TR, enabling perfect unidirectional heat conduction across broad gravitational parameter ranges. This effect exhibits an intrinsic trade-off between rectification efficiency and heat power. Extending beyond the single-particle limit, numerical simulations confirm that gravitationally induced TR persists in interacting many-particle systems. Notably, in interacting gas mixtures, the rectification direction can be reversed. Gravity-mediated control of heat currents thus provides new fundamental insights into thermal transport and suggests design principles for gaseous thermal diodes.

</details>


### [115] [Long-lived memory in sliding spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14383)
*Charles Stahl,Ethan Lake*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 研究了一对相互滑动的铁磁伊辛链（ferromagnetic Ising chains）在热浴中的非平衡动力学，发现磁摩擦（magnetic friction）可显著延长系统对初始磁化（magnetization）的记忆时间，从静态下的指数级增长至滑动状态下的超指数级增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维磁系统中非平衡驱动力（如相对滑动）如何影响有序化和热化（thermalization）过程，特别是磁摩擦能否作为调控系统记忆时间的简单机制。

Method: 构建两个耦合热浴的铁磁伊辛链模型，令其一维链以恒定速度（constant speed）v相对滑动，通过动力学分析研究系统的有序化和记忆时间随逆温度β、伊辛耦合J和滑动速度v的变化。

Result: 即使在中等的滑动速度下，磁摩擦也能显著提升系统的有序化能力。记忆时间从静态（v=0）时的exp(O(βJ))增长至v>v_c时的exp(O((βJ)²v ln v))，其中v_c为一个小常数。

Conclusion: 磁摩擦为一维磁系统提供了一种通过非平衡驱动参数化减慢热化的简单机制。

Abstract: We study a system of two ferromagnetic one-dimensional Ising chains coupled to a thermal bath, which are driven out of equilibrium by being moved past one another at a constant speed. We show that even at modest speeds, magnetic friction between the two chains significantly increases the ability of the system to order. In particular, at inverse temperature $β$, Ising coupling $J$, and sliding speed $v$, the dynamics retains memory of its initial magnetization for a time that increases from $\exp(O(βJ))$ at $v = 0$ to $\exp(O((βJ)^2v\ln v))$ when $v>v_c$, where $v_c$ is a small constant. Magnetic friction thus provides a simple mechanism for parametrically slowing down thermalization in a one-dimensional magnet.

</details>


### [116] [Memory of Initial Conditions in Self-Similar Diffusion: A Renormalization-Group Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14388)
*Ko Okumura*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过统一的重整化群（renormalization-group, RG）框架研究自相似动力学，发现保留相关长度尺度会自然产生不同类型的记忆保持固定点（memory-retaining fixed points），修正的密度相关扩散模型揭示了一个普遍标度结构，其中初始条件信息在渐近状态下仍然相关，Barenblatt方程作为特例出现，为普适性（universality）和反常标度（anomalous scaling）提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为普适性（universality）意味着渐近行为与初始状态细节无关。本文旨在挑战这一观念，探索在自相似动力学（self-similar dynamics）中初始条件信息是否可能持续保持渐近相关性。

Method: 采用统一的重整化群（renormalization-group, RG）框架分析自相似动力学，并结合一个修正的密度相关扩散模型（density-dependent diffusion model）来揭示标度结构。

Result: 保留相关长度尺度会导致出现不同类别的记忆保持固定点（memory-retaining fixed points），且初始条件信息在渐近极限下仍然相关。Barenblatt方程被证明是该普遍框架的一个特例。

Conclusion: 该研究重新定义了普适性的内涵，指出初始条件信息在自相似动力学中可以保持渐近相关的角色，从而为普适性（universality）和反常标度（anomalous scaling）提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Universality is usually associated with asymptotic behavior becoming independent of details of the initial state. Using a unified renormalization-group (RG) framework for self-similar dynamics, we show that retaining relevant length scales leads naturally to distinct classes of memory-retaining fixed points. A modified density-dependent diffusion model reveals a general scaling structure in which initial-condition information remains asymptotically relevant, with the Barenblatt equation emerging as a special case. These results provide a new perspective on universality and anomalous scaling.

</details>


### [117] [Moment-Resolved Readout and Reservoir Diversity in Nonequilibrium Langevin Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14520)
*JiZheng Duan,MingYang Zhao,YanWei Chen,Lei Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于矩分辨读出（moment-resolved readout）的非线性热力学计算机（thermodynamic computers）范式，利用朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）中的热涨落作为计算物理基底。通过构造由原始多项式矩（包括一阶、二阶和四阶矩）组成的响应向量，并引入异构多储层架构（heterogeneous multi-reservoir architecture），在MNIST手写数字识别任务中达到了96.95%的准确率，初步优于单储层模型。该工作为有限时间朗之万计算（finite-time Langevin computing）提供了高阶多项式矩读出和储层异构性两个候选设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，四次约束下的涨落自由度可作为热力学神经元（thermodynamic neurons），在有限观测时间内实现非线性函数逼近。但先前的工作仅限于均值读出（mean-only readout），未充分利用更高阶的矩信息来提升计算能力。本文旨在将该范式从均值读出扩展至矩分辨读出，以更充分地提取驱动储层（driven reservoir）中的计算信息。

Method: 本文的核心方法包括两个层次。第一，使用元素级原始多项式矩\(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}]\)、\(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}^{\odot 2}]\)和\(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}^{\odot 4}]\)构造响应向量，将每个驱动储层从仅依赖一阶矩（first moment）扩展为包含位移与中心形状贡献的高阶矩表示，这些可观测量的形式与局部驱动动力学中的线性、二次和四次项自然对齐。第二，引入异构多储层架构，将三个具有不同初始化和训练历史的储层联合形成一个2304维的联合响应表示，并通过特征级融合（feature-level fusion）进行集成。

Result: 在固定的MNIST（60,000/10,000划分）重现协议下，特征级融合达到了96.95%的最佳准确率（9695/10,000），而最强单储层模型为96.82%（9682/10,000），等权对数几率平均为96.84%（9684/10,000）。精确配对McNemar检验（McNemar test）未建立相对于最强单储层的统计显著改善，但消融实验（ablation）和错误集重叠分析（wrong-set overlap）提供了互补性分类错误（complementary classification errors）的暗示性证据。

Conclusion: 本文的结论是，高阶多项式矩读出（higher-order polynomial-moment readout）与储层异构性（reservoir heterogeneity）可作为有限时间朗之万计算的两个候选设计原则。尽管特征级融合尚未在统计显著性上超越最强单储层，但错误互补的实验证据表明，该方向具有进一步探索的价值。

Abstract: Nonlinear thermodynamic computers based on Langevin dynamics exploit thermal fluctuations as a physical substrate for computation. Recent work has shown that quartic-confined fluctuating degrees of freedom can act as thermodynamic neurons capable of nonlinear function approximation at finite observation times. Here we extend this paradigm from mean-only readout to moment-resolved readout. Instead of representing each driven reservoir solely by its first moment, we construct a response vector from the elementwise raw polynomial moments
  \(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}]\),
  \(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}^{\odot 2}]\), and
  \(\mathbb{E}[\bm{x}^{\odot 4}]\).
  These observables combine displacement and central-shape contributions and are naturally aligned with the linear, quadratic, and quartic terms of the local driven dynamics.
  We further introduce a heterogeneous multi-reservoir architecture in which three reservoirs with distinct initialization and training histories form a joint \(2304\)-dimensional response representation. Under the fixed MNIST \(60000/10000\) reproduction protocol, feature-level fusion achieves the best observed accuracy of \(9695/10000=96.95\%\), compared with \(9682/10000=96.82\%\) for the strongest single-reservoir model and \(9684/10000=96.84\%\) for equal-weight logit averaging. An exact paired McNemar test does not establish a statistically significant improvement over the strongest single reservoir, but the ablation and wrong-set overlap results provide suggestive evidence of complementary classification errors. These results motivate higher-order polynomial-moment readout and reservoir heterogeneity as candidate design principles for finite-time Langevin computing.

</details>


### [118] [The distribution of eccentricities in random regular graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14799)
*Dor Lev-Ari,Ofer Biham,Eytan Katzav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了由 N 个度数为 c 的节点构成的随机正则图（random regular graph, RRG）中离心率分布（distribution of eccentricities, DoE）的闭式解析表达式，给出了尾部概率分布的精确形式，并得到了平均离心率、众数和方差的解析结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离心率（eccentricity）在大规模稀疏网络的广播和全局信息传播等实际应用中至关重要，因为网络性能由最长延迟时间决定。此前缺乏关于随机正则图中离心率完整分布而非单一特征尺度（characteristic length scale）的解析刻画。

Method: 采用解析推导方法，基于随机正则图的结构特性，得到了离心率分布的尾部概率闭式表达式 $P(E > \ell) \simeq 1 - \exp \left[ - \exp \left( - \frac{ e^{b \ell} - \mu}{\beta} \right) \right]$，其中形状参数 $b = \ln (c-1)$、尺度参数 $\beta = \frac{c-2}{c} N$、位置参数 $\mu = \frac{c-2}{c} N \ln N$。进一步推导了平均离心率、众数和方差的解析形式。

Result: 平均离心率表达式为 $\langle E \rangle \simeq \frac{\ln N}{\ln (c-1)} + \frac{\ln \ln N}{\ln (c-1)} - \frac{\ln c - \ln (c-2)}{\ln (c-1)} + \frac{1}{2}$；众数满足 $E_{\rm mode} = {\rm Round} \left( \langle E \rangle \right)$，且随网络规模 N 呈阶梯状（staircase profile）；方差 ${\rm Var}(E)$ 随 N 呈现振荡（oscillations）行为。

Conclusion: 尽管所有节点度数相同，其离心率仍表现出非平凡（non-trivial）的变异性。所得解析结果可作为大规模稀疏网络中离心率计算的算法基准（benchmark），并对受最长延迟时间决定的网络应用具有参考价值。

Abstract: We derive a closed-form analytical expression for the distribution of eccentricities (DoE) in random regular graphs (RRGs) that consist of $N$ nodes of degree $c$. The DoE is given by the tail distribution $P(E > \ell) \simeq 1 - \exp \left[ - \exp \left( - \frac{ e^{b \ell} - μ}β \right) \right]$, where the distance $\ell$ takes integer values, $b = \ln (c-1)$ is the shape parameter, $β= \frac{c-2}{c} N$ is the scale parameter and $μ= \frac{c-2}{c} N \ln N$ is the location parameter. By providing the full distribution rather than a single characteristic length scale, we present a detailed view of the large-scale structure. In spite of the fact that the degrees of all the nodes are the same, their eccentricities exhibit non-trivial variations. We derive a closed-form expression for the mean eccentricity, which is given by $\langle E \rangle \simeq \frac{\ln N}{\ln (c-1)} +
\frac{\ln \ln N}{\ln (c-1)} - \frac{ \ln c - \ln (c-2) }{ \ln (c-1) } + \frac{1}{2}$. We calculate the mode of the DoE, which exhibits a staircase profile as a function of the network size. Interestingly, the mode is given by $E_{\rm mode} ={\rm Round} \left( \langle E \rangle \right)$, where ${\rm Round}( x )$ is the nearest integer to $x$. We also calculate the variance ${\rm Var}(E)$ and show that it exhibits oscillations as a function of the network size $N$. The results presented in this paper may serve as benchmarks for algorithmic approaches to eccentricity calculations in large sparse networks. The eccentricities are important in practical applications such as broadcasting and global dissemination, where the network performance is determined by the longest delay times.

</details>


### [119] [Learning the Fermion sign structure in path-integral Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15060)
*Jarvist Moore Frost*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从概率数值（probabilistic numerics）视角重新表述路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo）中的费米子符号问题（Fermion sign problem），将费米子可观测量（Fermionic observable）的算术计算转化为统计推断问题。通过按置换群共轭类（conjugacy class）分箱的费米子交换循环学习方案，结合贝叶斯先验（Bayesian priors）和LSTM神经网络残差建模，并引入主动重要采样（active important sampling），在均匀电子气和二维谐振势电子系统中实现了在符号问题严重区域对费米子能量的稳定推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统路径积分蒙特卡洛方法在处理费米子符号问题时，直接比率估计（direct ratio estimator）在符号问题严重区域失效。本文旨在克服这一局限，将费米子可观测量计算重新定义为统计推断问题，从而在符号问题严重的情况下仍能稳定提取能量。

Method: 首先，将费米子交换周期按置换群共轭类（称为“置换族（permutation family）”）分箱，对每个置换族的概率和能量分别用蒙特卡洛样本训练模型。其次，以DuBois等人的线性模型为基线，施加贝叶斯先验使其在渐近极限下满足Feynman的物理直觉模型；然后使用长短期记忆（Long Short-Term Memory, LSTM）神经网络仅学习残差多体关联（residual many-body correlations）。最后，设计由这些模型驱动的主动重要采样方法，引导蒙特卡洛链向欠采样置换区域采样以降低方差。

Result: 在自旋极化均匀电子气（spin-polarised uniform electron gas）和二维谐振约束势中电子这两个基准系统的小规模实验中，该方法在直接蒙特卡洛采样因符号问题而失败的参数区域中，成功提取了稳定的能量估计值。

Conclusion: 基于推断的框架能够有效克服路径积分蒙特卡洛中的费米子符号问题，在传统方法失效的恶劣条件下仍能输出稳健的能量估计，为处理非均匀和更复杂费米子系统提供了可推广的途径。

Abstract: Starting from a \emph{probabilistic numerics} approach to the Fermion sign problem in path integral Monte Carlo, we recast the arithmetic calculation of a Fermionic observable as a statistical inference problem. We develop approaches that learn the behaviour of Fermion exchange cycles binned by the conjugacy class of the permutation group (which we term `permutation family'). This extends the work of DuBois, Brown and Alder\cite{dubois2017overcoming} to inhomogeneous and more complex systems. Monte Carlo samples are used to train models for both the probability of a permutation family and the energy of this set of exchange permutations. The overall Fermionic energy is then directly inferred from these models, without using a direct ratio estimator on the Monte Carlo samples.
  By imposing physical understanding as inductive priors, we produce accurate and useful fits that remain robust even in regimes with severe sign problems. We generalise the linear (ideal-gas style) models of DuBois et al. with Bayesian priors that enforce the intuitive models of Feynman\cite{Feynman1953A} at their asymptotic limits. These linear models serve as the baseline for a Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) neural network, which is tasked with learning only the residual many-body \emph{correlations} on top of the physical model. We develop active important sampling methods driven by these models, which direct the Monte Carlo chains toward undersampled permutation regions, to efficiently reduce the variance in the observable.
  We apply this framework to small experiments on benchmark systems: the spin-polarised uniform electron gas, and electrons in a 2D harmonic confining potential. In both cases we demonstrate that this inference-based framework can extract stable energies in regimes where direct Monte Carlo sampling fails due to the sign problem.

</details>


### [120] [Thermodynamic theory of voting and EU elections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15119)
*Klaus M. Frahm,Dima L. Shepelyansky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种投票的热力学理论（thermodynamic theory of voting），通过耦合非线性振子的系统能量与政党得票分数之间的类比，揭示了投票分布符合瑞利-金斯（Rayleigh-Jeans, RJ）热化与凝聚过程。该理论能够较好地描述欧盟选举中的政党投票分布、选民投票的洛伦兹曲线与帕累托曲线，并恢复法国总统选举首轮候选人之间的得票离散度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为投票行为提供一种基于统计力学（statistical mechanics）的理论框架，将投票分布理解为约束驱动凝聚现象，从而揭示选举结果中宏观统计规律的物理起源。

Method: 通过类比耦合非线性振子的系统能量与政党得票分数，引入能量守恒与概率范数守恒，推导出瑞利-金斯（Rayleigh-Jeans）热化与凝聚机制，并利用该理论拟合欧盟选举数据的洛伦兹曲线和帕累托曲线。

Result: 该理论很好地描述了欧盟选举中政党得票的分布，准确刻画了选票分布的洛伦兹曲线与帕累托曲线；同时，该理论也能恢复法国总统第一轮选举中候选人之间得票的离散度（dispersion of votes）。

Conclusion: 投票分布可以用统计力学中的约束驱动凝聚现象来解释，瑞利-金斯热化理论为选举结果的宏观统计特征提供了有效的理论描述，并且该框架与描述社会财富不平等的理论具有相似性。

Abstract: We introduce a thermodynamic theory of voting and show that it provides a good description of distribution of party votes in EU elections. The theory traces parallels between system energies of coupled nonlinear oscillators and party vote fractions. Such a classical system evolution is characterized by the conservation of total energy and probability norm that leads to the Rayleigh-Jeans (RJ) thermalization and condensation at low energy states. A similar thermalization also describes the wealth inequality in society. This feature belongs to the phenomena of constraint driven condensation known in statistical mechanics. We show that the RJ theory well depicts the Lorenz and Pareto curves obtained from the EU vote results. The theory also recovers the dispersion of votes between candidates of first round presidential elections in France.

### [121] [Confined acoustic phonon mode filtering in free-standing nanocrystalline silicon membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14417)
*Tiago E. C. Magalhães,Tânia M. Ribeiro,Oili Ylivaara,Jouni Ahopelto,Clivia M. Sotomayor Torres*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 通过飞秒时间分辨测量，本文实验证实多晶硅（nanocrystalline silicon）薄膜中存在由晶界（grain boundaries）导致的相干声学声子（coherent acoustic phonons）高阶模式强烈抑制效应，其散射率呈频率平方（f²）依赖关系，晶界对高频声子起到有效频谱滤波作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示纳米晶硅薄膜中晶界对相干声学声子（coherent acoustic phonons）传播与衰减行为的影响机制，以理解微结构（microstructure）依赖的声子散射过程。

Method: 采用飞秒时间分辨测量（femtosecond time-resolved measurements）技术，研究自由支撑纳米晶硅薄膜（free-standing nanocrystalline silicon membranes）中的受限声学声子，并与单晶硅（crystalline silicon）样品进行直接对比；同时通过热退火（thermal annealing）控制晶粒尺寸分布（grain size distribution）。

Result: 多晶样品中高阶声子模被强烈抑制，抑制程度具有强频率依赖性（frequency dependent），且随声子波长（phonon wavelength）接近特征晶粒尺寸而加剧；分离出由晶界导致的额外衰减通道，其散射率（scattering rate）呈近似 f² 的幂律依赖（power-law dependence）；测得声速与以往报道一致，反映了多晶取向引起的有效弹性响应（effective elastic response）。

Conclusion: 相干声学声子可作为探测纳米晶材料中微结构依赖散射的灵敏探针（sensitive probe），晶界对高频声学声子起到有效频谱滤波（spectral filter）作用。

Abstract: We report the femtosecond time-resolved measurements of confined acoustic phonons in free-standing nanocrystalline silicon membranes and compare them directly with the crystalline silicon counterpart. While the latter exhibit well-resolved higher-order modes, a strong suppression of these modes is observed in nanocrystalline samples with grain size distribution controlled by thermal annealing. The suppression is strongly frequency dependent and becomes more pronounced as the phonon wavelength approaches the characteristic grain size. By separating intrinsic and extrinsic contributions to the phonon lifetime, we identify an additional frequency-dependent decay channel associated with grain boundaries, with scattering rates following a power-law dependence close to $f^{2}$, where $f$ is the frequency. The measured sound velocity is consistent with previous reports for nanocrystalline silicon and indicates an effective elastic response arising from multiple crystallographic orientations. These results establish coherent phonons as a sensitive probe of microstructure-dependent scattering in nanocrystalline materials and indicate that grain boundaries act as an effective spectral filter for high-frequency acoustic phonons.

### [122] [Multiple Clausen values and deformed Apéry-like series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14646)
*Zhi-Wei Sun,Yajun Zhou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索广义中心二项式系数所定义的变形Apéry型级数的闭式表示，并建立其与分圆多重zeta值（cyclotomic multiple zeta values, CMZVs）之间的联系。

Method: 通过欧拉伽马函数（Euler's gamma function）将中心二项式系数推广至一般实数指标，构造变形Apéry型级数$\mathscr A_{s,n}$；利用多重Clausen值（multiple Clausen values, MCVs）——第三级分圆多重zeta值的子类——的代数关系进行表示与化简。

Result: 给出了两个具体级数的封闭表达式：$\mathscr A_{1,5}$由三个加权$L(χ_{-3},s)$函数线性组合表示；$\mathscr A_{4,4}$表示为双重zeta和$ζ_{5,3}$与有理倍数$π^8$之和。

Conclusion: 变形Apéry型级数可纳入多重Clausen值（MCVs）的代数框架内表示，这揭示了Apéry级数与分圆多重zeta值之间的深层结构关系。

Abstract: With generalized central binomial coefficients $ \binom{2x}{x}:=\frac{Γ(2x+1)}{[Γ(x+1)]^2}$ defined through Euler's gamma function, we represent deformed Apéry-like series \[ \mathscr A_{s,n}:=\sum_{k=1}^\infty\left.\!\frac{\partial^n}{\partial x^n}\frac{1}{x^s\binom{2x}{x}}\right|_{x=k} \] by multiple Clausen values (MCVs), which belong to a special class of cyclotomic multiple zeta values (CMZVs) at level $3$. For example, exploiting provable algebraic relations among MCVs, we show that \[\mathscr A_{1,5}=-\frac{9[495L(χ_{-3},6)-30π^{2}L(χ_{-3},4)-2π^{4}L(χ_{-3},2)]}{4}\]and\[\mathscr A_{4,4}=\frac{352ζ_{5,3}}{15}+\frac{752537π^{8}}{10206000},\]where $ L(χ_{-3},s):=\sum_{n=0}^\infty\left[(3n+1)^{-s}-(3n+2)^{-s}\right]$ and $ ζ_{5,3}:=\sum_{m=1}^\infty\sum_{n=1}^{m-1}m^{-5}n^{-3}$.

### [123] [Full-data accuracy with fewer labels for training and fine-tuning machine-learning force fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14486)
*Sheng Bi,Yi-Ze Wang,Jun Cheng*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于最后一层投影回归（last-layer-projection regression, LLPR）的主动学习工作流，用于高效构建机器学习力场（machine-learning force fields, MLFFs）的训练集。LLPR作为一种计算成本低廉的不确定性估计器，能够从小部分电子结构标签中挑选出紧凑高价值的训练集，在从头训练和基础模型微调（foundation fine-tuning）场景下均显著降低标签需求，并在迭代微调中实现自动终止，为MLFF训练提供可扩展的不确定性量化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习力场（MLFFs）仅在训练分布附近可靠，高效构建多样化的训练集成为从头训练（train-from-scratch）和基础模型微调（foundation fine-tuning）的主要瓶颈。标准模型委员会（model-committee）不确定性方法因每个委员会成员需要单独微调，在实际应用中不可行。

Method: 提出一种基于最后一层投影回归（LLPR）的主动学习工作流。LLPR是一种前向传播计算廉价的不确定性估计器（forward-pass-cheap per-configuration uncertainty estimator），通过最后一层的投影回归来估计每个构型的不确定性。

Result: 在分子、凝聚相和电解质系统中，LLPR挑选的紧凑高价值训练集仅用少量电子结构标签就能恢复全数据精度。在基础模型微调中，LLPR选择的构型用远少于随机选择的标签达到全池微调（full-pool fine-tuning）的性能上限。在迭代电解质微调中，LLPR能在密度泛函理论（DFT）标注前检测非物理的局域配位，提供绝对力误差阈值，并实现学习循环的自动终止。

Conclusion: LLPR生成的模型能够复现参考密度和离子配位结构，为各种MLFF训练模式提供了一种可扩展的不确定性量化（uncertainty-quantification）策略。

Abstract: Machine-learning force fields (MLFFs) are reliable only near their training distribution, making efficient construction of diverse training sets a major bottleneck for both train-from-scratch and foundation fine-tuning workflows. Active learning can reduce this cost, but standard model-committee uncertainty is impractical for foundation MLFFs because each committee member requires a separate fine-tuning run. We present an active-learning workflow based on last-layer-projection regression (LLPR), a forward-pass-cheap per-configuration uncertainty estimator. Across molecular, condensed-phase, and electrolyte systems, LLPR identifies compact, high-value training sets that recover full-data accuracy using only a small fraction of electronic-structure labels. In foundation-model fine-tuning, LLPR-selected configurations reach the full-pool fine-tuning ceiling with substantially fewer labels than random selection. In iterative electrolyte fine-tuning, LLPR detects unphysical local coordination before DFT labelling, provides an absolute force-error threshold, and enables automatic termination of the learning loop. The resulting models reproduce reference density and ion-coordination structure, providing a scalable uncertainty-quantification strategy across MLFF training regimes.

### [124] [Interaction energies of H$_2$ and CO on transition-metal surfaces computed by a range-separated hybrid van der Waals density functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15066)
*Per Hyldgaard*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文测试了一类范围分离杂化范德瓦尔斯密度泛函（RSH vdW-DFs）在描述H₂在Cu(111)表面解离化学吸附（DC）问题中的经典势垒能力，并提出了一种基于准粒子（QP）焦点的最佳非经验泛函版本AHBR(γ*)，实现了接近化学精度的势垒高度预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: H₂在Cu(111)表面的解离化学吸附（dissociative chemisorption, DC）是多相催化（heterogeneous catalysis）中的原型问题，其挑战在于对反映原子变形经典势、摩擦和非弹性散射的反应动力学进行建模。本文旨在测试一类新发展的范围分离杂化范德瓦尔斯密度泛函（range-separated hybrid van der Waals density functionals, RSH vdW-DFs）在该问题上的表现。

Method: 首先测试RSH vdW-DFs描述H₂+Cu(111) DC经典势垒的能力；其次，利用一种变体对分子准粒子（quasi-particles, QPs）进行快速准确预测，并在多个催化相关的小分子上验证其性能；最后，基于QP焦点提出并实现一种方法，以确定最佳的非经验（但吸附质特异性）RSH vdW-DF版本，命名为AHBR(γ*)。

Result: AHBR(γ*)泛函能够以接近化学精度（chemical accuracy）确定H₂+Cu(111) DC的经典势垒高度（classical barrier height）。此外，所采用的QP变体在一组催化研究中常见的小分子上表现出优异的预测性能。

Conclusion: DC建模可以作为检验这些RSH vdW-DFs背后物理机制更广泛适用性的测试平台。

Abstract: Dissociative chemisorption (DC) of H$_2$ on the Cu(111) surface is a prototypical problem for understanding elements of heterogeneous catalysis [Science 326, 832 (2009)]. The challenge lies in modeling the reaction dynamics that in turn reflects a classical potential for atomic deformations, friction, and inelastic scattering. Here, I test the use of a set of range-separated hybrid (RSH) van der Waals density functionals (vdW-DFs) [JPCM 37, 211501 (2025)] on their ability to describe the classical barrier for dynamics in this H$_2$+Cu(111) DC problem. I furthermore document use of a variant for fast accurate predictions of the molecular quasi-particles (QPs), finding excellent performance across a set of small molecules that are often studied in catalysis. Finally, I suggest and implement a way to use that QP focus to identify what I consider a best-possible non-empirical (yet adsorbate specific) RSH vdW-DF version, denoted AHBR($γ^*$) for H$_2$ DC modeling, navigating what are partly conflicting requirements on the molecule and metal sides. I find that the AHBR($γ^*$) can determine the classical H$_2$+Cu(111) DC barrier height close to chemical accuracy. I suggest that DC modeling can test broader relevance of the physics underpinning these RSH vdW-DFs.

</details>

### [125] [Interlayer sliding direction as a symmetry selector in altermagnetic bilayer Fe2WS4: Switchable anomalous Hall and anomalous valley Hall effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14459)
*Quan Shen,Jianing Tan,Tao Yao,Wenhu Liao,Jiansheng Dong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，发现在交变磁双层Fe₂WS₄中，层间滑移方向可作为对称性选择性控制参数，实现对铁电性、自旋纹理、谷极化及霍尔输运响应的非易失性调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）结合了共线补偿磁序与动量依赖的自旋分裂，为耦合自旋与谷自由度以及铁电性和贝里曲率驱动输运提供了平台，但实现这些纠缠自由度的非易失性与选择性控制仍是一个关键挑战。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究双层交变磁体Fe₂WS₄中不同方向层间滑移对对称性、电子结构与输运性质的影响。

Result: 对角滑移打破反演对称性，产生两种具有相反面外极化的滑移铁电态，铁电极化反转可切换动量依赖的自旋纹理并反转反常霍尔电导率，实现铁电可开关的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）；轴向滑移保持反演对称性但打破联系X与Y谷的晶体对称性，产生可逆谷极化与可开关的反常谷霍尔效应（anomalous valley Hall effect）。

Conclusion: 层间滑移方向可作为非易失性对称性选择器，用于控制二维交变磁双层中的铁电性、自旋纹理、谷极化及霍尔输运响应。

Abstract: Altermagnets combine compensated collinear magnetic order with momentum-dependent spin splitting, offering a promising platform for coupling spin and valley degrees of freedom with ferroelectricity and Berry-curvature driven transport in the absence of net magnetization. However, achieving nonvolatile and selective control of these intertwined degrees of freedom remains a key challenge. Here, using first-principles calculations, we show that the direction of interlayer sliding serves as a symmetry selective control parameter in altermagnetic bilayer Fe2WS4. Diagonal sliding breaks inversion symmetry and produces two sliding ferroelectric states with opposite out-of-plane polarizations. Reversal of the ferroelectric polarization switches the momentum-dependent spin texture and reverses the anomalous Hall conductivity, revealing strong magnetoelectric coupling and enabling a ferroelectrically switchable anomalous Hall effect. In contrast, axial sliding preserves inversion symmetry but breaks the crystalline symmetry relating the X and Y valleys, leading to reversible valley polarization and a switchable anomalous valley Hall effect. These results establish the direction of interlayer sliding as a nonvolatile symmetry selector for controlling ferroelectricity, spin texture, valley polarization, and Hall transport responses in two-dimensional altermagnetic bilayers.

</details>


### [126] [Multistate ferroelectricity and switchable layer-locked anomalous valley Hall effects in bilayer ReIrGe2Se6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14461)
*Tao Yao,Quan Shen,Jianing Tan,Jiansheng Dong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，在AA堆叠的ReIrGe2Se6双层材料中预测了多态铁电性，这种多态性与层自由度及贝里曲率（Berry curvature）紧密耦合，实现了反常谷霍尔效应（anomalous valley Hall effect）与层锁定反常谷霍尔效应之间的非易失性切换，为可编程拓扑输运和多功能谷电子学器件提供了微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维多铁材料兼具磁性与铁电（ferroelectric）有序以及强磁电耦合，是高密度信息存储和低功耗多态电子器件的理想平台。然而，传统铁电性的固有双稳态（bistability）限制了在单一材料中实现多个非易失态和可编程贝里曲率驱动输运响应的能力。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对AA堆叠（AA0-stacked）的ReIrGe2Se6双层体系进行电子结构、铁电极化构型及其切换路径的理论模拟。

Result: 该体系具有四种能量稳定的铁电（FE）极化构型，其中三种通过可逆切换路径相连，第四种呈现单向切换路径。不同FE构型导致电子结构出现循环式半导体-金属-半导体演化。铁电极化切换与层自由度和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）深度耦合：FE构型决定的层相关静电势控制能带边缘态的层特征，从而将贝里曲率锁定在特定层通道中。该体系可在反常谷霍尔效应（anomalous valley Hall effect）与层锁定反常谷霍尔效应之间切换，实现层、谷和自旋分辨输运响应的非易失性控制。此外，磁化反转可在保持层分辨特征的同时切换谷和自旋通道。

Conclusion: 双层ReIrGe2Se6被确立为一种多态铁电平台，可实现可编程的贝里曲率相关输运，为基于拓扑的多功能电子学和谷电子学（valleytronics）器件提供了微观层面的理解。

Abstract: Two-dimensional multiferroic materials, which combine magnetic and ferroelectric (FE) orders with strong magnetoelectric coupling, represent ideal platforms for high-density information storage and low-power multistate electronics. However, the intrinsic bistability of conventional ferroelectricity poses a substantial challenge to realizing multiple nonvolatile states and programmable Berry-curvature driven transport responses within a single material. Here, using first-principles calculations, we predict multistate ferroelectricity in AA0-stacked bilayer ReIrGe2Se6. The system hosts four energetically stable FE polarization configurations, among which three are connected through reversible switching pathways, while the fourth exhibits a unidirectional switching pathway. The distinct FE configurations further give rise to a cyclic semiconductor-metal-semiconductor evolution in the electronic structure. Notably, FE polarization switching is intimately coupled to layer degrees of freedom and Berry curvature. The layer-dependent electrostatic potential associated with different FE configurations controls the layer character of the band-edge states, thereby locking the Berry curvature to specific layer channels. As a result, bilayer ReIrGe2Se6 enables switching between an anomalous valley Hall effect and a layer-locked anomalous valley Hall effect, providing nonvolatile control of layer, valley, and spin-resolved transport responses. In addition, magnetization reversal switches the valley and spin channels while preserving the layer-resolved character. These results establish bilayer ReIrGe2Se6 as a multistate ferroelectric platform for programmable Berry-curvature related transport, offering microscopic insight into topology based multifunctional electronic and valleytronic devices.

</details>


### [127] [Fractional quantum ferroelectric control of spin-valley locking and valley Hall effects in altermagnetic monolayer Cr2S2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14465)
*Tao Yao,Quan Shen,Jiansheng Dong,Jianing Tan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文通过第一性原理计算，证明单层Cr2S2可实现分数量子多铁材料（fractional quantum multiferroics），通过分数量子铁电性（FQFE）与交变磁性（AM）的耦合，实现极化可切换的自旋-谷锁定（spin-valley locking）和谷霍尔效应（valley Hall effect），为非易失性电控谷电子器件提供了新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子多铁材料中FQFE与AM的耦合为动量依赖自旋分裂的非易失性控制提供了前景，但该耦合在谷自由度（valley degrees of freedom）和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）驱动的谷霍尔效应方面的研究尚属空白，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）方法，对单层Cr2S2的电子结构和拓扑性质进行模拟分析。

Result: 单层Cr2S2实现了二维FQFE-AM平台，具有两个可通过复合对称操作（结合分数晶格平移与时间反演或宇称-时间反演）切换的FQFE态；FQFE切换可逆转AM自旋极化能带结构，在不旋转奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的情况下互换X和Y谷的自旋特性，实现极化可切换的自旋-谷锁定；两种FQFE态具有相反的贝里曲率分布，结合切换后的自旋-谷锁定，在电子和空穴掺杂下均可实现极化控制的谷霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于对称性的机制，用于非易失性电控AM自旋分裂、自旋-谷锁定和谷霍尔效应，为基于FQFE-AM耦合的低功耗谷电子器件（valleytronic devices）提供了通用路线。

Abstract: Fractional quantum multiferroics, arising from the coupling between fractional quantum ferroelectricity (FQFE) and altermagnetism (AM), provide a promising platform for nonvolatile control of momentum dependent spin splitting in systems with zero net magnetization. However, extending this FQFE-AM coupling to valley degrees of freedom and Berry curvature driven valley Hall effects remains largely unexplored. Here, using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that monolayer Cr2S2 realizes a two dimensional FQFE-AM platform with two switchable FQFE states connected by composite symmetry operations combining a fractional lattice translation with time reversal or parity-time reversal. We show that FQFE switching reverses the AM spin-polarized band structure and interchanges the spin characters of the X and Y valleys without rotating the Néel vector, thereby enabling polarization switchable spin-valley locking. Moreover, the two FQFE states exhibit reversed Berry curvature distributions, which, together with the switched spin-valley locking, enable polarization controlled valley Hall effects under both electron and hole doping. These results demonstrate a symmetry based mechanism for nonvolatile electrical control of AM spin splitting, spin-valley locking, and valley Hall effects, offering a general route toward low-power valleytronic devices based on FQFE-AM coupling.

</details>


### [128] [Second-Order Optical Nonlinearity of AlScN Films Grown By Molecular Beam Epitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14590)
*Joongwon Lee,Thai-Son Nguyen,Len van Deurzen,Debaditya Bhattacharya,Chandrashekhar Savant,Siddhartha Ghosh,Patrick Shea,Carl Bernard,Huili Grace Xing,Debdeep Jena,Farhan Rana*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）直接在氮化c面蓝宝石衬底上生长AlScN薄膜，测量其二阶光学非线性（second-order optical nonlinearity），发现d31可高达4.92 pm/V，比AlN大60倍，而d33被抑制。该材料有望用于与Si、GaN和AlN集成的节能非线性光学器件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AlN合金作为非线性光学材料平台已迅速发展，但以往研究常受厚AlN缓冲层干扰，难以准确测量AlScN薄膜的本征非线性响应。本文旨在通过直接生长方法分离并测量AlScN的真实二阶光学非线性。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）在氮化c面蓝宝石（c-plane sapphire）上直接生长AlScN薄膜，省去厚AlN缓冲层，以隔离薄膜自身的非线性光学响应。

Result: 与AlN相比，AlScN薄膜的d31显著增强，而d33被抑制。d31最高可达4.92 pm/V，是AlN的60倍。

Conclusion: AlScN基光子器件能够实现节能的非线性光学操作，并可通过外延生长方式与基于Si、GaN和AlN的电子及光子器件集成。

Abstract: Alloys of AlN have rapidly emerged as a material platform for nonlinear optics. In this paper, we measure the second-order optical nonlinearity of AlScN films grown directly on nitrided c-plane sapphire by molecular beam epitaxy. This direct growth approach, which bypasses a thick AlN buffer layer, allows us to isolate the true nonlinear response of the AlScN film. Our results show a large enhancement of d31, but a suppression of d33 in AlScN films compared to AlN. We observe that d31 can be as high as 4.92 pm/V , which is 60 times larger than that of AlN. The development of AlScN-based photonic devices can enable energy-efficient nonlinear optical operations that can be epitaxially integrated with electronic and photonic devices based on Si, GaN and AlN.

</details>


### [129] [Direct observation of anisotropic exciton dispersion in the 2D semiconductor CrSBr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14712)
*Yiwen Song,Peiyi He,Weizhe Zhang,Wenyuan Ouyang,Wenjing Liu,Jinlong Du,Zuxin Chen,Jiuyu Sun,Peng Gao,Yu Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过去焦电子能量损失谱（defocus-engineered electron energy-loss spectroscopy）和第一性原理计算，在多层 CrSBr 中测量了激子（exciton）的动量分辨色散，发现显著的面内各向异性：沿 ΓY 方向在 |q| < 0.007 Å⁻¹ 范围内呈现线性色散（斜率 7.02 eV Å），而沿 ΓX 方向几乎无色散。这种各向异性归因于长程电子-空穴交换相互作用，受过渡偶极矩（transition dipole moment）方向选择规则的调控。跨磁相变（顺磁到 A 型反铁磁）的对比测量表明激子传播与磁序之间的耦合可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究低对称性层状半导体 CrSBr 中激子的动量分辨色散及其各向异性起源，并考察激子传播与磁序之间的耦合关系。

Method: 采用去焦工程电子能量损失谱（defocus-engineered electron energy-loss spectroscopy）进行动量分辨测量，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）进行理论验证。

Result: 观测到显著的面内各向异性：沿 ΓY 方向在 |q| < 0.007 Å⁻¹ 范围内激子呈现线性色散，斜率高达 7.02 eV Å，属于低维系统中报道的最大值之一；沿 ΓX 方向几乎无色散。计算结果表明该线性色散为内禀性质。跨顺磁—A 型反铁磁相变的测量显示色散基本不变。

Conclusion: 该各向异性色散由长程电子-空穴交换相互作用（long-range electron–hole exchange interaction）主导，该相互作用受强面外约束增强，并由过渡偶极矩（transition dipole moment）的方向选择规则调控。激子传播与磁序耦合可忽略，表明 CrSBr 可作为研究低对称性层状半导体中各向异性激子动力学的模型体系。

Abstract: We report momentum-resolved measurements of exciton dispersion in multilayer CrSBr using defocus-engineered electron energy-loss spectroscopy, supported by first-principles calculations. A pronounced in-plane anisotropy is observed, with the exciton exhibiting a linear dispersion along $Γ$Y within $\lvert \boldsymbol{q} \rvert$ < 0.007 Å$^{-1}$, while remaining nearly dispersionless along $Γ$X. The slope reaches 7.02 eV Å, among the largest reported in low-dimensional systems. The calculations reproduce the experimentally observed linear dispersion, confirming its intrinsic origin. We attribute the anisotropic dispersion to the long-range electron--hole exchange interaction, enhanced by strong out-of-plane confinement and governed by the directional selection rules of the transition dipole moment. Comparative measurements across the magnetic phase transition from the paramagnetic to the A-type antiferromagnetic state show that the dispersion remains essentially unchanged, indicating negligible coupling between exciton propagation and magnetic order. These results establish CrSBr as a model system for investigating anisotropic exciton dynamics in low-symmetry layered semiconductors.

</details>


### [130] [Tunable Magneto-Excitonic Coupling in Alloyed van der Waals Antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14723)
*Maciej Smiertka,Oliwia Janikowska,Katarzyna Olkowska-Pucko,Grzegorz Krasucki,Katarzyna Posmyk,Paulina Peksa,Alessandro Surrente,Dimitar Pashov,Kseniia Mosina,Zdenek Sofer,Mark van Schilfgaarde,Adam Babinski,Maciej R. Molas,Gabriela Komorowska,Esteban Zamora-Amo,Andres Castellanos-Gomez,Federico Mompean,Mar Garcia-Hernandez,Michal Baranowski,Swagata Acharya,Paulina Plochocka*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过磁光光谱和第一性原理计算，揭示了氯元素掺入如何同时调控CrSBr反铁磁半导体的电子结构、激子（exciton）特性和磁相互作用，使两种激子态向Frenkel-like局域化转变，并系统降低了磁场诱导的能量重整化（renormalization），从而将激子类型与磁-激子耦合直接联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状磁性半导体中磁序与光生激子（photo-generated excitons）之间的独特耦合为控制光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions）提供了有力机制，而CrSBr中的这种耦合尤为强烈且在两种共存激子态中表现迥异。本研究旨在通过元素掺入（compositional alloying）来主动调控这种磁-光相互作用（magneto-optical interplay）。

Method: 结合高达85 T的磁光光谱学（magneto-optical spectroscopy）与基于准粒子自洽GW（quasiparticle self-consistent GW, QSGW）方法在合金超胞（alloy supercells）上的最新计算。

Result: 氯掺入使激子波函数（excitonic wavefunctions）逐渐局域化（localises），驱动两种激子态向更类似Frenkel激子的行为转变；同时伴随磁场诱导的能量重整化（magnetic-field-induced energy renormalisation）的系统性降低，其中扩展性更强的XB激子变化最为显著。

Conclusion: 该工作直接将激子类型（exciton character）与磁-激子耦合（magneto-excitonic coupling）联系起来，并确立了组分合金化（compositional alloying）作为在范德华磁性半导体（van der Waals magnetic semiconductors）中工程化磁性与光学性质耦合的有效策略。

Abstract: The unique coupling between magnetic order and photo-generated excitons, electron-hole pairs bound by Coulomb interaction, in layered magnetic semiconductors offers a powerful mechanism for controlling light-matter interactions. In the van der Waals antiferromagnet CrSBr, this coupling is exceptionally strong and manifests distinctly between two coexisting excitonic states: the localised, Frenkel-like XA exciton and the more delocalised, Wannier-Mott-like XB exciton, providing a unique playground for the optical control of magnetism. Here, we reveal how chlorine incorporation reshapes the magneto-optical interplay in CrSBr1-xClx by simultaneously modifying its electronic structure, excitonic properties, and magnetic interactions. Combining magneto-optical spectroscopy up to 85 T with state-of-the-art quasiparticle self-consistent GW (QSGW) calculations on alloy supercells, we show that Cl insertion progressively localises the excitonic wavefunctions and drives both states toward a more Frenkel-like regime. This evolution is accompanied by a systematic reduction of the magnetic-field-induced energy renormalisation, most prominently for the XB exciton. Our work connects exciton character directly to magneto-excitonic coupling. Furthermore, it establishes compositional alloying as an effective strategy for engineering the coupling between magnetic and optical properties in van der Waals magnetic semiconductors.

</details>


### [131] [Boson peak and medium-range elastic heterogeneity in calcium silicate hydrate probed by terahertz spectroscopy and low-temperature calorimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14764)
*Xiangyu Li,Ying Chen,Jipeng Luo,Ya Chen,Linhao Wang,Lidan Tian,Gan Ding,Zeyu Lu,Zhangli Hu,Biqin Dong,Yue Li,Zongjin Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过太赫兹时域光谱（THz-TDS）和低温量热法两种振动动力学探测手段，首次系统表征了水泥水化硅酸钙（C-S-H）中玻色峰（boson peak）随钙硅比（Ca/Si=0.5–1.7）的变化规律，发现两种方法在峰频位置（~1 THz）上吻合但在强度上存在解耦，并从中提取出中程动力学关联长度（~1 nm）和弹性非均匀性参数γ（0.98→0.48），将纳米尺度振动动力学与混凝土宏观耐久性联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻色峰（boson peak, BP）作为无序固体中普遍的振动反常现象，已在理论上被预测存在于水化硅酸钙（calcium silicate hydrate, C-S-H）中，但尚未被系统表征。C-S-H是硬化水泥的结合相，理解其振动动力学对揭示混凝土宏观性能至关重要。

Method: 采用太赫兹时域光谱（terahertz time-domain spectroscopy, THz-TDS）和低温量热法（low-temperature calorimetry）两种互补的振动动力学探测手段，覆盖五种钙硅比（Ca/Si = 0.5–1.7），并对晶体杂质进行了布鲁格曼校正（Bruggeman correction）。

Result: 两种探测手段将玻色峰定位在~1 THz附近，峰频一致但强度存在分叉。太赫兹积分谱权重和量热Cp/T³峰谷随Ca/Si单调下降，而表观太赫兹峰高在Ca/Si=1.0处最大。中程动力学关联长度为0.3–2 nm（量级~1 nm），弹性非均匀性参数γ从0.98降至0.48，德拜归一化玻色峰频率ν_BP/ν_D = 0.15–0.17与硅酸盐玻璃相当。

Conclusion: γ作为组成分辨的定量描述符，可关联C-S-H的固有蠕变（creep）和热输运（thermal transport）行为，将纳米尺度振动动力学与混凝土宏观耐久性（durability）联系起来。该双探针玻色峰分析方法可推广至其他非晶固体，包括低碳水泥的辅助胶凝材料（supplementary cementitious materials）。

Abstract: The boson peak (BP), a universal vibrational anomaly of disordered solids, has been predicted but not systematically characterized in calcium silicate hydrate (C-S-H), the binding phase of hardened cement. Building on a preliminary terahertz survey, we characterize the BP across five Ca/Si ratios (0.5-1.7) using terahertz time-domain spectroscopy (THz-TDS) and low-temperature calorimetry, two probes of vibrational dynamics that complement the static picture of conventional structural methods. After Bruggeman correction for crystalline impurities, both probes locate the BP near 1 THz; they agree on frequency but diverge in intensity. The terahertz integrated spectral weight and the calorimetric Cp/T3 peak both fall monotonically with Ca/Si, whereas the apparent terahertz peak height is maximal at Ca/Si = 1.0, where damping is low and oscillator strength still substantial. This decoupling marks a structural crossover between silicate-chain depolymerization and interlayer calcium filling. From the BP we obtain a medium-range dynamical correlation length of order 1 nm (0.3-2 nm) and a coherent-potential elastic-heterogeneity parameter that decreases from gamma = 0.98 to 0.48 as Ca/Si rises; the Debye-normalized BP frequency (nu_BP/nu_D = 0.15-0.17) places C-S-H within the range reported for silicate glasses. Because gamma governs the distribution of energy barriers for local structural rearrangements, it provides a quantitative, composition-resolved descriptor relevant to the intrinsic creep and thermal transport of C-S-H, linking nanoscale vibrational dynamics to the macroscopic durability of concrete. The dual-probe boson-peak approach is transferable to other amorphous solids, including the supplementary cementitious materials of low-carbon cements.

</details>


### [132] [Computing binary alloy phase diagrams with explicit configurational and vibrational entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14795)
*Sarath Menon,Marvin Poul,Tilmann Hickel,Jörg Neugebauer,Ralf Drautz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过非平衡热力学积分与非理想构型熵的显式采样，结合原子团簇展开势（Atomic Cluster Expansion potentials）和密度泛函理论（DFT）数据，构建了Au-Cu二元合金的组分-温度相图，发现非理想构型熵的采样显著降低了有序-无序转变温度，使其更接近实验值，同时强调交换关联泛函的选择对预测准确性具有更大影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分固溶体中的相稳定性依赖于超越理想混合极限的构型熵（configurational entropy），但如何在同一原子框架内同时捕捉构型熵与振动熵（vibrational entropy）仍具挑战性。

Method: 将非平衡热力学积分（non-equilibrium thermodynamic integration）扩展至组分依赖的转变，通过对相互作用的炼金插值（alchemical interpolation），结合蒙特卡洛身份交换移动（Monte Carlo identity exchange moves）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics），沿积分路径对振动熵与非理想构型熵进行采样。采用基于LDA、PBE和r2SCAN泛函的DFT数据训练的原子团簇展开势（Atomic Cluster Expansion potentials），从原子自由能直接构建Au-Cu二元合金的组分-温度相图。

Result: 显式构型采样将基于LDA数据的ACE势预测的AuCu有序-无序转变温度从约810 K降至约710 K，更接近实验值683 K，并显著拓宽了固溶体的稳定范围。同时，对交换关联泛函（exchange-correlation functional）的敏感性远大于此，表明该一致性不应被解释为普遍的预测准确性。

Conclusion: 为获得二元相图的可靠原子描述，必须对非理想构型熵进行显式采样，并审慎选择交换关联泛函。

Abstract: Phase stability in multicomponent solid solutions depends on configurational entropy beyond the ideal mixing limit, but capturing it together with vibrational entropy within the same atomistic framework remains challenging. Here, we extend non-equilibrium thermodynamic integration to composition-dependent transformations through an alchemical interpolation of the interactions, combined with Monte Carlo identity exchange moves and molecular dynamics that sample the vibrational and non-ideal configurational entropy along the integration path. We apply the framework to the Au-Cu binary alloy using Atomic Cluster Expansion potentials trained on density functional theory data using the LDA, PBE, and r2SCAN functionals, and construct composition-temperature phase diagrams directly from atomistic free energies. We find that explicit configurational sampling lowers the AuCu order-disorder transition temperature predicted by the ACE potential trained on LDA data from approximately 810 K to 710 K, closer to the experimental value of 683 K, and substantially widens the stability range of the solid solution. At the same time, the much larger sensitivity to the exchange-correlation functional shows that this level of agreement should not be interpreted as general predictive accuracy. Non-ideal configurational entropy must therefore be sampled explicitly, alongside a careful choice of functional, for a reliable atomistic description of binary phase diagrams.

### [133] [SevenNet-Polar for MultiTask Prediction of Energy, Forces, Stress, and Born Effective Charges: Development and Application to ZrO$_2$, Li$_3$PO$_4$, and Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14827)
*Anh Khoa Augustin Lu,Shungo Arai,Yutack Park,Seungwu Han,Tsuyoshi Miyazaki,Satoshi Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了SevenNet-Polar，一个基于等变图神经网络（equivariant graph neural network）的框架，用于快速准确地预测玻恩有效电荷（Born effective charge, BEC）张量。该模型在高温、含缺陷的训练数据下仍能达到极低误差，并支持多任务学习（同时预测能量、力、应力和BEC），在多GPU超算上可处理多达150万原子的模拟，使电场下的电荷感知分子动力学模拟更加可行。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻恩有效电荷（Born effective charge, BEC）张量的精确预测对建模电场下的材料至关重要，但传统计算方法计算成本高昂。现有方法难以兼顾精度与效率，因此需要一种快速、高精度的BEC预测框架来桥接这一差距。

Method: 基于SevenNet架构构建等变图神经网络（equivariant graph neural network）框架SevenNet-Polar；采用BEC-only预测器和all-in-one多任务模型（同时预测能量、力、应力和BEC）；利用FlashTP加速技术实现大规模模拟。

Conclusion: SevenNet-Polar提供了一种高效、高精度且可扩展的BEC预测方案，使得电场下的大规模电荷感知分子动力学（charge-aware molecular dynamics）模拟变得更加可行。对角与非对角BEC分量展现出不同于能量、力和应力误差的标度指数，提示BEC预测具有独特的误差标度行为。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of the Born effective charge (BEC) tensor is crucial for modeling materials under electric fields but remains computationally expensive. To bridge this gap, we present SevenNet-Polar, an equivariant graph neural network framework based on the SevenNet architecture for fast and accurate BEC predictions. Our BEC-only predictors can achieve an RMSE as low as 0.0043 e on ZrO$_2$, Li$_3$PO$_4$, and perovskites, despite the presence of high-temperature (up to 2,000 K) and defect-laden training data. Our all-in-one multitask models for predicting energy, forces, stress, and BEC in ZrO$_2$ and Li$_3$PO$_4$ achieve high accuracy with an RMSE of 1.0 meV/atom for energy, 12 meV/angstrom for forces, 0.05 GPa for stress, and 0.0029 e for BEC. BEC accuracy is not degraded by multitask training. Scaling analysis reveals distinct exponents for diagonal and off-diagonal BEC components, both of which exhibit less favorable scaling than energy, force and stress errors. SevenNet-Polar generalizes robustly when tested on scenarios containing structural environments absent from the training set, such as along nudged elastic band (NEB) trajectories or grain boundaries in ZrO$_2$. Accelerated by FlashTP, SevenNet-Polar enables simulations containing up to 1.5 million atoms on multi-GPU supercomputers and up to approximately 15,000 atoms on a single consumer-grade GPU. This makes charge-aware molecular dynamics simulations under electric fields more accessible.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 尽管文献数量庞大且普遍认为这些方法具有可重复性，但仅有少数研究严格探讨了合成可重复性问题。关键实验参数（critical experimental parameters）经常报告不足，统计分析（statistical analyses）极少被纳入，从而限制了实验室间的可比性（inter-laboratory comparability）和可重复性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，系统综述和荟萃分析可作为识别可重复性差距（reproducibility gaps）的有效工具，并引导材料科学领域开发更透明、更可靠的合成协议。

Abstract: Reproducibility remains a major challenge in materials synthesis, particularly for nanomaterials whose properties are highly sensitive to experimental conditions. Here, we present a systematic review and meta-analysis evaluating the reproducibility of two widely used synthesis routes: the Turkevich method for gold nanoparticles (AuNPs) and the chemical vapor deposition (CVD) growth of MoS2. An adapted PRISMA-based protocol combined with a modified SPIDER framework was applied to assess methodological transparency, parameter reporting, and experimental consistency across the literature. More than 1,300 articles for each case study were retrieved from Scopus and Web of Science and systematically screened using structured checklists and a Python-based text classification algorithm validated against independent human reviewers. Despite the extensive literature and the widespread perception of these methods as reproducible, only a small fraction of studies rigorously addressed synthesis reproducibility. Critical experimental parameters were frequently underreported, and statistical analyses were rarely included, limiting inter-laboratory comparability and reproducibility. These findings demonstrate the value of systematic reviews and meta-analyses as tools for identifying reproducibility gaps and guiding the development of more transparent and reliable synthesis protocols in materials science.

Abstract: We demonstrate the use of high-resolution spot-profile analysis low-energy electron diffraction to determine the mean grain size of plasma-enhanced chemical vapor deposition grown few-layer graphene on sapphire (Al$_2$O$_3$). The diffraction patterns exhibit broadened graphene spots, pronounced diffuse scattering, and azimuthally extended features, indicating finite crystallite size and rotational disorder. By analyzing the finite-size broadening of the specular (00) spot with an Airy-type diffraction profile, we determine a mean grain diameter of 3.7$\,$nm for the as-grown graphene layer. Post-growth annealing under ultrahigh-vacuum conditions increases the mean grain size to about 5.7$\,$nm and 6.8$\,$nm, respectively. These results establish SPA-LEED as a sensitive reciprocal-space method for quantifying the structural coherence of directly grown graphene on insulating substrates.

### [136] [Self-organized defect clustering and concentration-dependent vacancy diffusion in MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14951)
*Aaron Flötotto,Benjamin Spetzler,Martin Ziegler,Erich Runge,Christian Dreßler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫空位迁移对基于MoS₂的忆阻器（memristors）和忆阻晶体管（memtransistors）等器件的电子输运和功能行为具有关键影响；近期的原子模拟表明空位迁移通过合作性、空位辅助的硫跳变进行，意味着强烈相关的缺陷动力学（correlated defect dynamics），因此需要系统研究其集体行为。

Method: 采用动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte-Carlo）模拟，其跃迁速率（transition rates）来源于基于机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential）的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟。

Result: 识别出三种输运regime：低浓度下空位不可迁移或局限于小团簇；高浓度下呈现经典扩散输运（classical diffusive transport），扩散系数恒定，且空位聚集为各向异性延伸团簇（anisotropically extended clusters）；中间regime中团簇合并为连通的波动网络，扩散系数依赖于浓度，且团簇尺寸分布广泛。

Conclusion: 空位扩散系数对平均缺陷浓度的强依赖性，为理解MoS₂中观察到的忆阻行为（memristive behavior）的起源提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Sulfur vacancy migration has a crucial impact on electronic transport and the functional behavior of MoS$_2$-based devices such as memristors and memtransistors. According to recent atomistic simulations, vacancy migration proceeds via cooperative, vacancy-assisted sulfur jumps, implying strongly correlated defect dynamics. Here, we investigate the collective behavior of sulfur-vacancy clusters in MoS$_2$ using kinetic Monte-Carlo simulations with transition rates derived from machine learning interatomic potential molecular dynamics simulations. We identify three transport regimes: At low concentrations, vacancies are immobile or confined within small clusters, whereas at high concentrations, classical diffusive transport with a constant diffusion coefficient is observed, and vacancies aggregate into anisotropically extended clusters. A well defined intermediate regime is characterized by clusters merging into a connected, fluctuating network with a concentration-dependent diffusion coefficient. This regime is characterized by a broad distribution of cluster sizes. The strong dependence of the vacancy diffusion coefficient on the average defect concentration provides new insights into the origin of memristive behavior observed in MoS$_2$.

Abstract: Using a combination of static and dynamic density functional theory simulations, we systematically investigated how phosphorus doping and oxygen vacancies on the CeO$_2$(111) surface influence the oxidation mechanisms of formaldehyde (HCHO). Our results reveal that P cations (P$^{5+}$) substitutionally replace Ce$^{4+}$ in the lattice, forming Ce$-$O$-$P bonds that reduce the band gap (from 2.26 eV to 2.09 eV) and generate localized Ce$^{3+}$ states through charge redistribution. This synergistic effect of P doping combined with oxygen vacancy strengthens HCHO adsorption by decreasing the adsorption energy from -0.62 eV on pristine CeO$_2$(111) to -2.65 eV on the defective P-doped surface. Importantly, P doping lowers the C$-$H bond cleavage barrier by 0.84 eV relative to pristine CeO$_2$(111), accelerating formaldehyde oxidation on the defective surface. In addition, the rapid desorption of CO$_2$ and H$_2$O ($τ\sim 0.59 s$ at 300 K) indicates weak product-surface interactions, which favor efficient catalyst regeneration during continuous operation. These findings highlight P-doped CeO$_2$(111) as a promising system for low-temperature HCHO oxidation and provide insights into the design of ceria-based catalytic materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用单层SiO₂硬掩模（hard mask）结合多步氧基ICPRIE（感应耦合等离子体反应离子刻蚀）工艺，实现金刚石薄膜的完全贯穿蚀刻，金刚石与SiO₂的选择比（selectivity）为15:1；随后将蚀刻后残留的氧化物层用作键合表面，通过O₂等离子体表面活化与硅酸钠中间层（sodium silicate interlayer）在室温下完成键合。

Result: 该方法可实现数十微米深度的蚀刻，具有清晰的侧壁（sidewalls）、保持的表面粗糙度（surface roughness）以及可忽略的微掩蔽效应（micromasking）；键合形成的硅氧烷薄膜（siloxane film）在可见光谱范围内光学透明，且不引入可检测的寄生光致发光（parasitic photoluminescence），保留了嵌入NV色心的光学读出能力。

Conclusion: 该深蚀刻与室温键合工艺为从体金刚石薄膜到金刚石-二氧化硅异质结构（diamond-on-silica heterostructures）提供了一条可扩展且无污染的路线，适用于集成量子光子学（integrated quantum photonics）和传感应用。

Abstract: Single-crystal diamond is a leading material platform for high-power electronics and solid-state quantum technologies, yet many device architectures require micrometer-scale membranes with deeply etched features, patterned from commercially available substrates. In this work, we demonstrate a complete through-etch of a 16 μm -thick NV-doped single-crystal diamond membrane using a single-layer SiO2 hard mask combined with a multi-step oxygen-based ICPRIE process. With a diamond-to-SiO2 selectivity of 15:1, this non-metallic mask strategy can achieve etch depths of few tens of μm with well-defined sidewalls, conserved surface roughness and negligible micromasking. Furthermore, we use the oxide layer that remains after etching to serve as the bonding surface in a subsequent integration step. The etched microstructures are transferred onto SiO2 substrates and bonded at room temperature using O2 plasma surface activation and a sodium silicate interlayer. The resulting siloxane film is optically transparent across the visible spectrum and introduces no detectable parasitic photoluminescence, preserving the optical readout of the embedded NV centers. Together, this deep-etch and room-temperature bonding process provides a scalable and contaminationfree route from bulk diamond membranes to diamond-on-silica heterostructures for integrated quantum photonics and sensing applications.

### [139] [Modeling the Fatigue Behavior of Amorphous Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14994)

TL;DR: 本文通过线性化Long塑性模型推导出材料疲劳寿命的Basquin定律（Basquin's law），得到指数m=3及预因子A的解析表达式，并在三种非晶聚合物（PS、PMMA、PVC）的实验数据中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料耐久性预测非常重要但非常困难，现有经验性的Basquin定律（Basquin's law）缺乏理论推导，其指数m（通常在3到12之间）和预因子A的物理起源尚不清晰。

Method: 利用Long塑性模型（Long's plasticity model）的线性化版本对材料在周期性振荡载荷下的疲劳行为进行理论推导。

Result: 在该理论框架下推导出Basquin定律，得到指数m=3，并给出了预因子A的解析表达式。理论预测与三种非晶聚合物（PS、PMMA、PVC）的实验数据吻合良好。

Abstract: Prediction of material durability is both very important and very difficult. In many cases, material durability is measured by subjecting a sample to repeating oscillatory cycles (in shear or tension-compression) until it fails in either ductile or brittle fashion. Typically, the stress amplitude is denoted S, and the number of cycles N, so the resulting dependence is known as the SN-curve. For many materials, SN curve has been shown to obey the empirical Basquin's law, N = AS^(-m), where the prefactor A was a function of the temperature, load frequency, and sample history, and the power law m was a real number, usually between 3 and 12. Here, we derive the Basquin's law using a linearized version of the Long's plasticity model and demonstrate that within this framework, m = 3. We also derive the expression for the prefactor A. Finally, we show that our theory successfully describes experimental data for three amorphous polymers, PS, PMMA, and PVC.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将谷电子学（valleytronics）从动量空间中的分立点推广到连续线，使无散能带（dispersionless bands）成为可调控自由度，从而克服传统平带系统缺乏外部调控的局限。

Method: 基于共线自旋层群（collinear spin layer group）对称性分析，在二维交替磁体中引入脊-自旋-层耦合机制，利用动量空间中的一维连续无散电子态（脊）同时锁定自旋极化与原子子层，并通过对称性筛选出三种候选材料：Mg₂Mo₂(PO₅)₂、Ca(FeP)₂和Mg₂V₂(SO₅)₂。

Result: 三种候选材料均具有交叉脊结构（crossed-ridge structure），每个脊对应一个自旋通道和一个子层；RSLC机制实现了倒易空间中脊取向的层选择性切换、实空间中的自旋过滤输运以及独特的电霍尔响应（electric Hall response）。

Conclusion: 脊电子学为方向甄别电流（direction-discriminating currents）提供了可调控平台，弥合了无散能带与多功能器件操作之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Extending valleytronics from discrete points to continuous lines in momentum space transforms dispersionless bands into a controllable degree of freedom. Here we introduce ridge--spin--layer coupling (RSLC) in two-dimensional (2D) altermagnets, where a one-dimensional continuous line of dispersionless electronic states (a ridge) in momentum space locks to both spin polarization and atomic sublayer. This ridge-induced quenching of kinetic energy mimics flat-band physics, yet crucially, RSLC grants external control, allowing for layer-selective switching of ridge orientation in reciprocal space, spin-filtered transport in real space, and a distinct electric Hall response. Guided by collinear spin layer group symmetry, we identify three 2D candidate materials, namely Mg$_2$Mo$_2$(PO$_5$)$_2$, Ca(FeP)$_2$, and Mg$_2$V$_2$(SO$_5$)$_2$, each featuring a crossed-ridge structure with two ridges, one per spin channel and sublayer. Our work establishes ridgetronics as a controllable platform for direction-discriminating currents, bridging dispersionless bands with multifunctional device operation.

### [141] [Recent progress on liquid transport growth of quantum materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15032)
*Jiaqiang Yan,Brenden Ortiz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了液相输运生长（liquid transport growth, LTG）技术，该技术通过熔融助熔剂（molten flux）而非气相作为输运介质，在温度梯度驱动下实现溶质输运，从而将溶解与结晶过程空间分离。LTG适用于窄温区结晶及结晶温度敏感的量子材料，并讨论了实验设计要点与未来发展前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统助熔剂法受限于平衡溶解度约束，且溶解与结晶在同一空间耦合进行，不利于某些窄温区结晶或结晶温度敏感材料的单晶生长。LTG通过空间分离溶解与结晶过程，旨在突破这些限制，提高单晶生长产率与质量。

Method: LTG是一种水平助熔剂生长技术，与化学气相输运（chemical vapor transport）类似，但以熔融助熔剂替代气相作为输运介质。在人为施加的温度梯度驱动下，溶质从溶解区持续输运至结晶区，实现溶解与沉淀的空间分离。

Result: LTG可在原料完全溶解前即开始结晶，解除了起始料与助熔剂比例对平衡溶解度的依赖，从而在一次生长中获得高单晶产率。该技术尤其适用于两类材料：仅在窄温度/成分窗口内结晶的化合物，以及化学计量比、缺陷浓度和物理性质对结晶温度敏感的化合物。文中列举了Fe₃Sn₂、CrTe₃、YFe₂Ge₂、UTe₂、CeRh₂As₂、MoTe₂、WTe₂及LuNb₆Sn₆等代表性量子材料（quantum materials）的案例。

Conclusion: LTG在高质量量子材料单晶生长中展现出独特优势。本文总结了炉体选择、生长时间、熔体稳定性和安瓿几何形状等实验设计实用因素，并展望了将LTG从经验性生长方法发展为更具预测性的晶体生长技术的未来方向。

Abstract: Liquid transport growth (LTG) is a horizontal flux growth technique that is closely analogous to chemical vapor transport, with the key distinction that a molten flux rather than a vapor serves as the transport agent. Unlike conventional flux growth, LTG spatially separates charge dissolution and crystal precipitation and couples them through continuous solute transport under a deliberately imposed temperature gradient. This enables crystal growth to begin before the charge is completely dissolved, removes the equilibrium solubility constraint on the starting charge/flux ratio, and allows large yields of single crystals to be obtained from a single growth. Recent studies have further shown that by spatially separating dissolution and crystallization and maintaining crystallization at a nearly constant temperature, LTG is particularly effective for two classes of materials: compounds that crystallize only within a narrow temperature and/or composition window, and compounds whose stoichiometry, defect concentration, and thus physical properties are sensitive to the crystallization temperature. In this review, we discuss representative examples including Fe$_3$Sn$_2$, CrTe$_3$, YFe$_2$Ge$_2$, UTe$_2$, CeRh$_2$As$_2$, MoTe$_2$, WTe$_2$, and LuNb$_6$Sn$_6$ to illustrate the unique capabilities of LTG for producing high quality single crystals of diverse quantum materials. We also summarize practical considerations for LTG experimental design, including furnace selection, growth time, melt stability, and ampoule geometry, and discuss future opportunities for transforming LTG from an empirical growth method into a more predictive crystal growth technique.

</details>

Result: Cr2AlC为弱场线性金属顺磁体，以Pauli顺磁性为主导；非单调温度依赖由反铁磁耦合的Cr-Cr二聚体贡献描述，低温Curie型上升仅来自痕量局域Cr中心。红光照射下SQUID未检测到宏观光磁响应；4K下ESR显示可逆光致降低的局域磁信号，但光学改性自旋仅占Cr亚晶格数十ppm。ai-BSE计算表明光激发可在相邻Cr位点间重新分布自旋极化。

Abstract: Cr2AlC MAX phase is synthesized by high-pressure solid-state annealing and investigated as a candidate platform for optically responsive magnetism. Structural characterization confirms the formation of the Cr2AlC phase, while magnetic and optical-magnetic properties are examined by superconducting quantum interference device (SQUID) magnetometry, electron spin resonance (ESR), and first principles calculations. SQUID magnetometry identifies Cr 2AlC as a weak, field-linear metallic paramagnet dominated by Pauli-like susceptibility of itinerant Cr-derived states. Its non-monotonic temperature dependence is described by an additional contribution from antiferromagnetically coupled Cr-Cr dimers, whereas the low-temperature Curie-like upturn originates from only a trace population of localized Cr centers. Under red-light illumination, SQUID magnetometry does not reveal an intrinsic macroscopic optomagnetic response. In contrast, ESR at 4 K shows a reversible light-induced reduction of a local magnetic signal, but the optically modified spin population corresponds only to several tens of ppm of the Cr sublattice. Ab initio Bethe-Salpeter equation (ai-BSE) calculations combined with the maximally localized Wannier function analysis suggest that optical excitation can redistribute spin polarization between neighboring Cr sites with the opposite local moments. The combined experiment-theory approach therefore establishes the hierarchy of magnetic contributions in Cr 2AlC and identifies the microscopic origin of its local optical sensitivity. This provides a reference for designing MAX phases and related MXenes in which defects, surface terminations or reduced dimensionality may enhance optically active magnetic states.

### [144] [Emergent d-wave altermagnetism in chlorine-adsorbed FeSe monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15197)

Abstract: The recent emergence of altermagnetism has opened new frontiers in condensed matter physics, yet material platforms capable of hosting both intrinsic altermagnetic order and superconductivity remain exceedingly rare. Here, based on symmetry analysis and first-principles calculations, we propose a realistic route to engineer robust altermagnetism in monolayer FeSe, a prototypical iron-based superconductor. By designing a stoichiometric Fe2Se2Cl structure through single-side Cl adsorption and introducing gate-tunable hole doping, we achieve a highly stable altermagnetic ground state. ### [145] [Hyperfine driven spin relaxation of charge carriers in metal-halide perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15224)
*Guillaume Lague,Frédérick Bernardot,Mauricio Calvo,Olfa Selmi,Sofia Masi,Christophe Testelin,Hernan Miguez,Ivan Mora-Sero,Maria Chamarro*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超精细相互作用在半导体局域载流子自旋弛豫中起主导作用，该机制在III-V族材料和量子点中已有充分研究，但在金属卤化物钙钛矿（metal halide perovskites, MHPs）中的关键作用近年才被发现。MHPs的反转型能带结构导致超精细耦合的层级与常规材料相反（空穴相互作用占优），且近期MAPbI3实验表明载流子自旋处于中间关联区间，传统单指数近似失效，亟需更精确的理论描述。

Method: 将原本用于μ子自旋谱学（muon spin spectroscopy）的自旋弛豫模型进行改进，使其能够精确描述任意超精细关联时间（hyperfine correlation time）下局域载流子的纵向自旋弛豫。该模型不依赖单指数近似假设，能够覆盖从快速到慢速关联的完整区间。

Result: 分析揭示了两种不同的超精细弛豫通道：电子主要耦合于卤素原子核，而空穴受金属原子核主导。基于此提出预测——含有轻卤素和轻金属阳离子的钙钛矿具有显著延长的自旋寿命。将该模型应用于两种钙钛矿样品的时间分辨法拉第旋转（time-resolved Faraday rotation）数据时，成功提取了载流子局域化体积和超精细关联时间等关键微观参数，并证明精确动力学解优于单指数近似。

Conclusion: 研究提供了MHPs中超精细驱动自旋弛豫的微观机制理解，建立了一种表征载流子局域化和自旋动力学的稳健理论框架，为设计长自旋寿命的钙钛矿材料提供了指导。

Abstract: Spin relaxation of localized charge carriers in semiconductors is primarily governed by hyperfine interaction with the surrounding nuclear spin bath. While this mechanism is well-established in III-V bulk materials and quantum dots, its critical role in metal halide perovskites (MHPs) has only recently emerged. Their inverted band structure induces an unusual hierarchy of hyperfine couplings, with hole interactions dominating electron interactions, particurlaly in Pb-based perovskites. Here, we adapt a spin relaxation model - originally developed for muon spin spectroscopy - to provide an exact description of longitudinal spin relaxation for localized carriers across arbitrary hyperfine correlation times. This approach is motivated by recent experimental evidence in MAPbI3, which places carrier spins in an intermediate correlation regime, where conventional mono-exponential approximations fail. Our analysis reveals distinct hyperfine relaxation channels: electrons couple primarily to halogen nuclei, whereas holes are governed by metal nuclei. This leads to a key prediction - perovskites with lighter halogens and metal cations exhibit significantly extended spin lifetimes. Applied to time-resolved Faraday rotation data obtained from two perovskite samples, our model extracts key microscopic parameters - including the carrier localization volume and hyperfine correlation time - demonstrating the necessity of the exact dynamical solution over a single-exponential approximation. These findings provide microscopic insight into hyperfine-driven spin relaxation in MHPs and establish a robust framework for characterizing carrier localization and spin dynamics.

</details>

### [146] [A Modern Multimodal Assistant on a 6 GB 2011 GPU: Stage-Validated, All-GPU CUDA Inference for Fermi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14568)
*A. C. Opus,J. Q. Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究在2011年的NVIDIA Tesla C2075 (Fermi架构) GPU上全GPU部署了现代多模态助手MiniCPM-V-4.6，通过8位权重量化、分块delta规则重写循环层、以及基于供应商SGEMM的注意力核优化，实现了从2k到10k tokens下几乎平坦的长上下文推理性能（361 tok/s），端到端图像问答耗时1.7秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续同系列研究中在老旧硬件上运行大模型的探索，该工作转向研究"模型能完全放入GPU时的表现"。目标是利用一块仅6GB显存的Fermi架构GPU（sm_20），全GPU部署一个现代多模态助手，验证其可行性与性能边界。

Method: 部署MiniCPM-V-4.6（SigLIP2视觉编码器+16倍视觉token压缩+混合门控delta网络骨干）。采用三重优化：(i) 8位权重量化后一次反量化并调用供应商SGEMM，达到FP32峰值的64%；(ii) 将循环层改写为分块delta规则（chunked delta-rule rewrite），比顺序扫描快2.8倍；(iii) 对朴素注意力核中O(N²)的预填充瓶颈，改用逐头供应商GEMM调用写入现有得分缓冲区（零额外内存），消除二次复杂度。

Result: 全GPU引擎达到FP32峰值的64%（手写GEMM仅37%）。分块delta规则加速2.8倍。8位解码快于4位（Fermi半速率半字节解包）。视觉端全流水线验证误差1.4e-5，发现位置嵌入桶化在有理数相等时存在浮点tie-breaking实现定义问题。优化后预填充速度：2k tokens 408 tok/s，10k tokens 361 tok/s（17x提升）。图像编码时间降至0.93秒（6x加速），端到端图像问答1.7秒。

Conclusion: 即使在2011年的Fermi架构GPU上，通过针对硬件特性的精细优化，现代多模态助手仍可实现可用的全GPU推理性能。研究揭示了老旧硬件的几个反直觉行为（8位优于4位、朴素注意力的O(N²)墙被短基准掩盖），并给出了可推广的工程经验：浮点tie-breaking的索引算术是实现定义的，应调用参考算子而非重新实现。

Abstract: A companion study ran a 35B mixture-of-experts model on a 2011 NVIDIA Tesla C2075 (Fermi, sm_20, 6GB) as a GPU-prefill/CPU-decode hybrid, because the 4-bit model did not fit in device memory (arXiv:2606.24031). This report keeps the hardware and asks what a model that fits can do: we deploy MiniCPM-V-4.6, a modern multimodal assistant pairing a SigLIP2 vision encoder and window-attention merger (16x visual token compression) with a compact hybrid gated-delta-net backbone, entirely on the GPU. Three results. (i) An all-GPU engine built on measured foundations: projections that dequantize 8-bit weights once and call the vendor SGEMM still in the last Fermi toolchain (64% of FP32 peak; our best hand-written GEMM hit 37%, wrongly called the ceiling); a chunked delta-rule rewrite of the recurrent layers, 2.8x faster than the sequential scan once attribution exposed one bad kernel; and a measured negative: 4-bit weights make decode slower than 8-bit here, since Fermi issues nibble-unpacking shifts at half rate. (ii) The vision side is a port with a proof obligation: we translate tower, merger, and projector to sm_20 CUDA, validating every stage against a locally generated reference forward (full tower 1.4e-5). One failure, position-embedding bucketization differing on exact rational ties, generalizes to a rule: float tie-breaking in index arithmetic is implementation-defined; call the reference operator, do not reimplement it. (iii) Long context exposes an O(N^2) wall short benchmarks hide: prefill falls from 114 tok/s at 2k tokens to 21 at 10k in a naive attention kernel; per-head vendor-GEMM calls writing into the existing score buffer (zero extra memory) restore a flat profile (408 at 2k, 361 at 10k; 17x), verified by exact needle retrieval from 60% depth. The same rewrite cuts image encoding 6x, to 0.93s. The system answers an image question end-to-end in 1.7s.

### [147] [Quantum Markov Chains for an Asymmetric Mixed Ising-XY Model on a Cayley Tree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14343)
*Farrukh Mukhamedov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究半无限有根二阶Cayley树上的混合量子Ising-XY模型，利用树指标量子马尔可夫链的相容性准则，推导出平移不变边界方程并显式计算局部转移算子。证明了该边界方程对所有参数存在唯一正平移不变解，从而模型存在唯一的平移不变量子马尔可夫链。此外，证明了约化边界律动力学无大于1的周期点，并计算了自然三-site团簇上的局部两-site纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在树状格点（tree lattice）上研究量子自旋模型，探索平移不变边界条件的存在性与唯一性，以及边界律动力学（boundary-law dynamics）的周期行为与局部纠缠（local entanglement）性质。

Method: 采用树指标量子马尔可夫链（tree-indexed quantum Markov chain）的相容性准则，在归一化迹（normalized trace）下推导平移不变边界方程，显式计算一步部分迹映射（one-step partial-trace map）作为局部转移算子。

Result: 证明了对于所有 $J_I, J_{XY} \in \mathbb{R}$ 和 $\beta > 0$，边界方程存在唯一的正平移不变解，从而模型存在唯一的平移不变量子马尔可夫链。约化边界律动力学不存在大于1的允许周期点（admissible periodic points）。

Conclusion: 该混合量子Ising-XY模型在Cayley树上的平移不变边界条件唯一，边界律动力学无高阶周期行为，局部纠缠可在三-site团簇上显式计算。

Abstract: We study a mixed quantum Ising-$XY$ model on the semi-infinite rooted Cayley tree of order two. For every vertex $u$, the edge $\langle u,(u,1)\rangle$ carries an $XY$ interaction and the edge $\langle u,(u,2)\rangle$ carries an Ising interaction. Using the compatibility criterion for tree-indexed quantum Markov chains and consistently working with the normalized trace, we derive the translation-invariant boundary equation and compute explicitly the associated local transfer operator, namely the one-step partial-trace map which propagates successor boundary data to the parent vertex. We prove that the boundary equation has a unique positive translation-invariant solution for all $J_I,J_{XY}\in\mathbb R$ and $β>0$. Hence the model admits a unique translation-invariant quantum Markov chain generated by a positive translation-invariant boundary condition. We also show that the reduced boundary-law dynamics, i.e. the induced finite-dimensional recursion for the boundary-law parameters, has no admissible periodic points of period greater than one and compute the local two-site entanglement on the natural three-site cluster of the tree.

### [148] [On Factorizing Aggregate Counting Distributions into Independent Latent Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14409)
*Israel Klich*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了关于概率生成函数正因子分解（positive factorization）的数学理论，引入正因子分解偏序集（positive factorization poset）和因子化熵（factorization entropy），证明了严格的熵不等式，并在多个维度和几何性质上刻画了可因子分解区域的结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 给定一个聚合计数变量（aggregate counting variable）的概率分布，如何判断是否存在独立的潜在计数过程（independent latent counting processes）与之兼容？这等价于问：一个概率生成函数（probability-generating function）何时能分解为具有非负系数的归一化多项式之积。该问题在统计物理、信息论和概率论中具有基础意义。

Method: 引入正因子分解偏序集，其元素为所有按细化（refinement）排序的正因子分解；定义因子化熵，用于度量与观测分布兼容的最大潜在香农熵（Shannon entropy）。通过分析支撑集（support-based）障碍、实根（real-rooted）与 Hurwitz 稳定（Hurwitz-stable）区域、局部稳定性定理以及精确计算和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）实验来探究几何性质。

Result: 证明了严格的熵不等式，并刻画了等号成立条件（潜在加法映射的单射性）；展示了熵优化可限制在极大原子化（maximal atomizations）上，并给出不同极大原子化具有不同熵的例子。确定了二次和三次情形下的可因子分解区域；精确计算了四次 Hurwitz 体积；通过支撑集障碍刻画了正因子分解的局限性。

Conclusion: 正因子分解偏序集是概率生成函数的一个自然代数对象，为研究聚合计数统计中的潜在独立结构提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Given only the probability distribution of an aggregate counting variable, what independent latent counting processes are compatible with the observation? Equivalently, when does a probability-generating function admit a factorization into normalized polynomials with nonnegative coefficients? We develop a mathematical theory of such positive factorizations.
  We introduce the positive factorization poset, whose elements are all positive factorizations ordered by refinement, and define the factorization entropy, measuring the maximal latent Shannon entropy compatible with the observed distribution. We prove a sharp entropy inequality, characterize the equality case by injectivity of the latent addition map, show that entropy optimization may be restricted to maximal atomizations, and exhibit examples where distinct maximal atomizations have different entropy.
  We further establish support-based obstructions to positive factorization, characterize the real-rooted and Hurwitz-stable sectors, prove a local stability theorem for coprime factorizations, determine exactly the factorable regions in degrees two and three, obtain an exact quartic Hurwitz volume, and investigate the geometry of the factorable region inside the probability simplex through exact calculations and Monte Carlo experiments. These results identify the positive factorization poset as a natural algebraic object associated with probability-generating functions and provide a framework for studying latent independent structure in aggregate counting statistics.

</details>

Method: 将Dirac算子表示为极形式，即通过一个指定矩阵的左乘（left-multiplication）来刻画该算子，并利用这一表示推导其右预解式。
