### [150] [A C++ implementation of the G-Scheme stiff ODE solver with multi-resolution sparse hash-table kernel lookup](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14918)
*Riccardo Malpica Galassi,Mauro Valorani*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并实现了一个生产级C++版本的G-Scheme（cpp-gscheme），利用多分辨率稀疏哈希表（multi-resolution sparse hash-table）替代在线雅可比核集（kernel set）计算，在33种正庚烷（n-heptane）自燃机理上实现了100%的核集检索命中率、零在线特征分解（eigen decomposition），并展现出相对于CVODE求解器2.7倍至9.3倍的加速比，计算成本缩放约为N^1.4，显著优于CVODE的N^1.9。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: G-Scheme的计算开销主要由每时间步的核集（kernel set）评估主导，原始的在线特征分解（online eigen decomposition）成本高昂，亟需一种高效策略来降低计算负担，同时保持数值精度与行为一致性。

Method: 采用多分辨率稀疏哈希表（multi-resolution sparse hash-table）策略，将在线核集计算替换为从预计算查找表（precomputed lookup table）中检索；通过位级精确的检索挂钩（bitwise-inert retrieval hook）和完全原生的化学源项评估路径（native evaluation path），确保C++实现与Python参考版本在缩放、分箱（binning）和哈希语义（hashing semantics）上行为等价。

Result: 在33种正庚烷自燃机理（56–459种组分）及详细654种组分机理上，哈希表化C++ G-Scheme实现100%核集检索命中率与零在线特征分解；相对于CVODE求解器加速比从2.7倍（56种组分）提升至9.3倍（654种组分）；计算成本缩放约为N^1.4，低于CVODE的N^1.9。精度评估表明求解器对总误差贡献可忽略，主要误差源于骨架简化（skeletal reduction）。

Conclusion: C++实现的哈希表化G-Scheme在保持高精度的同时显著提升了计算效率，使得80种组分的骨架机理（skeletal mechanism）在5%点火延迟（ignition-delay）目标下相对于详细机理上的CVODE实现了225倍加速；相关软件、训练集构建工具与基准驱动代码均已开源发布。

Abstract: The G-Scheme is an explicit, adaptive integration framework for stiff systems of ordinary differential equations that exploits a local time-scale decomposition provided by the eigensystem of the Jacobian (the kernel set). Its computational cost is dominated by the evaluation of a new kernel set at each time step. In a recent paper [R.Malpica Galassi and M.Valorani, Combust. Theory Model. 2025], we introduced a multi-resolution sparse hash-table strategy that replaces online kernel computation with retrieval from a precomputed lookup table, demonstrated in Python. Here we present cpp-gscheme, a production-grade C++ implementation of both the G-Scheme and the multi-resolution hash table, together with the porting methodology that guarantees behavioural equivalence with the Python reference: identical scaling, binning and hashing semantics, a bitwise-inert retrieval hook in the integrator, and a fully native evaluation path for the chemical source terms. On 33 n-heptane autoignition mechanisms spanning 56-459 species plus the detailed 654-species mechanism, the hash-tabulated C++ G-Scheme retrieves 100 percent of the kernel sets, performs zero online eigen decompositions, and outperforms the natively compiled CVODE solver by a factor increasing from 2.7x (56 species) to 9.3x (654 species), with observed cost scaling of approximately N power 1.4 versus CVODE's N power 1.9. A three-metric accuracy assessment (ignition delay, equilibrium state, and accumulated entropy-progress error) shows that the solver contributes negligibly to the overall error budget, which is dominated by skeletal reduction. Consequently, a 5 percent ignition-delay target is achieved by the 80-species skeletal mechanism with a 225x speed-up over CVODE on the detailed mechanism. The software, training-set builders, and benchmark drivers are released as open source.

</details>


### [151] [Quasi-Pfaffian Solutions to Integrable Systems via Sylvester-Moutard Transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15013)
*Claire R Gilson,Chen Shu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种名为“准Pfaffian”（quasiPfaffian）的数学结构，它类似于非交换（noncommutative）设定中代替行列式（determinant）使用的准行列式（quasideterminant）。基于准Pfaffian的Sylvester恒等式，作者提出了一种新的变换——Sylvester Moutard变换，该变换可为Moutard可变换的可积系统（如Novikov Veselov方程和二维正弦Gordon方程）生成新解。文章还简要回顾了经典Moutard变换在准Pfaffian框架下的形式，并讨论了该新结构的若干附加性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非交换代数背景下，传统的行列式概念不再适用，需要发展替代性数学结构。准Pfaffian的引入旨在扩展准行列式的思想，为处理Moutard可变换的可积系统（Moutard transformable integrable systems）提供新的代数工具。

Method: 首先形式化定义准Pfaffian结构，并建立其Sylvester恒等式；在此基础上构造Sylvester Moutard变换（Sylvester Moutard transform）；通过该变换生成Novikov Veselov方程和二维正弦Gordon方程（two dimensional sine Gordon equation）的新解；此外，在准Pfaffian框架下重新审视经典Moutard变换。

Result: 基于准Pfaffian的Sylvester恒等式推导出Sylvester Moutard变换，并验证了该变换能够为Moutard可变换的可积系统生成新解。文章还阐明了准Pfaffian与经典Moutard变换之间的内在联系。

Conclusion: 准Pfaffian是一种有前景的非交换数学结构，其衍生出的Sylvester Moutard变换为相关可积系统提供了新的求解途径。该工作同时揭示了准Pfaffian与经典Moutard变换的深层关联，并为进一步探索该结构的性质奠定了基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a mathematical structure called the quasiPfaffian. The quasiPfaffian is analogous to the quasideterminant, a structure used instead of a determinant in noncommutative settings. Building on the Sylvester identity for the quasiPfaffian, we develop a novel transformation, named the Sylvester Moutard transform, this generates new solutions for Moutard transformable integrable systems, such as the Novikov Veselov equation and the two dimensional sine Gordon equation. We also briefly review the classical Moutard transformation in the context of quasiPfaffians and discuss several additional properties of this new object.

### [153] ["Goldfish'' equations for infinitely many particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15237)
*Francois Leyvraz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨将“金鱼方程”（一类可精确求解的 N 体非线性常微分方程组）从有限 N 推广到无穷维情形（N →∞），核心困难在于从多项式过渡到整函数（entire functions）；非标准分析（non-standard analysis）方法留作后续研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金鱼方程因其优美的可解性而引人注目：通过将多项式系数变换为根的映射，可将非线性 ODE 转化为自由运动。将该精确求解框架从有限 N 扩展到无限 N（N → ∞），是自然且具有理论意义的推广。

Method: 沿用有限 N 情形的核心技巧——多项式系数到零点的变换，但在无限 N 下需将多项式推广为整函数（entire functions）。主要工作即处理这一推广过程中的数学困难。非标准分析（non-standard analysis）作为另一候选路径暂被搁置。

Result: 明确了从多项式过渡到整函数是实现无穷维推广的主要障碍；目前尚未完成完整推广，非标准分析方案亦未展开。

Conclusion: 金鱼方程的无穷维推广尚未解决，主要瓶颈在于整函数框架上的技术困难；非标准分析可能提供替代路径，有待未来探索。

Abstract: The ``goldfish'' equations, so named because of their striking beauty, are a system of $N$ nonlinear ODE's, where $N$ is an arbitrary integer. They can be solved exactly in a very simple manner, by transforming them to free motion using a transformation involving the transition from the set of {\em coefficients\/} of a polynomial to that of its {\em zeroes}. This paper aims to explore the possibility of extending this solution to the case in which $N$ is infinite. The main difficulty involves the transition from polynomials to entire functions. Another approach using non-standard analysis, is left to future work.

</details>

### [154] [Universal Asymptotics and Exact Enumeration of Eulerian Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14342)
*Ahmad Barhoumi,Roozbeh Gharakhloo,Nathan Hayford*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了带任意度序列的连通、标号、亏格 g 欧拉映射（Eulerian maps）在顶点数趋于无穷时的计数渐近行为，发现其首项具有普适性且仅依赖于有限个映射特征，常数因子与 Painlevé I 方程相关。方法结合了正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials）递推系数分析与多变量解析组合学（analytic combinatorics of several variables）。此外还导出了亏格 1 情形的精确计数公式，这是首次针对 g ≥ 1 的非正则（mixed-valence）映射的此类枚举结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填补亏格 g ≥ 1 且非正则（即混合价数）的欧拉映射枚举问题中渐近结果与精确公式的空白，此前这类问题缺乏系统性结果。

Method: 将正交多项式递推系数分析与多变量解析组合学相结合，用以处理具有任意度序列的连通标号欧拉映射的渐近计数。

Result: 在顶点数趋于无穷时，连通、标号、亏格 g 欧拉映射的计数渐近行为具有普适性（universal），首项仅由有限个映射特征决定，常数因子与 Painlevé I 方程相关。此外获得了亏格 1 情形的精确计数公式。

Conclusion: 这是首次给出 g ≥ 1 非正则（混合价数）映射枚举问题的渐近结果与精确公式，表明该计数问题的渐近行为具有普适性结构，且与 Painlevé I 方程存在深层联系。

Abstract: We calculate the asymptotics of the number of connected, labeled, genus $g$ Eulerian maps with an arbitrary degree sequence, in the limit as the total number of vertices tends to infinity. This asymptotic is universal, in the sense that the leading order term depends on only finitely many map characteristics. The constant factor in this formula is related to the Painlevé I equation. Our methods combine the analysis of the recurrence coefficients associated to a particular family of orthogonal polynomials, and the theory of analytic combinatorics of several variables. We also derive an exact formula for the number of connected, labeled, genus $1$ Eulerian maps. These are the first results on this kind of enumeration problem for $g\geq 1$, non-regular (mixed-valence) maps.

</details>


### [155] [Measures and generalizations of dual Littlewood identities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14362)
*Zhongren Cai,Bin Jiang,Naihuan Jing,Zhijun Li,Qianyi Ye*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过在Fock空间中引入三类由伴随顶点算子（adjoint vertex operators）构建的、以分拆（partition）为参数的向量族，建立了新的自由费米子构造，以行列式核（determinantal kernel）形式给出了与B、C、D型对偶Littlewood恒等式（dual Littlewood identities）相关的测度，并推导了涉及受限分拆（restricted partitions）的广义Littlewood恒等式，其中包含对(-n)-非对称分拆（asymmetric partitions）和李超代数（Lie superalgebras）情形的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摘要未明确说明动机，但从内容推断，作者旨在为B、C、D型对偶Littlewood恒等式和相关测度提供新的构造性证明，并推广Littlewood恒等式以涵盖更广泛的分拆族（如受限分拆和(-n)-非对称分拆），从而统一和发展已有的Littlewood型恒等式理论。

Method: 方法包括：在Fock空间中利用伴随顶点算子乘积引入三类参数化向量；通过对偶真空向量（dual vacuum vector）的商空间（quotient space）分析，建立特定分拆族张成该空间的结论；通过计算这些向量与单列分拆（one-column partitions）或广义分拆$(0^m)$索引的向量之间的内积（inner product），推导广义Littlewood恒等式。

Result: 主要结果包括：(1) 得出B、C、D型对偶Littlewood恒等式的新推导，并通过自由费米子构造证明Rains和Betea引入的相关测度关于显式关联核（correlation kernel）是行列式的；(2) 建立多个涉及受限分拆的广义Littlewood恒等式，其中对每个正整数$n$得到了(-n)-非对称分拆的恒等式；(3) 这些广义恒等式包含多个已知Littlewood型恒等式作为特例，并对李超代数的广义Littlewood恒等式给出了新证明。

Conclusion: 摘要未明确陈述结论，但可归纳为：本文提出的向量族框架为对偶Littlewood恒等式及相关测度的行列式结构提供了统一的构造性途径，并成功将Littlewood恒等式推广至更多分拆类型，深化了对组合恒等式与Fock空间表示之间联系的理解。

Abstract: We introduce three families of vectors $|\underlineλ^{so}\rangle$, $|\underlineλ^{sp}\rangle$ and $|\underlineλ^{o}\rangle$ parametrized by partitions in the Fock space by using products of adjoint vertex operators. We show that the quotient space of the dual vacuum vector is spanned by the partition vectors indexed by a special family of partitions. The partition-indexed vectors also help us to derive the dual Littlewood identities of types B, C, and D in a new manner associated to the special family of partitions. As an application, we obtain a new free fermionic construction to show that the measures related to dual Littlewood identities introduced by Rains \cite[Section 7]{Rai2000} and Betea \cite[Section 3]{Be2020} are determinantal with repect to some explicit correlation kernels.
  Furthermore we establish a number of generalized Littlewood identities summed over certain restricted partitions by computing the inner products with elements indexed by one-column partitions {or generalized partitions $(0^m)$} in the complete dual Fock space. {In particular, for each positive integer $n$, we obtain generalized Littlewood identities for $(-n)$-asymmetric partitions. We show that these generalized Littlewood identities contain several well-known Littlewood-type identities as special cases. Consequently we also give a new proof of the generalized Littlewood identity \cite[(5.25)]{LSV2008} for Lie superalgebras. } %We also produce infinite generalized Littlewood identities by calculating the inner products between these elements and some elements indexed by one-column partitions in the complete dual Fock space.

### [156] [Stochastic binary networks with asymmetric and time-delayed interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15215)
*Hantao Zhang,Sidra Gibeault,Matthew W. Daniels,Philippe Talatchian,Ursula Ebels,Advait Madhavan,Mark D. Stiles*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了含不对称相互作用和时间延迟的随机二元网络（stochastic binary networks），发现时间延迟会从根本上重塑反称耦合引发的动力学，产生强振荡时间关联，并在强耦合系统中驱动稳态概率趋于均匀分布，同时建立了一个统一的理论框架，表明不对称性和时间延迟可作为神经形态硬件中的功能性资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机二元网络广泛用于描述复杂系统中的集体动力学和神经形态计算，但现实网络通常同时包含不对称相互作用（asymmetric interactions）和有限信号传播时间延迟（time-delayed interactions），超出了现有常规理论的适用范围。本文基于耦合超顺磁隧道结（superparamagnetic tunnel junctions）的实验观测，研究含不对称性和时间延迟的随机二元网络。

Method: 采用理论分析与数值模拟相结合的方法，对含不对称和时间延迟相互作用的随机二元网络进行研究。理论方面给出延迟诱导均匀分布（uniform distributions）在广类随机网络中成立的解析证明。数值方面对含五个耦合自旋（spins）的网络进行模拟，验证效应在超过两个自旋的系统中仍然存在。

Result: 时间延迟使反称耦合（anti-symmetric couplings）诱导的动力学发生根本改变，产生与实验一致的强振荡时间关联（oscillatory temporal correlations）。足够长的时间延迟即使在强耦合系统中也驱动稳态概率趋于相等的态占据（equal state occupations），这些看似无特征的均匀概率分布与显著的时间关联共存，区别于平衡高温行为。对称性破缺的偏置场（symmetry-breaking bias fields）则恢复依赖相互作用的稳态，并定性改变系统行为。

Conclusion: 该研究在对称瞬时相互作用与不对称或时间延迟相互作用之间的中间区域内，为随机二元网络建立了统一的理论框架，并指出不对称性和延迟可以作为神经形态硬件和复杂网络动力学中的功能性资源加以利用。

Abstract: Stochastic binary networks are widely used to describe collective dynamics in complex systems and to perform neuromorphic computation, yet realistic networks often contain both asymmetric interactions and finite signal propagation times that fall outside conventional theories. Here we study stochastic binary networks with asymmetric and time-delayed interactions motivated by experimental observations in coupled superparamagnetic tunnel junctions. We find that time delay fundamentally reshapes the dynamics induced by anti-symmetric couplings, producing strong oscillatory temporal correlations consistent with experiment. At the same time, sufficiently long delays drive the steady-state probabilities toward equal state occupations even in strongly coupled systems. These apparently featureless probability distributions coexist with pronounced temporal correlations, distinguishing them from equilibrium high-temperature behavior. We further show analytically that delay-induced uniform distributions emerge in a broad class of stochastic networks, while symmetry-breaking bias fields restore interaction-dependent steady states with qualitatively modified behavior. Simulations of networks with five coupled spins demonstrate that these effects persist beyond minimal systems with only two spins. Our results establish a unified framework for stochastic binary networks in the intermediate regime between symmetric instantaneous interactions and asymmetric or time-delayed interactions, and suggest that asymmetry and delay can be exploited as functional resources in neuromorphic hardware and complex network dynamics.

</details>

### [157] [JT gravity on the worldline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14213)
*Ben Freivogel,Alessandro Fumagalli,Diego M. Hofman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究一维量子力学系统与欧几里得AdS JT引力耦合的效应，推导了观测者的欧几里得传播子与关联函数的精确表达式，发现引力导致观测者的总欧几里得时间（或逆温度）发生涨落，这种涨落半经典下集中于测地线距离附近，且在双喇叭口拓扑中变得很大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解动态量子引力（dynamical quantum gravity）中观测者的体验，研究一维量子力学系统与欧几里得AdS JT引力（Euclidean AdS JT gravity）耦合的效应。

Method: 在盘拓扑（disk topology）上，推导欧几里得传播子与关联函数的精确表达式；计算双喇叭口（double trumpet）拓扑对配分函数的贡献；进行半经典分析与洛伦兹解释。

Result: 引力导致观测者的总欧几里得时间（或闭合路径的逆温度）发生涨落，半经典极限下涨落集中在边界的测地线距离（geodesic distance）附近；涨落相对于均值很小，但相对于模型的有效普朗克尺度（effective Planck scale）很大，可被具有精细态密度（finely spaced density of states）的观测者分辨；双喇叭口拓扑中有效温度涨落很大，不存在光滑的半经典鞍点（semiclassical saddle point）。

Conclusion: 耦合引力后，量子力学系统的演化时间或温度发生非平凡涨落，盘拓扑下涨落可控，而双喇叭口拓扑中涨落剧烈，揭示了不同拓扑下观测者体验的显著差异。

Abstract: Motivated by the problem of understanding the experience of an observer in dynamical quantum gravity, we study the effects of coupling a one-dimensional quantum mechanical system living on a bulk worldline to Euclidean AdS JT gravity. On the disk topology, where the worldline stretches between two boundary points, we derive exact expressions for the Euclidean propagator of the observer and for its correlation functions, and discuss their holographic interpretation. The main effect on the quantum mechanics is the fluctuation of the total Euclidean time for which the observer evolves, or its inverse temperature for closed Euclidean paths. This turns the standard quantum mechanical evolution operator into an average of those, weighted by a measure over Euclidean times which in the semiclassical limit is peaked around the geodesic distance between the boundary points. We characterize the fluctuations around this value, finding that they are small compared to the mean, but large compared to the effective Planck scale of the model. These fluctuations can be resolved by an observer with a finely spaced density of states. We also discuss the Lorentzian interpretation of these Euclidean calculations. Finally, we compute a contribution to the partition function of the observer coupled to gravity coming from the double trumpet. In this case the fluctuations of the effective temperature are large, reflecting the absence of a smooth semiclassical saddle point.

</details>


### [158] [Anti-scrambling and euclidean folds from observer correlators in de Sitter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14215)
*Daniel Harlow,Ying Zhao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引力计算发现德西特视界（de Sitter horizon）表现出“反混乱化”（anti-scrambling）现象，这与标准多体量子系统的行为相反，并基于欧几里得时间中的折叠关联函数（folded correlators）提出了一种上下都有界的哈密顿量可实现该现象的量子系统方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特视界的行为在性质上与黑洞视界（black hole horizon）有本质差异，这给发展德西特空间的量子描述带来了根本性挑战。本文旨在通过引力计算收集关于该问题的“数据”，以揭示德西特时空特有的量子行为。

Method: 采用引力计算（gravitational calculations）方法，分析生活在时空中观察者世界线（worldline）上的关联函数（correlation functions）。特别地，通过对比两点函数（two-point function）和四点函数（four-point function）的行为来揭示反混乱化现象。

Result: 两点函数表现为常规的热关联子（thermal correlator），但四点函数却展现出反混乱化（anti-scrambling）行为，这与标准多体量子系统的行为相反。

Conclusion: 反混乱化可以在一个哈密顿量同时有上界和下界的量子系统中实现，具体方案是利用在欧几里得时间（Euclidean time）中折叠的关联函数。

Abstract: The de Sitter horizon behaves in a qualitatively different way from a black hole horizon, which poses a challenge to any attempt to develop a fundamental quantum description of de Sitter space. In this paper we gather some ``data'' on this problem using gravitational calculations, seeing that they lead to an ``anti-scrambling'' phenomenon that is contrary to the behavior of standard many-body quantum systems. We organize our discussion in terms of correlation functions computed on the worldline of an observer living in the spacetime, with the two-point function looking like a conventional thermal correlator but the four-point function showing anti-scrambling. We propose that anti-scrambling can be realized in a quantum system whose Hamiltonian is bounded from both above and below using correlators that are folded in Euclidean time.

### [159] [Ising the way into de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14219)
*Giovanni Galati,Stathis Vitouladitis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了受相关热算子扰动的二维伊辛模型（Ising model）在德西特时空（de Sitter spacetime）上的严格解，通过费米子化方法（fermionisation）精确计算了宇宙学关联函数，并在非微扰层面揭示了晚期微扰级数中的发散性世俗项（secular terms）如何被重新求和。德西特伊辛模型为德西特空间中的量子场论动力学提供了一个最小可解实验室。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特时空中的量子场论（QFT in de Sitter space）在非微扰层次上知之甚少，尤其是其晚期行为（late-time behaviour）常常受到微扰理论中世俗发散项（secular divergences）的困扰。作者旨在构建一个既有强相互作用又严格可解的模型，以揭示非微扰效应如何修复微扰理论的病理行为。

Method: 论文采用二维伊辛模型，在欧几里得（Euclidean）形式下利用费米子化将其转化为可解的自由费米子理论，计算了重正化的球面配分函数（renormalised sphere partition function）以及热算符和类后裔算符（descendant-like operators）的精确两点函数。随后将两点函数解析延拓至洛伦兹德西特时空（Lorentzian dS₂），并利用德西特表示理论（de Sitter representation theory）分析其晚期行为。对自旋算符（spin operator）和 disorder 算符（disorder operator）也进行了类似分析，并与共形微扰论（conformal perturbation theory, CPT）进行比较。

Result: 精确的晚期两点函数表现出与主序列标度维度（principal-series scaling dimensions）相关的振荡行为。共形微扰论的晚期微扰级数中出现了发散的世俗项（secular terms），而精确非微扰结果自然地将这些发散项重新求和（resummed），给出有限且行为良好的物理可观测量。自旋和 disorder 算符的晚期标度维度受到非微扰约束。

Conclusion: 德西特伊辛模型作为一个严格可解的例子，明确展示了晚期微扰病理如何被非微扰效应修复。该模型为德西特空间中的量子场论动力学提供了一个最小可解实验室（minimal solvable laboratory），有助于理解更一般德西特量子场论的非微扰结构。

Abstract: We study the two-dimensional Ising model deformed by the relevant thermal operator and placed on de Sitter (dS) spacetime. Despite being strongly interacting in its original formulation, the theory is exactly solvable on account of fermionisation. We compute exact cosmological correlators and compare them with conformal perturbation theory. In the Euclidean formulation of the model, we first compute the renormalised sphere partition function and the exact two-point functions of the thermal operator and descendant-like operators. We analytically continue the two-point functions to Lorentzian dS$_2$. Their late-time behaviour is governed by de Sitter representation theory and includes oscillations associated with principal-series scaling dimensions. We then analyse two-point functions of the spin and disorder operators, which are non-local in the fermionic variables, and derive non-perturbative constraints on their late-time scaling dimensions. In both cases, we compare the exact answers to conformal perturbation theory (CPT) and we show that divergent secular terms generically spoil the perturbative series at late times. The de Sitter Ising model shows explicitly how late-time perturbative pathologies are resummed in non-perturbative cosmological observables and provides a minimal solvable laboratory for quantum field theory dynamics in de Sitter space.

</details>


### [160] [Non-perturbative saturation of Krylov complexity, and its implications in quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14220)
*Andrew Lucas,Amit Vikram*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究有限维量子系统中 Krylov 态复杂度的动力学行为。发现基于离散能谱构造的正交多项式在 Krylov 指标增大时会从态密度低的区域“挤开”（crowd away）。这一结果的物理含义是，即使在全局能谱上定义最简形式的 Krylov 态复杂度，该复杂度在每一个低能态中也会在略超过海森堡长度（Heisenberg length）之后被证明停止增长。该发现对 Krylov 复杂度与二维量子引力中虫洞长度（wormhole length）之间关系的猜想具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究有限维量子系统中 Krylov 态复杂度的增长行为，特别是其在低能态下的截止机制，并检验该复杂度与二维量子引力中虫洞长度关联猜想的有效性。

Method: 基于离散能谱构造正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials），分析它们在 Krylov 指标（Krylov index）增大时的分布行为；采用定义在整个能谱上的最简形式 Krylov 态复杂度（minimalist Krylov state complexity）进行分析。

Result: 正交多项式在大的 Krylov 指标下会从态密度低的能谱区域“挤开”；在每一个低能态中，Krylov 复杂度在略超过海森堡长度后停止增长。

Conclusion: Krylov 态复杂度在低能态中的增长受到海森堡长度量级的天然上界限制，该结果对 Krylov 复杂度与二维量子引力中虫洞长度之间的猜想提供了约束性见解。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of Krylov state complexity in finite-dimensional quantum systems. Orthogonal polynomials built on a discrete energy spectrum crowd away from regions where the density of states is low at large Krylov index. The physical implication of this result is that, even using a minimalist Krylov state complexity which is defined over the entire spectrum, the Krylov complexity provably stops growing a little past the Heisenberg length in every low-energy state. This has interesting implications for the proposal that Krylov complexity is related to the wormhole length in 2D quantum gravity.

</details>


### [161] [Gravitational Effective Theories with Maximal Supersymmetry and a Peculiar Parity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14230)
*Justin Berman,Simon Caron-Huot,Aditi V. Chandra,Henriette Elvang,Aidan Herderschee,Loki L. Lin,Roger Morales*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究四维 $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力（supergravity）的紫外完备化（ultraviolet completion）空间。通过树级因子化（tree-level factorization）和“特殊宇称”（peculiar parity）条件，导出四点 Wilson 系数（Wilson coefficients）的非线性约束，并结合正定性（positivity）将允许区域压缩为两个尖角点：闭超弦 Virasoro–Shapiro 振幅（closed superstring Virasoro–Shapiro amplitude）和无限自旋塔振幅（infinite spin tower amplitude）。进一步要求第一质量层附近状态数有限时，仅保留 Virasoro–Shapiro 振幅。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力在紫外完备化框架下的可能低能有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）空间，明确哪些理论能够通过一致性条件存活下来。

Method: 基于树级散射振幅的因子化条件，结合“特殊宇称”性质（仅能施加于标量振幅子集），推导四点 Wilson 系数的非线性约束，并与正定性条件联立，在参数空间中刻画允许区域。

Result: 允许区域被压缩为包含两个尖角点的非凸域（non-convex domain）：一个对应闭超弦 Virasoro–Shapiro 振幅，另一个对应所有自旋态处于同一质量的无限自旋塔振幅。数值与解析分析均表明，要求第一质量层附近状态数有限时，仅 Virasoro–Shapiro 振幅符合条件。

Conclusion: $\mathcal{N}=8$ 超引力的一致紫外完备化空间在强约束下大幅缩小，唯一可行的候选者为闭超弦理论对应的 Virasoro–Shapiro 振幅。

Abstract: We study the space of four-dimensional ultraviolet completions for $\mathcal{N}=8$ supergravity that are described at low energies by weakly-coupled effective field theories (EFTs) with maximal supersymmetry and $\mathrm{SU}(4)\times\mathrm{SU}(4)$ R-symmetry. We show that tree-level factorization of the 4-, 5-, and 6-point EFT scattering amplitudes, together with a certain ``peculiar parity'' condition, leads to nonlinear constraints on the 4-point Wilson coefficients. This peculiar parity is a property that can only be imposed on a subset of scalar amplitudes. Combining the nonlinear constraints with positivity, we find that the allowed region of 4-point Wilson coefficients is reduced to a non-convex domain with two sharp corners: one being the closed superstring Virasoro--Shapiro amplitude, the other an infinite spin tower amplitude exchanging states of every spin at the same mass. We show both numerically and analytically that requiring a finite number of states near the first mass level leaves only the Virasoro--Shapiro amplitude.

</details>


### [162] [Non-Hermitian Holographic Flows to Little Rip Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14284)
*Daniel Arean,David Garcia-Fariña,Juan F. Pedraza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息对偶（holography）证明，在满足零能量条件（null energy condition, NEC）的物质支撑下，类空奇点（spacelike singularities）通常属于Belinski-Khalatnikov-Lifshitz（BKL）范式；但通过在全息模型中可控地违反NEC（对应于非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$-对称强耦合量子场论），可得到全新的非Kasner黑洞内部几何，其深内部描述了一个各向同性FLRW宇宙，经历超加速膨胀并趋近于Little Rip。该奇点结构在两粒子重算符关联函数中留下特征印记，可作为区分标准Kasner内部的观测量，并建立了Little Rip/CFT对应的全息框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准BKL范式要求物质满足零能量条件（null energy condition, NEC），而现实宇宙学或全息理论中可能存在违反NEC的情形。作者期望探索在{\cal PT}-对称非厄米量子场论的全息对偶中，可控的NEC违反是否会导致不同于Kasner的黑洞内部几何，并为Little Rip宇宙学提供全息实现。

Method: 采用全息对偶方法，构建一个与强耦合非厄米$\mathcal{PT}$-对称量子场论（QFT）对偶的重力模型，研究黑洞内部区域在$\mathcal{PT}$恢复相（$\mathcal{PT}$-restored phase）内的几何结构。

Result: 发现了一种新颖的非Kasner区域（non-Kasner regime），其深内部几何描述了一个各向同性FLRW宇宙，经历超加速膨胀（super-accelerated expansion）并趋近于Little Rip奇点。该奇点结构在两粒子重算符关联函数（two-sided heavy-operator correlators）中留下特征可观测印记，使之能够与标准Kasner内部区分开来。

Conclusion: 该工作为Little Rip宇宙学提供了具体的全息实现，并奠定了Little Rip/CFT对应的基础，使得此类宇宙学奇点区域可以通过非厄米量子场论中的可观测量进行探索。

Abstract: Spacelike singularities supported by matter satisfying the null energy condition (NEC) are expected to fall within the Belinski--Khalatnikov--Lifshitz (BKL) paradigm. We show that controlled violations of the NEC in holography can lead to different black hole interiors. In a holographic model dual to a strongly coupled non-Hermitian $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric QFT, we uncover a novel non-Kasner regime within its real, $\mathcal{PT}$-restored phase. The deep-interior geometry describes an isotropic FLRW cosmology undergoing super-accelerated expansion and approaching a Little Rip. This regime leaves a characteristic imprint on two-sided heavy-operator correlators, allowing it to be distinguished from a standard Kasner interior. Our construction provides a concrete holographic realization of a Little Rip cosmology and lays the groundwork for a Little Rip/CFT correspondence, in which such cosmological regimes can be explored through observables in a non-Hermitian quantum field theory.

### [163] [Dynamical Entropy Is a Noether Charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14289)
*V. R. Shajiee,M. M. Sheikh-Jabbari,V. Taghiloo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个用于一般动力学、非平衡黑洞系统的动力学熵（dynamical entropy）框架，将其定义为满足狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）的演化类光曲面（evolving null surface）上的诺特荷（Noether charge）。通过引入“动力学零定律”（dynamical zeroth law）所要求的物理几何条件，唯一确定了与动力学熵对应的对称生成元，并证明该诺特荷密度严格满足热力学第二定律，从而在无需事件视界（event horizon）那种目的论最终条件（teleological final conditions）的前提下，实现了时间局域的第二定律证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对于一般动力学、非平衡状态下的黑洞热力学缺乏一个严格的定义框架。传统的事件视界热力学依赖于全局的最终条件，无法描述黑洞在实时演化过程中的熵和热力学第二定律。

Method: 将动力学熵定义为演化类光曲面上的诺特荷，施加狄利克雷边界条件，并基于几何条件唯一确定对称生成元（即曲面上的类光矢量），从而引入“动力学零定律”的概念来约束生成元的选取。

Result: 该诺特荷密度在每一瞬时严格满足热力学第二定律，无需背景平稳性（background stationarity）假设，也无需依赖事件视界那种目的论式的最终条件。动力学熵及其第二定律在时间上是局域的，适用于一般动力学引力系统。

Conclusion: 该工作拓展并推广了Hollands等人先前提出的动力学熵概念，消除了对背景平稳性的依赖，建立了时间局域且普遍适用的非平衡黑洞热力学第二定律。

Abstract: Black hole thermodynamics for generic dynamical, non-equilibrium regimes remains a fundamental challenge. We establish dynamical entropy as the Noether charge associated with a generic evolving null surface subject to Dirichlet boundary conditions. We uniquely specify the symmetry generator associated with the dynamical entropy, which is a null vector on the null surface, upon requiring physically motivated geometric conditions that yield a notion of ``dynamical zeroth law.'' We prove that this Noether charge density satisfies the second law of thermodynamics strictly at each instant in time, bypassing the teleological final conditions traditionally required by event horizons. Thus, we extend and generalize the notion of dynamical entropy introduced in \cite{Hollands:2024vbe}, in some different ways: We do not impose background stationarity; our dynamical entropy and the associated second law are local in time and work for generic dynamical gravitational systems.

### [164] [The variational approach to infrared divergencies: Applications to black hole action integrals and holographic Wilson loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14330)
*M. Arroyo,D. Arteaga,M. Bañados,A. Faraggi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过重整化（renormalization）在壳作用量变分（on-shell action variation）而非作用量本身的方法，利用其通用形式和作为泛函空间上1-形式（1-form）的自然解释，统一处理了多种黑洞和全息Wilson圈（holographic Wilson loops）的计算，结果与标准全息重整化（holographic renormalization）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统重整化作用量（renormalizing the action）的方法在处理在壳作用量时存在体贡献（bulk contribution）非零、需进行体抵消项（bulk subtractions）等问题。该论文旨在通过重整化作用量变分来克服这些困难，提供更简洁、普适的重整化框架。

Method: 论文提出重整化在壳作用量变分的方法。核心步骤包括：(1) 利用该变分的通用形式——体贡献自动为零，将重整化问题局域化于边界；(2) 将该变分解释为泛函空间（functional space）上的1-形式（1-form），通过区分精确1-形式（exact 1-forms）与非精确1-形式（non-exact 1-forms）给出清晰的重整化判据。然后将该算法应用于多种黑洞及全息Wilson圈的计算。

Result: 该方法成功应用于 Kerr-Newman、Kerr-Newman-AdS、Taub-NUT、Taub-Bolt 和 STU 黑洞等例子，以及全息Wilson圈的计算。所有计算结果均与标准结果一致，特别是与全息重整化（holographic renormalization）的结果相符。

Conclusion: 重整化在壳作用量变分方法相较于重整化作用量本身具有两大优势：体贡献自动为零，重整化问题自然局域于边界；其作为泛函空间上1-形式的解释提供了清晰的重整化判据。该方法通用且与标准结果一致，证明其有效性和普适性。

Abstract: Renormalizing the on-shell action variation offers two important advantages over renormalizing the action itself. First, the variation of the action has a universal form in which the bulk contribution vanishes identically. As a result, the renormalization problem is automatically localized at the boundary; no bulk subtractions are required. Second, the variation of the action admits a natural interpretation as a 1-form on functional space. The distinction between exact and non-exact 1-forms provides a clear renormalization prescription. We apply these ideas to the computation of on-shell black hole actions. After presenting the general algorithm, we discuss some examples, including Kerr-Newman, Kerr-Newman-AdS, Taub-NUT, Taub-Bolt, and STU black holes. We also apply the same techniques to the computation of holographic Wilson loops. All results agree with standard results, in particular with holographic renormalization.

### [165] [Lectures on Open Systems and Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14351)
*Enrico Pajer*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文介绍了开放系统（open systems）的算符形式与Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分方法，重点阐述其在开放有效场论（open effective field theories）和暴涨宇宙学（inflation）中的应用，面向初次接触这些领域的研究生和研究者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际物理系统大多与环境存在相互作用，其约化动力学（reduced dynamics）会表现出耗散、噪声、退相干、记忆效应等封闭系统不具备的特征。在引力和宇宙学中，暗物质、暗能量等问题的微观本质未知，且引力系统缺乏守恒能量概念，天然呈现非平衡动力学，因此亟需发展分析开放系统的理论工具。

Method: 采用算符形式（operator formalism）和Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分（Schwinger-Keldysh path-integral）构建开放系统的理论框架，将相关自由度系统化处理，同时对环境和微观自由度进行参数化描述而非显式求解，从而建立开放有效场论（open effective field theories）。

Result: 系统地介绍了开放系统理论的基本工具，强调了开放有效场论在宇宙学关键问题——暴涨（inflation）、暗物质（dark matter）、暗能量（dark energy）——中的应用前景，为相关研究提供了入门性的方法论指导。

Conclusion: 开放系统理论为处理微观本质未知且主要通过引力效应观测的宇宙学问题提供了合适的理论框架；该讲稿面向初学者，旨在降低进入这一交叉领域的门槛。

Abstract: Open systems are ubiquitous in physics. Many realistic systems interact, at least weakly, with environmental degrees of freedom that may be too numerous, too complicated, inaccessible, or unknown. When only a subset of degrees of freedom is observed, its reduced dynamics can differ qualitatively from that of a closed system, displaying dissipation, noise, decoherence, memory effects, or loss of information into unobserved sectors. When the microscopic description is also unknown, one is led to an open effective description, in which the relevant degrees of freedom are treated systematically while the environment and the microscopics are parametrized rather than solved for explicitly.
  This perspective is especially important in gravity and cosmology. The main open problems of cosmology, including inflation, dark matter, and dark energy, involve spacetime-filling sectors whose microscopic nature is unknown and whose observed effects are primarily gravitational. At the same time, gravitational systems often lack a preferred notion of conserved energy because they are time dependent, and naturally display out-of-equilibrium dynamics. These lecture notes introduce the operator formalism and the Schwinger-Keldysh path-integral as tools to study open systems, with emphasis on open effective field theories and inflation. They are aimed at master students, PhD students, and researchers approaching these topics for the first time.

</details>


### [166] [Birman-Schwinger Formulation of the Faddeev--Popov Zero-Mode Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14425)
*Daniel G. Tedesco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过构造一个有界无量纲算子，将朗道规范下的Gribov视界条件（horizon condition）简化为一个普通的谱阈值问题，并明确了Gribov无极点估计（no-pole estimate）作为波恩阶截断（Born-order truncation）的适用范围，同时利用周期横向SU(2)背景场的精确解验证了该构造的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对Gribov视界（Gribov horizon）的表征——无论是通过Zwanziger视界函数（horizon function）还是Gribov无极点条件——都只能近似地编码Faddeev-Popov算子的正定性，而本文旨在发展一种直接的算子表述，以更精确地刻画该视界。

Method: 移除常数规范模式后，朗道规范下的Faddeev-Popov算子与一个由背景场和自由拉普拉斯算子（free Laplacian）组装而成的有界无量纲算子相合（congruent），从而将视界条件简化为一个普通的谱阈值：当该算子的某个特征值越过-1时阈值条件达成。自伴性（self-adjointness）在此表述中仅由朗道横截性（Landau transversality）导出，无需额外假设。

Result: 该构造揭示了鬼传播子中的Gribov无极点估计本质上是该算子对角预解式（diagonal resolvent）的领头阶波恩截断，从而划定了该估计的可信区间与失效区间。对周期横向SU(2)背景场给出了精确解，阈值、波恩近似及其高阶修正均具有闭合形式，且作用量与模式计数熵（mode-counting entropy）在四维中按体积标度而平衡。

Conclusion: 该周期背景场族为视界机制提供了一个可精确求解的参考案例，但将其推广至一般杨-米尔斯构型（Yang–Mills configurations）是一项独立的后续工作，文中明确列出了推广所需的条件。

Abstract: Characterizations of the Gribov horizon have so far proceeded indirectly, through Zwanziger's horizon function or through Gribov's no-pole condition on the ghost propagator, each of which encodes the positivity of the Faddeev--Popov operator only approximately, whereas the construction developed here supplies a direct operator statement. Once the constant gauge modes are removed, the Landau-gauge Faddeev--Popov operator becomes congruent to a bounded, dimensionless operator assembled from the background field and the free Laplacian, so that the horizon condition reduces to an ordinary spectral threshold, attained when an eigenvalue of that operator crosses $-1$. Self-adjointness, ordinarily postulated as an independent hypothesis, follows in this formulation from Landau transversality alone, while the first-order character of the perturbation fixes an analytic scale distinct from the one governing the familiar Schrödinger problem. Because the ghost dressing function coincides with the diagonal resolvent of the same operator, Gribov's no-pole estimate emerges as its leading Born-order truncation, an identification that at once delimits the regime in which the estimate is trustworthy and the regime in which it fails. The construction is tested against an exact solution for a periodic transverse $SU(2)$ background, for which the threshold, its Born approximation, and the corrections beyond Born all admit closed forms, and for which the associated action and mode-counting entropy scale with the volume so that the two balance in four dimensions. The periodic family thereby furnishes a solvable reference case for the underlying mechanism, whereas extending the claim to generic Yang--Mills configurations constitutes a separate undertaking, whose requirements are stated explicitly.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用系统性的分类方法研究高维玻色子SPT相中的超越上同调现象；利用配边（cobordism）理论（Thom发展的分析框架）将问题与Dijkgraaf-Witten相位联系起来，并揭示其与Steenrod经典问题（同调环流是否存在流形代表元）的对偶关系。

Result: 发现第一个重要的超越上同调非平凡现象是模3（mod-3）的，而非费米子相位中常见的模2（mod-2）现象；指出存在一类Dijkgraaf-Witten相位，它们在一般单纯复形（simplicial complexes）上非平凡，但在流形（manifolds）上变为平凡。

Conclusion: 高维玻色子SPT相中的超越上同调行为与Steenrod问题及Thom配边理论有深刻的对偶联系，且模3现象标志着玻色子与费米子SPT相在更高维度上的本质差异。

Abstract: Bosonic invertible and symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases are well-known to be described by ordinary cohomology groups in low dimensions, but `beyond-cohomology' phases appear in higher dimensions. We make a systematic study of them, and find that the first major non-triviality is a mod-3 phenomenon, and not a mod-2 phenomenon as in the case of fermionic phases.
  We also point out that this is a dual manifestation of the classic question of Steenrod, namely the issue of the existence of homology cycles without manifold representatives. Thom developed the theory of cobordisms to answer this question, and we explain how the same analysis leads to Dijkgraaf-Witten phases which are nontrivial on general simplicial complexes but become trivial on manifolds.

### [168] [Cosmological Collider Signals at Strong Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14891)
*Xiangwei Wang,Yi Wang,Yunke Zhao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究具有恒定转向导数混合的双场暴胀系统中的宇宙学对撞机信号（cosmological collider signatures），利用精确超几何解和Mellin-Barnes方法构建混合传播子，分析了重场在挤压极限下对三点函数（bispectrum）的贡献，得到了幂律包络和对数振荡的解析结果，并给出了大质量JWKB展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解早期宇宙暴胀（inflation）期间重场对宇宙学关联函数的非微扰贡献，特别是通过宇宙学对撞机（cosmological collider）机制探测暴胀时期的粒子物理。

Method: 采用精确超几何解（exact hypergeometric solutions）非微扰地处理正则化曲率扰动与质量等曲率场之间的二次混合；利用Mellin-Barnes方法分离重场携带的非解析晚时分支，构造混合传播子（mixed propagators）以及三点函数（bispectrum）的挤压极限（squeezed limit）积分。

Result: 对于三次等曲率自相互作用，挤压三点函数呈现幂律包络（power-law envelope）和对数振荡（logarithmic oscillations），振荡频率编码重场质量，振幅和相位保留完整的混合依赖关系；推导了大质量条件下的JWKB展开，给出了等曲率场的Wightman函数积分表示，并将解析结果与数值结果进行了比较。

Conclusion: 本文方法能够在非微扰层面处理混合效应对宇宙学对撞机信号的影响，为从暴胀时期宇宙学关联函数中提取重场质量与混合参数提供了解析框架。

Abstract: We study cosmological collider signatures in a two-field inflationary system with constant-turn derivative mixing between the canonically normalized curvature fluctuation and a massive isocurvature field. Building on recently derived exact hypergeometric solutions that treat the quadratic mixing nonperturbatively, we construct the mixed propagators constituting the cosmological correlators. A Mellin-Barnes approach helps isolate the pair of nonanalytic late-time branches carried by a heavy field. For a cubic isocurvature self-interaction, these branches contribute towards a squeezed bispectrum with a power-law envelope and logarithmic oscillations. The oscillation frequency encodes the heavy mass, while the amplitude and phase retain the full mixing dependence rather than a perturbative expansion. We perform the squeezed limit integral analytically and compare it with numerical results across representative masses and mixing strengths. At fixed mixing we derive the large-mass JWKB expansion of the squeezed correlator and its phase. We also give integral representations for the isocurvature Wightman function. ### [169] [Observers, local measurements, and topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15007)
*Michele Cirafici*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出，在动态引力（dynamical gravity）时空中传播的观测者所拥有的可观测代数（algebra of observables）构成一个含迹的冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra with a trace）。观测者利用该代数中的投影（projection）进行局域测量，并基于世界线（worldline）上的测量记录构建了一个单纯复形（simplicial complex）。作者认为，即使时空本身存在涨落（fluctuating），该复形也能捕捉其拓扑信息（topological information）。

Method: 利用动态引力时空中观测者可访问的冯·诺依曼代数及其投影结构，将观测者世界线上记录的局域测量结果组织成一个单纯复形，以此编码时空的拓扑结构。

Conclusion: 观测者的局域测量数据可以用于重建时空的拓扑性质，为量子引力中非微扰（non-perturbative）的拓扑信息提取提供了一种基于代数（algebraic）框架的新途径。

Abstract: An observer which propagates in a spacetime with dynamical gravity has access to an algebra of observables which is expected to be a von Neumann algebra with a trace. The observer can use projections from the algebra to perform local measurements. ### [170] [Casimir effect for a massive scalar field confined between parallel plates with a spatially varying effective mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15070)
*R. L. Araújo Xavier,M. H. B. Chaves,E. R. Bezerra de Mello,Herondy Mota*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了两块完美反射平行板之间、具有位置依赖有效质量的大质量实标量场的Casimir效应。通过求解Klein-Gordon方程得到精确简正模，发现横能量谱呈现类Landau结构。利用广义zeta函数正则化与重整化程序计算真空能量，将其分为类Landau贡献和有效质量空间依赖引起的附加项。在强耦合区域两项均呈指数压制；在弱耦合极限下，类Landau贡献平滑回归标准结果，而附加项因谱的有效域限制出现奇异性。除该奇异点附近，真空能主要由类Landau部分主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索位置依赖有效质量——即标量背景场耦合标量场机制——如何影响平行板间有质量实标量场的Casimir效应，为空间不均匀相对论系统中的Casimir现象提供新的精确可解框架。

Method: 通过求解带有位置依赖有效质量的Klein-Gordon方程获得精确简正模；采用广义zeta函数正则化（generalized zeta-function regularization）结合重整化（renormalization）程序计算量子化后的真空能量。

Result: 横能量谱呈现类Landau结构（Landau-like structure），无需外磁场；重整化真空能自然分为类Landau贡献与有效质量空间依赖引发的附加项；强耦合下两项均指数压制；类Landau项在弱耦合极限平滑回归标准Casimir能，附加项则在该极限下出现奇异性；除奇异点附近，真空能由类Landau部分主导。

Conclusion: 位置依赖有效质量与边界诱导的量子真空现象之间存在直接联系，提供了一个新的精确可解框架，用于研究空间不均匀相对论系统中的Casimir效应。

Abstract: We investigate the Casimir effect for a massive real scalar field confined between two perfectly reflecting parallel plates in the presence of a position-dependent effective mass, a mechanism for coupling a scalar background to a scalar field. Exact normal modes are obtained by solving the corresponding Klein-Gordon equation, leading to a transverse energy spectrum that exhibits a characteristic Landau-like structure despite the absence of an external magnetic field. Upon quantization of the field, the vacuum energy is evaluated by means of generalized zeta-function regularization together with an appropriate renormalization procedure. The renormalized vacuum energy naturally separates into a Landau-like contribution and an additional term induced by the spatial dependence of the effective mass. We show analytically and numerically that both contributions are exponentially suppressed in the strong-coupling regime. In the opposite limit, the Landau-like contribution smoothly reproduces the standard vacuum energy for a massive scalar field confined between parallel plates, whereas the additional contribution becomes singular owing to the restricted domain of validity of the exact spectrum. Except in the vicinity of this singular limit, the vacuum energy is shown to be dominated by the Landau-like sector. Our results establish a direct connection between position-dependent effective masses and boundary-induced quantum vacuum phenomena, providing a new exactly solvable framework for the investigation of Casimir effects in spatially inhomogeneous relativistic systems.

Result: 建立了X与X^{!}之间的三维镜像对称关系，给出了从X到X^{!}的SYZ构造，并揭示了在Y与Y^∨的镜像对称下X与X^{!}角色互换的对应关系。同时利用DT理论与离散对称性构造了相应的三维A-膜与B-膜。

Abstract: Given a compact CY3 $Y$, its A-side (resp. B-side) universal intermediate Jacobian $X$ (resp. $X^{!}$) admits a natural hyperkahler structure. Both $X$ and $X^{!}$ determines 3d Rozansky-Witten theories, in both A-model and B-model. We describe some surprising 3d mirror symmetry phenomena between $X$ and $X^{!}$.
  This includes (i) a 3d SYZ construction of $X^{!}$ from $X$ via moduli of certain 3d A-branes in $X$ constructed from $D^{b}\left( Y,Ω\right) $ with varying stability conditions given by $\varpi $; (ii) The 3d B-brane on $X^{!}$, constructed from varying $D^{b}\left( Y,Ω\right) $ with fixed $\varpi $, is realized as the 3d SYZ transformation of a cotangent fiber 3d A-brane in $X$.
  Under mirror symmetry between $Y$ and $Y^{\vee }$, the roles for $X$ and $% X^{!}$ got interchanged.
  We also construct 3d A- and B-branes in $X$ and $X^{!}$ via DT theory and discrete symmetries on $Y$ and $Y^{\vee }$.

*Ankur Dey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将缺陷极值面（defect extremal surface, DES）方案推广至全息界面共形场论（ICFT），在薄膜张力大、引力耦合弱的极限下，该广义DES方案精确复现了从薄膜-边界组合进行部分维度约化后得到的有效低维结果，并进一步计算了与二维永恒黑洞耦合的辐射子系统中半无限二分纯态的纠缠熵及Page曲线.

Method: 首先构建一个全息ICFT$_2$模型：两个CFT$_2$通过一个界面耦合，对偶于两个渐近AdS$_3$几何体经由一个余维为一的末端世界（EOW）薄膜连接。通过对薄膜-边界组合进行部分维度约化，得到薄膜上耦合引力的有效低维描述，从而可利用岛公式（island formula）计算精细纠缠熵。在薄膜张力大极限下，将广义DES方案的结果与有效低维结果进行对比.

Result: 在大薄膜张力极限（对应EOW薄膜上弱引力耦合）下，广义DES方案精确复现了有效低维描述对有限子系统在时间无关场景下的纠缠熵结果。进一步计算了与二维永恒黑洞耦合的辐射子系统中半无限二分纯态的纠缠熵，并得到了相应的Page曲线.

Conclusion: 广义DES方案可成功应用于全息ICFT，并在弱引力极限下与基于岛公式的低维有效描述一致，表明DES方案在全息纠缠熵计算中具有更广泛的适用范围.

Abstract: We propose a generalization of the defect extremal surface (DES) prescription to holographic interface conformal field theories (ICFTs), extending its applicability beyond the AdS$_3$/BCFT$_2$ framework. We consider a holographic ICFT$_2$ comprising two CFT$_2$s coupled across an interface, dual to two asymptotically AdS$_3$ geometries joined by a codimension-one end-of-the-world (EOW) brane. In the corresponding effective lower-dimensional description obtained via partial dimensional reduction on the brane-boundary combination, the theory on the brane is coupled to gravity, thereby enabling the computation of fine-grained entanglement entropy via the island formula. We demonstrate that the generalized DES prescription exactly reproduces the effective lower-dimensional results for finite subsystems in time-independent scenarios in the large brane tension limit, corresponding to weak gravitational coupling on the EOW brane. We further compute the entanglement entropy of semi-infinite bipartite pure states in radiation subsystems coupled to $2d$ eternal black holes, and obtain the corresponding Page curves.

### [173] [Type I/II Vortex Dynamics With Excited Normal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15187)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用数值方法分析阿贝尔-希格斯模型中的涡旋动力学，重点关注激发态形状正常模对涡旋间力的影响。通过对I型（静态吸引）和II型（静态排斥）两种参数区域的系统进行模拟，考察涡旋-涡旋及涡旋-反涡旋（vortex-antivortex）对的运动行为，包括谱壁存在性分析及长寿命准束缚态（quasi-bound states）的演化。

Result: 发现形状正常模能与静态涡旋间力竞争，导致激发态I型涡旋间出现排斥、激发态II型涡旋间出现吸引。观察到谱壁的存在，在I型体系中阻止束缚态的形成，在II型体系中阻止束缚态的解离。研究还发现了由竞争力和有效离心力（effective centrifugal forces）诱导的长寿命准束缚态和轨道运动，且该效应足够强，能使涡旋-反涡旋对沿长寿命轨道运动。

Conclusion: 激发态正常模对涡旋动力学的影响显著，可使不同类型涡旋间的相互作用发生反转，并诱导出谱壁、长寿命准束缚态及涡旋-反涡旋对轨道等丰富动力学行为。这些结果加深了对阿贝尔-希格斯模型中涡旋系统非平衡动力学的理解。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of excited normal modes on vortex dynamics in the Abelian Higgs model in the type I (static attraction) and type II (static repulsion) regimes. We demonstrate that shape normal modes compete with the static inter-vortex forces. This can result in excited type I (II) vortices repelling (attracting). In addition we observe the existence of spectral walls that prevent the formation (break up) of bound states in type I (II) systems. We study the long lived quasi-bound states and orbits induced by their competing forces and the effective centrifugal forces. Finally, we observe that the effect is strong enough to induce vortex-antivortex pairs to follow long-lived orbits.

I examine the cases of timelike Lorentz violation, of spacelike Lorentz violation in the direction of the magnetic field, of spacelike Lorentz violation in the direction perpendicular to the magnetic field, and of spacelike Lorentz violation in the direction of the compactified extra dimension. Abstract: We study how the leading string-inspired quartic correction $α'^2 F^4$ modifies holographic fermionic observables in a bottom-up $AdS_4/CFT_3$ model. The gauge sector is described by Maxwell electrodynamics supplemented by the quartic interaction, while the geometry is kept fixed in the probe approximation. We first analyze the nonlinear electrostatic background and derive an exact first integral of the gauge equation, the associated constitutive relation for the radial electric field, the critical coupling for globally regular solutions, and weak-coupling expansions for the electrostatic potential and chemical potential. We then use these backgrounds to compute the retarded Green's function and spectral function of charged probe fermions. The quartic interaction increases the chemical potential, lowers the effective ratio $T/μ$, shifts the Fermi momentum, and enhances the spectral weight without destroying the holographic Fermi surface. We further show that the fermionic observables inherit the even-power dependence on $α'$ implied by the analytic structure of the gauge sector. The resulting probe-limit analysis makes explicit how quartic bulk nonlinearities propagate from the bulk to boundary fermionic observables.

### [176] [New exact bispectrum shapes in multifield inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15251)
*Lucas Pinol*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用多场暴胀（multiple inflationary fluctuations）的有效场论，首次解析计算了曲率与等曲率涨落之间二次混合被非微扰（non-perturbatively）处理的原初双谱（primordial bispectrum），并证明所有标度不变的树级双谱可简化为单个顶点图，通过Schwinger参数积分评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微扰计算方法在处理曲率与等曲率涨落之间的二次混合时存在局限性，尤其是在强混合区域，因此需要发展非微扰解析方法以准确描述大振幅的多场原初非高斯性（multifield primordial non-Gaussianities）。

Method: 基于精确线性解的算子表示，推导出混合模函数的简化积分表示；证明所有标度不变的树级双谱可归约为单一顶点图，并通过独立预计算腿核（leg kernels）上的Schwinger-参数积分进行评估。

Result: 在弱混合（小混合）下，三次时间导数相互作用$\dot{\pi}^3$导致纯粹单场等边（equilateral）现象学；在强混合下，双谱形状偏离等边模板，变为真正的多场特征且振幅增大。压缩极限（squeezed limit）在任意无量纲混合强度$\lambda$下解析封闭，并呈现由有效质量$\nu_{\rm eff}=i\mu_f=\sqrt{9/4-m^2/H^2-\lambda^2}$决定的宇宙学碰撞信号（cosmological collider signal）。

Conclusion: 该方法统一了微扰极限（$\lambda \ll 1$）下的结果，并超越了该极限，为研究大振幅多场原初非高斯性开辟了新的解析途径。

Abstract: Using the effective field theory of multiple inflationary fluctuations, we present the first analytical calculation of the primordial bispectrum in which the quadratic mixing between curvature and isocurvature fluctuations is treated non-perturbatively. Building upon the operator representation of the exact linear solutions proposed in Ref.~\cite{Huenupi:2026abj}, we derive a simpler integral representation for these mixed mode functions. We prove that all scale-invariant tree-level bispectra reduce to a single vertex diagram, which can be evaluated with a Schwinger-parameter integral over independent pre-computable leg kernels. We showcase the power of our approach by considering the cubic time-derivative interaction $\dot{\pic}^3$, which leads to a purely single-field, equilateral phenomenology at small mixing. On the contrary, at strong mixing the obtained bispectrum shapes decorrelate from the equilateral template and become genuinely multifield, with a large amplitude, motivating a dedicated data analysis. The squeezed limit is obtained analytically in a closed form at any dimensionless mixing strength $\la$ for an isocurvature field of bare mass $m$ and features a cosmological collider signal set by $ν_{\rm eff} = i \muf=\sqrt{9/4-m^2/H^2-\la^2}$, with an effective mass dressed by $\la$, as previously evidenced in numerical or semi-analytical calculations. Our results encompass the $\la \ll 1$ limit of usual perturbative calculations, where the amplitude of the signal is necessarily small, but they also surpass them, thus opening a new analytical window into large multifield primordial non-Gaussianities.

</details>


### [177] [Relativistic time-commutative dynamics with $κ$-plane noncommutativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15261)
*Alessandro Moia,Stefano Stocchetti,Giovanni Amelino-Camelia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了首个完全自洽且完全相对论性的第一量子化模型，描述两个粒子在具有"时间交换κ-平面"（time-commutative κ-plane）类型的非对易时空（noncommutative spacetime）中传播与相互作用。该模型完整刻画了形变的庞加莱对称代数（deformed Poincaré symmetry algebra）及其伽利略极限（Galilean limit），建立了携带形变伽利略代数（deformed Galilei algebra）不可约表示的单粒子量子模型，并给出了两个通过形变谐振势相互作用的量子粒子的两种一致伽利略相对论描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时空非对易性及其关联的相对论对称性形变在量子引力现象学中备受关注，但相关数学结构的物理意义仍存在争议，关键环节缺失或理解不足。此前有建议认为，通过设计恰当的第一量子化（first-quantized）玩具模型可获得重要洞见，但已有研究多为启发式且未能完整描述形变相对论对称性。

Method: 本文严格遵循第一量子化方法，构建了时间交换κ-平面非对易时空上的两粒子传播与相互作用模型。具体步骤包括：完整刻画形变庞加莱对称代数及其伽利略极限；建立携带形变伽利略代数不可约表示的单粒子量子模型；在伽利略相对论框架下给出两粒子通过形变谐振势相互作用的两种一致描述。

Result: 成功获得了形变庞加莱对称代数的完整表征及其伽利略极限；构建了单粒子量子模型并实现了形变伽利略代数的不可约表示；给出了两粒子系统在形变谐振势作用下的两种一致伽利略相对论描述，发现两粒子对称性生成元（symmetry generators）的结构与相互作用律的形变密切关联。

Conclusion: 本文实现了首例完全自洽且完全相对论性的非对易时空第一量子化两粒子模型，弥补了此前研究的不足，为非对易时空与形变相对论对称性的物理理解提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: In the last decades, spacetime noncommutativity and the associated deformations of relativistic symmetries have attracted a lot of interest, as several phenomenological windows into quantum gravity are approaching genuine Planck-scale sensitivity. However, the physical significance of the mathematical structures introduced to deal with spacetime noncommutativity is still debated, and some crucial pieces are missing or poorly understood. From time to time it has been suggested that valuable insight into these conceptual challenges could come from the analysis of appropriately designed first-quantized toy models, in which major technical and interpretive issues can be effectively managed or sidestepped altogether. In this paper we take seriously this suggestion and develop the first fully consistent and fully relativistic first-quantized model of two particles propagating and interacting on a noncommutative spacetime. The specific spacetime noncommutativity implemented in our model, which we call 'time-commutative $κ$-plane', had already been proposed as a suitable arena for a first-quantized analysis, but previous studies were mostly heuristic and failed to provide a full description of the deformed relativistic symmetries. We here go much beyond those pioneering attempts: we find a full characterization of the appropriate deformed Poincaré symmetry algebra as well as its Galilean limit; we build a single-particle quantum model carrying an irreducible representation of the deformed Galilei algebra; we exhibit two consistent, Galilean-relativistic descriptions of a system of two quantum particles interacting via a deformed harmonic potential, finding that the structure of the two-particle symmetry generators is intimately connected with the deformation of the interaction law.

</details>

### [178] [Spinless charged excitation at the interface between a conventional topological insulator and a topological Mott insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14221)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索两种拓扑不同的绝缘相——整数量子霍尔相与手征自旋液体相——之间的界面（interface）物理，揭示该界面可能承载的新奇激发模式。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法对三角晶格Hofstadter-Hubbard模型进行大规模计算；通过空间变化的相互作用强度（spatially varying interaction strength）在模型的不同空间区域分别实现整数量子霍尔态和手征自旋液体态，并利用电荷泵浦（charge pumping）、自旋泵浦（spin pumping）及低能激发态的直接计算来识别界面和体相激发。

Result: 在整数量子霍尔-手征自旋液体界面处发现了一种无自旋的带电激发（spinless charged excitation），该激发被束缚在界面上；在手征自旋液体相中观察到分数化（fractionalization）现象；在整数量子霍尔相中发现了自旋三重态激子（spin-triplet exciton）的形成。

Conclusion: 界面束缚的无自旋带电激发是两种拓扑绝缘相界面的关键特征，手征自旋液体中存在分数化激发，整数量子霍尔相中则存在自旋三重态激子，丰富了人们对拓扑相界物理以及相关强关联体系的认识。

Abstract: We investigate the interface separating two topologically distinct insulating phases of matter using extensive density-matrix renormalization group calculations to study the triangular-lattice Hofstadter-Hubbard model with a spatially varying interaction strength, chosen to realize both integer quantum Hall and chiral spin liquid states in different spatial regions. We find that the integer quantum Hall-chiral spin liquid interface hosts a spinless charged excitation that is bound to the interface. This mode at the interface is identified through charge and spin pumping, and by direct calculations of low-lying excited states. We also characterize bulk excitations in both phases, finding evidence for fractionalization in the chiral spin liquid and for spin-triplet exciton formation in the integer quantum Hall phase.

### [179] [AutoHF: a general Hartree-Fock solver utilizing direct energy minimization with automatic differentiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14263)
*Ryan Levy,Brandon Eskridge,Lukas Weber,Miguel A. Morales,Shiwei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了 autohf，一个通用且易于使用的平均场（mean-field）求解器，用于量子多费米子哈密顿量（quantum many-fermion Hamiltonians）。它通过直接最小化变分能量（variational energy）并利用机器学习社区的自动微分（automatic differentiation）与优化工具，自动寻找最优的斯莱特行列式（Slater determinant），从而避免为每个哈密顿量编写专用程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法需要针对每个多体哈密顿量（many-body Hamiltonian）H 破译其平均场（mean-field）形式并编写定制的求解程序，过程繁琐且不通用。autohf 旨在绕过这一步骤，提供一个无需为每个 H 单独编程的通用解。

Method: autohf 采用变分方法（variational approach），直接最小化变分能量 $\langle H \rangle$，以轨道系数（orbital coefficients）为变量、在对称性约束（symmetry constraints）下寻找最优斯莱特行列式（Slater determinant）。该方法利用了机器学习社区发展的自动微分（automatic differentiation）与优化工具。

Result: 摘要未报告具体的数值或实验对比结果，仅描述了 autohf 作为通用平均场求解器的功能特性：通用性、易用性，以及能够自动完成原本需要人工定制的求解过程。

Conclusion: autohf 通过变分自动微分方法，使得平均场求解过程更加通用和便捷，有望降低量子多费米子系统模拟的门槛。

Abstract: We present autohf, a general, easy-to-use mean-field solver for quantum many-fermion Hamiltonians. It allows the user to bypass the process of deciphering the mean-field form for each many-body Hamiltonian $H$ and thus avoid setting up a tailored program for each $H$. Rather, autohf finds the optimal Slater determinant $|Ψ\rangle$, written in terms of orbital coefficients and subject to symmetry constraints, by directly minimizing the variational energy $\langle H \rangle$. By embracing this variational approach, autohf makes use of the growing power of automatic differentiation and optimization tools developed by the machine learning community.

</details>


### [180] [The two-particle density matrix of a Luttinger liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14402)
*Harini Radhakrishnan,Matthias Thamm,Hatem Barghathi,Bernd Rosenow,Adrian Del Maestro*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过构造性玻色化方法推导了Tomonaga-Luttinger液体中无自旋费米子的等时双粒子约化密度矩阵的封闭有限大小表达式，发现了第二个表征手征间关联的指数λ，并通过与密度矩阵重整化群计算对比验证了其定量准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双粒子相干性是约化密度矩阵层次结构（reduced-density-matrix hierarchy）中第一个包含单粒子可观测量无法获取的关联信息的层级，然而即便在一维系统中，解析的双粒子密度矩阵也极为罕见。因此，需要建立一种能够解析描述双粒子关联的理论框架。

Method: 采用带有显式紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）的构造性玻色化方法（constructive bosonization），推导了Tomonaga-Luttinger液体中无自旋费米子的等时双粒子约化密度矩阵的封闭有限大小表达式。

Result: 除已知的由Luttinger参数K决定的衰减指数γ²=(K+K⁻¹-2)/2外，结果揭示了第二个指数λ=(K⁻¹-K)/2，该指数编码了相反手征性之间的关联并控制非对角结构。双粒子约化密度矩阵的对角极限给出密度关联和静态结构因子，而其相干性则解析描述了排斥相互作用下的2k_F电荷密度波关联和吸引相互作用下的奇宇称p波配对关联。在通过单粒子密度矩阵固定截断后，解析结果定量重现了相互作用J-V链在Luttinger液体区域内的密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算结果。

Conclusion: 该结果将普适的Luttinger液体标度行为与有限微观系统的可观测量联系起来，为理解一维强关联体系中的双粒子关联提供了解析工具。

Abstract: Two-particle coherence is the first level of the reduced-density-matrix hierarchy that contains correlations inaccessible to single-particle observables, yet analytic two-particle density matrices are rare even in one dimension. We derive a closed, finite-size expression for the equal-time two-particle reduced density matrix of spinless fermions in a Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid using constructive bosonization with an explicit ultraviolet cutoff. In addition to the familiar Luttinger parameter $K$-dependent exponent $γ^2=(K+K^{-1}-2)/2$ which governs the spatial decay of matrix elements, the result exposes a second exponent, $λ=(K^{-1}-K)/2$, which encodes correlations between opposite chiralities and controls the off-diagonal structure. The diagonal limit of the two-particle reduced density matrix yields density correlations and the static structure factor, while its coherences resolve algebraic $2k_F$ charge-density-wave correlations for repulsion and odd-parity p-wave pairing correlations for attraction. After fixing the cutoff from the one-particle density matrix, the analytic result quantitatively reproduces density matrix renormalization group calculations of the interacting J-V chain within the Luttinger liquid regime. The result connects universal Luttinger liquid scaling with observables in finite microscopic systems.

</details>


### [181] [Emergence of a monopole phase in the $J_1{-}J_2$ Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice for small magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14766)
*Sasank Budaraju,Shi Feng,Josef Willsher,Johannes Knolle,Frank Pollmann,Federico Becca*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过变分蒙特卡罗方法（variational Monte Carlo）研究了三角晶格上 $J_1{-}J_2$ 海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）在外加塞曼场（Zeeman field）中的基态相图，重点考察零场下在 $J_2/J_1=1/8$ 处检测到的自旋液体相（spin-liquid phase）在外场下的演化。研究发现，在 $J_2/J_1 \approx 1/8$ 附近，孤子凝聚（monopole condensation）态在相图中占据显著区域，该相具有有限标量手征性（scalar chirality）但无横向磁序，且其稳定性得到了包含自洽随机相位近似（self-consistent random-phase approximation）的场论方法确认。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究三角晶格 $J_1{-}J_2$ 海森堡模型中可能存在的自旋液体相在外加塞曼场下的稳定性与相变行为，尤其关注 $J_2/J_1=1/8$ 附近零场下已检测到的自旋液体相在外场中的演化命运。

Method: 使用变分蒙特卡罗方法在 $0 \le J_2/J_1 \le 0.2$ 和 $0 \le H/J_1 \le 2$ 的参数范围内进行系统研究；对若干候选态提出简单变分尝试波函数（variational ansatze），并在大尺寸团簇上比较其能量以构建相图；同时采用包含自洽随机相位近似的场论方法对单极子相（monopole phase）的稳定性进行交叉验证。

Result: 当 $J_2/J_1 \lesssim 1/6$ 时，观察到从无能隙的“Y”相（gapless "Y" phase）到有能隙的“up-up-down”相（gapped "up-up-down" phase）的连续相变，与自旋波理论（spin-wave theory）一致。在 $J_2/J_1=1/8$ 附近，零场下自旋液体中的无质量规范激发（gapless gauge excitations）——单极子（monopole）的凝聚态在小的塞曼场区域的相图中稳定存在，该相具有有限标量手征性但无横向磁序。单极子相与“Y”相之间的边界无需自由参数即可确定。

Conclusion: 三角晶格 $J_1{-}J_2$ 海森堡模型中，在 $J_2/J_1 \approx 1/8$ 附近存在一个稳定的单极子凝聚相区域，该相由零场自旋液体的单极子激发在外场下凝聚形成，具有独特的标量手征性序而无横向磁序，且其稳定性得到了变分蒙特卡罗与场论方法的共同支持。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state phase diagram of the $J_1{-}J_2$ Heisenberg model on the triangular lattice under an external Zeeman field $H$ by using the variational Monte Carlo approach. We span a region with $0 \le J_2/J_1 \le 0.2$ and $0 \le H/J_1 \le 2$, to assess the fate of the (putative) spin-liquid phase that has been detected for $J_2/J_1=1/8$ at zero magnetic field. Simple variational ansatze are proposed for a few candidate states, and their energetics are compared on large clusters to obtain the phase diagram. For $J_2/J_1 \lesssim 1/6$, a continuous transition from a gapless "Y'' phase to a gapped "up-up-down'' phase is obtained, as predicted by spin-wave theory. Most importantly, around $J_2/J_1=1/8$, a condensate of monopoles (which are gapless gauge excitations of the spin liquid at $H=0$) is stabilized in a significant region of the phase diagram, for small Zeeman fields. Here, a finite scalar chirality is present, while no transverse magnetic order is detected. The stability of the monopole phase is confirmed by a field-theory approach that includes a self-consistent random-phase approximation of the low-lying spin fluctuations. The boundary between the monopole and "Y'' phases is also obtained with no free parameters.

### [182] [Monopole Spin Density Wave States in Magnetic Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14829)
*Xi Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）中源自相同手性外尔节点费米面嵌套的粒子-空穴对形成的单极自旋密度波（SDW）序，证明了其序参量具有非平庸配对贝里相位并由单极调和函数描述，同时发现弱耦合极限下配对量子几何张量实现理想量子几何，为拓扑自旋电子学提供新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外尔半金属中拓扑与磁性的相互作用为新型量子相提供了丰富可能性，但现有的单极调和序参量研究仅涵盖超导和电荷密度波，自旋密度波通道尚属空白。本文旨在填补这一空白，引入并表征单极自旋密度波态。

Method: 通过粒子-空穴配对（同一手性外尔节点嵌套费米面之间）构造单极SDW序；利用配对贝里相位与单极调和函数分析序参量的拓扑性质；基于具体晶格模型计算能带、费米弧分布及表面自旋极化模式。

Result: SDW序参量继承非平庸配对贝里相位，其能隙函数具有拓扑保护节点结构；螺旋和摆线SDW序在能带、费米弧和表面自旋极化中产生可区分的特征；弱耦合极限下，配对量子几何张量实现理想量子几何，量子距离涨落完全由贝里曲率决定。

Conclusion: 该工作统一了跨配对通道的单极序态理解，为区分ReAlX（稀土元素与Si/Ge化合物）材料中的竞争磁序提供了实验途径，并启示拓扑自旋电子学中的潜在应用。

Abstract: The interplay between topology and magnetism in Weyl semimetals has recently emerged as a fertile ground for novel quantum phases. While monopole harmonic order parameters have been established for superconductivity and charge density waves in these systems, their spin density wave counterparts remain unexplored. Here we introduce monopole spin density wave (SDW) states arising from particle-hole pairing between nested Fermi surfaces enclosing Weyl nodes of the same chirality. We demonstrate that the SDW order parameter inherits a nontrivial pairing Berry phase and is described by monopole harmonic functions that exhibit topologically protected nodal structures in the gap function. Through a concrete lattice model, we show that helical and cycloidal SDW orders produce distinct signatures in band structures, Fermi arc distributions, and surface spin polarization patterns, which can be directly resolved by spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy. Remarkably, we find that the quantum geometric tensor of the monopole pairing realizes ideal quantum geometry in the weak-coupling limit, where quantum distance fluctuations are entirely governed by Berry curvature. Our results not only unify the understanding of monopole ordered states across pairing channels but also provide experimental avenues for distinguishing competing magnetic orders in ReAlX (Re=rare earth elements, X=Si, Ge) materials and suggest potential applications in topological spintronics.

</details>


### [183] [Optimization dynamics of Transformer backflow neural quantum states for the two-dimensional Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14875)
*Zong-Yu Liao,Jia-Qi Wang,Rong-Qiang He,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Transformer反向传播神经量子态（neural quantum state）在掺杂二维Hubbard模型中的优化动力学，分析了更新范数阈值、Transformer宽度、行列式通道数和蒙特卡洛批量大小等超参数对收敛行为的影响，并验证了该工作流在不同体系下的适用性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用由神经网络反向传播（neural-network backflow）初始化、监督式Transformer预训练以及变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）中的矩自适应重配置启发式算法（Moment-Adaptive ReConfiguration Heuristic, MARCH）主能量优化构成的三阶段流程。以掺杂$4\times4$周期Hubbard模型（$U=8$）为基准，系统测试更新范数阈值、Transformer宽度、行列式通道数和蒙特卡洛批量大小对收敛的影响。

Result: 适度更新约束能提升MARCH优化效率；更大的Transformer宽度和更多的行列式通道数可增强ansatz的表达能力；更大的蒙特卡洛批量可降低更新方向上的采样噪声。该工作流在半填充、弱相互作用、开边界条件以及更大的$8\times8$掺杂晶格上同样有效。

Conclusion: 研究识别了Transformer反向传播神经量子态（Transformer backflow NQS）的实用优化趋势，强调了ansatz表达能力、MARCH更新稳定性与蒙特卡洛采样质量三者之间的平衡。

Abstract: Building on the multi-determinant Transformer backflow neural quantum state (NQS) ansatz and the associated multi-stage training workflow for the doped two-dimensional Hubbard model, we investigate how the optimization dynamics of the NQS depend on several key optimization and architectural hyperparameters. The workflow consists of neural-network backflow (NNB) initialization, supervised Transformer pre-training, and main energy optimization using the Moment-Adaptive ReConfiguration Heuristic (MARCH) within variational Monte Carlo. Using the doped $4\times4$ periodic Hubbard model at $U=8$ as a baseline, we examine how the update-norm threshold, Transformer width, number of determinant channels, and Monte Carlo batch size affect convergence. We find that a moderate update constraint improves the efficiency of MARCH optimization, larger Transformer width and more determinant channels improve the expressive capacity of the ansatz, and larger Monte Carlo batches reduce sampling noise in the update direction. We further test the same workflow at half filling, weaker interaction strength, open boundary conditions, and on a larger $8\times8$ doped lattice. These results identify practical optimization trends for Transformer backflow NQSs and highlight the balance between ansatz expressivity, MARCH update stability, and Monte Carlo sampling quality.

</details>


### [184] [Sizable Ligand-Mediated Bond-Dependent Interactions in a Spin-1 Triangular Antiferromagnet NiI$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14893)
*Hao Xu,Weiqin Zhu,Shufan Cheng,Yanyan Shangguan,Song Bao,Junbo Liao,Bo Zhang,Zihang Song,Shuai Dong,Maofeng Wu,Stanislav E. Nikitin,Travis J. Williams,Changsong Xu,Jinsheng Wen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过非弹性中子散射等多种实验与计算方法，在范德瓦尔斯磁体NiI₂中首次实验证实了由配体离子驱动的Kitaev相互作用机制，为在磁离子自旋-轨道耦合较弱的体系中实现强键依赖各向异性提供了具体路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于键的Kitaev相互作用是Kitaev模型的核心，该模型因潜在承载量子自旋液体态（quantum-spin-liquid states）和分数激发（fractional excitations）而备受关注，但实验上实现此类相互作用的材料仍然十分稀少。

Method: 综合运用了非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）、磁化测量、磁结构分析、第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）以及线性自旋波模拟（linear-spin-wave simulations）等多种手段，对自旋S=1的范德瓦尔斯磁体NiI₂的磁激发进行了系统研究。

Result: 识别出一个包含显著Kitaev相互作用和离对角Γ相互作用（off-diagonal Γ interactions）的最小模型，这些相互作用共同稳定了倾斜磁基态（canted magnetic ground state）并在自旋波谱中打开了能隙。这些相互作用源自配体离子上的强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），尽管磁性Ni²⁺离子的轨道矩已被淬灭。

Conclusion: 提供了配体驱动Kitaev机制（ligand-driven Kitaev mechanism）的有力实验证据，证明在磁离子本身自旋-轨道耦合较弱的体系中也能产生强键依赖各向异性，从而显著拓宽了潜在Kitaev材料的范围。

Abstract: The bond-dependent anisotropic Kitaev interactions are the key for the Kitaev model, which has attracted intense interest for its potential to host quantum-spin-liquid states and fractional excitations. However, experimental realizations of such interactions remain scarce. Here, we investigate the magnetic excitations of NiI$_2$, a van der Waals magnet with spin $S=1$. By combining inelastic neutron scattering, magnetization measurements, magnetic structure analysis, first-principles calculations, and linear-spin-wave simulations, we identify a minimal model that features substantial Kitaev and off-diagonal $Γ$ interactions, which together stabilize the canted magnetic ground state and open a gap in the spin-wave spectrum. Notably, these interactions arise from strong spin-orbit coupling on the ligand ions, despite the quenched orbital moment of the magnetic Ni$^{2+}$ ions. Our results provide compelling experimental evidence for the ligand-driven Kitaev mechanism. This demonstrates a concrete pathway to generating strong bond-dependent anisotropy in systems where the magnetic ions themselves have weak spin-orbit coupling, thereby substantially broadening the range of potential Kitaev materials.

</details>


### [185] [Derivation and application of a general scaling relation between the dc and asymptotic high-frequency optical Hall responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15043)
*E. Abelev,R. Romero,N. P. Armitage*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于 Kramers-Kronig 关系推导了一个通用表达式，将低频频域的准直流霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）与高频光频霍尔响应（及其在 Kerr 和 Faraday 效应中的表现）关联起来，适用于时间反演对称破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking, TRSB）系统，并在铁磁体、TRSB 超导体以及磁场中的金属中进行了理论验证和实验检验。研究利用该关系预测铜氧化物超导体在赝能隙温度下应存在约 0.1 Ω⁻¹·cm⁻¹ 的反常霍尔效应，并鼓励实验搜寻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为时间反演对称破缺（TRSB）态（如铁磁体、TRSB 超导体及磁场中的金属）建立一种普适关系，将难以直接测量的低频准直流霍尔电导率与相对更易获取的高频光频霍尔响应（以及 Kerr 和 Faraday 效应）联系起来，从而为实验探测提供理论工具。

Method: 基于 Kramers-Kronig 关系（Kramers-Kronig relations）推导出一个通用表达式，将低频准直流霍尔电导率与高频光频霍尔响应相关联。通过参数化绘图，在单模回旋共振（cyclotron resonance）的精确情形下验证该关系的严格性，并在铁磁体和 TRSB 超导体的理论模型中检验其近似有效性。最后将该关系应用于多种铁磁体系的实验数据，并用于预测铜氧化物超导体的反常霍尔效应。

Result: 该关系在单模回旋共振的精确情形下严格成立，在铁磁体与 TRSB 超导体的理论模型中近似成立。在多种铁磁体系的实验数据上取得了合理一致。基于该关系，从铜氧化物超导体在赝能隙温度下的自发 Kerr 效应（spontaneous Kerr effect）大小，预测出应存在约 0.1 Ω⁻¹·cm⁻¹ 的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect），属于实验可及的小信号水平。

Conclusion: 研究所建立的 Kramers-Kronig 型关系为从高频光频霍尔响应推断低频霍尔输运性质提供了可靠的理论框架。该预测鼓励实验学家在铜氧化物超导体中搜寻预测的反常霍尔信号。尽管未显式涉及量子几何（quantum geometry），该方法与基于量子几何关系约束物理量的研究思路有相似之处。

Abstract: Based on the Kramers-Krong relations, we derive and apply a quite general expression that that relates the low frequency quasi-dc Hall conductivity to the asymptotic high frequency optical Hall response (and its manifestations in Kerr and Faraday effects) for time-reversal symmetry breaking (TRSB) states of matter like ferromagnets and time-reversal symmetry breaking superconductors as well as metals in magnetic field. Parametric plots shows this relation is obeyed exactly for the trivial single-mode case of sharp cyclotron resonance, and approximately for theoretical models for ferromagnets and TRSB superconductors. We also apply it to the experimental data from a variety of ferromagnetic systems and show reasonable agreement there as well. We use the relation to predict, from the size of the spontaneous Kerr effect at the pseudogap temperature of the cuprate superconductors that cuprates should exhibit an anomalous Hall effect of approximately 0.1 Ohm$^{-1}\cdot$cm$^{-1}$. This is a small value, but one within experimental reach and we encourage the search for it. Although not explicitly quantum geometric, our treatment has some similarities to efforts to set bounds on physical quantities based on quantum geometric relations and limited physical information.

</details>


### [186] [Fast two-dimensional tensor-network contraction via subspace iteration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15158)
*Yining Zhang,Philippe Corboz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于子空间迭代（subspace-iteration）的角转移矩阵重整化群方法（SI-CTMRG），通过QR分解构建投影算子，将原本耗时的奇异值分解（SVD）从大矩阵转移到小矩阵上，显著加速了无限投影纠缠对态（iPEPS）的张量网络缩并过程，在GPU上实现了比标准CTMRG高达两个数量级的加速，并在三角晶格海森堡反铁磁模型上达到了当前最优的iPEPS计算结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准CTMRG是iPEPS的核心缩并方法之一，但其计算开销主要来自重复的大矩阵截断奇异值分解（SVD），在高性能计算环境下存在明显的效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出子空间迭代CTMRG（SI-CTMRG），采用基于QR分解的投影算子构建策略，将大矩阵SVD替换为远小矩阵的SVD，从而将主要计算成本从矩阵分解转移到张量收缩（tensor contraction）上。

Result: SI-CTMRG在GPU上相比标准CTMRG实现了高达两个数量级的加速；在三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体（triangular-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet）上，单块H100 GPU仅需约10小时即可达到当前最优的iPEPS结果。

Conclusion: SI-CTMRG通过重构CTMRG的核心线性代数操作，显著降低了计算复杂度并天然适配GPU加速，为大尺度iPEPS模拟提供了一种高效的替代方案。

Abstract: The corner transfer matrix renormalization group (CTMRG) is one of the standard contraction methods for infinite projected entangled-pair states (iPEPS), but its computational cost is dominated by repeated truncated singular value decompositions (SVDs). We introduce subspace-iteration CTMRG (SI-CTMRG), a QR-based projector construction that replaces each large-matrix SVD with an SVD of a much smaller matrix. The resulting algorithm shifts the dominant cost from decompositions to tensor contractions, making it highly suited to GPU acceleration and yielding speedups of up to two orders of magnitude over standard CTMRG. We demonstrate the efficiency and accuracy of the method for the triangular-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet, reaching state-of-the-art iPEPS results on a single H100 GPU in approximately 10 hours of computation.

### [187] [Driven-dissipative superconductivity in moiré heterostructure without attraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15169)
*Tsung-Sheng Huang,Atac Imamoglu,Mohammad Hafezi,Sebastian Diehl*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于驱动-耗散（driven-dissipative）协议的方案，利用二维莫尔异质结构（moiré heterostructure）中的层自由度作为赝自旋（pseudospin），通过光诱导空间操作实现超导配对，并证明局域耗散可自然来源于弱色散玻色模式，从而实现超导稳态制备；反之，在集体耗散 regime 下该系统会表现出早期超辐射（superradiant burst）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不依赖于增强吸引相互作用的超导制备路径，即通过耗散性制备（dissipative preparation）量子序来获得超导态。

Method: 设计了一个驱动-耗散协议，利用双层莫尔平台中作为赝自旋的层自由度，通过光诱导空间操作实现配对所需的赝自旋结构；并利用异质结构中自然存在的弱色散玻色模式提供局域耗散。

Result: 该方案可在二维莫尔异质结构中实现超导作为稳态（stationary state）；在局域耗散 regime 下可稳定制备超导，而在集体耗散 regime 下同一平台会表现出早期超辐射现象。

Conclusion: 驱动-耗散莫尔异质结构是制备超导态的有前景平台，并且揭示了稳态配对（steady-state pairing）与瞬态超辐射（transient superradiance）之间的内在联系。

Abstract: Dissipative preparation of quantum order offers a route to superconductivity that does not rely on enhancing attractive interactions. Here we propose a driven-dissipative protocol to prepare superconductivity as a stationary state of a two-dimensional moiré heterostructure. The key ingredient is a bilayer moiré platform in which the layer degree of freedom acts as a pseudospin, allowing the pseudospin structure required for pairing to be implemented through optically induced spatial operations. This preparation scheme requires local dissipation, which we show to arises naturally from weakly dispersive bosonic modes in the heterostructure. In contrast, in the opposite regime of collective dissipation, the same platform exhibits an early-time superradiant burst. Our results establish driven-dissipative moiré heterostructures as a promising platform for preparing superconductivity, while also revealing a connection between steady-state pairing and transient superradiance.
