### [188] [Fermiology of the kagome compound LuNb6Sn6 probed by de Haas-van Alphen oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15248)
*Tucker Beekmann,Caue Kaufmann Ribeiro,Kyryl Shtefiienko,Jiaqiang Yan,Brenden R. Ortiz,Christopher A. Mizzi,Keshav Shrestha*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过扭矩磁强法（torque magnetometry）、磁化强度（magnetization）和热容（heat-capacity）测量，对近期发现的kagome金属LuNb6Sn6进行了详细的de Haas-van Alphen (dHvA)效应研究。实验发现电荷密度波（CDW）转变发生在T_CDW=85 K，且该转变为一级相变（first-order transition）。量子振荡测量识别出两个主要的dHvA频率F_α~20 T和F_β~200 T，其角度依赖性与椭球状费米面（Fermi surface, FS）口袋一致。Landau扇图分析揭示F_α口袋存在非平庸贝里相位（Berry phase），指示可能的非平庸电子拓扑性质。基于Lifshitz-Kosevich公式的振荡分析获得了各向异性的量子输运参数。第一性原理计算显示狄拉克型能带交叉（Dirac-like band crossings）、平带（flat band）及多个范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities），但基于纯净相的计算无法完全复现实验观测的量子振荡频率，表明CDW诱导的费米面重构（FS reconstruction）对基态电子结构起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: kagome材料因其几何阻挫与电子关联的结合而展现出丰富的量子物态，但对其费米面拓扑与电子结构的全面理解仍需深入。LuNb6Sn6作为新发现的kagome金属，其基态电子结构——特别是电荷密度波（CDW）转变对费米面的影响——尚待系统研究。

Method: 采用扭矩磁强法（torque magnetometry）、磁化强度（magnetization）和热容（heat-capacity）测量进行宏观热力学表征；利用de Haas-van Alphen (dHvA)量子振荡测量提取费米面信息；结合Landau扇图分析贝里相位；使用Lifshitz-Kosevich公式分析温度与磁场依赖的振荡行为；辅以第一性原理计算进行电子结构理论分析。

Result: 确定CDW转变温度为85 K，且热滞回线证实其一级相变性质。识别出两个主要的dHvA频率F_α≈20 T和F_β≈200 T，对应椭球状费米面口袋。F_α口袋的Landau扇图分析显示非平庸贝里相位，暗示非平庸电子拓扑。Lifshitz-Kosevich分析揭示了各向异性的量子输运特性。第一性原理计算发现狄拉克型能带交叉、平带和范霍夫奇点，但无法完全复现实验量子振荡频率。

Conclusion: CDW诱导的费米面重构（FS reconstruction）对LuNb6Sn6的基态电子结构起决定性作用。这些结果增进了对kagome材料费米面拓扑与电子性质的理解，并为该体系中非平庸电子拓扑的存在提供了实验证据。

Abstract: We report a detailed de Haas-van Alphen (dHvA) study of the recently discovered kagome metal LuNb6Sn6 using torque magnetometry, magnetization, and heat-capacity measurements. Temperature-dependent torque and heat-capacity data reveal a charge density wave (CDW) transition at T_CDW = 85 K. The thermal hysteresis observed in both measurements establishes the first-order nature of the transition. Quantum oscillation measurements identify two major dHvA frequencies: F_alpha ~ 20 T and F_beta ~ 200 T, and their angular dependence is consistent with ellipsoidal Fermi surface (FS) pockets. Landau fan diagram analysis reveals evidence for a nontrivial Berry phase associated with the F_alpha pocket, indicating possible nontrivial electronic topology in LuNb6Sn6. Analysis of the temperature and magnetic field dependence of the oscillations using the Lifshitz-Kosevich formula yields electronic parameters that indicate anisotropic quantum transport properties. First-principles calculations provide further insight into the electronic structure, revealing Dirac-like band crossings, a flat band, and multiple van Hove singularities near the Fermi level. Our calculations based on the pristine phase cannot fully reproduce the experimentally observed quantum oscillation frequencies, suggesting that CDW-induced FS reconstruction plays a crucial role in the ground-state electronic structure of LuNb6Sn6. These results provide new insight into the FS topology and electronic structure of LuNb6Sn6, enriching our understanding of the electronic properties of kagome materials.

</details>


### [189] [Single-component twisted $\mathbb{Z}_3$ orthogonal metal in an $e/3$-anyon fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15274)
*Zhaoyu Han,Ashvin Vishwanath,Eslam Khalaf*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过掺杂1/3分数量子陈绝缘体（Fractional Chern insulator）实现的新型非常规金属相——扭曲ℤ₃正交金属（twisted ℤ₃ orthogonal metal），该相可作为任意子超导（anyon superconductivity）的母态，并允许任意手征中心荷（chiral central charge）。配对分数化费米面（fractionalized Fermi surface）可移除拓扑序并产生一系列超导体，其手征中心荷由BdG能带拓扑直接决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超越基于2e/3任意子构建的任意子超导方案，寻找更普遍的非常规超导母态，并理解分数量子霍尔态掺杂后涌现的金属相及其超导配对机制。

Method: 理论构造了扭曲ℤ₃正交金属：电子准粒子权重为零，但存在一个由电荷为e/3的费米子与Dijkgraaf-Witten扭曲ℤ₃规范场（gauge field）耦合形成的明确费米面（Fermi surface）。该相具有谷对称性（valley-symmetric）且谷带隙（valley-gapped），并基于波函数ansatz进行显式构造。

Result: 配对分数化费米面可移除拓扑序，产生超导家族，其手征中心荷由配对e/3费米子的BdG能带拓扑直接设定，物理序参量（order parameter）的角动量被约束为3的倍数。该金属相本身具有“分数费米学”（fractional Fermiology）特征：e/3散粒噪声（shot noise）、反常量子振荡（quantum oscillations）以及介导超导之间约瑟夫森耦合时的6π交流约瑟夫森效应（ac Josephson effect）。该构造可推广至更高Laughlin态但不可推广至Jain态。

Conclusion: 该相可成为任意子超导的母态，实现任意手征中心荷的超导态，超越了传统任意子超导构造框架，并通过谷间任意子排斥（inter-valley repulsion）相对竞争态获得稳定。

Abstract: We propose an unconventional metallic phase emerging on doping the $1/3$ Fractional Chern insulator, which can serve as a parent state to anyon superconductivity with arbitrary chiral central charge. It is a twisted $\mathbb{Z}_3$ orthogonal metal: a state with vanishing electron quasiparticle weight but a single well-defined Fermi surface of emergent charge-$e/3$ fermions coupled to a Dijkgraaf-Witten twisted $\mathbb{Z}_3$ gauge field. It is manifestly valley-symmetric and valley-gapped. Pairing this fractionalized Fermi surface then removes the topological order and produces a family of superconductors whose chiral central charge is directly set by the BdG band topology of the paired $e/3$ fermions, while the angular momentum of the physical order parameter is constrained to be a multiple of three. This scenario provides a route to superconducting states beyond anyon-superconductivity constructions based on $2e/3$ anyons. The metallic phase itself carries distinctive ``fractional Fermiology'' signatures: $e/3$ shot noise, anomalous quantum oscillations, and a $6π$ ac Josephson effect when it mediates the Josephson coupling between superconductors. We construct explicit wavefunction ansatz realizing the phase, and argue that inter-valley repulsion between anyons stabilizes this phase compared to competing states. We show that the construction extends to higher Laughlin states but not to Jain states.

</details>

Result: 证明了散射波算子（scattering wave operators）的存在性与完备性；刻画了解的弱局域（weakly localized）非散射部分的一些性质。

### [191] [Semiclassical measures through Coulomb collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14313)
*Nicholas Lohr*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了吸引性库仑算符（attractive Coulomb operator）能量 E<0 的本征函数序列的半经典测度（semiclassical measure）恰好是能量超曲面 Σ_E 上在正则化开普勒流（regularized Kepler flow）下不变的、由 Moser 构造的概率测度。文章解决了 Keraani 提出的一个开放问题，主要工具包括 Moser-Fock 映射和 Ψ_ħ^0(S^d) 中的算子扩充引理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 问题的来源是作者此前已证明了“若测度在正则化开普勒流下不变，则它是半经典测度”这一方向的结论，而本文旨在证明其逆命题：任何半经典测度都必须满足该不变性条件，从而给出充要刻画。此外，在精确库仑算符（exact Coulomb operator）的本征函数情形下，该结果直接回应了 Keraani 提出的一个公开问题。

Method: 采用 Moser-Fock 映射将库仑问题变换为球面（sphere）上的正则问题，并引入 Ψ_ħ^0(S^d) 中的算子扩充引理（operator extension lemma）。该引理结合标准本征函数浓度界（eigenfunction concentration bounds），允许处理符号在无穷远处非衰减的一般符号类（general symbol class），从而证明半经典测度质量完全从原点反射（reflect off of the origin）。

Result: 建立了充要刻画：μ 是吸引性库仑算符能量 E<0 的本征函数序列的半经典测度，当且仅当 μ 是 Σ_E 上在正则化开普勒流下不变的概率测度。本文还独立给出了逆方向的证明，并证明了在一般符号类下半经典测度质量不会在原点积聚。该结果完全解决了 Keraani 提出的问题。

Conclusion: 半经典测度在库仑系统中的结构被完整刻画，正则化开普勒流的不变性是必要且充分的条件。该工作不仅解决了具体公开问题，也为更一般奇异势（singular potential）下半经典分析的符号类扩展提供了技术框架。

Abstract: We prove that $μ$ is a semiclassical measure associated to a sequence of eigenfunctions of energy $E<0$ of the attractive Coulomb operator if and only if $μ$ is a probability measure on the energy (hyper)surface $Σ_E$ invariant under the regularized Kepler flow due to Moser. The converse was shown in recent work by the author, and the present article proves the other direction (as well as an independent proof of the converse). We prove the main theorem for a general symbol class allowing certain non-decay at infinity, which implies that semiclassical measure mass entirely reflects off of the origin. In the special case of semiclassical measures of sequences of eigenfunctions of the exact Coulomb operator, this article solves an open problem posed by Keraani. The main tools include the celebrated Moser-Fock map along with a technical operator extension lemma in $Ψ_{\hbar}^0(\mathbb{S}^d)$, which utilizes standard eigenfunction concentration bounds.

</details>


### [192] [Sharp decay thresholds in weighted $L^\infty$ for wave kinetic equations with power-law dispersion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14892)
*Xilu Zhu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维空间中具有幂律色散关系 ω(p)=|p|^a 的四波动理学方程，在加权 L^∞ 空间中确定了尖锐的适定性阈值 s_c=4β+3−a/2，分别证明了 s>s_c 时的局部适定性和 s<s_c 时的不适定性，揭示了核的高频强度与共振流形几何之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在精确刻画四波动理学方程（four-wave kinetic equations）在加权 L^∞ 空间中的适定性阈值，理解高频增长（high-frequency growth）与共振流形（resonant manifold）几何结构之间的竞争关系对方程解的行为的影响。

Method: 通过建立全增益-损失碰撞算子（full gain-loss collision operator）的三线性界（trilinear bounds）证明 s>s_c 时的局部适定性；通过构造集中在高低-低-高共振构型（high-low-low-high resonant configuration）附近的初始数据证明 s<s_c 时的不适定性。

Result: 确定了尖锐的适定性阈值 s_c=4β+3−a/2，其中 β 度量碰撞核的高频增长，a 为色散关系的幂律指数。当 s>s_c 时方程局部适定，当 s<s_c 时方程不适定。

Conclusion: 适定性阈值由核的高频强度与共振流形几何之间的平衡决定，并且证明表明在最微妙的参数区域中，增益-损失抵消（gain-loss cancellations）机制是必不可少的。

Abstract: We study four-wave kinetic equations in space dimension three with power-law dispersion $ω(p)=|p|^a$ and collision kernels with high-frequency growth measured by $β$. In weighted $L^\infty$ spaces, we identify the sharp decay threshold $$ s_c=4β+3-\frac a2. $$ For $s>s_c$, we prove local well-posedness by establishing trilinear bounds for the full gain-loss collision operator. For $s<s_c$, we prove ill-posedness by constructing data concentrated near a high-low-low-high resonant configuration. This threshold captures the balance between the high-frequency strength of the kernel and the geometry of the resonant manifold. The proof also shows that gain-loss cancellations are essential in the most delicate regimes.

</details>


### [193] [Semiclassical estimates near threshold energies and resonance counting on Schwarzschild black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15145)
*Thomas Stucker*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了史瓦西黑洞在实轴下方扇形区域内的拟正规模（QNM）数量满足Weyl律，增长阶为Cλ³。为此引入了一种新的拟微分算子演算（pseudodifferential operator calculus），结合复伸缩方法（complex scaling）和椭圆理论，处理了含排斥反平方势的半经典谱问题。此外，作者研究了截断史瓦西预解式（Schwarzschild resolvent）的影响，证明不会导致极点取消（pole cancellations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拟正规模是黑洞微扰理论中的核心对象，描述黑洞受扰动后衰荡信号的频率与寿命。然而，其数量增长规律（即Weyl律）在黑洞背景中尚未被严格证明。本文旨在从数学上证明史瓦西黑洞低能区域QNM计数满足Weyl律，填补该领域的理论空白。

Method: 研究引入了一种新的拟微分算子演算，专门用于处理阈值能量附近的半经典谱问题（semiclassical spectral problems）。该演算中的椭圆理论（elliptic theory）可与复伸缩方法结合，对在无穷远处表现为带排斥反平方势的半经典Schrödinger算子，给出零能量附近的均匀预解式估计（uniform resolvent estimates）。将该方法应用于Regge-Wheeler势，推导出高角动量QNM的缺失特性。最终结合Hitrik与Zworski近期得到的渐近描述，导出计数增长律。

Result: 研究结果包括：1）史瓦西黑洞在实轴下方小扇形区域内的QNM数量，当模长不超过λ时，增长阶为Cλ³，确证了Weyl律成立；2）高角动量QNM在一个半径随角动量线性增长的圆盘内不存在；3）对史瓦西预解式在远离事件视界处进行截断，不会导致任何极点取消。

Conclusion: 本文从严格数学上证明了史瓦西黑洞拟正规模计数的Weyl律，所发展的新拟微分算子演算和均匀预解式估计方法有望推广至其他黑洞背景或更一般的色散系统（dispersive systems）。此外，预解式截断不会改变极点结构的结论，对数值计算和近似方法具有指导意义。

Abstract: We prove a Weyl law for the number of quasinormal modes (QNM) of a Schwarzschild black hole contained in a sector below the real axis. This requires introducing a new pseudodifferential operator calculus tailored to the study of semiclassical spectral problems near threshold energies. Elliptic theory in this calculus can be combined with the method of complex scaling to give uniform resolvent estimates near zero energy for operators that behave at infinity like a semiclassical Schrödinger operator with a repulsive inverse-square potential. Applied to the Regge-Wheeler potential, our methods imply the absence of high angular momentum QNM from a disc whose radius grows linearly with the angular momentum. Together with the asymptotic description of Schwarzschild QNM recently obtained by Hitrik and Zworski, this shows that the number of QNM contained in a small sector below the real axis and with modulus bounded by $λ$ grows as $Cλ^3$. We also study the effect of cutting off the Schwarzschild resolvent away from the event horizon and show that such a cutoff does not lead to any pole cancellations.

</details>

### [194] [Lyapunov spectrum scaling transition for quasiperiodic nonlinear unitaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14549)
*Xiaodong Zhang,Barbara Dietz,Sergej Flach*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文研究了准周期势（quasiperiodic potentials）下热弱非线性幺正映射（thermal weakly-nonlinear unitary maps）的Lyapunov谱标度（Lyapunov spectrum scaling），发现其从长程到短程标度的交叉（crossover）相对于安德森无序（Anderson disorder）案例被显著延迟，提示准周期局域本征态的长程关联（long-range correlations）在相互作用存在时仍可能产生影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准周期势对非线性系统Lyapunov谱标度行为的影响，并与经典安德森无序情形进行对比，以理解局域化长度（localization length）ξ变化时标度交叉行为差异的物理起源。

Method: 通过数值计算分析准周期势下热弱非线性幺正映射的Lyapunov谱标度，并对比线性情形下本征态的统计分析，以评估准周期势与安德森无序对局域化效应的区别。

Result: 线性情形的统计比较显示，在相同局域化长度ξ下，准周期势具有更强的局域化效应；然而在非线性情形中，准周期势下从长程到短程标度的交叉相比安德森无序被强烈延迟，仅在异常小的ξ值下才被观测到。

Conclusion: 这些发现暗示准周期局域本征态的长程关联可能对此延迟现象起关键作用，并且这种关联在相互作用存在时（即使打破可积性并导致热化）仍可能持续存在。

Abstract: We study the Lyapunov spectrum scaling of thermal weakly-nonlinear unitary maps in the presence of quasiperiodic potentials. We search for the crossover from long-range to short-range scaling as the localization length ξ decreases and compare the details to the case of uncorrelated Anderson disorder [Phys. Rev. Res. 6 L012064 (2024)]. A comparative statistical analysis of the eigenstates for the linear case shows that quasiperiodicity has a stronger localization impact at the same value of ξ. Therefore we expect that the scaling crossover should be enhanced as well. However, the numerical analysis shows that it is strongly delayed as compared to Anderson disorder, and is observed at anomalously small values of ξ. These findings hint at the potential impact of long range correlations of quasiperiodic localized eigenstates, which persist in the presence of interactions even in the case of integrability breaking and thermalization.

</details>

### [195] [Fermion-doubling problem in Chiral discretizations of Quantum field theory: Definitive proof, Fixing, and Computation of two-point correlation function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14874)
*Dogukan Bakircioglu,Pablo Arnault*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了用于量子模拟与量子场论（尤其是量子电动力学）基础的狄拉克量子胞元自动机（Dirac QCA）确实存在费米子加倍（FD）问题，但其严重程度仅为标准离散时间格点规范理论（LGT）的三分之一。文中给出了(1+1)D Dirac-QCA的两点关联函数（格林函数）的简洁解析形式，并将其与连续时间LGT在近似连续极限方面的表现进行了定性与定量比较。此外，还计算了通过添加人工味道解决FD问题的Flavored Dirac QCA（FQCA）的格林函数，其结构极为简单，可直接由原模型格林函数的四个手征分量表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确认Dirac QCA（已被用于量子模拟与量子电动力学(QED)的算法基础）是否存在费米子加倍(FD)问题，并量化其严重程度；同时评估该模型在远离连续极限时（受实验条件限制）对狄拉克方程的近似质量。

Method: 在(1+1)D  Dirac-QCA模型中严格证明了费米子加倍(FD)的存在，推导了单时间步的两点关联函数（格林函数）的解析形式；并将其与标准离散时间格点规范理论(LGT)以及连续时间LGT的空间离散化方案进行对比。

Result: Dirac QCA确实存在费米子加倍(FD)，但其严重程度仅为标准离散时间LGT的三分之一。Dirac QCA的格林函数具有惊人的简洁性，与狄拉克方程的格林函数形成鲜明对比。在远离连续极限时，Dirac QCA在极端相对论区表现更优，而连续时间LGT在非相对论区表现更优。FD修正后的Flavored Dirac QCA(FQCA)的格林函数结构极为简单，可用原模型GF的四个手征分量简洁表达。

Conclusion: Dirac QCA虽然存在费米子加倍，但其加倍效应比标准格点规范理论更轻，且其格林函数的简洁性使其在量子模拟中具有优势。Flavored Dirac QCA (FQCA)通过仅引入人工味道而非手征交错的方式，成功修正了FD问题，且其格林函数保持了极简结构。

Abstract: We give the definitive proof that the Dirac Quantum Cellular Automaton (QCA) used for both quantum simulation and algorithmic foundations of Quantum Field Theory (QFT), and especially of Quantum Electrodynamics (QED), as put forward in References https://doi.org/10.1007/s11128-019-2555-4 and https://doi.org/10.22331/q-2023-11-08-1179, does exhibit Fermion Doubling (FD), albeit thrice as less severe as discrete-time standard Lattice Gauge Theories (LGTs) -- as shown in Reference arXiv:2505.07900 -- , which are naive regarding the spacetime discretization of differential operators acting on fermionic fields. The proof is done for the $(1 + 1)$D Dirac-QCA model. We show that the (one-time-step) two-point correlation function, also called Green's function (GF), of the Dirac QCA, is of astonishing simplicity, which is in contrast with the GF of the Dirac equation. We also compare, both qualitatively and quantitatively, this Dirac QCA to the continuous-time-LGT spatial discretization of Dirac fermions regarding how well these two lattice models approximate their naive continuum limit -- which is nothing but the Dirac equation -- even when far away from that limit, a situation which must be considered because of experimental limitations in quantum simulation -- : the Dirac QCA is better for ultrarelativistic regimes, whereas continuous-time LGT is better for non-relativistic regimes. In a second part of this work, we compute the GF of the FD-fixed model put forward in the last cited reference, called Flavored Dirac QCA (FQCA) -- which staggers an extra, artificial flavor \emph{only}, on a diamond spacetime lattice, and does not stagger chirality as staggered fermions in usual LGT. The structure of this FQCA two-point correlation function is of extreme simplicity, and can be expressed in a very simple manner in terms of the four chiral components of the FD-suffering, original-model GF.

</details>
